jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvaliḥ namo gurubhyaḥ śāstrakṛdbhyaśca  nibandhakartṛparicayaḥbhāratīyadārśanikeṣu jñānaśrīnāmnā prasiddhau dvāvācāryāvāstām  tayoḥ kāśmīrābhijanaḥ pramāṇaviniścayavyākhyātā bhūyasāṃ bauddhaśāstragranthānāṃ bhoṭabhāṣānuvāda vidhāyakojñānaśrībhadronyataraḥ itaraśca gauḍadeśodbhavo vikramaśīlācārya suvikhyātakītirjñānaśrīmitraḥ  anayodvitīyotrādhikṛtaḥ  kutracidasya jñānaśrīnāmnā nirdeśaḥ kutraciccajñānaśrīmitranāmnā  svagranthapuṣkiāsu tu mahāpaṇḍitācāryajñānaśrīmitrapāda ityupādhi maṇḍitaṃ tasya nāmadheyamāyāti  vaṅgamagadhamaṇḍaleśvareṇa dharmapālena pratiṣṭhite tadanvavāyasaṃbhavairupalālite ca vikramaśīlāmahāvihāre bhāratetaradeśebhyopi vidyārthino vividhavidyāvāptaye samājagmuḥ śāstrāṇi tu sarvāṇi bauddhapramukhānyadhigamya bahuśrutebhya ācāryebhyastebhāratavarṣasyādhyātmikasampadā svaṃ svaṃ deśamalaṃcakruḥ  śrūyate ekādaśe sṛṣṭaśatake vidyāvihāretra catvāro dvārapaṇḍitāḥ dvau ca mahāstambhau babhūbuburiti  jñānaśrīmitraśca teṣudvitīya mahāstambhapadaṃ bhūṣayāmāsa ādāvayaṃ jñānaśrīmitraḥ saindhavasampradāyabhuktaḥ śrāvaka āsīt tadanu ca tantrayānamāśritavāniti śrūyate  āsīdatra mahāvihāre saindhavānāmatiprābalyam  kadācittantragranthā herukapratimā ca kācit tairvahāvāhutīkṛtāḥ  rājñā ca te na daṇḍitāḥ eteṣu saindhaveṣu śrīmitranāmadhāriṇo janā dṛśyante  vaṅgadeśodbhavaistantrayānānusāribhireteṣāṃ vivāda itivṛttaviśruta eva bhoṭadeśīya granthebhyo jñānaśrī mitramadhikṛtyaitadanyacca vivaraṇaṃ samupalabhyate  svadeśeviśuddhabauddhadharmapracāraṇāparāyaṇena bhoṭamahīpena hra lā ye śe od ityākhyena vikramaśīlācāryaṃ dīpaṅkaramatīśamāmantrayituṃ svajanāḥ preṣitāḥ  parijñāya teṣāṃ vikramaśīlāgamanakāraṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca rājopāyanādikaṃ rājasammānalābhāya vā dhanasañcayanārthaṃ vā bhoṭadeśagamanaṃ na tadā svīkṛtavānācārya   anantarametadarthaṃ punarāgatebhyo bhoṭadeśīyebhyo rājñastasyadharmārthaṃ dhanasaṃgrahaparasya śatrubhirbaṃndhanaṃ kārāgāre jīvanāvasānaṃ ca viditvā karuṇāparavaśodīpaṅkaraḥ saddharmapracārāya duḥkhasaṅkalāṃ bhoṭadeśayātrāmaṅgīcakāra  ime ca bhoṭadeśīyānāropāntasya saṃvardhanāṃ vikramaśīlāyāṃ pratyakṣīcakruḥ  ativṛddhoyamācāryotīśasya dakṣiṇaṃprastāvanāṃjñānaśrī mitrasya ca vāmaṃ bāhumāśritya śivikātovatatāra  bhoṭadeśāya prasthānātpūrvaṃ dīpaṅkaro jñānaśrīmitrād guhyamupadeśamadhigamya tadanuṣṭhitavānityapi śrūyate etebhyo jñānaśrīmitrasya vikramaśīlāyāṃ maryādātirekaḥ parijñāyate dīpaṅkarastūnaṣaṣṭivarṣadeśīya ekacatvāriṃśadadhikaikasahasrata me khuṣṭa saṃvatsarevasantata bhārataṃ varṣaṃ tatyāja  tatkāle jñānaśromitropi svīyapāṇḍityena granthanirmāṇanaca parāṃ prakhyātimadhijagāmeti śakyānumānam upalabhyamānānāṃ jñānaśrīmitranibandhānāṃ pariśīlanāj jñāyate vācaspatipramukhānāṃnaiyāyikānāṃ sandarbhāstena nāmagrāhamuddhṛtāḥ khaṇḍitāśceti  vācaspatestu nyāyasūcīnibandhanirmāṇakālastasyaiva svavacasā vasvaṅkavasuvatsara iti vijñāyate  paraṃ tu vatsa royaṃvikramābdaṃ vā nirdiśati śakābdaṃ veti vipratipattisthānaṃ paṇḍitānāmāsīt  adhunāśakasaṃvatsara eva vācaspatinollikhita iti nipuṇagaveṣaṇayā nirdhāritam nyāyavārtikatātparyaṭīkāyāṃ      jarannaiyāyikasya jayantabhaṭṭasya mataṃvācaspatinā parāmṛṣṭamiti tātparyapariśuddhāvudayanācāryokti  jayantaśca kāśmīrādhipasyaśaṅkaravarmaṇomātyapadamalaṃ cakāreti jayantakṛtādāgamaḍambaranāṭakāt parijñāyate  ayaṃśaṅkaravarmā sṛṣṭīyapañcāśītyadhikāṣṭaśatatamāndād prabhṛti dvayadhikanavaśatatamābdaṃ yāvatkāśmīramahīṃ bhunakti smetītivṛttavidāṃ matam  nyāyavārtikatātparyaṭīkāpariśiṣṭabhūtonyāyasūcīnibandhastu tadanusāraṃ na vasvaṅkavasumite vikramānde   khuṣṭadhabde janimarhati paraṃ tu tatsaṃkhyakaśakasaṃvatsare   vṛḥ  iti draṣṭavyam  vācaspatināsvagranthānāmanukramo bhāmatyāṃ pradarśitaḥ  tadanusāraṃ nyāyagranthadvitayānantaramapi tena ratnakīrtinā sahodayanācāryakṛtiṣu khaṇḍita ityagrepradarśanīyamasmābhiḥ  ratnakīrtiḥ svagurorgranthānāṃ sārasaṅkalanaṃ kṛtavāniti tannibandhabhūmikāyāṃ pradarśitam  ataevodayanonayoḥ kanīyān na granthaparyālocanātaḥspaṣṭībhavati  pramāṇavārtikasthailokaviśeṣa  vyākhyāvasare svagurortamapi pradarśitametena  suvarṇadvīpavāsino dharmapālācāryasya śiṣyatvasvīkāropyasya śrūyate  svasampradāya sthiravratakena Stcherbatskyprajñākarānuyāyināṃ tredhā vibhāga pradarśitaḥ  teṣu vibhāgeṣu jino ravigupto yamāriścapravaktāraḥ saṃjātāḥ  prajñākara śiṣyo ravigupto jñānaśrīsamakālaṃ kāśmīreṣūvāsa  yamāriścakāśmīrakasya jñānaśriyaḥ śiṣyaḥ kāryakṣetraṃ cāsya vaṅgeṣviti tena pratipāditam  atharaviguptakṛtijinena svagranthe khaṇḍitā jinakṛtiśca yamāriṇā iti tata eva śrūyate jñānaśrīmitrastu kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasyāntime bhāge kañcanācārya ravināmānaṃ dvedhānāmagrāhaṃ sasammānaṃ collikhati  etaṃ viṣayaṃ manasi nidhāya raviguptajñānaśrīyamāriṇāṃparasparasaṃbandhaḥ punarvivecanamarhati  sarvaṃ ime vaṅgamagadhapracalite prajñākarīye prasthānentarbhūtā na veti raviguptayamāryorantarā ca jñānaśrīmitrasya sthānamuta jñānaśrībhadrasyeti capunaravekṣaṇīyam  atra nirṇayastu jñānaśrīmitranibandhaiḥ saha bhoṭabhāṣānuvādanibaddhābhyāṃraviguptasya yamāreśca kṛtibhyāṃ sādhyena tulaneneva saṃbhāvyate  upalabdhanibandhaparicayaḥupalabdhānāṃ jñānaśrīmitranibandhānāṃ kaścit paricayotrāpekṣita iti kṛtvāsvalpaparisareṇaiva sa prastūyate prastāvanā kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyākhyaḥ sarveṣāṃ vastūnāṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanaparo mukhyatamo jñānaśrīmitranibandhaḥ  eṣa ca granthāntarasyādhyāyaviśeṣa iti na mantavyam  etasyaiva catvāraḥparicchedāḥ santi  atra nyāyavedistambhabhūtānāṃ śaṅkarabhāsarvajñatrilocanavācaspatīnāṃmatāni samunmūlya svamataṃ sthāpitamiti granthakṛtā kaṇṭhata evāpāditam  dṛśyate cātratattanmatāni proddhṛtya bāhulyena khaṇḍitānīti yat sat tat kṣaṇikaṃ yathā jaladhara  santastu bhāvā imesattā śaktirihārthaṃkarmaṇi miteḥ siddheṣu siddhā na sā nāpyekaiva vidhānyadāpi parikṛnnaiva kriyā vā bhaveddvedhāpi kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṃgatirataḥ sādhye ca viśrāmyati ityādimaśloke śāstrārtha saṃgṛhītaḥ  tataścaturṣu paricchedeṣu pakṣadharmānvayavyatirekāhetukavināśādhikārākhyeṣu sthiravādaṃ dīrghaviśleṣaṇena khaṇḍayitvā svamataṃ pratiṣṭhāpitam vicāraścātra pūrṇāṅgo mārmikaśca  vyāpticarcā tu bauddhopajñavyāptisvarūpa pradarśanaparo nibandha  vyāptiścabhāratīyadarśanaprasthāneṣu cārvākān prahāya sarvaiḥ svīkriyate  kiṃ tu tasyā mūlaṃ svarūpaṃcādhikṛtya teṣu matabhedo vartatetarām  naiyāyikā vyabhicārājñānaṃ sahacārajñānaṃ cavyāptiniścayopāya iti kathayanti bauddhāśca tādātmyatadutpattibhyāmabhāvena ca vyāptimupapādayanti  atra tu prāsaṅgike vicāre trilocanavācaspatiprabhṛtīnāṃ matānyuddhṛtyakhaṇḍitāni  ante ca pratyakṣānupalambhasaṃbhavaiva hetuphalabhāvasvabhāvavyāptisiddhiritiniṣkarṣaḥ pradattaḥ  jñānaśriyo nibandhāvalau bhedābhedaparīkṣā hastratamā  jñānajñeyayoḥ saṃbandhavicārosyā viṣaya iti bhāti  tayorbhedameke āmananti aikyaṃ cāpare  pakṣayorubhayorapidoṣāḥ pradiṣṭā itītare bhedābhedapakṣamurarīkurvanti  bhedasvīkāreṇābhedapakṣasya abhedāvalambanena ca bhedapakṣasya doṣā apayantīti teṣāmāśaya  siddhāntastu jñānaśriyobhedapakṣapātī bhedābhedasvīkāre ubhayapakṣaparidṛṣṭadoṣāṇāṃ sannipātāpatteḥ  anupalabdhirahasyamapi kṣudramākāreṇa bauddhadārśanikasvīkṛtāyā anupalabdhelaṃkṣaṇaṃ bhedāśca samāhṛtya śāstragranthebhyotra carcitāni prastāvanā sarvaśabdābhāvacarcā tvanupalabdhi rahasyasya khilarūpeṇa svīkāramarhatiśabdasāmānyābhāve kāryānupalabdhisāmarthya vivecanāt  śabdasāmānyābhāve ca na siddhātino vimatiḥ prastute kāryānupalabdhisthale svabhāvānupalabdhipratiṣṭhāpanamevātra tasyakṛtyam  apohaprakaraṇaṃ bauddhasiddhāntānusāraṃ śabdārthavivecanaparamatīva gambhīrārthakam śabdestāvanmukhyamākhyāyaterthastanāpohastadguṇatvena gamyaḥ arthaścaikodhyāsato bhāsatonyaḥsthāpyo vācyastattvatto naiva kaścit iti prakaraṇārthasaṃgrāhakaḥ iloko jñānaśrīmitrasya  eṣa grantho bāhulyena khaṇḍita udayanācāryeṇa tadanusāriṇā ca śaṅkaramiśreṇeti bauddhādhikāracarcāniratairavadheyam  īśvaravādastu viśvanirmātunityasya parameśvarasya khaṇḍanaṃ vidadhāti  prathameparicchede śaṅkaravācaspativittokabhāsarvajñatrilocanaśatānandānāṃ jagatkartṛsādhakānimatāni tattadvacasā samupasthāpya dvitīye bauddhadṛśā sāmānyatastatkhaṇḍanam  tṛtīye cavistaravyākhyānam dharmakīrtikṛtapramāṇavārtikastheśvarakhaṇḍanaparasya ślokasaptakasyatṛtīyopi paricchedastredhā vibhakto granthakāreṇa  svasiddhāntānusāraṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvanirṇaya kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhī vihitojñānaśrīmitreṇa  trikapañcakacintetyasyāparaṃ nāmadheyam  dharmayoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvasthāpanadharmottarasyavidhāvupalambhānupalambhānāṃ saṃkhyā nirṇayamadhikṛtya bauddheṣu matavirodhaḥ pañcakapakṣaḥ jñānaśrīmitrasya tu trikapakṣaḥ  gadyapadyanibaddhetra granthe kārikāsu siddhāntaḥpradarśitaḥ gadyabhāge ca tadarthako vicāraḥ  jñānaśrī mitra nibandhe vayameka eva bhoṭabhāṣāyāmanūditobhūt  yoginirṇayaprakaraṇe yogisvarūpaṃ tatpratyakṣaṃ ca bauddhasammataṃ vivecitavānācāryaḥ  advaitabinduprakaraṇaṃ sākāravijñānavādavyākhyānaparam  atra jñānajñeyayostāttvikabhedanirāśaḥ kṛtaḥ  sākārasiddhiśāstraṃ sākāravijñānavādameva mahatā āḍambareṇa prapañcayati dharmaṃkītirasya vādasya pravartaka iti śrūyate  prajñākareṃṇāyaṃ viśadīkṛtaḥ  atra śāstreprastāvanāvādasyāsya vyākhyānaṃ nāgārjunamaitreyanāthāsaṅgādiprācīnācāryasammatipradarśanapuraḥsaraṃsamupalabhyate  dharmakīrteḥ prajñākarasya ca matāni pradarśitāni  ṣaṭsu paricchedeṣu vibhaktamidaṃ śāstram  prathame nirākārajñānavādavivecanam dvitīye saṃkleśavyavadānacarcā tṛtīyemadhyamāvatārapradarśanam caturthe citrādvaitaprapañcanam pañcame svasaṃvedanavicāraḥ ṣaṣṭhe cayogācāravijñānavādena mādhyamakasiddhāntasya maulikamaikyaṃ samāgacchanti  sākārasaṃgrahasūtraṃ tāvat sākārasiddhiśāstrasya padyātmakaḥ sārasaṃgrahaḥ atra tu catvāraḥ paricchedāḥ  teṣveva śāstrasthānāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ paricchedānāṃ viṣayāḥsamāhṛtāḥ  prastutanibandhānāṃ kartṛtvavicāraḥatra kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyaṃ vihāyaikādaśanibandhā mātṛkāmekāmavalambyaiva sampāditāḥ bahutra ca granthakṛnnāmanirdeśa puṣpikāyāṃ nāyāti  ataeva prastutanibandhānāmekakartṛttvasvīkārakāraṇaṃ spaṣṭīkaraṇīyam    kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye puṣpikāsuna granthakārollekha  antimaśloke tenastātparapāragastribhuvane jñāna śriyoyaṃ jana ityatra tasya saṃketa iti pratibhāti  ratnakīryudayanavādidevādibhiḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasthāḥ ilokā jñānaśrīnāmnā samuddhṛtāḥ    vyāptinirṇayastu jñānaśrī mitrakṛtireva puṣpikāyāṃ tathā nirdeśāt  bhedābhedaparīkṣāpi jñānaśrīmitranirmitā tadīyasākārasiddhau tathā kathanāt   anupalabdhi rahasyasya sarvaśabdābhāvacarcāyāśca kartā nollikhitaḥ navetaratra tadupalambhaḥ  apohaprakaraṇastha sandarbho vādidevena jñānaśromitrasyaiveti nāmagrāhaṃ gṛhītaḥsyādvādaratnākare  īśvaravādakartureva granthāntaraṃ trikapañcakacinteti īśvaravāde nirdiṣṭam sākārasiddhiśāstre ca tatkartubṛhadīśvaravādaḥ samullikhitaḥ  trikapañcaka cintāparākhyā kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhirjñānaśrī mitrakṛtiriti tasyagranthasya bhoṭabhāṣānuvādāt parijñāyate prastāvanā ratnakorte sarvajñasiddherādhārabhūto yoginirṇaya iti bhāṣāsāmyād viṣayasāmyācca samāyāti  sākārasiddhī jñānaśrī mitra granthatvenādvaitabinduprakaraṇasyollekho dṛśyate  sākārasiddhiśāstraṃ sākārasaṃgrahasūtraṃ ca puṣpikānirdeśāj jñānaśrīmitrakṛtī eva etat sarvaṃ manasi nidhāya ekāṃ śailī sarvatra cāvalokya vimṛśya caikamātṛkāyāṃsarveṣāṃ samupalambhaṃ dvādaśa ime granthā jñānaśrī mitranirmitā iti nirṇayaḥ svata evāpatati ebhiḥ sahānupalabdhā sarvajñasiddhirjñānaśrī mitrasya samullekhamarhati  sāpi ratnakīrtināsvasarvajñasiddhau vyavahṛteti pratibhāti  sākārasiddhau vyāpticarcāyāṃ ca jñānaśrī mitreṇasarvajñasiddhiḥ kācidullikhitā yoginirṇaye ca jñānaśrīmitrakṛtiḥ sarvajñasiddhiḥ anyatrayoginirṇaye sarvajñasiddheḥ ślokārdhoddhāro dṛśyate  ekaiva sarvajñasiddhirjñānaśrīmitrakṛtāsarvatrāmṛṣṭeti pratibhāti kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye hetuphalagrahaṇe vyavasthitapratisandhātṛvādastu prastoṣyatenekāntacintāyām iti nirdeśadarśanena jñāyate jñānaśrīmitrasyābhipretamanekāntavādamālambyagranthāntaramāsīditi  sā tvanekāntacintā nirmitā na veti na parijñāyate  prastutanibandhānāṃ kālakramaḥsaṃskaraṇetra mātṛkādṛṣṭagranthakrama evānusṛtaḥ  itaretarollekhadarśanāt kutracidanyathābhāvasaṃbhavepi mātṛkāyā ekatvād viparivartanamatra na yuktiyuktam  na ca pūrṇo granthakramonyataḥ kutaścidāgacchati  nibandhāścātra parasparanirapekṣāḥ  udayanācāryakṛteātmatattvaviveke jñānaśrīmitramatakhaṇḍana vidhāvapi nibandhanirmāṇakramo nānusṛta iti lakṣyate itaretarollekhadarśanabalena prāptaṃ granthakramavivaraṇamatra prastūyate anupalabdhi rahasyam sarvaśabdābhāvacarcā yoginirṇayaprakaraṇam sākārasaṃgrahasūtraṃ canibandhāntare nāmagrāhaṃ nopāttāni  ato jñānaśrīmitrakṛtiṣu teṣāṃ kramikasthāna nirdeśona śakyakriya  vyāpticarcāyām apohaprakaraṇe īśvaravāde coddeśāt tebhyaḥ prākkṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasya sthānam  īśvaravādāt pūrvaṃ vyāpticarcā nirmitā tasyāstatrollekhāt sākārasiddhāvullikhitā bhedābhedaparīkṣā tataḥ pūrvaṃ dharmakīrtimudayanaṃ cāntarāsamāgatānāṃ taiyāyikānāṃ bahūni matāni jñānaśrīmitra svanibandheṣu vidhṛtavāniti nyāyaśāstrālocakānāṃ kṛte ime nibandhā bahumūlyā ityatra na vartate saṃśayaleśopi sākaṃ vācaspatiḥ pratidvandvitvena svīkṛta itidṛṣṭacaram prastāvanāudayanakṛtagrantheṣūpalabhyamāneṣvātmatattvaviveka eva prathamaḥ  tatra tvādita ārabhyajñānaśrīmatameva vivicya khaṇḍitamiti jñeyam  satyapi siddhāntabhede jñānaśrīnibandhaiḥ sahāsyavartate viṣayagataṃ sāmyam  jñānaśrīpaṃktyuddhāraḥ tatkṛtaślokoddhāraścātra dṛśyete  ekatra tukaṇṭhataḥ pratidvandvitvena jñānaśriyo nāmollekhaḥ  pravacanavyavahāre khaṇḍanaprakāre cobhayoḥsāmyam  ātmatattvavivekakalpalatākāreṇa śaṅkaramiśreṇa bahudhodayanadhṛtāni jñānaśrīmatānināmagrāhaṃ pradarśitāni  upalabhyante ca tāni prastutagrantheṣvakṣaraśaḥ ātmatattvaviveke kṣaṇabhaṅgabhaṅgastāvat prathamaparicchedasya viṣayaḥ  atra jñāna śriyaḥkṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyagatā viṣayā ādita eva pūrvapakṣatvena samāgacchanti turīyenupalambhavādākhyeparicchedepi jñānaśrīmataṃ khaṇḍitam  īśvarasādhanaṃ sāmānyata ātmatattvaviveke viśiṣyaca nyāyakusumāñjalī samāgacchati  atra prathame granthe jñānaśriya īśvaravādasamālocanaṃsuspaṣṭameva  citrādvaitavādopi jñānaśrīparigṛhītaḥ khaṇḍita ātmatattvaviveke  śaṅkaramiśreṇa tu tatra ratnakīrtimatakhaṇḍanaṃ kṛtamityucyate  vartate ratnakīrterapi citrādvaitavādākhyogranthaḥ  sa tu jñānaśrīkṛtasya sākārasiddhiśāstrasya siddhāntasaṃgrahapara iti dhyeyam kiraṇāvalo kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyānusaraṇena kṣaṇabhaṅgavādasāro grathitaḥ  tātparyapariśuddhīcānekatra jñānaśriyo matāni ślokāyuddhārapūrvakaṃ khaṇḍitāni siddhānteṣu dvayoranyatarasya vā vaiśiṣṭyapratipādanasya nātrāvasaraḥ  parasparasaṃbandha dyotakeṣu ca bahuṣu sandarbheṣu sthajñānaśrīmitraślokaṃ samuddiśatīti bhāti gaṅgeśopādhyāyaśca tattvacintāmaṇau  pratyakṣakhaṇḍe pṛ   kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasthaṃdṛṣṭastāvadayaṃ ghaṭotra ca patan dṛṣṭastathā mudgarodṛṣṭā kharparasaṃhatiḥ paramitobhāvo na dṛṣṭaḥ paraḥ tenābhāva iti śrutiḥ ka nihitā kiṃ vātra tatkāraṇaṃsvādhīnā kalasasya kevalamiyaṃ dṛṣṭā kapālāvalī mādhavācāryakṛte sarvadarśanasaṃgrahe  pṛ   kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyagato yat sat tatkṣaṇikam ityādiśloko jñānajñīmitranāmollekhapuraḥsaraṃ samuddhṛto dṛśyate  atra saṃgrahebauddhadarśana paricchede jñānaśrī mitraprabhāvonyatrāpi prasphuṭaḥ jñānaśrīmitranibandheḥ śaṅkaramiśrasya pratyakṣaparicaya āsīt  ātmatattvavivekakalpalatāyāṃ tenāpohaprakaraṇādvaitabindusākārasiddhisākārasaṃgrahebhyaḥ ślokāḥ gadyasandarbhācoddhṛtāprastāvanāvivecitāśca  vādivinode ca prakhyātānāṃ bauddhācāryāṇāṃ gaṇanāvasare bhadantajñānaśrīrapismṛtaḥ śaṅkareṇa śaṅkarasya kāle bauddhaśāstrasya dhārā niruddhā babhūva tataḥ pūrvameva bauddhavidyāvihārāṇāṃ tadgranthasampradāyasya pakṣadharmādhikāraḥ lb  namo buddhāya ādityabandhoḥ kiraṇairivānyairātanyamāne kṣaṇabhāji loke suptā ivāniṣṭavilāpino tastalaprahārādiva cetayadhvam  yat sat tat kṣaṇikaṃ yathā jaladharaḥ santastu kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanāya  atastallakṣaṇānavadhāraṇaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhipratibandhamādadhīta kārye  kāryāntaradarśane tu tatrāpi tadanumānaprasavaḥ krameṇa kena vāryate  idānīṃtvarthakriyāsamarthasyaiva vastutvamupasthāpitamityucyate  tadapi yat kiñcit anubhave pramāṇāntaracintāyā niravakāśatvāt  dṛśyate hi śāstrīyalakṣaṇānullekhepyabhyāsabhāvitapratyakṣodayamātrād vastutvamavasāyapravṛttiravisaṃvādabhāginīti kimatra kriyatām  evaṃ tu syāt  yadi paramārthatorthakriyāsāmarthyameva vastutvaṃ tadā idamato jāyata iti janmādhiraṇaṃ vastūlikhatā adhyakṣeṇārtha kriyāsāmarthyamevollikhitam  athānyadeva vastulakṣaṇaṃ tadā tadevollikhitam  yathātriguṇamayatvamitaradvājnullikhitā tadabahirbhūtaṃ nīlaṃ nīlagrāhiṇā gṛhītamevātatsiddhamadhyakṣeṇaṃ vastutvamaṅkurā kāryatāvādepi kāryāntarādarśanepi kāraṇasya sādi paṭi a  nosantaḥ ra  halasya a  tāvaditi nāsti ra  dhovidheya ra neti nāsti a  sādhanopapari ra kṣaṇe a prāyaḥ a   tāvastu ra ā naṃ varodha ā   sāmarthanasahameva ā   matarad ra   mavasthāyitaṃ ā  bharita ā kriyātā a dhyeṣaṇārtha ra ā  ṇīmayatva ā ra  meva tatsi a mevā ra nastattamaṅkurādeḥ ra  kāryatāmasvāmi ajñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalaubījāderarthasāmarthyamavasthāpayatīti  kāryaṃvat tarhi bījādikamapi pratyakṣodayādevāstuvastusat kimarthaṃ sāmarthyagaveṣaṇeneti cet  na vai vastuvyavahāre pratyakṣapāṭavaṃ paribhūyārthaśaktimanusarāma tasyā api pratyakṣādhīnatvāt  kiṃ tu kṣaṇabhaṅgamaṅgīkārayitum pratyakṣakṛto hi vastuvyavahāra uktakrameṇa tadatallakṣaṇasādhāraṇoṃ na kṣaṇikatvasādhāniyamena prabhavati  arthakriyāsāmarthyaṃ tu vastulakṣaṇamabhavadapi yatra svayaṃ vartate tatrāvaśyaṃtadanupanīya na svarūpasattāmā viśati  tataḥ sādhanatvenāsya prastāvotra na vastulakṣaṇatveneti sthitam evaṃ jñānepi svarūpasaṃvedanaṃ sattvāvyabhicārīti sarvaṃ pūrvavat  tadanenāpi viṣayasyasāmarthyasiddhiravyāhateti veditavyam  pareṇa hi paravedane bhrāntiśaṅkāvakāśaḥ svarūpavedane punaḥ sarvathā tadabhāva eva  atha svavedane vipratipadyeta tadaikārthasamavāyināpijñānena vedanasvīkāreṅkurādivadeva pareṇāpi svarūpopadhānānna kaścid doṣaḥ  anyathādṛṣṭārthavyavahārahāniḥ sarvathā prasajyeta nanu viṣayajñānayorhetuphalabhāva eva kathamavagantavyaḥ upalambhāt pūrva viṣayasyānupalambhāt  vyatirekabalāditi brūmaḥ  sati ca bāhyerthe sthiretaratvanirṇayārambhaḥ tasmādarthakriyākārikadambakapakṣīkaraṇavat pramāṇagocaracakrapakṣīkaraṇepi nāśrayasvarūpa dvārā dvividhāpyasiddhirasthirasādhanasya athārthaśakteḥ sarvathā sūkṣmavicārāsahatvād a rtha  śaktaṃ sarvamiti kapakṣīkaraṇamkiṃ vā sādhanamiti cet  nanu bījāderaṅkarādiṣu dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ nahi dṛṣṭe anupapannaṃ nāma sarvasya hi vicāranāmnaḥ pramāṇasthānubhava eva sīmā  kiṃ caivamanicchan prāmāṇikaḥ kathaṃdhūmādapi dahanamanumāsyati  jalajvalanayorvātātapaśītātaṃḥ sadṛśīṃ pravṛttimālambetaapravṛtti vā  bhavāneva kathaṃ vā mithyāśaktimāropayatā pareṇa sādhana upanyaste tadabhāvaṃvidvānevaitatparājayāśaṃsī dūṣaṇopanyāsottaritosti  tatrāpyasiddhayādikameva vaktumādriyase na tu jātyuttaram  tadetadāyātam nātmanāpi pratyaya iti  tasmād brūyā kiñcitkenacit pratāritaḥ  durapahnavā tu śaktirartheṣu  sābhāsā cet  saṃvṛttyā na paramārthena astu yathā tathā saṃvṛttyā paramārthena vā kimatra nirbandhena  prastuptaṃ a vāstukimartho ra  sādhanīya ra  svarūpatāmā ra  sādhanake ra viṣayasāma ā  hīti nāsti ra  parato vedane ra  jñānenāsvīkāreṅkurādivade va rasvīkārāṅkurādiva a  jātyuttaraḥ a ttaraṃ rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāraḥmatiḥatha bhāvasāṃvṛtaśaktisamanvayinī kṣaṇikatāpi sāṃvṛtī syānna pāramārthikīti tatrāpyucyate  iha tattvābhyāsobhyudayaniḥśreayasaphalaheturitinityānityādivicāramā rabhante santaḥ tadaniścayebhyāsānupapatteḥ  sa cābhyāsonityeśvarādidattasāhāyakastannirapekṣo vā tatphalahetu syāditīdṛśi prakaraṇe pramāṇaparīkṣādakṣāṇāṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgāvatāraḥ  atra yadi paramapuruṣārthasādhanamaniṣṭaparihāreṇaśaktisthitināntarīyakatayā saṃvṛtireveyam kṣaṇikatāpi saṃvṛtirevāstu paramapuruṣārthopayogenaiva kṣaṇikatāyāmādarāt  kimasmākaṃ paramārthacintayā yatra na pramāṇaprameyavibhāga sādhyasādhanavyavahāro vā kaścit  atha paramārthepyevaṃ saṃbhavati tadā tadā kṛṣṭaḥ śaktisambhavaḥ tadanvayī  vā kṣaṇabhaṅgo na pāramārthikatvamāpatati  pramāṇaprameya vibhāgādyabhāve tu sarvathā caitanyavyāvṛttau svacinmātravyavasthitau vā pakṣadharmatvādyabhāvaniścayakālavat kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhirabhavantyapi na pīḍayati  tatra kṣaṇikatāsiddhiratāttvikīti yastrāsayati sa svargāpavargaphalaprāptirapāramārthikīti kiṃ na trasyati tasmād yāvat sādhyasādhanabhāvavyavahāraḥ tāvat parīkṣākṣamamityeva pāramāthiṃkatvam mūladūṣaṇaṃ  prati sūkṣmavicārāntarasyāsatkalpatvāditi  alamativistareṇa etena yadasthānābhiniveśinā nyāyabhūṣaṇakāreṇa bhāṣyakārīya kāryakāraṇabhāvadūṣaṇaprabandhamutthāpya varṇitam tat sarvaṃ nirupayogamiti pratipāditam  tathāhiyadyetāvata śramasyāsiddhatodbhāvanāyāmevopayoga kimanena kartavyam  asiddhidhaparihṛtā puruṣārthasamīyā vastutattvanirūpaṇapravṛttasya śaktisiddhināntarīyakavyāpāratvāt  tata eva tathā kramākramābhyāṃ kāryotpattirvyāptetyetadapyasiddhamitiyaduktaṃ tadapi niravakāśam  yadapyanena tattadāśaṅkayottarābhimānāt paryaṃnte sāṃvṛtatvārthakriyāpātātarthaṃkriyāsamarthaṃ yat tadatra paramārthasat pra vā   atheti nāsti a  bhāva iti nāsti ra  syāditi nāsti ra  atrāpyu ra  sadāra dṛśī a  tava yadi ra  śaktimiti ra  neti nāsti ra  sambhavatasta a sveti nāsti ra   siddhiśva pīḍayanti ra  tatrā a  parīkṣākṣamamiti nāsti a bhāṣiṇaṃ ā ra  bhāṣyakārya  ā  bhramasyā a  vastutva ra  kāryopapatti rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvaloityuktiveyathyaṃmudbhāvya likhitam  yathā saṃvṛtyārthakriyāsamartha tathā tat paramārthasaditicet  sāmānyāvayavisaṃyogādeḥ kiṃ na tathā sattvamiṣṭam  tasya saṃvṛttyāpyasāmarthya miticetna anvayavyatirekapratibhāsasyobhayathā tulyatvāt  tathāhi yatra yatra cakṣuḥ pravartatetatra tatra taimirikakeśādivanna stambhādipratibhāso bhavatīti stambhāde sāmarthyagatiḥ tathā mahiṣādiṣu gavādyanvayabuddhirna bhavati  paramāṇumātreṣu saṃyogādirahiteṣucāvayavisaṃyogabuddhirna bhavatīti sāmānyāderapi sāmarthyagatiriti  tadapyasāram nahi saṃvṛtirityeva parigrahastyāgo vā bālasaṃvṛterapi grahaṇaprasaṅgāt  paṇḍitasaṃvṛterapiparamapuruṣābrthasādhanapravaṇāyāstyāgaprasaṅgāt  avicāritaramyā hi pratītiḥsaṃvṛtiḥ  asti ca bālakasya darpaṇatalāvalīnasatyavadana graho vicāravidhuraḥ puruṣārthasādhanagraho vā paṇḍitānāṃ tvadvicāreṇa vidhurito na ca tyājyaḥ tatparityāge kṣaṇabhaṅgaparīkṣānapekṣāyā iṣṭatvāt atha bauddhasyāyaṃ vicāro mama tvatrāniṣṭireva  tato bauddhasyaiva siddhānta virodhaḥ sādhanasya ca vādyasiddhatā doṣa iti cet  sa tāvadayaṃ vicāra pramāṇamapramāṇaṃ vā  pramāṇatve tavaivāyaṃ na mameti vibhāgānupapattiḥ  pratyuta pramāṇādbahirbhāvasvīkāre nādhikāra  prativādepi tavetyāyātam  athāpramāṇam tadā yadināmāgamapradeśapratipāditorthaḥ kaścinna samartha   prakṛtasya tu na kṣatiḥ  tadetadāyātam yadi kiñcit kacicchāstre na yuktaṃ pratiṣidhyate bruvāṇo yuktamapyanyaditi rājakulasthitiḥ pra vā  iti  sautrāntikasamayasthitasya hi kṣaṇabhaṅgaṃ prasādhayataḥ sthityantaravirodho nabādhakaḥ  anyathāākāśaṃ dvau nirodhau ca nityaṃ trayamasaṃskṛtam abhidharmakośe ityanena kiṃ navābhidhānam  naiyāyikasya copamānaṃ pramāṇamicchato vaiśeṣikāpekṣayā kathaṃ na siddhāntavirodha  bhinnaprasthānatvaṃ tu samānam  śaktisaṃśrayaśca na iti vyakti ra   miti cetara anvaya ra  vattasta ra  tathā hi ra  govālaṃ sa  vṛte ra  pramāṇāyā ra   syaivāyaṃ ra  riva ra   syāya ra  tavāya ra  māyama rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāraḥsautrāntikanītimatikramya   yadi tu tatrāpi na syāt śaktisthitiḥ tadā svapratibhāsamātramācaṣṭe na bauddhasiddhāntasthita iti syāt  tasmānnayāntaravirodhepi na siddhāntavirodhayogaḥ nāpi vādyasiddhiḥ  na ca vastubalapravṛttānumāne śāstrānurodhaḥ kaścit tadvicāraprāmāṇye tu sāṃvṛtatvepyathaṃśakteravaśyābhyupagantavyatayā tadupanītakṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhibādhitanityābhimatasāmānyasamavāyādikalpanamadharasaṃvṛtitvād bālasaṃvṛtivannopādeyamarthakriyāśaktau  aśaktī sva viṣayajñānajananepyayogyasya sattvābhyupagama saṃvṛtirastukiṃ tvadharatopyadhareti niścayaḥ  ataevādharādharasaṃvṛtyapekṣayottarottarāsu paramārthatvenavyavasthāpyamānāvaśyābhyupagantavyā niruttarārthakriyaiva saṃvṛti paramārtha iti tathā satparamārthaṃsaducyate  tathāhi bālasya darpaṇatale vadanagrahamapekṣyāsadeva vadanamatrakhyātīti paramārtha iti ucyate  tadapekṣayā ca darpaṇapratihativyāvṛttyā netrāṃśavaḥsvamukhameva gṛhṇātīti paramārtha  evamuttarottaraparikalpeṣu balavatsu pūrvapūrvaḥ saṃvṛtiruttarottaraḥ paramārtho yāvadarthakriyāsthitiḥ  tadatikrame hi grāhyagrāhakabhaṅgādāyātaṃ pratibhāsamātravyavasthānamiti kva saṃvṛtervārtā  tasmāt saṃvṛtīnāma antimārthakriyāśaktirevaparamārthaṃśabdavācyeti na saṃvṛtimātratvena sāmānyādisaṃvṛtistatkalām adhirohati tadvicāraprāmāṇyaṃ tu gajanimīlikayāvadhīrya tattvatta eva śaktiḥ paramārthastatra tatrocyate sāmānyādayaśca saṃvṛtisanta iti  evamavayavisaṃyogādayopi saṃvṛtisantastadvadubhayathā veditavyāḥ śakte paramārthatayā nityatābhyupagamatvāt kṣaṇasthitidharmatāyāḥ aṇava eva hi viśiṣṭotpannā dravyadvayaṃ vā saṃyogaśunyaṃ tattadbuddhisādhanamiti kimavayavyādinā  tat kathaṃ sāmānyādiparigrahaḥ saṃvṛtimātratvenārthakriyā samīkriyate yadi ca tāvataiva sāmyaṃ kimupapattighoṣaṇena  mā bhūdhara saṃvṛtitvamiti niyamopanyāsaḥ  tacca śaktisamanvayinaḥ tadādhārasya vā kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṅgamena dunivāram  yathoktaṃprākśaktisamanvayābhāve tadādhārasthāpi saṃvṛtisattve kutastaddharmasya sāmānyāderadharasaṃvṛtitvaparihāra  tasmāt saṃvṛtimātratvameva sāmyam  tatra cokto doṣaḥ  yāceyamupapattirbuddhivyatireko nāma sāpyapohe cintayiṣyate  kramasya ra  stayā a  māviṣṭena a  sveti nāsti a  rtha kena ra vyamānāvasva ra vyasāmarthavaśyā a  ucyate iti nāsti ra  itīti nāsti a nirvikalpeṣu a  bhutkandhā ra   nimīlitena ra  aṇava hi ra  samāyate a  panyāsaḥ a  tinyāpanyāsā ra   kti samarthārthāyina  ra  samarthabhāve ra radharaṃ sa ra  sādhya ṣyate iti nāsti ra  sāpi kṣīṇā nahi buddhimātravyatirekeṇa vyatirekavastusiddhikramaḥ  ki tarhi vastvantarākāraparihāreṇayatrākāra viśeṣobuddheḥ sphuṭataravastutasya yadā nārthasya bāhyavastugrahaḥ tadvaghatirekavyatireka vastukathanamjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauyaccedamūce  kiṃ ca yadyanirūpitatattvā pratītiḥ saṃvṛtiḥ tata eva kāryakāraṇavyavasthitiriṣṭā tathā satyakṣaṇikānāmeva kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ sarvavyavahāriprasiddhonvarthojñeyaḥ kiṃ tatra sūkṣmavicāreṇeti  tadapyayuktam  tathāhi yastāvat tattvata evakṣaṇabhaṅgurabhāvagrāmasādhanāya sādhanamāha sautrāntikaḥ svacinmātrāsthitau sādhanadūṣaṇāvadhānābhāvāt tasya tāttvikameva sāmathyaṃ trividhaṃ pratyakṣānupalambhopalabhyam  kathaṃtasyāyamupālambhaḥ  paraviṣayapramāṇopasthāpitamanyaṃ vā parihṛtya kathamāsitumasausamartha  tāvatā ca tāttvikī kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhirakṣaṇikānāmeva kāryakāraṇabhāvaṃ sāṃvṛtamupapādayati iti kimasyāṅgīkaraṇaprayāsena  na ca vicāra parisphuranneva parihatu śakyachāyādravyatādiniṣedheśvarasiddhayādiṣvapyanādaraprasaṅgāt  tadaniṣṭavādinaḥ pratītasyāpi vicārasya sūkṣmatvāditi kṛtamidānīṃ śāstraparamparāpariśrameṇa  tataśca kiṃ tatrasūkṣmavicāreṇeti vimucya vicāraśvārurasau na bhavati yenākṣaṇikakṣepa iti vaktumucitam tacca na pratijñāmātreṇa sidhyati  asmābhistu nityamatyetuṃ sādhanamupanyastam  na ca tatradoṣaḥ atha prastutasūkṣmavicārādare sūkṣmavicārāntarasyāpyavakāśaprasaṅgo doṣa evayadāha  sūkṣmekṣikayā hi kāryakāraṇabhāvād bheda eva syāt tvaduktāt nyāyāditi idamapi śraddhājaḍasyaiva śobhate  yāvaddhi bhāvānāmarthakriyāśaktiparityāgaṃ na sahāmahetāvadavyāhataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgāṅgīkāro nityanigrahaśca  yadā tu śaktivivecana vibcārāntare ca balavati cetaḥ kramiṣyate tadā kṣaṇikatāvimokṣamapītyakṣamaḥ  samānasvāddaṇḍasya  na caivaṃ śakterupagamo nityatāmanityatāṃ ca pratyujjīvayituṃ śaknoti asādhāraṇatvāt  tathāhi na khalu śaktiriti pramāṇaśūnyameva kiñcit kacit kadācid astītyavimokṣaḥ  ki tarhi  etadvījādikamaṅkarādisamarthamityanenākāreṇa pratyakṣa prativedyatayaiva  tacca pratyakṣaṃ yathānvayavyatireke pramāṇamiṣṭaṃ tathā kāryāṇāṃ kramītaratvepītyevaṃ prakāreṇanyāyena śakti kṣaṇikatāyāṃ viśrāmyantī na nityasādhāraṇīti kathamubhayorapina caivamādhārarūpavyatirekeṇa rūpanirbhāsa  sāmānyādevikalpamātrasya tu kalpite sāmānye kvāpisāmābhyaṃ sāmānya miti  iti prānte kenacid yojitam  a  ddhobhyanujñeyaḥ ra   trividha ra  manvarthā a  śakyate ra  tāni ra dviṣvanā ra  apīti nāsti ra  nākṣaṇikatvakṣe ra  nityamityetuḥ a prasaṅga ra bhāvoccheda ra  syai va śobha ra  vivecini ā  cakāro nāsti a  bhramiṣyate a dhimokṣamaya ra  pratyavayituṃ a  bhramī a  śaktikṣaṇikatāyā ra ranī kathaṃ akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikārapratyujjīvanam  tadevaṃ balavati hetuphalatā bhraṃśaśaṃsinī vicāre śaktisiddhā kṣaṇika vāsti  sā saṃvṛtiḥ  nityatā tvadharasaṃvṛtireveti sāmānyavad bhāvyam  tadvicārabalane tu na kiñcidāśaṃkāsthānamiti siddhaiva śaktiḥ tatkathamucyatetathāpyasiddhatvānna sattvena kṣaṇikatvasiddhi  nāpyarthakriyāyāḥkramākramābhyāṃ vyāptisiddhiriti sāṃvṛtaśaktipakṣepi nirvāhasya darśitatvāt nanu yathā saṃvṛtau paramapuruṣārthaṃ prārthayamānasyopāyānveṣaṇapravṛttasya nārthaśaktimanāśritya sthātuṃ śaktiḥ tathā mayā tatphalalābhinā bhāvyamityupāyānveṣaṇānnityatāgrahopyavaśyamāyāta iti nityopi satsaṃvṛtisanna bhavatu kathamadharasaṃvṛtiviṣaya  nityātmā tucintāntaramarhati  na ca tanmātreṇopagamārhaḥ yataḥ saṃvṛtiviśeṣaviṣaya syāt  evaṃśakti grahonveṣaṇe prayojakostu  śaktyā ki kartavyamityabhidhīta nāma  na tu śakti vyatikramonena vacasā dalitaḥ śakti grahasyopāyānveṣaṇa  hetutvasvīkārāt  natvevamātmaniśakyam  śaktigrahopi saṃvṛttyeva prayojaka iti cet  astu saṃvṛttayā tattvena vā  śaktisiddhau ca  punarātmagrahasyāpi prayojakatvasiddhernāvaśyamātmasiddherākṣepa iti  nirṇayāpekṣaṇe kṣaṇikatvasiddhistadvādhanītyuktaprāyam  hetuphalagrahaṇe vyavasthitapratisandhātṛsiddhivādastu prastoṣyatenekāntacintāyām yadapīdamuktam sūkṣmekṣikayāpi tvanmata eva kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇaṃ naṣṭaṃ bhavatianyenānyasyāpratibaddhasya grahaṇānabhyupagamāt  pratibandhaśca dviṣṭha  pratyakṣeṇādvayagrāhiṇāna gṛhyata ityanumānasya tatrāpravṛtteḥ  asmanmate tu kāryakāraṇabhāvasthāpi na grahaṇānupapattiḥ pratyakṣasyaikakṣaṇaviṣayatvaniyamānabhyupagamāt  tathā ca vyāptigrahaṇa samarthana prastāvesmadādipratyakṣamapyatītānāgatādiviṣayaṃ kadācidadṛṣṭādihetuvaśāt pravartata iti samarthihyanyathā kāraṇatāvādapratīti   saṃbhavatīti  tadapi sakalaṃtam na phalabhāvabhra ra  vāntimāsa ra  tādhara ra  vācya ra  siddhiriti nāsti ra sāṃvṛti ra  lābhināṃ ra  cakārastyaktaḥ ra  darśita ra   ṣaṇe hetu ra  śakti siddhayaiva ra  prayojakatvā ra  prāya a  dviṣṭa ra  pratyakṣe dvaya ra  pravṛttiḥ ra pravartita ra  a  hā  nyathā ra  kāraṇabhāvādi ra  itīti nāsti ra jñānaśrīmitra nibandhāvaloviphalam  tathāhi pareṇa parasya vedanaṃ tāvadubhayorapi kṣaṇiketaravādinoriṣṭam  tatraca yadi pratyakṣeṇāadvayagrahaṇaṃ nāma nyāyaviruddhametat  dvayagrahaṇameva nyāyyam  tathāca sati kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇasya na vyāghātaḥ  kṣaṇabhaṅgavādyapi tathopagacchan  kiyatīṃkṣatimāsādayet  na hyadṛṣṭama niṣṭamevāsya pūrvamapyeṣa siddhāntaṃ svecchayeva gṛhītavān kathañcidanyaṃ sa punargrahītuṃ labhate na kim  pra vā  atha kathañcidadvayagrahaṇameva nyāyyam tadā tadviparītaṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇapravaṇamapi tvadiṣṭimātraṃ kutropayogi atha kṣaṇabhaṅgavāde kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇamapi na prāpnotītyākūtam tarhāṃstikāryakāraṇabhāva iti virodha udbhāvyatām nāsiddhiḥ  tatra ca vakṣyāmaḥ  yadapīdamuktamanādivāsanāta eveyaṃ pratītiriti cet  na atrāpi pramāṇābhāvāditi tatrāpi kāyacittavyatiriktātmadravyasamavāye vastvantaradharmādharmalakṣaṇaguṇaprasādhakamayaṃ pramāṇamupanyasituṃ śakto nāparaścetaḥ śaktiviśeṣaḥ karmetyasya prasādhakamiti mahatī śraddhā cittaśaktireva hi vāsanetyabhidhīyate  tasmādasaṃsṛṣṭakṣaṇamātravedanavādino hi vyavahāra syānādirabhyāsaḥ  tato vāsanā  tato mithyā pratītiriti  etat sarvamandhaparamparāvadapramāṇakamityapi dhandhāndhavilasitamiti mantavyam  asaṃsṛṣṭakṣaṇamātravedanavādī hiprastutaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgavādī sautrāntika ityarthaḥ  tasya kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītiḥ mithyāpratītiriti mahatī bhrāntiḥ  kāryakāraṇabhāvāpalāpī tu yogācāra svasaṃvinmātravedanavādīti vaditumucitam  na ca tasya dūṣaṇena kṣaṇabhaṅgavādinaḥ kiñcit  hetuphalāpalāpinopi yadi tadapalāpāya nyāyasaṃbhavaḥ tadā tadapi na dūramiti kimatra nirbaṃndhena  iti sthitametat yadi kārya kriyāśaktistāttvikī taditarā vā ubhayathāpi nāsiddhidūṣaṇāvatāra iti  pakṣadharmatādhikāro nāma prathamaḥ pādaḥ  phalgu ra  cakāro nāsti ra  ṇāduṣaṇa a  tāva a  kiyatā ra  pravaṇa itināsti ra  grahaṇameva prāpnotītvādbhutaṃ a  samavāyi ra  prasā naya a  rityevatat ra  manvaye a  hi prastutaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgavādīti nāsti ra  tasya ca kāryasya prabhāvaḥ ra ucitaḥ a  yadyeta a  nirbandho nāsthita rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyedvitīyaḥ pādaḥ  anvayādhikāraḥnāpyayaṃ viruddho hetuḥ sapakṣīkṛte jalabhṛti darśanāt sādhyaviparyayavyāptilakṣaṇasya viruddhasya sādhyavati darśanānupapatteḥ  nanu sāhasametat kacidapi dhiyaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgagocarīkaraṇasāmarthyānupalabdheḥ tathāvasāyābhāvāt  na ca pramāṇabalāvalambanādambude kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiḥ  pratyakṣato hi sa evāyaṃ toyada iti pratyabhijñānamasya kālāntarasthāyitāmevopasthāpayati  tadbādhitatvāccānumānamanavakāśam  na cānumānamanyadasti  sattvānumāne ca punanadarśanāntarasamīkṣāyāmanavasthāprasaṃgaḥ  tasmātsapakṣedarśanāt na  virodhaparihāraḥ  vipakṣībhūtembhobhṛti bhāvācca a virodha evānaikāntikatvasyāsattvasya  pakṣe ca kṣaṇabhaṅgapratijñāyā pratyakṣabādhā yadāha śaṃkara b pratyakṣeṇaiva sthitiviparyayābhāvasya siddhatvāditi  nacāyamekatāgrahaḥ pūrvāparakālayorapramāṇam saṃvāditvāt  tathā ca nyāyabhūṣaṇaḥ yathācedamasatkāryaṃmityasyāḥ pratītevisaṃvādābhāvādeva prāmāṇyaṃ tathānenetāni krameṇakṛtāni na yugapaditi pratīteḥ sa evāhaṃ sa evāyaṃ sphaṭika ityevamādipratyabhijñāyāścavisaṃvādābhāvādeva prāmāṇyameṣṭavyam tulyayogakṣematvāditi  tadetadasaṃgatam  aliṅgasya hi vikalpasyā visaṃvādo nāmārthakriyāprāptiḥ pramāṇāntarasaṃgatirvā syāt tatra sa evetyadhyavasāyamātrānnāparapramāṇavṛttiratra  arthakriyāpi naikapratibaddhā  siddhākācit bhinnenāpi tatsamānaśaktinā tādūgarthakriyāyāḥ karaṇāvirodhāt tathāhiyathaiko ghaṭo vāri dhārayatīti tatkālabhāvinopyanyasya na vāridhāraṇam tathā dvitīya kṣaṇepyanyo yadi vāri dhārayati tadā kīdṛśo doṣa syāt  visadṛśakriyāyāṃ tucintaiva nāsti  tasmāt yathā pāvakāde pākādikriyā pratibaddhā siddhānubhūyamānā jalakṛti a janabhṛti ra  cakārastyaktaḥ ra  nāvirodha ra  tathā tāne ra  saevāhamiti nāsti ra  sya vi a  nāsārthakriyāśaktiḥ ra   ti vā a  bandhā ra kāritaḥ a  tadeti nāsti rajñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalaudahanajñānasya saṃvādamāpādayati na tathā prathamacaramakālayore kī bhāvapratibaddhā kācitkriyopalabdhigocarā yayaikabhāvagrahopi saṃvādī syāt cetnayadyapi hi samānaśaktibhirekatvamavaseyaṃ tathāpi sarvairitisarveṣāṃ sarvakādhyavasāyasāmyāt kimaparasaṃvādāpekṣayetiasiddhatvāt na śakyamasarvavidā  atīndriyadarśināṃ suramuniyogināmullaṃghanīyatayā teṣu kaścitkadācit kṣaṇabhaṅgadarśī yadi syāt na virodha   adhikādhikaśaktidarśanaṃ casaṃbhāvanābījam  yadi tu svabhāva evāyaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅganāmā na bhavati na tairgrahaṇamitiyuktametat  tacca nirūpayitumārabdham  ato yāvanna svabhāvasiddhiḥ tāvannasarveṣāṃ kṣaṇadhvaṃsa niṣedhādhyavasāyasiddhi  atīndriyadarśidveṣiṇo hinānupalabdhimātreṇa niṣedhamabhidadhānā   sādhavaḥ atiprasaṅgāt  yogyānupalabdhistudeśādiviprakarṣiṇyasamarthetyāstāṃ tāvat  katipayasaṃpratipattistu taimirikakalitakeśādiṣvapi saṃbhavinī na saṃvādamavasthāpayituṃ śaknoti  etacca pratyakṣāpekṣayocyate anumānatastu kṣaṇabhede bhāvabhedaṃ pratiyantaḥ kimihāpi pariṣadi niṣedhuṃ śakyantetatsādhanābhyāsasya kacidanivāraṇāt  tasmānna sarveṣāmadhyakṣakṛtonumānātmā vāekādhyavasāyo niyamena bhedāvyavasāyaniṣedho veti na pramāṇāntaravat saṃvādasaṃvāditamasya prāmāṇyam lūnapunarjātakeśa kuśakadalakāṇḍādiṣu a vyabhicārācca  yatpunaranena viśeṣavacanābhimāninābhihitam atha visaṃvādinyapi pratyabhijñā dṛśyate kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītiḥ kiṃ visaṃvādinyapi na dṛśyate  yā visaṃvādinī sā kārya kāraṇa pratītireva na bhavati apramāṇatvāditi cet  samānamatrāpi  visaṃvādinīyā sā pratyabhijñeva na bhavati tadābhāsatvāditi syādetat yadi kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītivallakṣaṇabheda pratipādayituṃ śakyeta tathāhi kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītāvapi yadi vastumātreṇa jananaṃ dhūmādegṛhṇīyāt ṣa gardabhādivyabhicāreṇa vahnāvapi hastakaṃ tyajet  evamanvayamātreṇa  vyatirekamātreṇa vāyathāyogaṃ bhāvyam  yadā punaranvayavyatirekagrahaṇapravaṇapratyakṣānupalambhasambhavaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvapratyayaḥ puraskriyate yathā nirṇītamasmābhiḥ trikapañcakacintāyām  rekabhā ra  gocaro a  dāt pakṣa  sye  ti ra  aspaṣṭam a  kṣaṇadarśī a  syānnirodha a   dhāvasāya ra  hoti nāsti a  sabhidadhānā ra  kaṣiṇyastāntāvat ra anumānakṛto ekā ra  nakāratyaktaḥ ra   diṣva a  varṇakṣaṇa ra  aspaṣṭam a arthamātreṇa ra  vyatirekamātreṇeti nāsti a vācya ra   nirjñāta  akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraḥna sthitaṃ tatra nānyasmānātaṃ nāyātamanyataḥ yasya bhāve bhavet kāryaṃ na cettasyāna kasyacit iti tadā tvavyabhicāra   kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhau  evaṃ yadi pratyabhijñānepi lakṣaṇabhedo darśitaḥ syād darśayituṃ vā śakyo vyabhicārāvyabhicāropayogī tadā yuktametat  na caivamasti sarvatrātyantasadṛśa vastuni cāvaśyametāvatā kālena bhrāntibhraṃśopṛthagjana pratyabhijñāyā ekarasatvāt bhavatīti kālaniyama syāt tadāpyucitametat  yāvatā chinnodbhinnakeśapāśādaupuruṣāyuṣakṣayeṇāpi naikatābhramabhraṃśovaśyaṃ yatnavato bhavatyeveti cet na tatrāpiniyamābhāvāt  prayatamānasyāpi hi vacanamātramapramāṇa mupapattyantaraṃ ca durlabham yadi copapattyantaraṃ pratyabhijñāsikatvabādhakam prastutepi kiṃ naivamāsthīyate  kevalaṃpratyabhijñayātītamanumānaṃ varākamasamarthamidānī keśādau tava vacanamātramapi samarthamiti mahatī parāmarśaśakti  bhinnepi keśādāvabhedādhyavasāyadarśanād bhavatu tatrayathākathañcad bhedasaṃpratyaya iti cet  naṃ anyatrāpi bahulaṃ tathā darśanāt  na histambhamekamapanīya niveśite sadṛśe stambhāntare na bhavatyeva pratyabhijñānam evaṃ ghaṭapaṭasphaṭikādiṣvapi yatra yāvadatyantasadṛśalābhaḥ  bhinnakāladarśanecāyaṃ nyāyaḥ  samasamayaṃ tu ayogolakayugalopalambhepi bhavatyeva bhedavyavasāyaḥ tasmāt kālabhedenaikābhimatepi stambhādau bhinna eva kimayamekatvādhyavasāyastambhāntareṇeva  athābhinna iti saṃśaya pratyabhijñāyāḥ prāmāṇyapratiṣedhī kathaṃniṣedhyaḥ atha kṣaṇabhedenābhedasyādṛṣṭapūrvatvāntra saṃśaya iti cet  naitadapi sādhu na hyadṛṣṭamityeva nāstīti śakyate vaktum satopi sūkṣmatayānupalakṣāt  tatkṣaṇodayavyaya b dehopacayāpacayavat  tatonupalakṣaṇespi bhedasya sattāṅgollekhaśekharodurnivāraḥ saṃśayaḥ  etāvadvimarśābhāve tu itarajanasya niścala ekāvasāya syāt yauktastu sopi saṃśaya eva  kiṃ ca kṣaṇabhedenāpi bhedaḥ pramāṇaparidṛṣṭatvād dṛṣṭa eva  kva vyabhicāra ra  dṛśe vastu ra  bhaṅgo   mātra pramāṇaṃ ra  taveti nāsti ra bhedapratyaya ra  apīti nāsti a  bhedādhyavasāya ra  bhinna eveti nāsti a  kimanekatvādhyavasāyaḥ a  na bhedasyā a  pūrvaka ra  nupalakṣyamāṇatvāt ra  vyaya itināsti ra  nvalakṣaṇepi ra  ttāṃśollekha ra  yauktabhramepi  ajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauyathā dhārādau kiyatyapi nabhobhāgeparāparapayaḥpātepiviparyaṃyasthiteśca saṃbhavāt tadevedamudakamityavadhāraṇasyaanabhyāsadaśāyāmekatāgrahaḥ tatra stambhādau tvabhyāsavatopīti cet  nanukṣaṇabhedabhāvini viśeṣe sarvatraivāsmādṛśonabhyāsa ityupapāditameva  ambhaḥstambhādautu tatkriyāsārthasāmānyālambanaḥ sarvatrābhyāsaḥ sthūlaviṣayaḥ kṣaṇadvaye abhedasādhanavyāpāraḥ svīkatu śakyaḥ  ekāvasāyamātraṃ tu sadapi vyabhicārādasamartham tasmānna pratyakṣeṇananu sarvatra nīlādau pṛṣṭhabhāvinā vikalpena pratyakṣasya vyāpāronugamyamānaḥprāmāṇyamupanayati  tadekatāvasāyopyeka viṣayameva prāmāṇyamasya dīpayatviti cet  nakhalu sarvatra pṛṣṭhabhāvivikalpaviṣaye prāmāṇya mindriyajñānasya  marīciviṣayasyāpijalāvasāye jalaviṣaye prāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt  vikalpāpekṣaṃ tu prāmāṇyamiti tadanudayena prāmāṇyamiti nyāya  tadudaye tu saṃvādāpekṣameva tat  na caikādhyavasāyasyasaṃvāda   sa ityāveditametat nanu yatra  bādhaḥ tatrāprāmāṇyamabādhite prāmāṇyamiti kiṃ na paryāptam   iyaṃgatiravanatagaganapratibhāsepi deśakālanarāntaravyāpinī saṃbhavati nirūpyamāṇā truṭyatīti  pratyabhijñāyāmapi samānam bādhakasyakiṃ cāyamabādho nāma bādhāviraho bādhānupalabdhirveti vikalpayoḥ kramādasiddhiranekāntaśca duṣpratividhānaḥ  anupalabdhimātreṇa niṣedhāsiddhe cānumānasyābhidhāsyamānatvāt  atha pratyakṣasamākhyāteyaṃ pratyabhijñā kathamanumānenabādhyate  na cābādhyatvapratijñānādbādhakasya sadbhāvacintāvakāśenumānasyāpyavakāśaḥsvayameva dattaḥ  prāmāṇyasyaiva siddhibādhanayo radhikārāt pratyakṣamevāsyā bādhakamastviti cet  saṃvādadraḍhimni pratyakṣaśatenāpi kimasyā  tataḥ pratyakṣeṇāpi bādhanamasyāḥsaṃvādaśaithilyaṃ saṃbhāvayadanumānamapi sannidhāpayati  miteśca ra  graha ṇa  tantra ra   sa ca evāsmāṃ ra  vatkriyāparamvā ra  pratyakṣeṇa dvaye rapratyakṣeṇa kṣaṇa a  vaikalyena a  viṣayaprā a  viṣayaprā  tadanudayana ra  tadutpattisaṃvādā ra  pāṭho ghṛṣṭa a  yatra evā ra  iyaṃ ca bhinavatamaṃ    ra  ti abhijñā ra   ranaikāntikaśca ra  mātraniṣedhā a  cakārastyaktaḥ a  sadbhāve a bādhayo akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraapica māyākaraḥ śirasi nimajjitaṃ golakamāsyena niḥsārayatīti pratyabhijñā śirasi chidraprasaṅga saṅgatenānumānena bādhyamānā ki nopalabdhā  bādhyamānāna pratyakṣamiti prastutepyastu  ataḥ pratyakṣatvakīrtanamasyā yācitakamaṇḍanamātramatrāṇam  yathā cāvanatākāśapratibhāsaḥ sarvasaṃpratipattāvapi nābādhya eva tathā nāvisaṃvādyevetyapi vyaktam  tadvadeva caikatāgrahaḥ a sarvasaṃpratipattāvapi nāvisaṃvādī nahi tadaparādhyavasāyodayamantareṇa praṇatāmbarasaṃvedane sa evāyamiti pratyayeparaḥsaṃvādorthaṃkriyādisvabhāva  saṃbhavati  ataśca bādhakābhāvepi nāmāprāmāṇyavyavahārośakyasādhanaḥ  tadvadeva saṃvādena prāmāṇyamanvaśāsataḥ tadabhāvāt prāmāṇyavyavahāropi kutaḥ pratyabhijñāyā  ubhayaniścayābhāve ca tadubhayāvalambī saṃśayaḥsiddhaḥ  tallakṣaṇe kadalakāṇḍādau vyabhicāradarśanāt paripuṣṭāniṣṭāṅgaśca tatkutaḥprāmāṇyam ki ca ya evamāha visaṃvādinī yā sā pratyabhijñaiva na bhavati tadābhāsatvādititena śabdādau prameyatvaṃ hetukṛtya yat sādhyavyabhicāri prameyatvaṃ tatprameyatvameva nabhavati tadābhāsatvādityapi vaktavyameva atha pramāṇaviṣayatvamātraṃ prameyatvam tacca vyabhicāriṇopyakṣīṇam  evaṃrtāha pūrvāparekīkaraṇamātraṃ pratyabhijñārtha  tacca vyabhicāriṇyā apyasti  pratyabhijñānāma kriyatāṃ mā vā kevalaṃ sā pramāṇameva na  bhavatīti vaktavyam  prameyatvamapi yadvyabhicāri tat liṅgameva na bhavatītyapi brūhi  ekalakṣaṇatayā yathaikatravyabhicārastathānyatrāpi saṃbhavanna nivāryaṃta iti pratyabhijñānepi nāśakyam nanvagniratretyanumānamananumānaṃ ca hetvābhāsakāle samānākāram  tatkathamekatrāśvāso nānyatra  hetudvāreṇa viśeṣāt  yathā hi ekaṃ trirūpa liṅga niścayajanitamanyadanyathā yathā kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītireva kācitpariśuddhā yā adhyakṣānupalabdhisādhanā kācidanyatheti darśitam  tathā ca sati bhinnalakṣaṇatvāt nāśvāsānāśvāsasaṅkaraḥtathā na pratyabhijñāyāṃ śakyam anupahatendriyasyeva tajjñānasya vā vyabhicāriṇyāmapivyāpārāt  nāparaḥ parairapi paridīpite viśeṣa  dīrghakālānubandhamātraṃ tu bahala  na bādhya ra  sveti nāsti ra  ve tāyinā ma prāra  stadeva ra  manuśāra parimuṣṭani a  prameya hetū a  yā sā vyabhi ra  tatpramaiva ra  vyaktameva ra  jñānārtha ra nāmanakriyatāṃ sāvā ra  na tava bhava ra  nivārya iti ra  katrātmā a  dīpitoparidīpato ni ajñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalauvyāmohād adṛṣṭādihetuprabhāvād  viparyaya sāmagrīsamavadhānaparilambepyupapattimatyathoktaṃ prāk  yad vā yataḥ kutaścit parokṣārthapratipattimanumānamanumatya yatra vyabhicāraḥ taliṅgameva na bhavati anumānaṃ veti nirvṛttimālambamāna pakṣadharmatvādikaliṅgalakṣaṇaṃ tatprabhavamanumānaṃ kimarthamabhidadhyāt atha vyabhicāriṇopi vyabhicāradarśanamasamartham sāmagrīlābhavilambevyabhicārādarśanamātreṇa liṅgatvaprasaṅgād vaktavyameva lakṣaṇam yadīkṣaṇānnirvṛttiranī kṣaṇādanāśvāsaśca jāyate tato na prekṣastadanurūpānuṣṭhāna prārambhamāsādayet  santi hi pratyanī kadarśanasthānāṃ sādhanāni cirakālābhyāsabhāvitā samasamādhibalonmīladadhyakṣagocaravyabhicārāṇi  kṣaṇikatādisādhanavat  tatkimidānīṃvyabhicārādarśanamātreṇa bhāvinyā pramāṇānupapatteḥ sādhanānyeva bhavantu tadanurūpā   nuṣṭhānena vā viphalamāyāsamāviśatu prekṣa  pakṣadharmatvādilakṣaṇe tu tallakṣaṇanirūpaṇāyāṃ tadaprāptau tadaiva hastakatyāgānnāyāsamāviśati  tallakṣaṇaprāptau vā tadevaupādadīta  tanna vyabhicārāvalambanaṃ sādhu  vyatirekanirākaraṇāyaiva vivekārambhāt  tatkathaṃ lakṣaṇamavācyamiti cet  etat sarvaṃ pratyabhijñāyāmapi ālocayanyāvanna lakṣaṇabhedaṃ paśyasi tāvannaikasyāṃ vyabhicārādarśī vyabhicārādarśanamātreṇāparasyāmāśvāsa mekāntena katu marhasi  tasmāllakṣaṇayukte bādhāsaṃbhave tatkṣaṇavat kṣaṇāntarepikathaṃ kadācit kriyāviccheda  kṣaṇāntaranivartanīyakriyāsamarthasvabhāvatve vā kṣaṇāntaravattatrāpi kṣaṇe sajātīyetarakriyāprasavaprasaṅgaḥ  kṣaṇāntarepi hi tacchāmarthyasya saṃbhavājjananaṃtaccānyadāpyakṣīṇam kāryāṇi hi vilambante kāraṇāsannidhānataḥ samarthahetusadbhāve kṣepasteṣāṃ tu kiṃkṛtaḥ  tattva saṃgraha  etenākaraṇapakṣopi pratikṣiptaḥ  yadā vilambopyasahyaḥ tadā dūrotsāditamakaraṇam  asāmarthya vā samīhitasamayevyakaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ sadaikasvabhāvatvāt  svabhāvaaṃśe ca pratikṣaṇaṃ kṣayaḥ siddho jaladharasya  tatra prayogaḥ yad yadā yajjananasamarthaṃ yanna karoti na tattatra samartha yathā śālyaṅkaramakurvan kodravaḥ  na karoti cākaraṇakāle karaṇakālakāryāṃ kriyāmiti  sāmarthyāpekṣayā yad yat karoti na tat tatrāśaktam antyasāmagrīvat  karoti cāyaṃ
