tayostathaivābhyupagantavyaḥ  yathā sa eva hetuḥ svakāryaṃ prati śaktaḥ kāryāntaraṃ pratyaśakta ityekasyaivaviṣayabhedaṃ prati śaktyaśaktī na viruddhe tathā kālabhedenāpi śaktibhede śaktimadabhedasyapramāṇasiddherubhayatrāviśeṣāditi  etadapyasāram  etayā hiṇḍorapiṇḍāḍambaraṃviḍambayate  tathāhi na khalu  pramāṇasiddhirnāma pratyakṣānumāne paribhūyābhidhātuśakyate  tatra ca pratyakṣamiti na pratyabhijñāvikalpādanyat  sā ca nivāritā  mācaratī ra  naipuna ra  jajjanayatī ra  samākhyeyaṃ ra  śaktamāha a  evaṃ ra darśanaṃ ra  sarvajana ra  cakāro nāsti ra  laṃ janakaṃ ra  pūrṇanāśa ra  śaktāsvabhā ra  hīti tyaktam a  bhedosiddha ra  dṛṣṭayo ra  bhedepi ra  ubhayatra vi ra viḍambayati ra sa khalu ra  navāritā akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pakṣadharmādhikāraḥyaccānumānamāha śaṃkara sthirasiddhau notpattyanantaraṃ vināśī bhāvaḥ prameyatvāt vastuvyāvṛttivaditi  avidyamāna vipakṣatvādanvayyeva hetuḥ  prameyatvasya kṣaṇikatvenavirodhābhāvāt sandigdhavyatirekamiti cet  na khalu kṣaṇikatve kasyacit prameyatvaṃsidhyati kṣaṇasthitidharmaṇaḥ pramāṇakāletipātāt atītasya ca pratyakṣatvetiprasaṅgāt  tadapi manorathamātram  tathāhi  mā bhūdatītasya grahaṇam  vartamānasya cakṣaṇikasyaiva kṣaṇikena jñānena grahaṇaṃ bhaviṣyati  tasmādavirodha eva prameyatvakṣaṇikatvayoḥ atha kāraṇaṃ viṣaya iti jñānāt prāgapekṣitasattākorthaḥ kṣaṇāntarenanuvartamāno na grāhya eva syāt kṣaṇāntarānuvṛttau vā akṣaṇikatvameveti cet  tat kimiyaṃrājñāmājñā yadajanakena grāhyaṇa na bhavitavyamiti  ayamasya samaya eveti cet nyāyasyāyamavasaro na samayasya  tasmāt samayamanapekṣya vādavyasaninā nyāyopanyāsenaparo bodhayitavyaḥ samayasya hi sādhanatve sarvasiddhernyāyo nāma na kiñcit nyāyastu samayabādhanāyaiva kathaṃ samayameva śaraṇīkuryāt kathamajanitena grahaṇamatiprasaṅgaścaivamiti cet  janitenāpi kathaṃ grahaṇam  jāyamānaṃhi jñānaṃ viṣayamanubhavadupajāyate  tacca janmaviṣayakṛtamanyakṛtaṃ vā syāt koviśeṣa  atiprasaṅgastu sādhāraṇa cakṣurādināpi tasya jananāt  tasyāviṣayasvabhāvatvāditi cet  nanu gṛhyamāṇa eva viṣayo vyavahriyate na jātiniyataḥ kaścidviṣayo nāma  tatoviṣayatvādityagṛhyamāṇatvānna gṛhyata iti kvedamubttaraṃsaṃbadhyate  tathāhi  svabhāvādeva nendriyaṃ gṛhyata iti cet  na yogināṃ darśanasvīkārāt  pṛthagjanāpekṣayā niyama eṣa iti cet  pṛthagjanāpekṣayā tarhisūkṣmādayopi svabhāvenaiva gṛhyanta iti nātiprasaṅgaḥ  athavāpūrvikaiva tu sāmagrī sajñānaṃ viṣayakṣaṇam sālokarūpavat kuryād yena syāt sahavedanam  agrāhya ra kumbhavyāvṛti ra  na khalva a   syaiva kena a  vijñānātgrahaṇamiti prasa ra  tattu a  kṛtamanya iti nāsti ra  tarhi a  kathamati ra pūrvekevatta   dyaajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalautena vā svaviṣayaniyatamutpāditaṃ jñānaṃ tadekagrāhi tatkāraṇasāmagrayā vātanniyatamutpādita miti nirviśeṣaḥ  atastasyā eva te arthāne grāhyagrāhakabhāvaniyatajanmanī kathamatiprasajyeyātām atha sākāravedanavādino hi viṣayādeva tatsvarūpasaṃvitterutpattirabhimatātatrātītagrahaṇetiprasaṅgaḥ grahaṇakṣaṇānuvṛttī ca sthirasiddhiriti vivakṣitam  tatkimayaṃ prasaṅgaheturyatparopagamanamanapekṣya na bhavati  tathā ca sati viparyayaparyavasānāt tava sthirasiddhiratītagrahaṇaṃ veti na grāhyāttatsvarūpajñānotpattiriti syāt  evaṃca sati vyaktamanyad bhuktamanyad vāntamiti nyāya  sthiramārabdhaḥ sādhayitu tadviparyaṃyeṇa sākārabodhaṃ vidhurayatīti atha sautrāntikasyedamubhayamasamañjasamitīyanmātramucyate tadapi nāsti sākāravedanodayapakṣasthitī hi dvitīyakṣaṇānuvṛttāvapyarthasya jaḍatayā prakāśānupapatteḥ viparyayasarūpasvarūpa saṃvedanameva jñānasya viṣayavedanam  evaṃ ca na vartamānānurodhaatītepi tatpratyayāsatterapracyuteḥ  na cātiprasaṅgaḥ viṣayāntareṇāpi sārūpyasamarpaṇāt  na ca  tanmatanirvāhaḥ prakṛtaḥ  bhavatastu tanmatāśrayeṇāpi prameyatvahetuḥsthirasiddhaye na prabhavatīti siddhamanekāntaparihārāditi  tataḥ sthiravapuṣi pramāṇāntara siddheśyogāt vajropa pakṣakukṣī nikṣiptaḥ kiṃ punaḥ sphaṭiko varākaḥ  tadayaṃsakriyākriyāvasthayobhiṃdyamānaḥ kathaṃ kāmabhedenāvirodhe dṛṣṭāntībhavitumarhatīti yacca viṣayabhedeneva kālabhedenāpi śaktyaśaktyoravirodhapratipādanam tadapyanopayikam pratiyogī hi dharmo virodhakaḥ sarvatra  na ca svakāryakaraṇasya parakāryākaraṇaṃ pratyanīkam  kiṃ tu svakāryākaraṇameva  evaṃ parakāryākaraṇasyāpi parakāyaṃkaraṇaṃ pratyanīkam na svakāryakaraṇam  svakāryaṃ na karotīti vyavacchettameva hi svakāryaṃ karotītyucyate pratyakṣavyāpāraśca te svakāryakāriṇaṃ parakāryakāriṇaṃ ca bhāvabhedenāvasthāpayati kālabhede tu naikatāvyavasthāpaka pratyakṣam pratyabhijñāyā dūṣitatvāt  tataḥ svakāryasyakaraṇamakaraṇaṃ ca pariśiṣyamāṇaṃ na virodhaparihārāya paryāpnoti  rthakriyā ra   sānānu tta va ra sānāta na ca a  taditi nāsti a  kṣaṇānanu vṛttyā a   viṣayasarū a  tasmāt ra  prakṛti ra  neti nāsti ra  pramāṇa a oskriyeti nāsti ra  na virodhadṛ ra  sarvatrānavakā ra   meṣa hi a  cātra ra  kāryākā ra   dena vyavasthā rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraḥkālānekatvāpekṣasvakāryakaraṇākaraṇaṃ viruddhamiti cet  syādiyamapekṣāparabhāgabhāgino yadi viṣayabhedavadabhedāpādakapramāṇavṛttiḥ syādityuktaprāyam  bhavatopitadanapekṣya virodhasthitau ki pramāṇamiti cet  uktameva yad yadā yajjananasamarthalla tattadā janayatyevetyādi sahakāryapekṣāyāśca tatsannidhānāsannidhānayoḥkāryārjjanaprasaṅgena ranirastatvāt  tasmāt janayadrūpameva śaktivivakṣitā kṣaṇabhaṅgavādinaḥ  tasyāśca bhede kathaṃ na bhāvabhraṃśaḥ Ona cātrayacca nyāyabhūṣaṇena pralapitam yadyasya bhinnā śakti śaktimatobhyupagamyatetathāpi  nāvaśyaṃ śaktāśaktayorbhedaḥ  kasmāt  tvanmatepi dharmabhedād dharmibhedaniyamāsiddheḥ  tathā ca bhinnepi kārye sahakāriṇāṃ pṛthagupayogaṃ darśayatābhihitammṛtpiṇḍāde mṛtsvabhāvebhya ityādi hetubindu lekhitvā  yathā ca tatra mṛdātmatādisvabhāvabhedepi na kāryabhedaḥ tathā śaktāśaktādisvabhāvabhedepyabhedo bhaviṣyati abādhitatvādhyavasāyasya samānatvāditi tadapyanena pratyādiṣṭam  santi hi dharmā ye parasparavirodhinovirodhinaśca  na tu dharmā ityeva virodhāvirodha  na hi brāhmaṇyaṃvaiyākaraṇatvenāviruddhamiti cāṇḍālatvenāpyaviruddhamityabhidhātuṃ śakyam brāhmaṇyavyāptaṃ cāṇḍālatvam  na ca vaiyākaraṇatvenāpi viruddham  yathā cātra svapratiyogibrāhmaṇyetaratvameva virodhamādhatte na vaiyākaraṇatvena tathā janayadrūpamajananatayaivaviruddhabhāvāna vastusantānabhedena  nīlacaturasrāditā tu śvetaparimaṇḍalatādibhivirodhamāsādayatu na tu kacit kāryakāraṇādibhiḥ  ato yadi virodhagandhāsaṃbhavāt saṃsthānamṛtsvabhāvayorabhinnena dharmiṇā bhāvyam tat kimatyantapratyanīkayoreka kārya prati janayadrūpetarayorapīti kaḥ sacetanakaścintayet  viruddhāviruddhatvameva kathamavagantavyamiti cet  yadvyavacchedena yadvidhānam yadvidhānena vā yadvayavacchedaḥ tattena viruddham  na ca mṛnmayamiti vidhānena pṛthūdaratāvyavacchedaśaṅkāpisaṃbhavati  tajjanakābhidhānena cātajjanakatvaṃ vyavacchidyata eva atajjanakatvena catajjanakatvam  na tajjanakamityeva hyatajjanakamiti nañsamāsavākyamapi vismāri  kālaikatvāpekṣaṃ ra  svakāryakāraṇa a   svarūpaṃ ra  prasaṅgo na ra  bhedeyaṃ ra yadyabhinnā ra  tadāpi ra  tasmāt ra  niyamasiddhe ra  cābhinnepi ra  nakāronāsti a  tvāvasāya ra  dharma ityeva ra  virodhovirodho vā ra  viruddhadharmamiti ra majanayataiva ra  virudhyatāṃ  navarṇa ra  tato ra  svabhāvāpara ra  taditi nāsti a  rekakāryasmṛti a  tveti tyaktam ajñānaśrī mitranibandhāṃvalautasmād yayordharmayoryathā virodho dṛṣṭaḥ tathaivābhyupagantavya ityevameva viśeṣamabhipretyayuktaḥ naikakālāpekṣayā samānapramāṇayorapravṛtteḥ  yena hi kālabhedenābhinnamevavastu sakriyākriyanīlānīlatvādiyuktamabhyupagataṃ yasya vā tadātmani pramāṇaṃ pravṛttaṃtasya kacidvivādasaṃbhave kālabhedenāvirodhaḥ tadvatīti yuktam  tacca dvayamapi nāstītivyaktam  ata ekatvādhyavasāyasyābādhitaviṣaya viśeṣaṇamasiddham  ekatvādhyavasāyamātraṃ punaranaikāntikaṃ bādhakāpekṣameva  anyathā keśādāvapi na bādhakamapekṣeta  bādhakaṃcoktam  yadapyayaṃ  svapnāyamāna iva viplavate vaatha naivābhinnātmanaḥ kasyacit svabhāvabheda iṣyate evaṃ tarhi sahakāripṛthagupapayogakathanaṃ bālonmatta pralapitaṃ syāditi  tena yadi b dharmadharmaṇostādātmyatiraskāreṇa bhedāpādanamātramiṣṭam tadā na prakṛtopayogi  tathāhi dharmiṇaḥ sakāśāddharmā bhedabhāgino bhavantu na vā  santi tāvatkecidanyonyavirodhino ye svādhikaraṇaṃdharmiṇamabhitvā nocchvasituṃ śaknuvantīti vivakṣitaṃ kṣaṇikavādinaḥ  tatrānenatādṛśā dharmā eva na santi santopi vā kālādhupādhisāpekṣā bhedasādhava ityevavaktuṃ nyāyyam  pṛthagupayogāt sahakāriṇāṃ dharmiṇaḥ pṛthageva ta iti kimanena yadi tu svābhāvyabhāja eva bhedakā na bhidyamānā iti samayosya syātyuktametat  yāvatā valanādayopyavalanato bhedakā dṛṣṭā eva  te ca kriyādirūpatvādbhinnā eva  tasmāt kalpanoparacitavibhāgā bhavantu saugatamatena bhavanmatena vātāttvika bhedo dharmaṃdharmiṇo kimidānīṃ naikāntena  prastāvāntaraṃ hi tat  duṣpariharāstudharmā dharmiṇaṃ bhindānā ye virodhasthāyina iti siddhaṃ sādhyam atha kāryādabhedaśca  svabhāvānāṃ pṛthak sahakārikāraṇakalāpopayogaviṣayatvaṃceti duḥśliṣṭatāmātramudbhāvyate paranayasya tadāpi prastutakṣaterabhāvāt kimanena bhedavatāmapi bhedakatvād dharmāṇāṃ duḥśliṣṭatābhāsatā ca bhinnasamayasthānāṃ parasparamagaṇiteṣu sthāneṣu saṃbhavati  tattvaṃ tu kīdṛgiti tattatsthāna nirūpaṇe vyaktībhaviṣyati  ityeva ra  na bhinna a  tadvaditi ra  svata a   syābādhita viśeṣa masiddham aotena dṛśo ra yadaya a  kathaṃ na ra  syādityādi a  mabhitvo nāmittaṃ ra viti nāsti ra  bhidyamānā iti nāsti ra  cakrādi ra  vibhāgāt varṇa  ra dharmā iti nāsti a  ceti nāsti a  parasamayasya tathāpi ra  ṣṭrābhāsatā ca bhinnasamayasthānāṃ rakṣaṇabhaṃṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraḥtatra yadi prastutānupayogiyatkiñcidvistārayatā sthātavyamityabhimatam sarvasyaśakyametat  na caitāvataiva dharmadharmavādaparisamāptiḥ  tat kimasya garbhārbhakamanatiśayānasya nindāvacane nirbaṃndhena  tathā ca sati tasmānna dharmabhedādeva dharmibheda iti nigamanamavyasyāyuktam  bauddhaḥ kila na dharmāṇāṃ bhedamātreṇa dharmibhedamāha kiṃ tu virodhena  anyathā kṛtakatvānityatvādīnāmapi dharmabhedamācakṣīta  anenāpisvayaṃ viruddhadharmādhyāsādityakṣaramutthāpitam  tad yadi virodhabhedamātrayorviśeṣaṃ napaśyati yuktamāheti kimaparaṃ vaktavyam yadapyayamevāha  yo hyananta ra kāryakaraṇasvabhāvaḥ sa kathamādau tat kāryaṃ kuryāt atha kuryānna tarhi uttarakāryakaraṇasvabhāvaḥ  na hi nīlotpādanasvabhāvaḥ pītādikamapikaroti  na ca prathamottara kāryotpādanasvabhāvabhedāt tadvatopi bhedaḥ svabhāvabhedasya vyabhicāritvenoktatvāditi  tadapi niḥsāram  yadi hi svabhāvaśabdenasvalakṣaṇamabhipretam tadā tadbhede bheda eva vastūnām ka vyabhicāravārtā  tasmātsvabhāvabheda iti kalpitadharmāntvaṃ yuktam  na ca tanmātreṇa dharmabhedamāpādayatiparaḥ  kiṃtu virodhena  na ca tadvirodhepi dharmibhedavyabhicārosti  virodho hina bhedaṃ vyabhicarati  bhedastu virodhaṃ vyabhicaratītyuktaprāyam nanu yadi kalpitā eva te dharmā ka virodha ka vā a bheda iti cet iha dvividhamabhidheyaṃ kalpitaśabdasya tattadvyāvṛttavastusaṃbhave bhedamātraṃ kalpanāvabhāsitadapi kalpitaṃ kuvalayanīlatvādivat  kalpanāmātraniveśi ca kalpitaṃ karikeśaratriguṇīmayatvādivat  tatra yadyantima kalpitārtha syāt na bhedanirodhāditi yuktam  prācīnetu kalpitārthe vastusvabhāvasyaivāvyavasānād bhedo virodho vā vyavasthāpyamānaḥ saṃvāda mādāyaiva vartata iti na doṣaḥ yacvedam uttarakṣaṇe yatkāryaṃ kartumasya svabhāvaḥ tatkathaṃ prathamakṣaṇe kuryāt anyathottara kāryakāritaiva na svabhāvasyeti tadapyaparibhāvya bhāṣitam  sthirasvabhāvatvehi bhāvasyottarakālamevedaṃ kāryam na pūrvakālamiti kuta etat  tadabhāvāca kāraṇamapyuttara kāryakaraṇasvabhāvamiti kutaḥ  arthānurodhinyo hi vācaḥ śobhābhājaḥ navāganurodhādarthaṃtathābhāvo rājavat  kiṃ kurmaḥ uttarameva tasya janmeti cet  astu  niyamana ra  hyutarakāryaṃ  ra  bhedotatvato ra  tadbheda ra  dharmāṇāṃ nānā ra dharmi nāsti a  ceti nāsti ra  bhavato ra  yetara rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalausthiratve tu tadanupapadyamānamasthiratāmādiśatu sthiratvepyeṣa eva svabhāvaḥ tasyayaduttarakṣaṇa eva karotīti cet  hatedānīṃ pramāṇapratyāśā pramāṇabādhitepi svabhāvālambanena nistaraṇāt  dhūmādatrāgniragnerabhāvād vā neha dhūma ityuktepi hiśakyamabhidhātuṃ svabhāva evāyamasya yadidānīmatra niragnirapi dhūma iti  tasmāt pramāṇasiddhe svabhāvāvalambanam na svabhāvāvalambanena pramāṇavilopaḥ  pramāṇanirṇayaścavihita eva  nīlotpādanasvabhāvaśca na pītādika karotītyasamīkṣākhyānam  upādānatvena hi tatkaraṇaniṣedho na tu sahakārikāraṇatvenāpi sahakāritayā tatrāpi kathañcina cānyavarṇasyānyavarṇopādānatāniṣedha eva  dṛśyatedupayogasyāśakyabādhanatvāt hi pītaiva haridrā cūrṇasahakārikā raktasyopādānaṃ bhavantīti nidarśanamasaṅgatam  yadica yathā na nīlaḥ pītamutpādayati tathā nottarajanakaḥ pūrvamutpādayati  evaṃ tarhi yaścottarajanakaḥ yaśca nottarajanakaḥ tayorbhedopi kiṃ neṣyate yathā yannīlaṃ tannānīlamiti tadalamevaṃvidhapralāpeṣu nirbaṃndhena sthitametat parasparaviruddhadharmādhyāsād deśabhedavatkālabhedepi janakājanakasvabhāvayorbheda eva etena yadapi nyāyamañjarīkāraḥ prāha nanu kāryotpattiheturyeṣāṃ sannidhimapekṣatete khalvapekṣitasannidhayaḥ sahakāripratyayāstastha ki kurvanti  na kiñcit  kevalaṃkāryameva yeṣāṃ bhāvābhāvāvanuvidhattaṃ te kāryeṇaivāpekṣitasannidhayaḥ sannipatantaḥtadeva kāryaṃ vivakṣitaṃ hetunā saha kurvantīti sahakāriṇa ucyante na tu yena sahakurvanti tasyaiva kartāro bhavantaḥ sahakāriṇo bhavitumarhanti  b  tasmādakṣaṇikasyasvakāryanimāṇe dvividhaṃ sāmarthyam ekaṃ nijaṃ sāmarthyam dvitīyaṃ cāgantukaṃsahakāryantaram tayorabhāve tatkāryānutpatteḥ  tasmādeva hi dvividhāt sāmarthyātkāryotpatterabhyupagamāt  ekamakṣaṇikaṃ gṛhītvā tasmādeva kāryotpatti saṃbhāvayantaḥsāmarthyameva hetūnāmavijñātavantaḥ pare  yasmādakṣaṇikasyāpi kramavatīṣu tāsu tāsvarthakriyāsu kartavyāsu kramavatsahkāryaṃntarameva sāmarthyamaṅgīkurmaḥ  tathā ca kramavatsahakārinānātvādapi kramavatkāryanānātvopapatteraśakyaṃ bhāvānāṃ pratikṣaṇamanyatvamupapādayitumiti  tviti nāsti a   viśatu ra  vāvalambanena ra   kārakasyo a  te itināsti a  nna virudhyate ra  yasmāt a  dvayorabhāve tatkāryaṃ tayorabhāve ra  kāryānupapatteḥ akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāratadapyapāstam  yadyapi hetvantarakalpitaṃ  sāmarthya vijñātamasmākaṃ tathāpiyajjanayatīti vyavahāragocarībhūyamāpannaṃ svarūpamavaśyamabhyupagantavyam bhāvasya svalakṣaṇākhyaṃ sāmarthyaṃ saṃkhyātamasmanmate  tat kiṃ prāgapi paścādeva veti vikalpya dūṣaṇamudīritam  tatra kimanenoktaṃ bhavatīti niveditameva  yattu kāryeṇaivāpekṣitasannidhayaityupaskṛtam tadapi nirupayogam  yadi hi kāryameva svajanmani svatantraṃ syāt yuktametat  kevalamevaṃ sati sahakāriṇāmapi sāmarthyarūpatākalpanamaphalamiti hetoḥsāmarthyamanapekṣya svātantryādeva kāryaṃ kadācid bhavati kadācinna bhavatīti ki hetusāmarthyasamarthanavyasanena vyavahāramātraṃ vā sāmarthyamiti na tu kacit kiñcit samarthanāmeti prāptam  astu ko doṣa iti cet  santo hetavaḥ sarvathāsamarthāḥ asattukāryaṃ svatantrama viśuddhā buddhiḥ  utpattau tu sadrūpaṃ kāryaṃ kimarthamarthāntaramapekṣata itinirūpaya tāvat tasmāt sāmagrīmapekṣate kāryamityanenākṣareṇa sāmagrayeva jananasamarthā kāryasyetyevārtha  na ca sā samagrebhyo bhinnā  tataḥ samagrā eva janakāḥ  bhinnatvepi vārthātaramika sākalyamapi sahakārīti na viśeṣa  tato yāvantaḥ sahakāriṇastāvantaḥpratyekaṃ samarthā iti prāgvidyamānānāṃ kathaṃ kriyātikrama  sākalyameva hi paścādupapattimaditi samayaḥ tadapi vā tebhya eva sahakāribhyo labhyasaṃbhavaṃ prāgapi teṣvasatsu kathaṃ sattāviyuktaṃ kadācid yāvadekasyāpi prāgbhāvaḥ  atha kāryasyaivāyamaparādhoyadamīṣvasamartheṣu kadācinnotpadyata iti cet sarvāvasthāsamānepi kāraṇe yadyakāryatā svatantraṃ kāryamevaṃ syāttantra kārya tathā sati vārtikālaṅkāre iti kiṃ na paśyasi syādetat  na tadbhāvevaśyaṃ bhavatīti tatkāryamucyate kiṃ tu tadabhāve na bhavatyevetivyatirekaprādhānyāditi cet  yadyapi hi a yadyabhihitatvatvāri ra  paścādeveti ra   syāyukta ra  hetoḥ sāmarthyamasamarthavyasanena a  asatu ra sadravyamānaṃ ra  ntarameva a  saha stāvanta itināsti a  labhyaṃ saṃ  teṣu sa  tsu ra  viyuktā a  nnatat  hetubinduṭīkā pṛ  syānna kāryantat  vārtikālaṃ pṛ jñānaśrī mitranibandhāṃvalautadbhāvepi na bhāvaścedabhāve bhāvitā kutaḥ tadabhāvaprayuktasya  sobhāva iti tatkutaḥ vārtikālaṅkāre yadi hi svayaṃ bhavanaṃ bhāvayadeva kāryaṃ hetuḥ tadā tadabhāvaprayuktosyābhāvaityapi syāt  yadā tu hetau jananonmukhepi svātantryādeva na bhūtamiti kathaṃ tadabhāva prayojakosyābhāva iti pratītiḥ  tasmād yadi kāryakāraṇabhāva a tadā niyataṃyathaiva tadabhāve niyamena na bhavati tathaiva tadbhāvepi niyamena bhavet  abhavacca natatkāraṇatāmātmanaḥ kṣamate  tadayaṃ prayatnaparamparayāpi hetūnāṃ samarthāsamarthalakṣaṇodayavyayayogo jāragarbha iva gopayitumaśakyaścaturabuddhiṣu yadapyāha śaṅkaraḥ  na ca sarvatra sahakāribhedena kāryabhedādapi kāraṇasya bhedasidhyati  yathaikatvepi sahakāribhedād vijñānavartavikārajvālāntarāṇi pradīpaḥ karotina cāsau bhidyate tadabhedasya pramāṇasiddhatvāditi apūrvoyamasya dambhārambhaḥ  yadayamakṣepa kriyādharmā svabhāva śaktiśabda vācyaḥ sa kiṃ prāgapyasti yadi vā saṃpratyeveti vikalpya codyaśaktivācyaṃ mamasahakārisākalyamiti bravīti śaktyaśaktilakṣaṇaviruddhadharmādhyāsād bheda ityabhimatenakāryabhedāt kāraṇabheda iti samādhatte  kaḥ khalu kāryabhedāt kāraṇabhedaṃ vaktumupakrāntoyatraivamucyate sahakāribhadena yaḥ kāryabhedaḥ sa na kāraṇabheda iti api tu yasya yadāyajjananasvabhāvaḥ sovaśyaṃ tatkarotyeva  na hi pradīpa eva vijñānādikāryāṇi sakṛtkatu samartha kṣepeṇa janayati  tadvad vā kramabhāvinyapi kāryāṇi sajātīya vijātīyānikiṃ na tadaiva karoti  atasteṣāmanya eva kārako dīpa iti yuktam  evamanyatrāpyeṣaeva nyāyaḥ Oyatpunarāha pradīpādivyaktīnāmiva pratyekamutpattivināśakā raṇānupalabdherabhrāntaṃsphaṭikāderavasthitivijñānamiti tadapyandhaśarakṣepāyate pradīpepyanyānyasyotpattikāraṇasyānupalabdheḥ  vartisnehādayo hi pradīpahetavaḥ teca pratikṣaṇaṃ pratilavādi vā ktesya  hetubinduṭīkā pṛ   svayambhavantāva yadeva ra  tathaitadbhave ra bhavata ra  kāraṇabheda ra  bhedamvijñāna a  tadābhedasya ra  dharmo a  sa itināsti a  bhede varṇamupa ra  kāraṇabhedaka iti ra  yajjananaḥ sva a  bhāvīnya ra meva ra  devasthi rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāranyānyī bhavantītyadhyavasāyaḥ kasya saṃbhavati  anyathā sphaṭikepyanyānyībhavatipūrvaṃpūrvamanyadanyaduttarottarasya kāraṇamanvayavyatirekānuvṛtteriti ki na gṛhyate  yadyapica pradīpe kālabhedenānyabuddhirasti tathāpi na tailavartyoḥ tatkathaṃ pradīpādivyaktīnāmutpattikāraṇopalabdhirna sphaṭikasyetyucyate  vināśakāraṇaṃ tu cintayiṣyāmaḥ  nāpipradīpabhaṅa guratayā tatkāraṇabhaṅgaḥ saṅgato vaktum kāraṇābhedātkāryasyāpi pradīpasyābhedaprasaṅgāt atha vartisnehayoḥ kṣaya upalabhyate pradīpasyāpi kṣīyamāṇadeśavyāptiviyogātsa eva kṣaya iti cet  tailaṃ prabalamāsīdidānīmalpaṃ vartate  vatirapyevam pradīpopyanyānyatailavatibhāgaparihāreṇānyānyatadbhāgavyāpīti sarvathā nivṛttistu kathamavasātuṃ śakyā pratyabhijñānasya  tadavasthatvāt atha vartyādīnāmapacayakālevayave kriyotpadyate  tato vibhāgodayaḥ  tataḥsaṃyoganāśaḥ  tatopi tadārabdhadravyanāśaḥ  punaḥ kriyā saṃyogāt itaradravyodayaśca tinaikadravya nirvāha siddhiriti cet  anubhavabhuvamavatarannapi yadyayaṃ prapañcam ādriyatebauddhopyevaṃ svaprakriyāmudghoṣayan kathaṃ vāyaṃ  b pūrvakebhya sabhāgahetubhyaḥsahakāriṇamaparamarthamantato vātātapatimirādi  samāsādya  tebhya parasya samānaparimāṇasya yathā sahakāribalasaṅkataṃ nyūnasyādhikasya vā saṃbhava iti na sphaṭikaśatakoṭiprabhṛtīnāmekatānirvāhasiddhiḥ  yadā punaranena sādhanamevopanyastaṃ tadā nāsya prakriyāsiddhiḥ tvatprakriyayā bādhā vā  vātādayaḥ kimupacinvanti apacinvanti vāsphaṭikādau yena sahakāritayā kalpyante prāgbhāvitvamātreṇa kāraṇatvetiprasaṅgāditi cet  na ve  sthūla kaścidupacayopacayo vā kriyate taistasya  ataevātyantasadṛśodaya  sūkṣmastu  aśakyopalakṣaṇatayā yathedaṃtathā nirdeṣṭumayogyaḥ tathā niṣedhamapyayogya eva  evamanekavastusaṃkare kadācitkenacidupayoge na kiñcid vastu prastutopādānasya sahakāri syāditi na sarvathā sahakāryaṃntaravirahādekasya jananasaṅgatiravagantavyāityupanyāsasyārthaḥ  sthiratvasiddhau tu yadi tvamapi svaprakriyāṃ nirvāhayitumīśiṣe dinānyānyī ra  kāraṇamartha a  cakāro nāsti ra  lakṣyate ra  pramāṇavartirapyevam iti nāsti a  pratijñānasya a  saṃyoga itara ra   rādi sāsā    tebhyaḥ a pariṇāmasya a  aspaṣṭaḥ pāṭhaḥ a  sphaṭikāde ra  yeneti nāsti a  iti naitra acet iti nāsti a pāṭho ghṛṣṭa a  asti tatra a  aśakyopa ra kenaciditi nāsti ra  svakriyā rajñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalauīṣiṣya  bauddhasādhanavicārastāvat prastutoyam  tatra ca prastuteneka kāryeṇānekenabhāvyamiti kena karṇe bhavato niveśitam yataḥ pradīpadṛṣṭāntīkaraṇaṃ bhavataḥ śobheta tadidamucyate anyo vyādhiranyadauṣadhamiti yadapyāha yadeva ca sahakāribhedena kāryabhede pradīpasyābhedasiddhau sādhanaṃ tadevakramavatsahakāribhedena kāryabhedekramasyāpīti tadapyatyantamasaṃbaddham  advayākāramindriyapratyakṣameva hi bhedabhraṃśamāśaṃsati pradīpe  sapratighasya hi pradīpasya naikasthānam bhinnadeśasya cātyantasadṛśasthāpi bhedopalakṣaṇamanivārya māyāgolakavat  ata ekākāramindriyajñāna mekatāyāmeva pradīpamavasthāpayati  kālabhede hi bhinnepi vastunyatyantasadṛśe pratyabhijñānamupajāyamānamupalabdham  na ca pratyabhijñānādanyadekatāsādhanam tatkathaṃ tadeva sādhana miti na plavate  na ca sadṛśatayā kālabhedena pratyabhijñānasyasaṃśayāṅgatvaṃ vyabhicāradarśanāt lakṣaṇabhedavirahāt sakṛdabhedabhāsinyapi pratyakṣenāśvāsaḥ tathā kvacidadarśanāt  indriyajñāne hi  kramadarśanepi na yogyamarthadvayaṃpratighāti ekībhūyopalabhyamānamupalabdham  tatkathaṃ sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ  tasmādanupayoga pradīpadṛṣṭāntena pratyavasthānam etadeva rūpaṃ dṛṣṭāntīkṛtyābhiprāyāntaramasya dyotayan nyāyabhūṣaṇepi yadāhaapi ca yena svabhāvena rūpaṃ rūpāntaraṃ karoti na tenaiva rasādikam rasāderapirūpasvabhāvatāprasaṅgāt  tataḥ sarvaṃ rūpakāryaṃ cakṣuṣā gṛhyate  na caitadiṣṭam  tasmādyathā rūpaṃ rūpāntarotpādanasvabhāvena tadeva karoti vijñānotpādanasvabhāvena vijñānameva karoti na rūpādikam  rasotpādanasvabhāvena ca rasam aevaṃ gandhasparśanajananasvabhāvābhyāṃ tāveva janayati  tadvadakṣaṇikopyādyakāryotpādanasvabhāvenatadeva karoti  taduttarakāryajananasvabhāvena taduttarameva janayati  nādyamuttarottaraṃ vā evamuttarottara kāryeṣvananta kālabhāviṣvapi pratiniyatāḥ svabhāvā draṣṭavyāḥ  svabhāvāeva hetatro na svabhāvītyapyayuktam rūpasyāhetutvaprasaṅgāt svabhāvānāmeva hetutvāt atha na rūpasya svabhāvabheda iṣyate kiṃ tveka eva tathābhūtasvabhāvo yena bhinnākāraṃbhinnadeśaṃ kāryamutpādayati  tasya bhinnasvabhāvakāryotpādānurodhena svabhāvabhedaḥ kathitaiti  yadaiva ra  bhedi ra  kāryabhedākara  tyantāsamba a  bhedo hi ra  sadṛśa a bhramadarśane ra   mupalambhathaṃ ra  yogina a  svabhāvaprasa a  pāṭhospaṣṭa a  mevamiti ra  kāryapavantarakāla ra  tveti nāsti ra  atha rūpa rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraḥnanvevaṃ paropyabhinnasvabhāvasyaivākṣaṇikasya kramabhāvyanekasvabhāvakāryotpādanānurodhena bhāvasvabhāvaṃ kalpayannopālambhamarhatīti etadapīrṣyākaṣāyitadhiyaḥ paradhandhīkaraṇamātram  tathāhi yadi tāvadabhinnātmāpidīpavadanekamarthamandhakāranāśādi karoti kalpitasvabhāvabheda itīyanmātraṃ vivakṣitamhanta ko niṣeddhā  astyeṣa saṃbhavo yadane kameka karotīti  evaṃ pūrvāparakālayorapyekasvabhāvo yadyanekaṃ kuryānna vivāda  kevalaṃ kvacit kāryavilambaḥ kvacidakṣepakarmetiyuktam pradīpavat sakṛdanekakaraṇamastviti vyarthaṃ pradīpanidarśanam  athakramabhāvyanekamekātmanaḥ kāryamastviti vivakṣitam tadā samartham  na khalvadyāpi dīpodṛṣṭāntayituṃ śakyaḥ  evaṃ rūpepi nidarśane kriyamāṇe vaktavyam  nacaivaṃ nirvahatiyadanekaṃ tadanekenaiva kartavyam dīpakāryavat kālabhedabhāvi cānekaṃ kāryamiti na hyanekaṃjāyamānamekasyaiva kāryamāpadyate ekakarturapāye vānekajanmaiva na syādityupapādayituśakyam  dāhagāhanāderanekasyānekenaiva jalajvalanādinā karaṇadarśanāt  kālabhedābhinnamekaṃ vivakṣitamiti cet  anekakālāntaritairekātmabhirakaṃ na kriyamāṇamupalakṣayasi  evaṃ tu brūyāḥ ekamanekaṃ vā bhinnakālamabhinnakālaṃ vā nityādeva jāyataiti   tacca pratijñāmātrāviṣkaraṇamabhīṣṭātmanaḥ kasyacidarthasya na sādhanaṃ nāpiparaprayuktasādhanabādhana miti kimanena  tathāpi na dīparūpadṛṣṭāntena kiścit yadi ca kāryabhedenāpi bhāvaṃ bhindyādasthiravādī tathāpi rūpamevābhidyamānaṃ bhidyamānaurūparasau kathaṃ janayatītīyanmātreṇānekāntamudbhāvya svastho bhava  rūpasyāpi punarekatvasādhanena ka upayogaḥ siddhatvāt tataḥ śaṃkaropi na hi yena svabhāvena vartivikārasya hetuḥ tenaiva jvālopalambhayorapi tatsvabhāvatāprasaṅgādityabhidadhāno na kiñciñcetayata iti upalakṣyateekasyānekakaraṇāvirodhāt atha yathā bauddhobhyadhāt kṣaṇāntarepi yadi sa eva svabhāvo bhāvasyatadā saṃpratīva prāgapi jananaprasaṅgaḥ  na ca janayati  tataḥ b  svabhāvabhedobhāvasyeti  tathāhi yadi jñānajanakenaiva rūpeṇa vartivikāraṃ karoti dīpaḥ tadā tasyāpi danekameva   ra  nakāro nāsti a  kāraṇa a  sadaivaṃ ra   dirākāraṇa ra kālabhedabhi ra  ntaritairane kā mebhirerakaṃ ra  pāṭhospaṣṭa a   prayuktaṃ sādhanamiti ra  kathaṃ kathaṃ ra  sādhane ka ra  kāraṇā a  na bhāvasya rajñānaśrīmitranibandhāṃvalautattvaprasaṅgaḥ  na ca tattvamasti  tato dīpopi kiṃ bhinnasvabhāvostu  yathā cakāryāṇāṃ tādātmyavirahepi hetubhedābhāvaḥ tathā kāryāṇāṃ bhinnakālatvepi nahetubheda iti vivakṣitam  tadāpi bauddhena pramāṇabalamālambya janakājanakāvasthayoḥbhāvabheda āropitaḥ  tatra ca yadyakṣamā tadāsiddhayādidūṣaṇameva vaktuṃ sāmpratam tāvataiva tasya nirāśe kimanena prabandhena Jatha duṣṭameva tatsādhanam  tathāpi tena yat siddhaṃ tat siddhameva tāvat pradīpasya svabhāvabhedo bhavatu mā vā bhūtu tathāpi  kimasyopanyāsena  yacca dīpasyasvabhāvabhedasādhanāya sādhanaṃ kāryāṇāṃ tādātmyaviraho nāma sopi yadi siddhasvasādhyapratibandhaḥ tadā tena yadi yugapadapi bhedasiddhiḥ kasyacit tadā tadorṣyayākimanena bauddhasādhanena  prayāgavaṭaprayātāyātayoḥ dvitīyamūḍhakarṇāṭeneva svasādhyasādhanāya pravṛttinirāśa  kartavyaḥ  anyathānena bhede sādhite pradīpabhedasādhanameva kipravartate na vā kiñcidapi sādhanaṃ sādhyasādhanāya pravarteta dhūmādisādhanaṃ svasādhya sādhakaṃ dṛṣṭvā ruathedaṃ pradīpasvabhāvabhedasādhanamadhyakṣā vikṣiptaṃ svasādhyapratibandhavidhuraṃ vātadā tadeva naśyatu  na tadā bauddhasādhanasya kṣatiḥ  tathāpi kiṃ tasyopanyāsena yadi bauddhasparddhayā tadvimarśamasārīkatu mupamānabhūtaṃ vimarśāntaramevedamupanītamtadāyamasthitaḥ pakṣaḥ svabhāvabhedo dīpasyeti  evaṃ sati eka evāsau śaktiviśeṣoyasteṣāmutpādaka iti cet  etadapetāgamayuktikaṃ paraspardhayābhyupagamyamānamapi nanītiśīlān prīṇāti  pratiniyatasvabhāvopādānābhāve teṣāṃ sarvatrotpatteradṛṣṭapūrvatvādityādinā  tathā  svabhāvabhedābhāve ca kāraṇasya kāryabhedabhāve tasyākasmikatvaṃprasajyeta  tathā cākaraṇaṃ viśvasya vaiśvarūpyaṃ syādityanena ca kathaṃ svabhāvabhedameva svabhāṣayā draḍhayet  na cāyaṃ nyāyyaḥ  tathā hi yattāvaducyate yadi yenaiva svabhāvenadīpo vartivikāra hetustenaiva jvālāde  tadā jvālāderapi vartivikāratvaprasaṅgaḥ na caivam tasmādbhinnenaiva svabhāvena vartivikāre bhinnena ca jvālādau dīpaḥ pravartate iti viparyayārthaḥ  tatra ca pratyakṣabādhaiva ṣa niraṃśasya dīpādestatra bhāsanāt  anyathā kadamba  viraho a  bauddha ra  dṛṣṭa ra  tathāpi tat a  sādhanāya iti nāsti ra  pramātārthamāyā ra  pāṭhospaṣṭa a  kaṃ ra  madhyamo vikṣipta ra  pāṭhospaṣṭa a   supanāma ra   mavisamvādaka ra  praṇati ra  dṛṣṭaṃ parvatayā ra  bādhe ca akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāragolakavadanantasvabhāvaparikaritasyābhāsaprasaṅgāt  na cānupalabhyatvameṣāmabhidhātuśakyam pradīpasvabhāvatvenupalabhyatāyā virodhāt  yadi ca pradīpasvabhāvatvepyadṛśyatvaṃ viruddhamanurudhyase vartivikārakāraṇatvepi jvālādihetutāṃ kiṃ na saṃbhāvayasiyataḥ svarūparāśiṃparikalpanavyagrosi  tasmānnānupalabhyamānasya pradīpasvabhāvatā a upalabhyatve ca nādhyakṣādhikṣepaparihāraḥ  dīpādanyadeva dṛśyama dṛśyaṃ vāvastu dīpasvabhāva iti tu nāgalokabhāṣā  ananyarūpe hi svabhāvasvarūpasvalakṣaṇaśabdāḥ prasiddhāḥ  kalpanopasthāpite tu dharme bhinna ivābhāsamānepi tadadhyavasāyādevasvabhāvaśabdaprayogaḥ yathā nityatvaṃ śabdasya svabhāva iti  tato yadi sahakāriṇi śaktiśabdavadbhinnepi kvacitu svabhāvaśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ tathāpi svabhāvāntareṇa karotītivastvantareṇa sahakāriṇā karotīti yāvat  na ca svabhāvinaḥ karaṇavāraṇamabhimatam tataḥ svabhāviśabdo bāhyorthaḥ  tena svabhāvenābhinnenaiva bhinnāni kāryāṇi karotītyāyātam  kevalamanekasahakāriparivārita iti viśeṣaḥ  sa ca kasya neṣṭa  na ca sahakāriṇopi svamanīṣikayā kalpanīyāḥ kiṃ tu yāvantonvayavyatireka grāhaka pramāṇavyāpārāstāvanta eva  sa ca vyāpāra  tejastailavartyādivyatiriktasya nāstīti kimadhikavidhānena  pratyuta svabhāvaśabdābhidheyānarthān parikalpya ṣaṭpadārthyāmantarbhāvayan kiṃviphalamāyāsyasi  yadā caivaṃ paryante svabhāvaśabdābhidheyaṃ nijaṃ rūpamekamevānekakārya heturiti upapāditam tadā yadekena rūpeṇa janitaṃ tadekameveti na siddhā vyāptiḥ tathā sati prasaṅgavadviparyayasyāpi nānekāntaparihāraḥ  pratiniyatasvabhāvopādānatāpiteṣāṃ na pradīpasyaiva tāttvikā ne kasvabhāvatayā kiṃ tu tatsāmagrayāmapoddhāradvāreṇānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ kasyacittailaṃ kasyacid vatiḥ kasyacid dīpa iti kathaṃ sarvatrotpattireṣāmupalabhyate yattu kāraṇabhedād bheda iti tatra sāmagrīlakṣaṇakāraṇavaijātyāt kāryavajātyanimittābhyupagamaḥ  tathaiva pramāṇenārpaṇāt  na tu sāmagrathantargatakāraṇanānātvamekasyānekasvabhāvatayeti śāstra eva vipañcitam  tadalameṣāṃ pramāṇanirapekṣasvotprekṣāI paritasyā ra   labhyatā ra   bhāsane ra  yadiha kāriṇi ra  śabda itināsti ra  svato vāśabda ra  karaṇa ca kāraṇa ra  yāvatsva a  nainaṃ ra  dheyānnijaṃ a pratīpa ra  taditi nāsti ra  sarvatrotpatte ra  kāraṇavaijātyamityupagamaḥ a  mekasyaivāneka ra jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalaumātreṇa vikalpeṣu nirbandhena  na ca taiḥ svabhāvabhedairbhāvikaḥ siddharapyeṣāṃ kācidarthasiddhirityuktamevetyaphala evaiṣa bhāvaḥ yathā tarhi trilocanaścaryayati tathānayorapi nīyatāmabhiprāyaḥ  tathāca nyāyamañjarī asādhāraṇamapi sattvaṃ mādhyamikanyāyena śakyamudbhāvayitum tathā hi kṣaṇavādepi pūrvarūpakṣaṇo yena sva bhāvenānantarakṣaṇamutpādayati kiṃ tenaiva rasakṣaṇamapyāhosvit svabhāvāntareṇa  yadi tenaiva rasasyāpi rūpatvaprasaṅgaḥ na hyekasvabhāvāt kāraṇāt kāryabhedaṃ paśyāma viśvasyāhetukatvaprasaṅgāt  atha svabhāvāntareṇa karoti  yadyevamekasya viruddhaṃ svabhāvadvayaṃ prasajyeta  rūpajananasvabhāvo hi rasajananasvabhāvāntāvyabhicārī  tatra yadi svabhāvāntaraṃ bhavetbhavettatraiva tasya bhāvobhāvaśca  bhāvābhāvau ca sākṣādviruddhau pūrvakaṃ rūpalakṣaṇaṃbhintaḥ  na ca bhinno dṛśyate saḥ syādetat  pūrvakasya rūpakṣaṇasya rase kartavye svabhāvāntaraṃ pūrvaka bevarasakṣaṇo na ca viruddhaṃ svabhāvāntaramastīti  yadyevamakṣaṇikasyāpi kramavatīṣu kāryavyaktiṣu svabhāvāntaraṃ kramavat sahakāryantarameveti sarva samānamanyatrābhiniveśāt tasmādasādhāraṇamupādadānasya svabhāvabhedāpatteḥ kṣaṇikebhyo nivartamānaṃ sattvam  yenaca prakāreṇa svabhāvabhedo nirākriyate tasyākṣaṇikatvepi samānatvāt sattvamakṣaṇikānta nivartate  ato vyatirekāsiddheḥ pratibandhāsiddhiriti tatra tāvad yogācāraniṣṭhāmanālocayannayaṃ saugatasamayajñānābhimānī mādhyamikanyāyenetyāha  ubhayorapi hetuphalāpavādasya tatvatobhimatatvādityadharasiddhimuddhayasākārasiddhī darśitameva sthite ca hetuphalabhāvesmākamiyaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅga cintetyuktam sā ca sthiti grāhakabhāvasya tāttvikatve gṛhīte  tadā ca yadeva yasyānvayavyatirekānuvidhāyi tadeva kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca bhavatu bījākaravat  yathā ca kasyacidekamanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyi dṛśyamānaṃ kāryaṃ tathā yadyanekamapi kasyacidekasyānvaya kacida a  carvayati a  tathānayorapanīya a  pūrvo ra  yena svabhāventaramupādeyaṃ kṣaṇa ra  prasaṅgaḥ a   vāntara bhaveti ra  prasajyate ra  svabhāvāvyabhi ra sākṣādvirupalakṣaṇa ra  pūrvasya a  na tusva a  vyakti iti nāsti ra  cakāronāsti ra  tasya kṣaṇi a   raikasiddhaḥ ra  kaditya ra  hetuphalacinte a  yadāghara  kāraṇa cetarat bī ra  cakāro nāsti a  ekasya iti nāsti akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraḥvyatirekāvanuvidhīyamānamupalabhyate tadā kimanekenāpyeka kāryeṇa bhavitavyam paravedanāpalāpe hi ekamapyekasya kāryaṃ na syāt  anapalāpe tvanekamapi kāryamekasyakena vāryate  ataḥ paravedanā pavādivādimatāvatāraṇena na kiñcit  grāhyagrāhakasthitautvekavadanekasyāpyeka kāryatānyāyaḥ samānaḥ  tatkathamekātmanā janyamānamekākāramevabhavediti lavate yattūktam  nahyekasvabhāvāt kāraṇātkāryabhedaṃ paśyāma iti tadatisāhasam  kivāna paśyati pradīpamekaṃ vikārakāriṇamandhakārahāriṇaṃ ca taraṇi vā tamaḥkamalayonidhanapravodhavidhāyinam  sarvadāndhakāramagno vā bhavān paśyati vā sahasramaṃśu mālina kāryasahasrakāriṇa  ekasvabhāvāt tu kāraṇānna kāryabheda iti samānasāmagrathā na kāryavaijātyamityartha  ataeva na viśvasyāhetukatvam  tasmādekasmādane kotpattiravirodhinīṃ kāryadvāreṇa tu rūpaṃ rūpakāraṇaṃ rasakāraṇaṃ ceti samuccayenasvabhāvadvayavyavahāraḥ  ataeva na virodhavārtā  nahi samuccaye pramāṇasiddhe virodhagandhaḥ  vātātapayorivekasminnākāśadeśe yattuktam  rūpajananasvabhāvo hi rasajananasvabhāvatāvyabhicārīti tāvatāpibhedamātraṃ sidhyati na tu virodha kṛtakānityavat  yathāhi nīlābhāvāvyabhicāripītaṃ na nīlaṃ bhavitumarhati na tu tanmātreṇa virodha  na hi yad yato bhidyate tadaśeṣaṃtena viruddhamabhidhātuṃ śakyam  virodhastu yadyapyekasmin dharmiṇi dvayorasaṃbhavayoniyamaḥsaca kadācid vastunorekasya bhāvenyaparyādānād dahanatuhinavat  kadāciddharmayoḥsvabhāvenaiva ekādhiṣṭhitetyāsaṃbhavāt bhāvābhāvavat nīlatvānīlatvavad vā tatrayadi nīlapītadravyayorapyekabhāvenya paryādānamāpādayet sthādeva a sahānavasthānanāmā virodhaḥ  na tu tadabhāvāvyabhicāramātreṇa  bhedamātraṃ tu tāvatā  evaṃnīlatvapītatvayorapyabhāvavyabhicāramātreṇa bhedamātraṃ tu na tu virodha  virodhastunīlatvasvīkṛte dharmaṇi svayamevānīlatvabhedasya pītatvasyābhāvāt  anyathā kṛtakatvānityatvādīnāmapi tadabhāvāvyabhicāramātreṇa virodhaprasaṅgāt atha kathamatra tadabhāvāvyabhicāra  na hi kṛtakena satā nānityena bhāvyamityupapattirasti  yadyevaṃ rūpajanakena satā rasajanakena na bhāvyamityatrāpi kopapattiḥ  māni a  pyaika a  māna iti nāsti a   vidhinī a  riva kasmin ra  svabhāvābhāvā a   taka nitva a  kasvabhāve ra  syādeva ra  svīkārāt a kṛtakatva a  na nityena a  katvena rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaurūpajanakatvādeveti cet  na ayogavyavacchedena viśeṣaṇe kṣīṇatvādupapatteḥ anyayogavyavacchedasyāsiddhatvāt tathāhi ki rūpasya janakameva  atha rūpasyaiva janakamitirūpajanakam  tatra prathamapakṣe rūpaṃ pratyajanakatvasyaiva vyavacchedo na punaranyajanakatvasyavyavacchedo vidhirveti sādhanāntaramapekṣya tenaiva virodhe vyavacchedasyaiva asiddheḥ dvitīye tu pakṣe anyajananakṣepa siddhirasandigdhā  kevalaṃ na tatra pramāṇavyāpāraḥ  yathāhyekasya tannāntarīyakatvaṃ tathā dvitīyasyāpi yadi syānna doṣaḥ pradīpavat  na tu rūpajanakamityeva  rasajanakapratikṣepo rūpajanakatvasyāyogavyavacchedenāpi caritārthatvāditi na kāpyupapattiratrāpi  kevalaṃ kalpanābuddhī yathārthāntaramiva rūpajanakatvaṃpratibhāti tathā tadabhāvāvyabhicāri ca pṛthageva rasajanakatvamavasīyate  yataḥ pṛthakśabdapramāṇavṛttiḥ apekṣyate tāvataiva virodhamadhyavasyati  sāvagatiḥ kṛtakatvānityatvayorapi na vyavasīyate kenāpi  nāpi tatra virodhābhidhānena kaścidupayogaḥ  ekatradharmiṇyaparaparihārārthameva hi virodhaḥ sādhyate  tad yadi virodhepyekadharma samparkaḥkṛtaṃ virodhacintayā  nīlatvānīlatvādiṣu tu prayujyate parasparaparihārātmā virodhaḥ nanu parasparābhāvāvyabhicārāviśeṣepi kathaṃ keṣāñcid dharmāṇāmekadharmiṇyanavasthānātmā virodha keṣāñcit punarbhedamātraṃ na virodha  uktamatra yadvayavacchedena yasya vidhānaṃ yadvidhānena vā yasya vyavacchedo niyamena tattena pratiyogināviruddham  yatra neyaṃ gatiḥ tadaviruddhamityalaṃ punaḥ pariśrameṇa  tadevaṃ rūpajananarasajananayoḥ parasparābhāvāvyabhicārepi kṛtakatvānityatvavad bhedamātraṃ śabdapramāṇāntarākarṣi na tu virodha iti sthitam yattūktam  tatra yadi svabhāvāntaraṃ bhavedityādi  sa tarhi nyāyaḥ kiṃ kṛtakānityatvābhyāṃ bibheti  prasaṅga eva tatrāpi bhavatviti cet  nanu parābhyupagamenaprasaṅgaḥ na ca mayedamaṅgīkṛtaṃ parasparābhāvāvyabhicāramātreṇa virodha ekatrānavasthānaheturiti  kiṃ tavaiṣobhyupagama pramāṇavṛttirvā  ubhayathāpi na mamāparādhaḥ  bsidhyatutarāṃ ca kṛtakatvānityādīnāṃ virodho na caivaṃ tasmātparasparāvyabhicārasya tathāhi iti nāsti ra  rūpajanakatva ra  rasajanakatva ra  sā ca sati ra  kṛtakatva ni ra  vyavadhīyate a   bhidhāne kaści ra  nīlatvādiṣu ra  nanva a  paravyabhicārā ra  kṛtakatva a  vibhāti ra  eṣa ra  nanva a   mātreṇavyabhicāra iti nāsti rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraḥtādātmyaniṣedhe vyāpārāt na kṛtakatvamevānityatvam  aniṣedhe tvekasyaiva kṛtakatvasyabhāvobhāvaśca syāt  yathā vastuno nīlādanīlasyāvyavacchede tasyaiva bhāvobhāvaścasvīkṛtaḥ syādityucyate  nīlamiti hi tasya bhāvaḥ  anolamiti cābhāvaḥ tadabhāva vyāptasyānīlasya bhāvo na vyāpakaṃ tadabhāvamanākṛṣya sthātuṃ śaktaḥ bhāvābhāvayoścavirodha prasādhita evetyekardhāmaṇyanavasthānamiti yannīlaṃ tannānīlaṃ pītādivastu tathādharmopi yatkṛtakatvaṃ tannākṛtakatvamanityatvādi  yadrūpajananaṃ tannārūpajananaṃ rasajananādi  anyathaikatra kṛtakatvarūpajananādau  śabdapramāṇapravṛttāvanyatrānityatvarasajananādaupramāṇāntarānapekṣāprasaṅgaḥ na tadādhāratve bhāvābhāvadoṣasyatasmāt tādātmye bhāvobhāvaścaikatra syāditi doṣaḥ tau hi parasparaṃ bhinnau dharmo yadyekatra syātāṃ kīdṛśo doṣa bhedasādhanenaiva caritārthatvāt  śāstrepi hi viruddhadharmādhyāso bheda ukto navirodha  virodhalakṣaṇaṃ tvanyat prasiddhameva  tādātmyaniṣedhopi viśeṣaṇānapekṣasvabhāvānupalambhādukko na viruddhopalambhāt  tadevaṃ bhāvābhāvalakṣaṇaviruddhadharmasaṃsargāt taddhamitvena bhāsamānau dharmāveva bhinnau bhavata iti na tayorapi dharmivastunornānādharmayogamātreṇa bhedavārtā  yadā punastathā bhidyamānāveva dharmo yathoktaparasparapratidvandvinau bhavatastadā taddharmiṇopi bhedaḥ nīlatvānīlatvabhāvābhāvadharmivatekakārya prati jananājananavacca  tasmād bhāvābhāvau sākṣād viruddhau rūpajanakatvarasajanakatvalakṣaṇau dharmāveva svardhāmitvenābhāsamānau bhinta   na tayorapyādhāraṃ prācīna virūpalakṣaṇam svayaṃ virodhābhāvāt  ata eva na bhinnau dṛśyate saḥekakāryajanakājanakatve ca svayaṃ pratyanīkatayā svadharmiṇaṃ bhinta eva abhedadarśanaṃ capratyanīkāvasāyena virodhī yata iti anumānavṛttiśceti sarvamanavadyam ayaṃ tu svayameva na hyekasvabhāvāt kāraṇāt kāryabhedaṃ paśyāma iti na ca bhinnodṛśyate sa iti ca bruvannasvastha eva na nirbandhayogyaḥ  tasmānnaikasvabhāvāyāḥ sāmagrayāḥkāryavejātyamityavirodhaḥ  na tu svabhāvaparamparārahitāditi  tadevaṃ svabhāvasandehā nīlatvasya ra  bhāvena a  pramāṇavṛttā ra  tadātma ra  nānādharmayonama ra nīlatvā nāsti a  ekakāryajananā ra  bhinna ra  prācīnarūpa ra  nakāronāsti a  dharmaṇiṣṭhinta    rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaupohā yaduktam kṣaṇikebhyo nivartamānaṃ sattvamasādhāraṇamupā dadānasya svabhāvabhedāpattiriti tannirastam kālpanika iva bhedapratibhāso na tāttviko bhedaḥ  kiṃ ca tāttvikasvabhāvabhedāpattāvapi sattvamasādhāraṇamiti śraddhāvadheyameva  na hi vastūnāṃ parimāṇātirekeṇanityādiva kṣaṇikādapi vyāvṛttaṃ bhavati sattvam yatosādhāraṇamavadhāryeta  svabhāvabhūmani kaścinnityopi syāditi cet   tamanupatattaha sattvaṃ  a sādhāraṇamanaikāntikamāśaṅkayatām  tacca cintyam  bādhakānāṃ vyāttavadanānāṃ saṃbhavāt atha svabhāvaparamparāsaṃbhave bhāvasyeva paribhavāt kasya kṣaṇikatvamiti kṣaṇikādapi vyāvṛttamucyate tadapi nāsti  svayameva svabhāvebhyo bhinnasya svabhāvinaḥkriyāsamarthana rakṣāvidhānāt  na ca svabhāvabhedasaṃbhave mūlasya kṣayopi yuktaḥaparimitopādhisaṃbhavepi tadvato vyayāniṣṭaḥ  asmadarśanepi yadi nāma vastvantararāśerudayaḥ tathāpi prakṛtabhāvasya kīdṛśī kṣayopapattiriti vyaktametat  sa turāśi pramāṇamanviyānnaveti cintyam  bhavatu vā mūlāpalāpaḥ  ye tu svabhāvābhāvikā iṣṭāḥ tadātmani magnatvānmūlasyaikaṃ pṛthak sat kṣaṇikaṃ mā bhūt  bhūyāṃsastukṣaṇikāḥ santa ityupacaya eva kṣaṇikatāyā   kathaṃ kṣaṇikatāyāḥ sattvavyāvṛttiḥ tadevamevaṃvidhāḥ pralāpā grāmjanajanitamahimānasteṣveva śobhante na tarkakarkaśa kuśāgrīya buddhiṣu bauddheṣu  yā tu śikṣā svabhāvabhedasādhanāya syādetaditvādi saiṣāmevāstu anyonyasya svabhāva iti svasthasya vaktumaśakteḥ  svabhāvabhedastu sādhanāsaṃbhavādadhyakṣabādhanācca parihṛta eva  na ca bhavannapi prakṛtadoṣasaṃsparśī nāpisahakāryantarameva svabhāvāntaramiti dantaniṣkoṣikayā svabhāvabhedasādhanā hetavoviparyāsayituṃ śakyante  kṣaṇikavādī hi sahakāriṇa paśyanneva  prasiddhasvabhāvabhedasādhanāya sādhanamupanṣasya na kathamapyanena vacasā pratārayituṃ śakyaḥ  tadvaraṃ tatsādhanamasādhanameveti mukhyamākhyāyatāniṣṭasiddhavyāghātāditi  sandeho mohād ra  sattvena ca vastu na vastu dharmiṇāmasā a  tattva ra  tanna ra sattvamiti nāsti a  sū    nyasya ra   rāśi ra   rivyakta a  pramāṇemanvi ra  kṣaṇitāyāḥ a  jana iti nāsti ra  tyādi ra  svabhāvakābhi     bhedastadaiva ra  doṣasparśī a  kāryāntara a  niṣṇoṣika  ra  vākṣante ra  pretināsti rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraḥtatra coktamasmābhiḥ  na ca sahakārisādhanāyaiva apratyavasthāturayaṃ prayatnaḥ kāryeṇānubhūtānvayavyatirekā hi sahakāriṇaḥ pratyakṣādipramāṇasiddhā eva kimatrasādhyam  tatokṣaṇikābhimatasya kramavatīṣu kāryavyaktiṣu svalakṣaṇabhedasādhana upanyastedūṣaṇamanuktvā sahakāryantarameva svabhāvabheda iti lapanaṃ yadi svahṛdayasantoṣamālambeta ālambatām  na tu parasādhyaṃ bādhitamanena  tasmāt siddhamarthakriyākāritvamasthairyeṇa vyāptamiti yadapyanenoktam  kiṃ cedaṃ tāvadayaṃ kṣaṇikavādī praṣṭavyaḥ  pūrvasya kṣaṇasyottarasminnekasantānavartini kṣaṇe kartavye nānyat kiñcidapekṣaṇīyamasti  tataśca parotpattipratyanapekṣatvāt tanmātrānubaddhenottareṇāpi satyeva tasmin bhavitavyam  abhavan vātanmātrānubaddho na syāt api tu nimittāntarāṃpekṣo vijñāyeta  asabhāgotpattau tupūrve samānasantānavartana ekasantānāntarbhūtatvāviśeṣāt samarthā asamarthā vābhaveyuḥ  tena santānāntaravartikṣaṇapratibandhasāmarthya sāpekṣa kṣaṇa syāt  na tusabhāgakṣaṇapratibandhotpattau  tathā ca sati pūrvaṃkṣaṇasattāmātrānubandhitvāviśeṣāduttarottaraḥkṣaṇaḥ paurvāparyaṃ tyaktvā yugapadutpadyeta  tataśca prabandhāpekṣakāryabkṣaṇakālabhāvināṃkṣaṇānāṃ prabandha ucchidyeta  tataśca trailokyavatisakalavastusantānabhāvināmaneneva paryāyeṇaprabandhocchedādanyonyasaṃpī ḍi tā  kṛtsnā trilokī prasajyeta athāpi samayasamayabhāvitvāt savyetaragoviṣāṇayoriva kāryakāraṇabhāvonāstītyucyate yadyevamatīte kṣaṇe pūrvasmin vastvantara utpadyeta sati ca notpadyetaityapūrvoyamanvayavyatirekānugamaprakāra  etayāpi dvārā kṣaṇikānāmarthakriyākāritvamevānupapannamiti tadapi sarvamasaṃbaddham  tathāhi yat tāvat pūrvasyottare kartavye nānyatra kaciṃdapekṣeti tatra sabhāgā uttare sarva eva kṣaṇā abhipretā bhavataḥ  anyathā sarveṣāṃ yaugapadyaprasañjanamanupapannaṃ syāt  tatra yadi svābhiprāye dūṣaṇaṃ tadā na kaścid vipakṣa  atha saugata eva praṣṭavyaḥ tadā pūrvasya uttarasminnanantara eva kṣaṇe kartavye nirapekṣatvaṃ tatrevo a  sādhanāyai pra ra  nānukṛtā ra  mamuktvā a  naya  ye na ra yat a  syakṣaṇa iti nāsti a  kartavye iti nāsti a  bandhe a  bandho ra pūrvasa ra  rbhuvo viśeṣā a  bhāsaprambādhā ra  prabandho ra  ndhākṣepa ra saṃpītā a saṃpītitā ra  samasamabhāvi ra  kṣaṇāt ra  pūrvasminnuttara utpa ra tvamanupapanna ra  panna miti ra  vivakṣa  ra  kṣaṇa a jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalaunottare kṣaṇe  sa eva tarhi tasya svabhāvo nāsti yastadutpādakaḥ  tataḥ svabhāvasāpekṣatvātkathamanapekṣaḥ  sa tarhi svabhāvaḥ kadācidasya bhāvī na bhāvī tarhi tadapekṣa itivācoyukteḥ korthaḥ  ayamarthaḥ  yaducyate devadattotra kārye yajñadattāpekṣaḥ samarthaiti  tatra dvayaṃ pratīyate svayamasamartha iti yajñadattena saha samartha iti ca  na casarvo vyavahārastattvānurodhī  kiṃ tu kvacit kiñcit satyam  tadatrāpi svayamasamarthaityayamaṃśa ubhayasaṃmatatvād dupahnavaḥ  sa eva paścādanyena saha samartha ityatra tuvivādaḥ  ataeva sādhane bādhanāvatāraḥ  atastadaṃśāsiddheḥ  tadapekṣaṃ svayaṃ śabdamapyapanīya kvacit sāpekṣa ityasamartha ityevārtha  tata uttarottare karttavyeasaṃbhavini tadutpādanasvabhāve sāpekṣa iti korthaḥ  uttarottarakartavye samarthaḥ  tadatra yad dūṣaṇaṃ taducyatām ataevāparāparapratyayayogena pratikṣaṇabhinnaśaktayaḥ saṃtanvantaḥ saṃskārā yadyapi kutaścitsāmyāt sarūpā  pratīyante tathāpi bhinna evaiṣāṃ svabhāvastena kiñcideva kasyacitkāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ veti nyāyaḥ kāraṇamupayogo vānyā saṃbhavīti sāmānyatovikārakāraṇayogādaṅgasya svabhāvabhedaniścayaḥ  evamatrāpi bīje puruṣabuddhiprayuktakarasparśādasti svabhāvabheda sūkṣma hetuphalabhedabhāgīti sāmānyato durnivāro niścayaḥ tataḥ svābhavabhedasaṃbhavāt tadeva bījamupayujyate paramparayāpyaṅkuropajananānuguṇe viśeṣenānye bījakṣaṇā iti siddhametat yattūktaṃ na khalūpasarpaṇetyādi  tadetat kasya pratyakṣīkṛta  prastute parasparātiśayaniṣedhaḥ  nāpyanumānātyadyucyeta kṣityādau janayitavye tadupādānaṃ pūrvameva kṣityādibījasya rūpāntaramiti bhupa pā dayitu ra   māyāsyapi ra  apīti nāsti ra hetviti nāsti a  jananaguṇe viśeṣe a viśeṣa ra vasita ra  bādhasya a  na pratyakṣataḥ ra  yadyucyeta ityādi uktena krameṇa sattvaṃnivṛttamityasādhāraṇānaikāntāda ityanto bhāgaḥ patitaḥ akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraḥna tarhi bījaṃ tadapekṣaṃ kṣityādīnāṃ janakam tadanapekṣatve teṣāmaṅkarād bhedānupapatteḥ  nacānupakārakā apekṣanta iti tvayevoktam  na ca kṣaṇasyopakārasaṃbhavonyatra jananāttasyābhedyatvāt  tathā cārthakriyāyā ekatvānekatva sāpekṣa tvānapekṣatvavyāptatvāttṛtīyaprakāravirahāt  anayoranyataraniṣedhasyānyataravidhānanāntarīyakatvāt  akṣaṇikeca tadvyāpakayorekatvānekatvayoḥ sāpekṣatvānapekṣa vayoḥ prakārayorabhāvāt uktena krameṇasattvaṃ nivṛttamityasādhāraṇānaikā ntā davyabhicāriṇo liṅgasyānupadarśanādupadarśayitumaśakyatvācca  bādhakasyaiva vidyamānatvāt  tasmānnāniṣṭamātraghoṣaṇena kiñcit  etena nopakāropekṣārtha ityanapekṣaiva kṣaṇikasya sahakāriṣu nobhayavyāvṛtiḥ atha saṃbhūyakaraṇamapekṣārtha  tadapi yadi pūrvasthitasyeti viśeṣaṇāpekṣā tadāpikṣaṇikasya naiva kācidityanapekṣaitrākṣīṇā atha pūrvasthitasyeti nāpekṣate militāvasthitasya karaṇamātramapekṣārthaḥ tadāsāpekṣataiva nānapekṣā  tathāpi nobhayavyāvṛttiḥ b athāsmatsamayāpekṣayā apekṣāsthitiḥ  tadā sāpekṣamasamarthamevasamarthitavanto vayamiti yatkāryaṃ prati yadasa tatsāpekṣam yattu samartha tadanapekṣamiti vyavasthā  tadā caikaniṣedhenāparavidhānāt sāmarthyarahitaṃ  samarthameva bhavatya sāmarthyam  uktaṃ casamarthameveti natarāmubhayavyāvṛttiḥ kṣaṇikatve yaccāvocat api cāntyakṣaṇaprāptaṃ bījamanapekṣyāṅkarāvanipavanapāthastejāṃsijanayat  ki yenaiva rūpeṇākara janayati tenaiva taditarāṇyapi kiṃvā rūpāntareṇa na tāvattenaiva kṣityādīnāmapyaṅkarasvābhāvyāpatteḥ  na khalu kāraṇābhede bhedavat kāryaṃbhavitumarhati kāryabhedasyākasmikatva prasaṅgāt yadāha ayameva hi  bhedo bhedaheturvā yaduta viruddhadharmādhyāsaḥ kāraṇabhedaśceti  nāpi sāmagrībhedaḥ tasyā apyekatvāt  anyathā sahabhāvaniyamābhāvāt dityapekṣai asāmarthyameva rahita ra tasyāpye ajñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalaurūpāntareṇa taditareṣāṃ janakam  tathā hi bījamakaraṃ janayadupādānam tadvikriyayātadutpatteḥ  taditareṣu punarasya sahakāripratyayatā teṣāṃ tu pūrve pavanādayo yathā svamupādānāni tadvikriyayā tadutpādāditi cet  nanu sahakāritopādānate kimekaṃ tattvaṃnānā vā  ekaṃ cet kathaṃ rūpāntareṇa janakam  nānātve tu anayobajāda bhedobhedo vā  bhede kathaṃ bījasya janakatvam tābhyāmevāṅṅkarādīnāmupapatteḥ  abhede vā kathaṃ bījasya na nānātvam bhinnatādātmyāt  etayorvekatvamekatādātmyāt yadyucyeta kṣityādau janayitavye tadupādānaṃ pūrvameva kṣityādi bījasya rūpāntaramiti  na tarhi bījaṃ tadanapekṣaṃ kṣityādīnāṃ janakam  tadanapekṣatve teṣāmakurādbhedānupapatteḥ  na cānupakārakāriṇopekṣanta iti tvayaivoktam  na ca kṣaṇasyopakārasaṃbhavonyatra jananāt tasyābhedyatvāt  tathā cārthakriyāyā ekatvānekatvasāpekṣatvānapekṣatvavyāptatvāt  tṛtoyaprakāravirahās  anayoranyataraniṣedhasyānyatara vidhānanāntarīyakatvāt  kṣaṇikavad vyāpakayorekatvānekatvayoḥ sāpekṣatvānapekṣatvayoḥprakārayorabhāvāduktena krameṇa sattvaṃ nivṛttamityasādhāraṇānaikāntikatvaṃ gandhavattvāderiveti yadi manyeta anupakāriṇopi bhavanti sahakāriṇopekṣaṇīyāśca kāryeṇānuvihitabhāvābhāvatvāt  sahakāryakaraṇācca  nanvanena krameṇākṣaṇikopi bhāvonupakārakānapi sahakāriṇa kramavataḥ kāryeṇānukṛtānvayavyatirekānapekṣiṣyate kariṣyateca kramavatsahakārisamavadhānavaśāt krameṇa kāryāṇīti vyāpakānupalabdherasiddheḥ sandigdhavyatirekamanaikāntikaṃ sattvaṃ kṣaṇikatvasiddhāviti  tadapi pūrvameva nirastam yatpunarayamadhikamāha  nāpi a sāmagrībhedaḥ tasyā apyekatvāditi  tatrāpibrūmaḥ  yathā sāmagrayā abhedaḥ tathā kāryāṇāsapyabhedāt kathaṃ na kāraṇābhedānukāra nanu pratiniyatānekarūpāṇāṃ kāryāṇāmabheda iti keyaṃ vācoyuktiḥ  yadyevaṃ nakhalu samagrebhyo bhinnā kācidadhyakṣagocaraḥ  saugatamate ca cinteyam  tatobhinnāsāmagrīti samagrā eva pratiniyatānekamūrtayobhinnā ityapi kīdṛśī vācoyuktiḥ sāmagrīlakṣaṇakāraṇabhedābhedācca samavadhāraṇa ra rasiddhi a  khalva a  bhinna a  iti śabdo nāsti rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāravācaspaterucitaḥ anyathā bījamekaṃ kathamaṅkurasarodharaṇidhāmādi janayedityetāvataivagatametat  na kāraṇabhedād bhedaḥ atha bhinnātmānopi bījādaya kayācit pratyāsattyā ekavyavahāragocarī kiyante evamaṅkurādayopīti kāraṇābhedebhedopi siddhaḥ  tatra kāraṇānāmekaikārthaṃjanakatvamekavyavahārahetuḥ niṣedhobhedopapattirvā akriyaiva vā  tato vikalpārūḍharūpāpekṣayānekena rūpeṇānekakaraṇamitivyavahāramātraṃ na vastu  vāstavī ca cinteyam  tat kimanena vikalpitena kiṃ tenarūpeṇānyena veti  vikalpepi vānekenaiva visarjanaṃ vyavahāramātreṇa  na ca kaściddoṣaḥ dvitīyapakṣastvanekasvalakṣaṇadarśane satyupapadyate  na ca bīcasvalakṣaṇāni api kṛtakāni ra  labdha iti nāsti a  sveti nāsti a  bhede ca a rūpeṇāṅkuraṃ karoti ki tenaiva kṣitimiti  yenaiva sahakāriṇāṅkaraṃ janayati kiṃ tenaiva bhuvamiti  etacca kadocyate yadibījasyāṅṅkurakaraṇe nirjāte niyatarūpaḥ kaścit sahakārī vyāpāravān bhāvaḥsādhyetarayoraniścitānvayavyatireko gandhavattvādivadasādhāraṇo yuktaḥ  prakṛtavyāpakānupalambhabalācca sarvathārthakriyaivāsatīti tat kathamasādhāraṇānaikāntikī bhavitumarhati   asiddhidūṣaṇaṃ tu vaktumucitam  tatra coktameva atha kṣaṇikatve vyāpakābhāva ityuktam tanna sarvathāsattvamiti cet  evaṃ tarhividyamānaivārthakriyā kṣaṇikādeva vyāvartate tato niyamenākṣaṇike viśrāmyantītitena vyāpta iti viruddhatāpyastu atha sākṣādakṣaṇike tasyā bādhakasya sādhakasya vā virahāt sandeha iti cet vidyamānatve kṣaṇikād vyāvṛttireva sādhanī tasyāḥ sandeha manavakāśayati  vidyamānatāsandehe ca sandigdhāsiddhireva dūṣaṇam kiṃ ca prakṛtavyāpakānupalambhasya kṣaṇikavadakṣaṇikepi sāmarthyānapāyāt kathaṃbādhakasiddhirityasiddhiretra sarvathāyātā  śakyaṃ hi nityepi vaktuṃ na sahakāriṇi sakṛdaneka a  kṣitimiti  kiṃ tenaiveti nāsti ra  kāraṇenirjati ra  svaprasiddha ra na kāraṇa ra  atinirbandhana ra  lambhanācca ra  vāsatīta katha ra  prasiddha ra niyamena kṣa a  myantī tena a  vyāghāta a  viruddhatāstu a  bādhakāsiddhi akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyenvayādhikāraḥsāpekṣasya karaṇamupakārābhāvāt  na nirapekṣasya tena vinā karaṇāt  sthiraṃ cabījamakara jana venaiva rūpeṇa kṣitimutpādayati bhinnena vetyādi yadā visadṛśakṣityādizanmopālambhaḥ pradīpopi cākṣaṇika eva bhavatām  tatra vartivikāratailakṣayā vekenabhinnena vā rūpeṇaṃ kriyetāmiti samānam  yastu samādhi sahakāriṇa eva bhinnāḥtasya svarūpabheda iti evaṃ ca bruvatā paropyātmā ātmāpi para iti nivṛttedānīmātmaparādiśabdebhyaḥ pratiniyatārthapratyāyanapratyāśā  na ca devadattasya svarūpaṃ yajñadattaḥśuklasya vā nīlamityucitaṃ kvacidekakarmaṇi vyāpārepi tadetadapetāgamayuktikaṃ paraspardhayābhidhīyamānaṃ niyatamupahāsabhājanīkaroti sahakāriṇovadhīryaṃ ca svarūpaśabdavācyamarthaṃ pṛcchata  sahakāriṇottaramiti vyaktaṃ natena nānyena vātmanā janayati sthiropi bhāva iti niyatamanujñātaiva vyāpakānupa labdhi  anyasyāpi hi sa evātmā janako na svayamiti na kaścijjanakaḥ  tadayaṃ sthirāsthirayoḥ sādhāraṇo nyāyaḥ kriyāniṣedhasādhana iti  tasya dṛḍhatve sarvathā kriyaivanāstītyasiddhireva antataḥ kramayogapadyavirahalakṣaṇasyāpi doṣasyāparihārāt  sthirepikriyānivṛttiravaśyābhyupeyā kathamanyathā kṣaṇike kriyāniṣedhābhidhānena kevalenāsādhāraṇatāpratijñā nivṛttimālambeta  na hi sādhyād vyāvṛttirityevāsādhāraṇatā anyathā vipakṣād vyāvṛttirityeva kiṃ nāsādhāraṇatvamucyate kimiyatā prayāsena  nanu vipakṣād vyāvṛttyā sādhye niyamāddhetureva syāditi cet  sādhyād vyāvṛttyāvipakṣe niyamād viruddha eva a  syāditi samānam  tasmādarthakriyāyā pratijñāmātrepyasiddhireva athānyena prakāreṇa ubhayoraniścayamātraṃ sattāyāḥ khyāpyate tathā ca satyasādhāraṇatā yuktaiva  tadayuktam  vyāpakānupalambho hyekāntatobhāvaniścayakara evaṃ kathamaniścayaḥ  tatra yadi nāma kramādyanupalambhasya nityāt sattānivartakasya dāḍhayaṃmasaṃgatam tathāpi prakṛtasya kṣaṇinityatābādhanasya dṛḍhatvamabhipretameva anyathopanyāsāyogāt  tataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgarāt kriyāyā aikāntiko vyāvṛttireva vyāvṛttirasādhāraṇatāyāḥ  nahi gandhavatvaṃ kutaścidekāntena vyāvṛttamavasātuṃ śakyam  tadayaṃ vyā vākṣaṇikā ca bhavatā ra  samānamiti nāsti ra   tāsvapra ra  pṛta    ra  pratijñānevṛtti a  nakārastyavataḥ a  kriyāyāṃ sādhurasādhāraṇatāsādhane apekṣamāṇaśca sarvathā kriyāmevonmūlayatītyasiddhireva na sādhyasādhanabhāva   tasmādbāhyavedanaṃ bāhyavedakapramāṇasiddhāṃ cārthakriyāṃ vastusatīmāśritya vādaprakrame tasyāsādhāraṇatāvādinā na sādhyetarathorekatra vṛttirekato vyāvṛttirvopadarśayitavyā ki tūbhayatrasaṃśayamātraṃ śaraṇīkaraṇīyam  na ca vyāpakānupalambhe saṃbhavastasya  tasmānnasādhurasādhāraṇatopanyāsa iti sthitam na cakālāntarasyādetat  yadi bhinnakālakāryaṃjanmani janakasya svabhāvabhedaḥ tadā  bhinnadeśakāryotpādepyeṣa prasaṅgaḥ  tadavaśyaṃ sahakāryapekṣayaiva natathā deśabheda iti etādṛśasya bādhakasya deśabhedepi vaktuṃ śakyatvāt  yathā yatyatkāryaṃ tat taddeśaṃ yathopādeyābhimataṃ tatkāryaṃ ca kāryāntaramapīti tukāryāpekṣayā  ayogavyavacchedena ca tatkaraṇam  anyathā deśāntaravataḥ kāryasyakaraṇaprasaṅgāt  evaṃ tarhi kāle karotīti sa kāla   kāryasyaivādhāro niyamena hetostu sa cāsacca syāt  ayogavyavacchedena ratvekakālakāryakaraṇamiti kālāntara vatopi kāryasya karaṇamavirodhi  tasmāt kuśūlādisarvāvasthāsamānasvabhāvasthāpitadatatkālakāryaṃjananamupapannam bhinnadeśānekakāryārjanavaditi paryavasthatyakṣaṇike sarvathānupapadyamāneyaṃ sattā kṣaṇabhaṅganiyataiveti evaṃsattāvataḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ niyatasvabhāvabhedopasthāpanāt tadabhāvepi sattāsaṃśayakṣaṇaḥ pūrvapravṛttopisvayameva parigalati parigavati  saṃbhavattena niya rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikārayadi tu tadabhāvepi syāt tadā tasyāṃ satyāṃ niyamena kṣaṇikatvamityanvayopikatham  tasmāt sādhyābhāve sādhanasyaikāntiko vyatirekaḥ sādhane sati sādhyasyāvaśyamanvayo veti na kaścidarthato bhedaḥ  pramāṇavyāpārastu mukhyatorthataśceti dvidhāvyavahāraḥ  ataeva yatra yatra sādhyaviparyaye bādhakapramāṇaparyeṣaṇā  tatra sādhanesati sādhyānvayaḥ sādhakapramāṇaparyeṣaṇāpi tayopalakṣitā veditavyā  viparyayabādhakaśabdena punarubhayasaṃgraha eva  vyatirekarūpavyāptau hi sādhyaviparyaye bādhakaṃsādhanasya anvayarūpāyāṃ tu sādhyaviparyayasya bādhakaṃ sādhane satīti  tadubhayābhāvesādhanasya sādhyapratibandhānupapattirityayamarthaḥ  anyathā vyatirekaniścāyakapramāṇasyasākṣādalābhepi yadi sādhanasya sādhyenānvaya a niyamaprasādhakaṃ pramāṇamupadarśayet kastasya sādhyasiddhau pratibandho vyatirekasyānvayasyāpi sāmarthyākṣepāt anyathā sādharmyaprayogonupādeya eva syāt sākṣād vyatirekānupadarśanāt  tadyadi
