tadbhāvevaśyaṃbhāvi sādhyaṃ tadā phalitaḥ  sādhanasvīkāraḥ tasmāt sādhanavādinā  dvayamapi paryeṣaṇīyaṃ vikalpena vādinā caikopi prakārapramāṇasiddha upadarśayitavyaḥ parasādhaneṣu ca vyatirekavadanvayopi niyamavān durlabhaeveti veditavyam asmābhistu prakṛtasādhane niyamavānanvayaḥ prasaṅgaviparyaṃyābhyāṃ paurastyābhyāṃdarśita eva tau ca yadyapi sapakṣīkṛte jalabhṛti pravartitau tathāpi yo yatkaraṇasvabhāvaḥsa tajjanayatyeva yo yantra janayati na sa tatkaraṇasvabhāvaḥ ityevaṃ pravartamānausarvameva kriyāśaktiyuktakṣaṇikatve niyataṃ darśayata iti sarvopasaṃhāro vyatirekākṣepabījaṃdhūmādivat  yathā cādhyakṣaṃ dhūmasya dhūmadhvajena vyāpti pratiyato na varmahānasesattāmanupasaṃharat pratyeti tathā jalabhṛti kṣaṇikatāṃ pratiyadeva yathoktānumānaṃsāmānyena kriyāvataḥ sādhāraṇanyāyatayā kṣaṇikatayā vyāptimātanotīti  yaduktaṃ apīti nāsti a  yadaiva ra dharmoṣaṇa a  nvayasādhaka ra   dubhayabhāve ra anvayamaprasādhaka ra  prabhāvaka a  sādhyabhitau ra   syāyamānarthyā ra  nvayadarśa a apīti nāsti ra  sāti ra  pāṭhospaṣṭa a  prayuktakṛtī a  satīti nāsti ra phalinaḥ ra  vādini ra  narva ra  saṃharatā ra  pratipadeva rajñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalīprāk na sattvādanyadanumāna sthirasiddhau yatonavasthā na syāditiyathoktaprasaṅgaviparyaṃyayorapi tatsādhakatvāditi tadapāstamyadyevamanarthaṃkaḥ sattvahetūpanyāsa iti cet  brūmaḥ  kiṃ hetvantarasattāmātreṇabandhyaṃ sādhanāntaraṃ  uta pakṣīkṛte tasyāpyupanyāsāt athopanyasituṃ śakyatvātyadi vāvaśyopanyasanīyatvāt yad vā yadarthaṃkāri tadavaśyaṃ kṣaṇikamiti vyāptisiddhaujaladharavat kṣitidharāderapyarthaṃkāriṇaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiriti pakṣāḥ tatra prathamastāvat na yuktaḥ anekasādhanasaṃbhavepi vivakṣopanītasyaiva paropayogāt  ataeva śakyopanyāsatvamapi nānathaṃkyahetuḥ tādṛśasyāpyupanyāsātprāgaprāgalbhyāt  sādhyadharmiṇyupanyāsaścāsiddhī dṛṣṭāntadharmamātre upanyāsāt ataeva pakṣevaśyamupanyāsāpekṣāpyasiddhā tadvalād vyāptisiddhau saṃścāyaṃ capalacāmaraityetāvataiva sādhyasiddheḥ  antimastu doṣaḥ sarvatra sarvopasaṃhāravatyāṃ vyāptau asiddhāyāṃ śaṅkāmavakāśayati na ca tatra viparyayabādhakasyāpi viśeṣa kevala sāmānyena kriyāvati jhaṇabhaṅgitayā vyāpteḥ siddhepi viśeṣe pravṛttyathina saccedamityavaśyopanyasanīyatvāditi kimatra nirbandhena  nanu tathāpi dṛṣṭāntadharmaṇi tāvattadanumānamavaśyāśrayaṇīyaṃ vyāptisādhanāya b tadeva ca kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanaṃ svadharmiṇaḥevaṃ sati sādhyadharmiṇyapi tadupanthasyaiva nirvṛtirālambyatām kimiyatā prayāsenavibhāgena tadanumānāvatāraṇam  tena ca vyāptaṃ sattvaṃ pratītya sattvāt pakṣe kṣaṇabhaṅgaiti yadyevaṃ viparyaṃyabādhakapramāṇavādinopi samānaḥ paryanuyogaḥ tenāpi yad yadāyajjananasvabhāvamityādiprayogasya vyāptisiddhāvapekṣaṇāt sādhyadharmiṇi sāmarthyānapāyācca tasya  tasmāt pratipattuḥ pravṛttibhedamāśritya vibhāgotra kartavyaḥ yo hi prativastu yo yajjananasamarthaḥ ityādikamavatārayan kṣaṇikatāparīkṣaṇakṣama tasya tata evakṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiḥ kimanyahetunā  evaṃ parapratipādanepi pratyekavastuṣu tathaiva sādhayataḥkṛtamanyahetūpanyāsena  yastu tadapekṣayā pratibuddhabuddhiḥ sa ekatra tatsādhanavyāpāreṇa vāsara a capi  vāpi ra   mubhayasvīkṛta tasyā ra  yadi vā   yadarthakāni ra hi pakṣopa ra  yogī  gitāra  syopanyā ra  prākra asiddhāyāmiti nāsti ra  viparyānnākasyāpi a viparyavā    bādhaka ra  kevala a bhaṅgatayā a  cakāro nāsti a  sattvātayākṣaṇa ra   manavatā akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥnyāyena sarvasya kriyāvata iyameva gatiriti kṣaṇikatayā tadvyāptimanavadhārayanpratyekaṃ tannyāyāvatāraṇaprayāsamanāviśanneva yathā svayaṃ  yaṃ yamarthakriyāsamarthaṃ paśyatitaṃ tamasthiraṃ sthāpayatīti sattvahetorupayogaḥ tathā parapratipādanepi tannyāyasiddhavyāptikaṃ sattvameva vyāpārayatīti na doṣaḥ  tadatra prativastu tannyāyāvatāraṇaprayāsaḥasahya eva  agatikatayā tvādyaḥ pratipattā tamevāśrayet  dvitīyastu saprajñatayā ekatra pravṛttena tannyāyena jhaṭityeva kriyāmātramasthairyaparatantramavadhārayan sattvenaivaparamapi pratipādayati na tu tannyāyasya kacit kriyāvati kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanasāmarthya pratighātaḥ nāpi satvādisādhanabandhyataiva  sādhyamiṇyapravartita tannyāyapratyupanyāsādityalaṃ  bahunā tadāpitadevaṃ vyāptirvyāpakasya vyāpyavati bhāva eveti kartṛdharmānvayarūpavyāptisaṃpāditasāmarthyādeva sattvahetoḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhirapratihateti kimatra vipayaṃye bādhakapramāṇopaviparyayasyaivanyāseneti samarthitam  ataeva tadupanyāsāśakyatāpi na pīḍayati bādhakena sādhyasya siddhatvāt  śāstrepi prathamaniyame ca vyāptiranvayarūpā bījādivadanekāntaparihāravyājena vistarata prasādhitā  sphuṭataramanudbhedāttu vyatirekalakṣaṇāyā parikaramātrametadāropayati loka iti atrāpi tīthiṃkavacanavikrāntikṛtaṃ kautukamasti vyatirekarūpāyāmeva vyāptau ki tunāpyekaiva vidhānyadāpiparakṛd vā bhavetsthirābhimatasyānyadā pūrvaṃ paścād veti kramanirdeśaḥ naiva kriyā vā bhavetanyadā naivetyavadhāraṇānna pūrva nāpi paścāt kriyetyakrama nirdeśaḥ yadi tu prāk nyāyeneti nāsti a  yaṃ yamiti nāsti ra  samartha ra  yadājñatayā a mānarthya a  pāṭhospaṣṭa a  pravartita nyāya ra  badhika ra  pīḍati a sādhyasiddha ra  bījādinekāntapara ra  kinna ra  kṛtvā ra  ṇānuparne ajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaupaścād vā syāt kadācit kriyā tadā krama a evetyasaṅkīrṇamanayorlakṣaṇamākhyātaṃbhavati  yadyapi caikasyā eva samasamayāṃ kriyāmapekṣya yaugapadyaṃ bhinnasamayamapekṣya kramaḥtathāpyapekṣaṇīyabhedādasaṅkara eva pitāputravat  akriyāgrahaṇena ca vastvabhāva evavā sarvathāstu kriyāśūnyaṃ vā svarūpamavaśiṣyatāṃ matabhedena nātra nirbandhaḥ  tatranāpyekaiveti pūrvaparayorekatvamātra vivakṣayā jātinirdeśaḥ pūrvā parā vā punarekānekāvā kriyā syāt  ekadā kriyāpakṣe vobhayamapyakramaśabdavācyatāṃ nātipatati tatrāpyanekakriyaiva tāttvikī puñjātpuñjotpattestāttvikatvāt  śaṅkāmātreṇānavaklṛptyāvā ekaṃkriyābhidhānam  ataeva yaugapadyaśabdena tasyāpyupalakṣaṇādakramasaṃgṛhīta evārthoyaugapadyapadepyavagantavyaḥ śāstre  etasya ca kāryagatasya prakāradryasya kartuḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgaeva saṅgatirityatyantībhāvāvadhāraṇā vṛtyā nityād vyāvṛttiruktā  prādhānyenakṣaṇabhaṅgasaṅgatirityakṣaraṃ tu nityādiva kṣaṇikādapi sā vyāvṛtti  śaknoti lakṣayitum athavā vyāpyasya vā tatraiva bhāva ityanukaraṇārtham  etena nityasya kramayogapadyābhyāmarthakriyāvirodhāt tallakṣaṇaṃ sattvamavahīyate ataḥ kṣaṇikatva eva viśrāmyati tenavyāpyata iti kramayogapadyalakṣaṇavyāpakānupalambhād viparyaye bādhakāt sattvasyārthaṃkriyāśaktilakṣaṇasya kṣaṇikatvena vyāptisiddhirityuktaṃ bhavati  tatra kartṛdharmo yadārtha kriyā tadārthakriyā śaktiriti vā vyavahāra ekārtha  kevalaṃ karmadharmasya kramayogapadyābhyāṃ vyāptau kathaṃ kartṛdharmasya vyāptivyavahāra iti syādāśaṅkā  tatrāpi kramākramika kāryaviṣayatayā vyāpyamānā kāraṇaśakti kramākramavyāptetyucyate vyavahāralāghavārtha miti etena kṛtvā karaṇalakṣaṇaṃ kramamāśritya kṣaṇikādayaṃ kramo nivartayituṃ śakyaityasāraprabandhaṃ trilocanacodyaṃ nirastam  arthakriyāvirodhādityatra cārthakriyo kartṛdharma eva veditavyaḥ tallakṣaṇaṃ sattvamiti vacanāt athavā lakṣaṇamupalakṣaṇaṃ na svabhāva iti karmadharmovyastu  tadatra pakṣe kramākramābhyāmupalakṣitārthakriyā nityasya virudhyata ityartha  prathamapakṣe tu kramākrameṇopalakṣitārthakāritvaṃ nityasya virodhītyartha  kramayogapadyābhyāmiti tu viśeṣaṇānna kṣya yaugapadyamityataḥ kramastathāpya pe iti bhāga patitaḥ ra  vastubhāva ra  rekā vā ra  tārthāta a  pātreṇā ra  tasyā apyapa ra  tantībhā ra  sādhyāvṛttiḥ ra bhyattena ra   ritītyu ra  dharmadharmasya ra  śakyeti nāsti a  canādyaṃ a tallakṣaṇa vacanāditi nāsti   nityasyeti nāsti ra  ṣaṇānnartho śe akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥśeṣābhyanujñāśaṅkā hetutvārthamupādānāt  yasmāt kramākramābhyāmevārthakriyā tatonityasya virodhinī kramākramātikramādityarthāt kaḥ punaratra virodha  na tāvat sahānavasthānamubhayovastutva prāptanityaṃ sadevasyāt nāpi dvitīyaḥ  nityaṃ hi tadviparītenānityena virudhyeta  kramākramavyāptācārthakriyā anarthakriyayaiva virudhyata iti cet  pramāṇabalena nityetyantaṃ tasyābādhasādhanād virodha eva pramāṇāntarabādhādveti vacanāt  vastutastu parasparaparihāraeva niṣṭhāsyati  kiṃ b punaḥ pramāṇaṃ akṣaṇikerthakriyābādhaka miti cet yadyat kramayogapadyavatyāmarthakriyāyāṃ nopayujyate tannārthakriyāśaktam yathā haripadāravindam  nopayujyate ca nityābhimato bhāvaḥ kramākramadharmaṇi karmaṇīti vyāpakānupalambhaḥ  na hi kramākramābhyāmanyaḥ prakārosti yenārthakriyāsaṃbhāvanāyāṃ tābhyāmavyāptirasyā bhavet  tasmādarthaṃkriyāmātrānubaddhatayā tayoranyatarasya prakārasya ubhayorabhāve cābhāvāttābhyāmasyā vyāptisiddhiriti pakṣīkṛte tayorabhāve cārthakriyāśaktyabhāvasiddhī nānekāntastāvat tatra yat śaṅkaraḥ kramākramābhyāmarthakriyāniṣedhe prakārāntareṇa saṃbhāvayannāha na ca tṛtīyasya prakārāntarasyābhāvasiddhiḥ viśeṣaniṣedhasya śeṣābhyanujñāviṣayatvādititannirastam  hetutvārthavacanena yattūpalabhyasvabhāvatve nātyantābhāvasiddhirupalabhyasvabhāvatvādeva paṭādivat  anupalabhyasvabhāvatve tu nāsattāniścayo viprakarṣiṇāmitikathaṃ prakārāntarābhāvaniścayastannimittāyogāditi viplavate  tatra yadyādaraḥ hanta hataḥprakāreyattāparicchedadvāreṇa tattvavyavasthānanibandhanaḥ svargāpavargamārgānuṣṭhānabhedaḥ yadā hi prakāradvaye tṛtīyaḥ śaṅkayate traye caturthaścatuṣṭayādau pañcamādiḥ tadā sarvatrānanta  prakāratve prakāradvayatrayādiniyamakṛtaṃ tattvavyavasthānaṃ kutaḥ  yathā catvāri pramāṇāniṣaṭ padārthā  yadā ca pramāṇaprakāraśatamanyadapi saṃbhāvyate tadā caturbhiryanna siddhaṃtadanyena siddhaṃ catuḥsiddhaṃ cānyena bādhitamiti kathaṃ tadvāreṇa tattvavyavasthiti    kriyāto ra  syāt ra  nityenā ra  virupyata ra  vārtha ra  kriyaiva ra tasyā iti nāsti a  miṣṭasyeti ra  kṣaṇike a  yadā ra   mate a rabhāvārtha ra  nānekāntambhavet ra  tve ca ra  ghaṭādi ra  ti viplavate itināsti ra   reyatā ra  nānimitta ra  dvayera  sthāsthānaṃ ra  vyavasthiti rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāṃvalauevaṃ yadārthasahasre dravyādivyatirekiṇi sidhyati tattvapariniṣṭhāviplavāt kimabhyudayaniḥśreyasayorvātmānuṣṭeyamastu  kathaṃ cānityasya jñānakāritvākāritvapakṣau dūṣayitvānirvṛtamanena svayamevaṃ prakāreṇa prakāraśatasya niṣemaśakyatvāt kiṃ ca paśavopi yadayuktaṃ paśyanti na tadaiva tadācarantīti kathamanena sāhasamida manuṣṭhitam  anupalabdhedṛśyaviśeṣaṇāpekṣābhyāṃ prakāradvaitaṃ niyamya kramākramābhyāṃdvaitanirākaraṇaṃ nāma prakārāntarasyopadaśayitumaśakyatvāditi tu kramākramepi dvaitavādināṃ nāśakyam  tasmāt kimapyayaṃ jalpamahodadhināmaparipuṣṭaye viceṣṭatāmekaniṣedhenāpara vidhāne tāvadaśakyābhidhānaḥ prakārāntarasaṃbhavaḥ kiṃ ca ekakālakriyānantaraṃ kriyāntarasya bhāve kramavyavahārobhāve cākramaiti bhāvābhāvayorapi tṛtīyaśaṅkati mahattārkikatvam tadalaṃ nirbaṃndhena sthitametatkramākramābhyāmarthakriyāśaktervyāptireveti yadapi trilocanaḥ kaścit sahakāripratyayaḥ pratyakṣa  parokṣaścetaraḥ  a tataḥpratyakṣaparokṣasahakāripratyayasākalyamasarvavidā pratyakṣato na śakyaṃ pratyetum  tathā casati sādṛśasahakāripratyayasākalyavataḥ kramayogapadyasyātyanta parokṣatvāt tena vyāptaṃsattvamapi parokṣameveti kathaṃ pratibandha  pratyakṣeṇa sidhyatītyāha tadapi nirupayogam kāryadharmo hi kramākramau pratipāditau  tataḥ kāraṇasāmagrayāḥ sākalyāsākalyaniścayābhāvepi kramayogapadyaniyama kāryāṇāmadhyakṣagocara eva  ekadaiva kāryotpattiranyadāpi neti kathamagocara  pratyakṣasya  tadāpi  hi kāryamekamanekaṃ vā syāt  pratyakṣeṇavā tathā gṛhītamanekasaṃbhavepi caiṃka gṛhītamastu sarvathā kramākramābhyāmeva vyāptākāryaniṣpatiriti siddhametat nanu kṣaṇabhaṅgapakṣe nārthaṃkriyāpratītiḥ nāpi kramākramapratītiriti kathaṃ vyāptivyavasthā  tathā ca śaṅkaraḥ kṣaṇikatve sati sarvasaṃvittīnāṃ svabhāvaniyamena hetuphalayoḥsvarūpānvayavyatirekāsiddhau sarvatra tadbhāvasyāvagantumaśakyatvāt na hi kāryasaṃvittyā tasya hetubhāve bhāvaḥ pratīyate tadā tasya hetoratītatvāt  nāpi hetusaṃvittyā niṣṭhāvipūrvāt a  sayordharmonu ra  kathañca ni ra  dūṣitvā ra  prakāreṇetināsti a  sasidvamida ra  kramāthita a  vādinā śakyaṃ ra  tātmikā ra sahakārivataḥ ra  parokṣeṇa a  madhyago ra  ti anya a  tadapi ra sarvadā ra  sarvatra aśakyatvāditi nāsti ra  na ca akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikārakāryasya tadbhāve bhāvovasīyate tadā tasyānupapattereva na cātītānāgatayovaṃtaṃmānena siddhiratiprasaṅgāt  nāpi kāryaṃsaṃvityaiva hetusvabhāvasaṃvittiḥ adṛṣṭānvayavyatirekasyāpi dhūmegnijanyatvaviniścayaprasaṅa gāt  etena hetumātrasaṃvittyāṃ kāryasaṃvittirapāstā  hetuvyatireke tu kāryavyatirekaḥ svasaṃvittivādino manorathasyāpyaviṣayaḥ tasya hetvabhāve kāryābhāvapratipattāvupāyāsaṃbhavāt  nahi tacca nāsti tena capratipattiriti nyāyyam  tadayaṃ kāryasya hetusadbhāve bhāvaṃ tadabhāve cābhāvaṃ pratipadyamānovasthitaṃ  pratisandhātāraṃ prasādhayatīti  evaṃ ca yadyavasthikartṛsiddhiḥ tadāsādharaṇānekānta eva maula  sattvahetuḥ kimatra viparyayabādhakapramāṇopanyāsaḥkariṣyati  tadaniṣṭī tu vyāptigrahānupapatteḥ sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvamubhayorapi yathā ca kramiṇī hetuphale pratyetumaśakye evaṃ phale apīti na kramapratītiḥ nāpi yaugapadyasya yathāha sa eva nāpi yaugapadyasya bhinnākāreṇa jñānena pratiniyatākārāṇāṃyaugapadyasthāśakyasādhanatvāt  na tāvadbhireva jñāne yaugapadyaṃ pratyetavyam teṣāmitaretarāsaṃvedyatve santānāntaravat yugapadbhāvasyāsiddheḥ  na caikamanekākāram svabhāvabhūtākārabhede bhedasyāvaśyaṃbhāvitvāt  bhede tu vijñānasyākārebhyorthāntaratvaprasaṅgena viṣayasya tadākāratvaṃ samarthitaṃ bhaviṣyatīti atrocyate pratisandhātṛsvīkārastāvadasaṃbaddhaḥ  pratisandheyābhimatā bhirbuddhibhirbhedābhedavikalpākṣamatvāt abhede b hi sa eva vā syād buddhaya eva vā  atraca prathamapakṣe karmaṇaḥ pakṣāntare  karturabhāvāt kaḥ pratisandhānārtha  bhedepi buddhibhyobhidyamānasya jaḍasya kaḥ pratisandhānārtha  buddhiyogād draṣṭavat pratisandhātṛtvamiticet  buddhireva tarhi draṣṭrī pratisandhātrī ceti niyatasvīkāre tadyogādanyasyatathātvamiti kimanena yācitakamaṇḍanena  buddhīnāṃ kartṛtvābhāvāditi cet  taddvāreṇāpi tarhi tasyātmano draṣṭṛtvādivyavahārānupapatti  yadi hi buddhirhetoḥ phalasyavā draṣṭrī syāt tadānantaryapratiniyamasya cānusandhātrī kalpikā tadyogāttasya draṣṭṛtvaṃ avasīyate  vartamānena siddhiriti bhāga patita ra  etena hetu vyatireke iti bhāgapatitaḥ ra  sveti nāsti ra  tacca bhāvaṃ ta iti nāsti ra  pratī a  maula itināsti ra  panyāsaḥ niṣṭhāviti nāsti  nāsti ra sya śakya ra  ntara eva ra yugapada manekā iti nāsti ra  tad bhedasyā ra  atra saṃbaddhaḥ iti nāsti ra bhāvāt buddhi iti nāsti ra  kimanena maṇḍaneneti nāsti rajñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalaupratisandhātṛtvaṃ vocyata iti syādapi  prativiṣayamalabdhaviśeṣāyāṃ ca buddhau saṃbandhopina viśeṣa vyavahārayitumīśaḥ adhunā nibandhanādhigantā adhunā phalasya idānīṃpratisandhāteti  tathāvidhabuddhigata viśeṣasvīkāre tu kimapareṇa kartavyam tāvataivaparyāptatvād vyavahārasya  sthirātmānamantareṇa  saiva buddhirna syāditi cet kenaivaṃ pratāritosi  aho mohamāhātmyaṃ yadīdṛśānapi paravaśīkaroti tathāhi nedamidamantareṇeti yaducyate tat khalvanyatra pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ sāmarthyāvadhāraṇe sati yujyate vahnariva dhūme cakṣurādivad vā dṛṣṭakāraṇasāmagra kāryādarśanepaścād darśane ca kiñcidanyadapekṣaṇīyamastīti sāmānyākāreṇa  ādyaḥ pakṣastāvannāstīti vyaktam  dvitīyopi na saṃbhavī  nahi kāraṇabuddhisamanantaraṃ kāryabuddhau satyāṃniścayapravṛttasya idamasthānantaraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mayeti pratisandhānamadṛṣṭapūrvaṃ kadācid yatonyasyasāmarthyaparikalpanaṃ syāt  evaṃ smaraṇamapyanubhavāt kutaścit paramparayā śaktipariṇāmadvāreṇa kutaścit sākṣāt tat paripākabalāditi ra anyasyānubhave tarhi kathamanyasya na smṛtiḥ anyasyeti na saṃbandhī siddhaśrodyaṃ kimīdṛśam anubhavādibhyo bhinnasaṃbandhisiddhayadhikaraṇavivādaprakrame tameva siddhamāsthāyaparyanuyoga ityasaṃbaddhametat  tatsiddhau hi vivādaparyavasānāt kā parāpekṣā  tasmādanyasyeti vivādapadatvādapanīyānubhave kathaṃ na smṛtiriti pariśiṣyamāṇaṃ na prakṛtopayogi evaṃ tu yujyate codyārthaḥ yaddehasaṃbaddhonubhavastadanyatra dehe kasmānna smṛterudaya iti evaṃ ca vadatā yatkṣetrasambandhi bījaṃ tadanyatra kṣetre kiṃ nāṅkurajanmetyuktaṃ bhavati  sa cakutastyo nyāyaḥ nanu kāryakāraṇabhāvamātrādanubhavasmaraṇayorna kācidaparā pratyāsattiḥ na cakāryakāraṇabhāveya niyamo yadādhārameva kāraṇaṃ tadādhārameva kāryamiti viṣayādatyantadūrepi jñānakāryadarśanāt  evaṃ tarhi nāṅkarasthāpi kāryatāmātrādaparā pratyāsattiritijñānamivāra dūrepi bījaṃ janayet  nanu bījārambhiṇa a eva paramāṇavaḥkecidaṅṅkure samavādhikāraṇatāṃ pratipadyamānāḥ kathaṃ kṣetrāntareṅkuramutpādayitumīśate  kimapi pareṇa ra   nantareṇa ra  ṇaiveti ra  sāmagrayo ra  anyanyā aasyā ra   siddhādhi a  parīti nāsti ra  sambandhe a  vapatā akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥbhavatastu tathāvidhapratyāsattivirahāt  vijñānādinā sādhāraṇaṃ kāryatvamasyeti dūrepijananaprasaṅgonivāryaṃ iti cet  kasmāt punaraṅkura eva kārye bījaparamāṇavaḥ samavāyakāraṇatāṃ pratipadyante na jñānādau kāryatvena sarveṣāmekarasatvāt  tataḥ sarveṣāmaṅṅkuravattaddeśa eva jananaṃ jñānādivad vāṅkarasyāpi dūre jananaṃ kāryatvenāviśeṣāttadvadevāṅkurepi nimittakāraṇatvād bījasya ekatrasantānavyavasthānamanyatrananu yatraiva kārye bījaparamāṇavaḥ samavāyikāraṇatāṃ pratipadyante sa evāṅṅkuraḥtat kathamaṅkurādanyatra teṣāṃ samavāyikāraṇatā codyate  evaṃ tarhi kāryatvenaikarasatayāsamavāyikāraṇatāyā duṣpariharatvādakaraikarūpatvaṃ sarveṣāmekadeśatā ca prasahyāyātetisthāne phalitaṃ parihārapratyāśayā  yadi ca kāryatvena sarveṣāmaviśeṣaḥ kāryāṇāmkāraṇānāmapi sarveṣāṃ kāraṇatvenāviśeṣa iti viśvasya vaicitryamatrāṇam tasmātkāryatve satyapi na rītirekaiva sarveṣāmiti  yathā  nisargabhedāt kacit kiñcitsamavāyikāraṇatvena kacidasamavāyikāraṇatvena kacinnimittakāraṇatvenopayujyatebhavataḥ tathāsmākamapi kiñcit kāryaṃ samānadeśameva heturutpādayati kiñcid vyavahita deśam kāryaṃ ca kiñcinniyamena hetudeśa evotpattidharmakaṃ kiñcidanyathā  tathaikatra kāryepratyabhijñāsaṃbhavo nānyatra kāryatvāviśeṣepi dīpāntaravat jñānavacca  tādṛk kāryātatropādānakāraṇavyavahārosmākapekṣayā ca yatra bhavataḥ samavāyikāraṇavyavasthāmātmāderanyatra  tathāvidhahetuphalaparamparāyāṃ casahakāritvamātramiti prakriyābhedepi kāryadvaitaṃ tādṛg nisargasiddhamastīti bhavatopyaśakyamatikramitumiti sthitametat  tathābhūtabhedasaṃbhave ca yatkāryakaraṇādhikaraṇaevotpattidharmakaṃ tatkathamitaratrotpadyate  kāraṇaṃ vā svādhikaraṇa eva śakyotpādanaṃ kāryaṃkathamanyatra janayet  tadayamanubhavopi svādhikaraṇajanyaṃ smaraṇamaṅkuramiva bījātrakathamanyatrotpādayet  smṛtirvānubhavādhikaraṇaniyatotpattiraṅṅkuravat kathamanyatrotpadyetayato dehāntare smaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ codyamavakāśamāsādayet  ātmavāde tu duṣpariha rametatuvyāpinastasya tenaiva smṛtijananarūpeṇa dehāntarepi sthānāt  adṛṣṭāśrayaṇaṃ ca nityasyaiveti bījāṅkuravadanubhavasmaraṇayornyāyo nānyavaditi kathamavagantavyamiti cet  viti nāsti a  kāryatve viśe a  kāraṇaṃ ra  deśabhāva    a  prasajyā  ra sarveṣāṃ savi ra  mātrāṇaṃ a  tathā ra  kiñciditi nāsti a  kvacidasamavāyakāraṇatveneti nāsti a  tatraikatra ra  tvāna  la  vacca ra  tathāvidhaphala a  nisiddha ra  kārya kāraṇā ra  bījātmā ra  smaraṇanyāyo rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalībījāṅkurayorapi sa nyāyastathā darśanādevāvasīyate  tathā niyamadarśanaṃ cānubhavasmaraṇayorapyasti na hyanyadehenubhavavati b anyamūrtiḥ smṛtimatī nāma nanu dehaḥ kathamanubhavavān  tadādhāratayā tatkāraṇatayā tena saha samānakāraṇatayāvā saṃbandhavivakṣāstīti na kṣatiḥ  kiṃ cātmanopi kathamanubhavavattvam  samavāyabalāditi cet  nanu samavāyopīheti buddhiheturiṣyamāṇa ihetibuddhinibandhanakalpanaeva  asti ceha śarīre buddhiḥ ataḥ kiṃ na samavāyakalpanāpi  ayutasiddhatvābhāvāt śarīrabuddhayoḥ pṛthageva pratīyamānatvāditi cet  nanu pṛthakpratīyamānayorihedamiti pratītiniyama uparyaṃdhobhāvena hi bhāvadvaye paridṛśyamāne parasparāsaṅkareṇasaptamīprathama yonirdeśa upapadyeta yadā tu pṛthagdarśanameva nāsti tadā kathamihedamitibhedena nirdiśan prekṣāvattāyā na hīyate  samavāyaviṣaye kacidapi bhedasyādṛṣṭeriticet  ataeva svayamiheti buddhi vikalpamātratvena icchayā nirvartanayogyāmutpādyasamavāyo nāma kalpyate iheti buddheḥ samavāyasiddhirihetidhīśca dvayadarśane syāt na ca kacittadviṣaye dvayekṣā svakalpanāmātramatobhyupāyaḥ tena cāsaṃvidyamānasyaivātmano buddhimattāvyavahāra iti bandhyāputreṇa turagaśṛṅgasyakholighaṭanavṛttāntamanuharati  yat khalu yāvatopayogena kalpitaṃ tāvata upayogasyaanyena siddhireva tasyābhāvaḥ siddhaścātmanopi smṛtyādhupayogonyatheti  tasmāt naikakāyasthonubhavaḥ kāyāntare smaraṇakaraṇāya prabhavati nanu kṣaṇikatve dehāntara eva smṛterudayāt kathamidaṃ śakyaparihāram janmāntaraparigrahe vā tataḥ santānāntaratvenābhimatepi dehe kiṃ na prasaṅgonyatvasthāviśeṣāditicet  īdṛśaṃ dehāntaraṃ smṛtijananamātmanopi duṣpariharam tatonyatrāpi tatprasaṅgonyatvasyāviśeṣāditi samānam  yadyapi ca kāyasya kṣaṇikatvaṃ neṣṭam āśunāśitvaṃ punastairiṣṭameva tataḥ samāno doṣo yadbhayādātmavādasvīkāraḥ  athātmavādetasyātmanaḥ karmaṇābhisaṃskṛta eva dehe smṛtijananamiti na doṣaḥ nairātmyavāde tu kasyatat karma  śārīrātiriktā hi buddhireva kṣaṇikā saṃbhavati  ataeva ca na kartṛkṣaṇasya  darśanādavasī ra  bhavati a  buddhivataḥ ra  vipakṣe ra  syāpi dṛ a icchāni a  nivarttamāna a  vā ra  syāravīṇi ra  vyogina a kāryakṣaṇi rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥtatkarmasukhaduḥkhādi saṃvartanīyam tasya tadupabhogābhāvāt  yasya ca kṣaṇasyopabhogaḥsokarteti kṛtanāśākṛtābhyāgamadoṣastvatirikto bhavatu na tu kasyacit karmasiddhiryataḥprakṛtadoṣa parihāra syāt  na ca santānopi gīyamāno bhinnaḥ kaścidasti  na cakarmāṇi bhinnaṃ bhavatāmastītyabhitti citrakarmaṃ tatrādyādatrocyate  kartṛkṣaṇasya tāvat tatkarma tatphalopabhogābhāvepi nāpaham nahi dāhādikamakurvato atpāditena vahninā tadvān na bhavati naraḥ  antimakṣaṇasyāpi tatkarmopakārakatayā saṃbadhyate paramparayā tata evopabhogabhāgitvāt ekakālatā tu kāryakāraṇayorapi na saṃbhavati saṃbhavati ca merumandarayoḥ  tasmādupakāradvārakameva  bhede tasyedamiti ghaṭanam sa copakārontimasya tatkṛto mahānastitanmadhyavartināṃ ca tatsantānavartināṃ kṣaṇānāṃ tādṛgantimakṣaṇaprasūtisāmarthya sākṣātparaṃparayā vā utata eva karmaṇa ityupakāradvāraka eva teṣāmapi tatsambandhaḥ  evaṃ casarveṣāṃ karmasambandhavyavasthitau sthitāyāṃ tatkarmādhipatyenopanīyamāna eva śarīretatkarmābhisaṃbhūtānāṃ buddhidehakṣaṇānāmudayaḥ nānyatra tādṛk pratyāsatterabhāvāt  karmaca kāmaṃ na bhinnamasti vyatirekīva  ca nirdeśopi vyavahārānurodhena  yastu prāktanaḥkarmasaṃbaddha ityucyate kṣaṇaḥ sa tādṛg viśeṣabhūto jātaḥ yataḥ payaṃnte tatphalopabhoktṛkṣaṇaprasavasamarthasantānasaṃbhavaḥ tadanurūpaśarīrasantatisaṃbhavaśva viśiṣṭād yau buddhidehakṣaṇau alpatamaviśeṣayogināvupajātau saṃbhūyottarāvalpataraviśeṣau  janayataḥ tau cālpaviśeṣāvuttarī janayata ityanayā diśā tāvacchattilakṣaṇaviśeṣaprakarṣastaratamādibhāvenopacīyate yāvadantimajananasamarthodayastatontima iti ekasāmagracadhonatayā parasparānubaddhayorbuddhidehayoranyaparamparāṃ prati viśiṣṭayornaikavyatirekeṇa dvaitīyikaśāvakāśaḥ  janmāntaraparigrahepi tadāyuḥ saṃskārakṣīṇe kṣīyamāṇamūrtikṣaṇāntarasahakāriṇā manaḥkṣaṇena janitaṃ tasyānurūpaṃ vapuranyat pūrvavanmanasaḥsāhāyakamātanotīti na dehāntare smṛtibhoktṛtvacintāvakāśaḥ  na cātra santānanāmnābhinnena kiñcit kṣaṇānāṃ karmasaṃbandhasiddhidvāreṇaiva santānepi siddherapratibandhāt gābhāvāt syopabho iti nāsti ra  na tviti nāsti ra  yataḥ yataḥ ra   karmakurva ra  parasparapāta ra  vvakāraka ra  codakārontimasyā ra  tadeva a  nāpanīyamānaṃ ra  saṃskṛtānāṃ ra  nuro iti nāsti ra  bhūṣitā a  santāna iti nāsti ra aṇutama ra yogiṇā a ra  vaṇutra ra  cāṇuvi ra  kṣīṇe iti nāsti ra janitasyā a  siddha prati rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalautebhyastasya vyatirekāt  na ca mukhyataḥ santānadvāreṇa siddhāntopakramaḥ kiṃ tukṣaṇadvāreṇeti sarvamavadātaṃ mūlapariśodhanāditi yaduktamyasminneva hi santāne āhitā karmavāsanā phalaṃ tatraiva badhnāti karpāse raktatā yathā iti tat svābhimatasantānalakṣaṇaprasiddhau yattu nyāyabhūṣaṇakāra etad dūṣayānnāha  na sādhanadūṣaṇāsaṃbhavāt anvayādyabhāvānna sādhanam  na hi kāryakāraṇabhāvāt smṛtiḥ karpāse raktatādivadityanvayaḥsaṃbhavati  nāpi yatra na smṛtiḥ tatra na kāryakāraṇabhāva iti vyatirekosti  asiddhatvādyanudbhāvanānna dūṣaṇam  na hi pūrvabuddhadhanubhūterthe uttarabuddhīnāṃ smṛtiḥ saṃbhavatitatonyatvāt santānāntarabuddhivadityasya hetoḥ karpāse raktatāvadityanena na kaściddoṣaḥpratipādyata b iti  tadasamīkṣyābhidhānam sādhanārthāparijñānāt  na hīhailoke kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ smṛtau hetutvenopanyastaḥ pratīyate  kiṃ tarhi  karmavāsanā vāsanā hi karmaṇābhisaṃskāra   vasitaṃ hyabhisaṃskṛtamucyate  karmakṛto viśeṣo yatrasantāne utpāditastatraiva bhogādiphalabandho nānyatra  yatra nāsau viśeṣa iti pratijñāyakarpāse raktatā yathā iti vadataḥ saṃskārasantānabhedo vā heturabhipretaḥ sādhyaṃcānyatra  bhogādiphalaniṣedhaḥ tatsantāne tatphalayogyatā ca pratīyate  tadayaṃ prayogaḥyo yaḥ saṃskāraḥ kacitsantāne āhitaḥ sa tatraiva phaladānayogyo nānyatra  yathākarpāsasantāne bījāvasthāyāṃ rāgadravyayogajanita puṣpāvasthāyāṃ phalāvasthāyāṃ vā rāgaṃphalamunmīlayituṃ yogyo nānyasantāne saṃskāraścāyaṃ dānādikarmajanitaścittasantāna iti  svabhāvahetureva samudāya sādhyāpekṣayā  saṃskāramātrānubandhinī hi tatsantāne phaladānayogyatā anyasantānesarvathā tadayogyatā ceti nimittāntarānapekṣaṇāt  ekaikasādhyatve tu prathame svabhāvahetu  dvitīye tu viruddhavyāptopalabdhi svādhārādanyasantāne phaladānaviruddhena svādhāra yattaktaṃ ra  nakārastyaktaḥ ra   samīkṣitā ra  vadantaḥ ra  śvānyaja ra rāgaphalayituṃ ra  pekṣāyā a  vetirakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥtatra yadi saṃskārepi satisantāna eva phaladānena vyāptasya saṃskāratvasyopalabdheḥ tatra santāne phaladānayogyatā nimittāntaramapekṣeta prayatnena saṃskāraghaṭanamanarthakaṃsyāt  anyasantānepi phaladānasāmarthya ca dvitīyaprayatnavaiyarthyam  na caikāmalakyāṃ kṣīrāvaseke sarvāmalakī madhuraphalā  tasmātsvasantāna eva phaladānena vyāptiḥsaṃskārasyeti nānekāntaḥ saṃskāraśca karmakṛto viśeṣaścetasa ityāgamasiddhamabhyupagamyaivacodyavat samādhānamapīti nāsiddhiḥ  sapakṣe bhāvānna virodho vyāptyasiddhervā  athavāyo yaḥ santānaḥ sa svādhikaraṇa eva saṃskāre phaladānayogyo yathā karpāsasantānaḥsantānaścāyaṃ cittasantāna iti pūrvavat esmṛtyādiphalāpekṣayāpyayameva nyāya  yadi santānadvāreṇeyaṃ vyavasthā tadātato guruṇānubhūtādau śiṣyasyavidyāyonisaṃbandhaprasiddhepi santāne prasaṃgaḥ smṛtyādiḥ syāt evaṃ pituranubhavādau putrasya bhavet  netādṛśaḥ santānotra vivakṣitaḥupādānopādeyabhūtahetuphalaparamparārūpaḥ  kiṃ punarupādānopādeyalakṣaṇam  ekādhāratāniyamosati vicārakāraṇe vicārepi tadyogyatāniyamaḥ  vicitrā hi kāryakāraṇaparamparopapāditā pūrvam tatraivalakṣaṇā paramparā santāna ucyata ityapi sūcitameva  na caivaṃ guruśiṣyacetasoḥ pitāputramanasorvā astīti nātiprasaṅgadoṣo nyāyasantānopādānavyavasthayorvānyonyāśrayadoṣaḥ bhūṣaṇīyaḥ stadanāśrayatvapratipādanāt upādānavyavasthāyāathavā abhrānta a saṃmataikāvasāya prakṛtivikriye ubhī hetuphalasyopādānopādeyalakṣaṇam  hetuphalasantatau idamupādānamidamupādeyamiti pratyabhijñāpratyayenalakṣitaṃ veditavyam  visabhāgotpattau tu prakṛtirupādānasya vikṛtirupādeyasya lakṣaṇaṃsvabhāva eva  prakṛtivikṛtitvaṃ vā lakṣaṇamiti bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ kāṣṭhayūpavatkāṣṭhāṅa gāravañca  anekotpattāvapi bhinnā eva bhāgā upādānam  yathā badhūma uṣmādīnāmaṅa gārāṇām buddhāvapyeka puruṣaprajñaptirekāvasāya  asti ca viṣayoparāgaṃ vivecyacaitanyamātramāmṛśata ekapuruṣābhimatāyāṃ santatau saiveyaṃ buddhirityavasāya   te punaratrāśeṣasvarūpānanukārāt anukārasaṃbhavepi stambhāntaravadekāvasāyo bhrānta iti na meva sa a  sambaddha a tat ra  mapekṣate ra  api ra  na tvekā ra vicāla  a  vicārepi a vicānepi ra   nyo svāśraya ra  tato ra  ta viditavya va  lakṣaṇasvabhāva ra  dhūmabhasmādi ra  rāgaṃ saṃvivecya a  netaratra rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaupitāputrādāvupādānādivyavasthā  tadevamupādānādilakṣaṇamanapekṣya tādūvasantatīupādānādivyavasthāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ kīdṛśe santāne āhitā karmavāsaneti jijñāsāyāṃyatropādānādivyavastheti bhaṇitau na doṣaḥ yat punarayamevāhana sambandhaviśeṣābhāve kāraṇamātra viśeṣādupādānetaravibhāgānupapatteḥ yathāsmākaṃ janakatvāviśeṣepi samavāyyasamavāyinimittakāraṇavibhāga saṃbandhaviśeṣāt na tathā tava kāraṇānāmupādānetaravibhāgaṃ paśyāma iti etadapi dūṣitameva kāraṇatvasāmānyepi kāryāpekṣayā vibhāgasya darśitatvāt  kāryakāraṇayoranyonyaviśeṣānapekṣaṇe hi saṃbandhadvāreṇāpi vyavasthādausthyamāpāditam na ca samavāyaḥ kṣama ityapi leśena sūcitameva  tasmānna saṃskārasantānayordūṣaṇaṃkiñcit yadyapi cātra iloke karmavāsanāśabdaḥ prayukto na cāsyārtha karpāsamanveti tathāpi vāsanārthobhisaṃskārastāvadanvetīti sa eva hetuḥ sūcito grāhyaḥ  athavākarmaśabdenāpi kriyā  yatra santāne yayā kayācit kriyayā kṛtobhisaṃskāra ityarthaḥ etena vyāptipradarśanam pakṣadharmastu prastāvāda boddhavyaḥ  tataḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvaṃ sākṣātsmṛtau pratipādakamādāya yaduktaṃ tatsarvaṃ viplutam kāryakāraṇabhāvāśraya viśeṣānvayinītu smṛtirityanavadyam yatpunarasya sādhanaṃ na pūrvabuddhayānubhūterthe uttarabuddhīnāṃ smṛtirbhavatyanyatvātsantānāntarabuddhivaditi tatrotrarabuddhīnāṃ dharmiṇīnāṃ bhinna smṛtirūpabuddhisambandhoniṣidhyata uta smṛtirūpatvameva tāsāṃ vāryate atha smṛtyā phalavatyastā na bhavantītipratipādyate  prathamapakṣastāvadayukta    na hyanyā smṛtiranyā ca smṛtimatī matiriṣyateasmābhiryanniṣedha syāt api tu smṛtirūpaiva sā matiriti  athāśvasya smaratogavekṣaṇakāle tadarśanaṃ cānekagrahaṇābhāvopi sakṛt kathamabhimataḥ  ki sakṛdanekasaṃbhavābhāvāt grahaṇaprakārāsaṃbhavād vā prathamakalpe tāvat kathaṃ pradīpasya vartivikārāndhakārakṣayādaya tadā kriyantesvayamapi  asmākaṃ ākāśakāladigātmamanasāṃ paramāṇūnāṃca rūpāsiddhī hetorāśrayāsiddha rasiddhatvāt  sopi vyāpakānupalambho na trayīṃdoṣajātimatipatati  tatra kramayogapadyarahitatvamabhāvadharmo na sidhyatyāśrayāsiddharityuktam  na hi kramayogapadyarahitatvasya śaśaviṣāṇadharmatvaṃ prekṣāvantaḥ pratipadyante kiṃ ca yāvatteṣāmasattvaṃ pramāṇāntarānnāvagamyate tāvadabhāvadharmatvaṃ na sidhyati anyathāpakṣadharmatvasiddhī teṣāmasattvasiddhiḥ asatvasiddhau ca satyāmabhāvadharmatva siddhiritiitaretarāśrayatvaṃ dunivāram  bhāvadharmaṃtve cāsya viruddhatvaṃ syāt ubhayadharmatve cānaikāntikatvam sattāyāmiva soyamasattāyāmapi tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ nāpi dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ tatrāpi hi vyāpakanivṛttisahitā vyāpyanivṛttiḥ vyatirekaśabdasyārthaḥ  sā ca nivṛttirgamakāṅgatvādavaśyaṃ pratipattavyā bhavatīti yadyanubhavādgamyate tasya hetuḥ syādahetoragrāhyatvāditi heturanaikāntika syāt vyatirekasyānubhavakāritayā bhāvarūpatve sādhyakoṭinikṣiptatvāt  anvayavyatirekyorabhāvādasādhāraṇo heturagamakaḥ  tasmād vyatirekovaśyāṅgīkartavyovaśyajñātavyaśva jñātavyatvetajjñānaprasaṅgo darśitaḥ syādetat  vyatireko na sākṣātkārivijñānagrāhya iṣṭo yataḥ sākṣātkāriṇovijñānasya janaka syādapi tu vikalpayitavyaḥ na ca vikalpyamānorthaḥ svakīyasamanantarapratyayādhīnotpādasya a   vikalpasya heturupapadyate tat kimucyateheturanaikāntika iti  soyaṃ ra  mapatati  tat ra sanivṛ bhavantī yadya ra  bhavājnāsti ra  jñātavye ra   samantara a  nnānu ra   nivṛtti vyāpyeti nāsti rajanyate a  rekosyāṅgī ra  jñātavyaścetiatra patrakrarmo bhraṣṭaḥ akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥyatotadapyasaṅgatam yataḥ sarva eva vikalpo na catuṣṭayoṃ gatimatikrāmati  tathā hikaścidanubhavapṛṣṭhabhāvī nīlādivikalpaḥ aparaḥ sandigdhaviṣayaḥ piśācādivikalpaḥanya punarasadarthaḥ śaśaviṣāṇādivikalpaḥ vikalpaḥ punariha kaścilliṅgajaḥ  tatraliṅgajādārabhya sarvo vikalpaḥ avastunirbhāsād iti bruvatā pratyakṣābha uktaḥvastupratibhāsaṃ pratyakṣaṃ svalakṣaṇābhāve tatpratibhāsapracyuteḥ  na caivaṃ vikalpaḥ tatpratibhāsasya vastunyananurodhāt   tasmāt pratyakṣābho vikalpaḥ  liṅgajastu yathādhyavaseyamarthaṃprāpayatīti pramāṇam  na ca vyatireko vikalpyamāno liṅgābhāvālliṅgajena vikalpenavikalpyate anubhavapūrvakasya ca vikalpasya pāramparyeṇa vastujanmanopi na vastuniprāmāṇyam anubhavasyaiva pramāṇatvāt  anubhavaśva vyatirekāśrayaḥ saṃpratyeva nirasta itipāriśeṣyādasadarthaḥ sandigdhavastuko vā vikalpo niścāyayatīti sattvamavidyamānavyatirekaṃ sandigdhavyatirekaṃ vā na kṣaṇikatvasādhanāya paryāptam nāpi tṛtīyo vikalpaḥ  yataḥ kramayogapadyamakṣaṇikāt sattvamupādāya vyāvarta mānaṃ svena vyāpyena saha kṣaṇikatve vyavatiṣṭhata iti pratibandhasiddhitirekasiddhipūrvikāgamyate vyatirekaśca pūrvoktena krameṇa nirākṛta iti tadevamnityaṃ nāsti na vā pratītiviṣayaṃ tenāśrayāsiddhatāhetoḥ svānubhavasya cākṣatirataḥ kṣiptaḥ svapakṣopi ca śūnyaṃ ca dvitayena sidhyati na vā sattāpi sattā yathāno nityena virodhasiddhirasatā śakyā kramāderapi iti dūṣaṇasaṃgrahaḥ tatrāmī evaṃ paryanuyujyantedharmasya kasyacidavastuni mānasiddhābādhāvidhivyavahṛtiḥ kimihāsti no vā kvāpyasti cet kathamiyanti nadūṣaṇānināstyeva cet svavacanapratirodhasiddhiḥ  vastuṣvana a  vā ra  nakāro nāsti ra  ratna niba    tula ā tavi  ratnaniba   pariśuddhi jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalona hi kasyacid dharmasya vidhiniṣedhavyavahāro nāma saṃvādavān vastvekaniyataḥkiṃ tvavastunyapi  athāvastuni nāstyeveti bhaktiḥ tatra kathametaditi paryanuyukto narājaśāsanamāśrityaiva stheyamiti yadi kiñciddhemupādīta kathamāśrayāsiddhiparihāra mūkībhūyāvasthānaṃ sati vacanasāmarthya nocita iti yat kiñcilapato na pratimallaḥ nāpi pararatena pratipādito bhavati ki cāvastuni nāstyeva vidhipratiṣedhavyavahāra ityevaṃ vadataiva avastuni niṣedhavyavahāraḥ svīkṛtaḥ hetau paraṃ paro vañcitaḥ na hi niṣedhamavadhūya nañonyadarthasaṃbhāvanāsaca niṣedho yadi na pramāṇasiddhaḥ kathamādriyate  kiṃ vāsya vacanena  pramāṇasaddhisvīkāre ca na tāvadadhyakṣa mevā vastuniṣedhayoḥ sādhanam adhyakṣasya tadviṣayavirodhādarthaṃ sāmarthyāpekṣaṇāt  anumānāśraye tu b āśrayāsiddhiraśakyaparihāreti atovastuprastāve mūkataiva prāptā  na ca pratijñāmātrasyāpyavakāśaḥ  na caivaṃ śakyaṃyāvanna rājadaṇḍenāvastuprastāvavāraṇam  prastāve tvavaśyaṃ satā saṃbhavino vacanamanuṣaṅgiparyanuyogasaṃbhavāt    vacanasya ca vidhiniṣedhābhyāṃ nāparo vyāpāraḥ  tato navacanaṃ nāvacanamiti mahati kaṣṭasaṅkaṭe praveśaḥ tathā ca saṃpratyeva nityentarālakamalavat kramākramābhāvāt nārthasāmarthyamitiprastāvenāvastuni kasyaciddhamaṃsya vidhiniṣedhāviti viduṣāpi bhavatā na mūkībhūyasthātuṃ śakyam kiṃ tu kṛta eva niṣedho bauddhābhimatāyā asati kramākramābhāvenasāmarthyanivṛtteḥ nivṛttyabhāvastu vidhirvastubhāvosatopi san tadabhāvastu  nāstīti paśya dhāṣṭaryavijṛmbhitam pra vā  ityanta raślokaḥ atha nityasya koṣṭhaśuddhayā vastutvānna pramāṇānniṣedhavirodhaḥ kasyaciddharmasyatat kimidānīṃ gagananalinasyāpi koṣṭhaśuddhayā vastutvameva  vastutve vā nāvastuko kintvavastvanvayi a  tula ā ta vi pṛ   kiñca vastuni ra  vā a ra patrakrame vyatikrama a  sambhavācca a  cakāro nāsti ra  nāparī vacanavyāpāra ra kramabhāvā ā  prastāvena  vastuni ra  vidhi iti nāsti a  samarthānivṛ ra vastvabhāvastu pra vā  bāndhya pra vā bālya ra  kauṣṭha rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāravikalpaḥ saṃṅkalpayituṃ śakyaḥ  tadavastuni nabhastāmarase kramādivirahādarthakriyā sāmarthya virahostu na vā  ubhayathāpi nāvastuni vidhi pratiṣedho vetyasyāḥ pratijñāyānirvāhaḥ  kathametaditi pramāṇagaveṣaṇe ca pratyakṣābhāvenumānamāśrīyamāṇamāśrayāsiddhigrastaṃ samastam apramāṇavacanamātrasya cānapekṣitatvāt praśnakṛtā prekṣeṇa  na cobhayābhāvobhidhātuṃvidhiniṣedhayorbhāvābhāvasvabhāvā dekaniṣedhenāparavidhānāt vidhiniṣedho hi niṣedhaḥ pratiṣedhaśca vidhistat kīdṛśoparaḥ  astu cobhayaniṣedhapratijñāhetorupādīyamānasya nāśrayāsiddhiparihāraḥ śakyaḥyaccedamuktam koṣṭhaśuddhayā vastveva nityamiti tataḥ kim  na hi tadvastutvenaiva dharma āśrayāsiddhidūṣaṇasyānavakāśaprasaṅgāt  paropagamāpekṣayedamucyata iticet  prasaṅgahetustarhi avastutvānnityāśrayāsiddha  kramādiviraho na heturityarthaḥ evaṃ ca satyavastuni heturāśrayāsiddhatvena vyāpto vaktavyaḥ na hi pratibandhamantareṇakavituḥ  pakṣadhamaṃtāmātre paropagamāpekṣayā tu prasaṅga ucyate na tu vyāptāvapi tadupagama eva  kadācidevamapi syāditi cet  tathāpi na pareṇāvastuni heturāśrayāsiddhatvenavyāptobhyupagataḥ nitya evāvastuni hetupraṇayanāt  tataśca yatrevāvastuni vastutvāthetorāśrayāsiddhirupanīyate tatreva pratijñāyāḥ paribhavo nāvastuni vidhiniṣedhāvityasyāḥ yadi ca paropagamādeva vyāptirapi vivakṣitā avastunyavastutvānapakṣadharmaṃtāprayukto aheturiti tarhi tava nedamanumatamiti tathāpi nāvastuni vidhipratiṣedhāviti vyāhatampratiṣedhasya svayaṃ svīkriyamāṇatvāt nañonyārthābhāvāt ki ca sarvaḥ prasaṅgo viparyayaparyavasitavyāpāra iti nyāyāt yadyavastu nityaṃtadāśrayāsiddhiḥ na cāśrayāsiddhiḥ tannāvastu nityamiti ki vivakṣitam  tadāpiyathāśrayāsiddhirdoṣa  prastuto nāsti siddhamavastutvaṃ nityasya dharmiṇa iti nāvastunityamiti kathaṃ na viplavate  tasmāt svatantra evāyamavastutvādāśrayāsiddhiravastunihetoriti hetudūṣaṇapravṛttasya prakṛtaḥ  tathā ca nāvastuni vidhiniṣedhāviti dūrīkṛtametat vyāpakānupalambhaścāyaṃ svabhāṣayā prayujyate āśrayatvasya vastutvena vyāptyabhimānāt sa cābhimānaḥ svavacanavirodhānava bodhāt  na hi nāvastuni vidhiniṣedhādhāratvamitisvavacanavirodhaṃ manyamānasya vastutvena dhamitvasya vyāptyabhimāno mānasaṃ spṛśati virahārtha ra  vidhe ra  pratijñāyā iti nāsti ra  prakṣepaṇa a  pratiṣedhaśca vi ra avastuko ra  tadvastunaiva ra   siddhiḥ ra  praṇayaṇāt a praṇayanati ra  deva ca ra āśrayasi ra   siddhidoṣa ra  viplaveti a  virodhāt rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauki svaparibhāvakatayeti sāmānyanyāyaḥ  ki cāmī svayamavastuni vidhiniṣedhavyavahāramātanvanto vyāpakānupalambhaṃ cāpramāṇayantaḥ paraṃ pratikṣipantīti ka eṣa krama nyāyabhūṣaṇakāro hi na hyasati dharmiṇi hetoḥ pakṣadharmatvamiti bruvāṇovastunihetoḥ pakṣadharmatāniṣedhaṃ vyaktamā  kathametaditi yuktigaveṣaṇe ca dharmiṇosattvāditihetumabhipreti  anyathā ca vacanamātre ka ādara  athākṣaṇikaṃ naiva pratīyate kathaṃ tasyakramākramābhyāṃ virodhovagamyata iti bruvāṇaśca vyaktaṃ pratītyaviṣayatvena virodhāvagamābhāvamāha  sa cāvastvantarasādhāraṇo dharmo nityevyavastusaṃmate āsajyate anyatrāvastuni yadyayaṃ na  nyāyo nityepi kathamabhidhātuṃ śakyaḥ anyathāśaṅkaropyetadeva sphuṭayati avastuni pratītyaviṣayatvena na virodhāsiddhiriti anyathā prabandhavaiyarthyāt nanvasya ṣaṣṭhīsaptamīnirdeśābhāvādasatā saha sato na virodha ityabhiprāyāt na doṣaiti cet  adyāpyasatopratīyamānatvāditi svayamabhivyakto heturapekṣaṇīya evetikathamasato dharmabhāvavyāpakānupalambhayo  paribhavaḥ  tena saha virodhāsiddhī hitasya pratītiviṣayatvābhāvo hetuḥ  yadi ca tṛtīyānirdeśenāśrayāsiddhiparihāra manumanyatebhavān kramākramayorapi nityena saha yogābhāvādarthakriyāśakterapi nityena saha yogābhāvaiti na kṣatiḥ  evaṃ pakṣeṇa yoga eva sapakṣeṇaiva yogo vipakṣeṇāyoga eveti hetostrairūpyaṃvakṣyāmaḥ  śāntirastvāśrayāsiddhiprahārasya  tasmāt vivakṣāmātrabheda eva na vastubhedaiti kimanena kāyavratena kiṃ ca b asatā saha tāvad virodhabādhanamevamastu yadā punaḥ sata evasatā saha virodhaḥ kimastu na veti praśnestvitisvīkāraḥ sthitaṃ bauddhasiddhānteneti viphalaupanyāsaḥ  atha neti svīkāraḥ tadā sa evāpratīyamānatvāditi heturapekṣitavyaityavastuni niṣedhanaṃ virodhasya vyāpakānupalambheneti punarboddhasiddhāntasiddhiḥ  tathānāsiddhe bhāvadharmostipra vā  ityatrāpi eṣa evaṃ nyāya śaraṇam  vaktumāha ra  dhavacā  ca  sābhā ra  nityaṇya ra  āsajyete a  nakārastyaktaḥ ra anyāpya ra  dharmabhāva ra  lambho ra  hīti nāsti ra  nirdenā a  sahapakṣe ra  eṣa ra  patrakena ra  kiṃ ca satā ra  sādhanamastu ra  punarasata eva rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥtathā ca trilocana svākṣareṇa sphuṭayati kramayaugapadyarahitatvamabhāvadharmo nasidhyati āśrayānupalabdheriti  atra hi vyaktamabhāvo dharmī kramādirahitatvamasya dharmoniṣidhyate āśrayānupalabveriti hetoriti  evamasato dharmitvaṃ pratijānāna evānantaraṃna hi kramayogapadyarahitaśaśa viṣāṇadharmatvaṃ prekṣāvantaḥ pratipadyanta iti evaṃ bruvan mahānsāhasiko yadayamātmānamātmanaiva nopahasati  abhāvādeva hi śaśaviṣāṇasya dharmitvaṃniṣeddhavyam svīkṛtaṃ cābhāvasyāpi dharmitvamiti kaḥ pratirodhasturaṅgaśṛṅgādeḥ athābhāvasya dharmitā kramādirahitatvaniṣedhena svīkṛtā kathaṃ kramādirahitatvenaivāstu aho buddhivaibhavam  abhāvasya śaśaviṣāṇasya kramādirahitatvaniṣedhena dharmitvaṃ manyatena kramādirahitatvena  ubhayathāpyavastuni vidhiniṣedhavyavahārasvīkārād dunivārasaugatakṛtānta iti varaṃ kramādirahitvenaiva dharmitvamubhayatrāstu kimuttarāpathaṃ praviśyatāvataiva mūlyena turagatyāgino gardabhakrayaṇavṛttānta āśriyate athavātisūkṣmā buddhiḥ sthavīyāṃsamasamañjasaviśeṣamiyantaṃ na paśyatīti kimatrakriyatām  tathāpyakṣiṇo nimīlya cintaya tāvat ki śaśaviṣāṇaṃ kramādiyogibhavati na vā  yadi bhavatīti bhaṇasi kimatra vaktavyamasmābhiḥ  sabhyādayaḥ pramāṇam atha neti pakṣaḥ tadā kramādirahitaṃ tattatkathaṃ kramādirahitatvaniṣedhena dharmīkaroṣi ubhayathā ca hetuṃ paryaṃnuyujyāvaśyamavastutvāditi vakṣyāmītya vistareṇa evaṃ bandhyāsuto vaktā na vetyevaṃvidhepi prastāve niṣedhamapratijñāya na sthātuṃśakyamacetanatvādavastutvādityādisādhanamanupanyasya vā na kaścidevamāśate  yadīdṛśamuttarayitavyamiti cet  kutaḥ  tadavastu tāyā prasiddhatvāditi cet  punastadevāyātambandhāsutasya dharmiṇo vakṛtvenāśaṅkanoyatāniṣedhaḥ suprasiddhāvastutvāditi heturiti  naca suprasiddhatvepi sarvathā śaṅkāvirahaḥ  niḥsīmo hi mohamahimā  dṛṣṭo hi śāstrakārāṇāmapi a kramādirahitatvaniṣedhaḥ śaśaviṣāṇe ityevaṃprakāro bhramaḥ  tatoyathā śabde cākṣuṣatvādanityatvaṃ saṃbhāvayannasiddhatvena niṣidhyate tathehāpi sthātāṃ śaṅkāniṣedhau na virodhaḥ  tasmād vastunīvāvastunyapi kasyaciddharmasya vidhiniṣedhavyavahārodurvāraḥ āhatya vipratipannānāmapi śāstrakārāṇāṃ niṣedhavākyenaiva svīkārāt  pratijānana eva ra vakṣyasītya ra  ahṛtya ra  rahitasya a   syevaradṛṣṭehaṃ ra  vāraṇāmapi a kramavirahitatvanitya tve na ra kramaḥ a   bādhastunya rajñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalītatredānīmavastuṣu bandhyāsutaparyanteṣu kathaṃ dharmatvam  pratītyabhāve kathaṃ vyavahāraḥ  pratītijanakatve kathaṃ na vastutvam  na ca vacanamātrapramāṇamupādeyamiti yaḥ kaściddheturupādīyate sa sarvaḥ kathaṃ nāśrayāsiddhaḥ  tadetadāyātamyaścobhayoḥ samo doṣa ityādi yadi ca niścitāvastubhāveṣvapi naite doṣāḥ tat kiṃ sādhanātprāgasandigdhasattākenitye bhaviṣyati  kaḥ punaratra paramārtha   na hyavastuni kasyaciddharmasya vidhiniṣedhavyavahāraḥ śakyaparihāraḥ prāmāṇikasya  na caite doṣāḥ sānuṣaṅgiṇa iti ceducyatena tāvadavastuno dharmitvābhāvaḥ  yatraiva hi idameva miti parāmarśaḥ tadevedamityanenākāreṇa dharmi evamiti dharmaviśeṣayogaḥ  yathā ghaṭo nīla evaṃ bandhyāsuto na vaktetighaṭasya nīlatvamiva bandhyāsutasya vaktṛtvaṃ dharmaḥ pratīyata iti na dharmitvābhāvobhāve kevalaṃ kaściddharmo vastuniyato nīlatvādiḥ kaścida vastuniyataḥ sarvopākhyāvirahādiḥ kaścidubhayasādhāraṇonupalambhamātram  tatra vastudharmaṇāvastudhamitvaniṣedha itiyuktam  na tu dharmaṃmātrāṇām svavacanavirodhasya bādhakatvāt  pratītyabhāvena vyavahāraityapyayuktam  na punarubhayorekaprakāraiva pratītiraṅgaṃ vyavahārasya  vastuno hi svasāmarthyabhāvinī pratītiḥ vikalpaścādhyakṣa liṅgābhyāṃ pāramparya kārya  avastunastusandigdhavastubhāvasya vā vikalpamātram  sāmarthyābhāve hi tayorabhāve vikalpamātramapiyadi na tatpratītiravasthāpyate sarvathāvyavahārya eva syāt  iṣṭaśca vyavahāraḥ ato vikalpanamātraṃ tatra pratotiḥ tadupasthāpitameva ca tayoḥ svarūpaṃ nānyat  yathā vastunaḥpratyakṣānumānopanītameva svarūpam evamavastunaḥ sandigdhavastubhāvasya vā vikalpopasthāpitaevātmā nānya iti  nātaḥ samayādaṅgamākarṣantaḥ santā bhavitumarhanti yattuhetutvameva yuktijñāḥgrāhyatāṃ viduḥpra vā   yadi viniści ra  prāk sandi ra  sattāko a  bhaviṣyanti ra  nānuṣaṅgiṇa a tadevamityākā ra  bhāvo ra   viraha ra  mānaṃ ra    dharmeṇa svavacana itipatitam ra  tyapi a   pratipattiraṅga ra  lpaśca kāryaḥ iti patitam ra  tatra ra tato ra  nānyataḥ rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraityuktam tanmānasapratyakṣa prastāve grāhakād bhinnameva grāhyamapekṣya eva nyāya iti sthitametat na hi svasaṃvedanepyeṣatathā ca nyāyabhūṣaṇa evāha na hi tvayārthāntaramajanakaṃ pratītiviṣayatveneṣṭamiti  na cāvastvarthāntaram  artha eva hyanyamarthamapekṣyārthāntaramucyate nanatvavastu  b tadbhāvaniṣedhamātraṃ tat  tasmādarthāntaratvābhāvānna svajanyajñānāpekṣānarthasya  tato vikalpamātramatra śaraṇam  tadākārollikhitaścāsya svabhāvo nāparaityapyavaśyaṃ svīkartavyam  anyathā śaśaviṣāṇādiśabdānāmanuccāraṇameva prasajyeteti kathaṃ vyavahāraḥ  tathā hi kharaśṛṅgādiśabdena śabditamartha manudyāvaśyaṃ kiñcidvidheyam yathā na kramādirahitatvaṃ śaśaviṣāṇadharmastatsahitaṃ vā yathā vā nāsatākasyacidvirodhabodhaḥ nāvastudharmīti vā  tatra śaśaviṣāṇāsa davastuśabderyadinābhimatorthaḥ pratyāyyate abhimatādanya evārtho dhvanijanitavikalpasya tadā vidhīyamāna kramākramaniṣedhādi kasya pratīyatām  tatpratītyabhāve ca śabdoccāraṇamanarthaṃkamāyātam  asti ca kūrmaromādiśabdavyavahāraḥ tasmāt sa eva tasyārthaḥarthasyāpi sa eva niścayaḥ  dṛṣṭepi vikalpa eva niścayaḥ  evaṃ tarhi vikalpa evāstusarvatrāśrayaṇīyaḥ kiṃ darśanena  naivaṃ darśananirākṛte vikalpacetasyākāramātrasphuraṇādvastutvasādhanātha bādhanārthaṃ vā pramāṇāntarāpekṣaṇam  darśanena tu viṣayī kṛte vastuniyāvati rūpe vikalpaḥ tāvati sa eva niścayaḥ asati sādṛśyād vipralambhe  tasmātavastunyapi vikalpamātraṃ śaraṇam avastuni tu tadeva śaraṇam  tadākārabāhyādhyavasānamevahi pramāṇāntarasāpekṣaṃ tatra prārthyate  tacca vikalpenaiva siddham  pramāṇavṛttau tu na pramāṇāntarāpekṣā  tatastena vikalpena yat svarūpamullikhitaṃ tatparāmarśena yathā kramākramarahitatvaniṣedhādikamupasthāpayanti santastadarhatayā tathā tadrūpapratyanīkākāreṇa sahavirodhavyavasthāyāṃ kīdṛśo doṣa  yathā vā bandhyāsutasya saundaryādiniṣedhonurūpaḥtathā ca vastutāvirodhasya ko virodhaḥ yadi cānubhavābhāvādvirodhapratirodhonubhavābhāvādeva saundaryaniṣedhopi mābhūtu tato vidheyasya kasyaciddharmasyābhāvebhāvābhidhāyināmanuccāraṇa prasaṅgastadavasthaḥ na ca tacchakyamityapi niveditam  vasthāntaraṃ ra  tadabhāvaniṣedhanaṃ tu ra  mātraṃ śaraṇaṃ a  ityasya svī ra  raṇaṃprasajyate iti ra  bodha iti nāsti ra  pratyāyya te tadeti patitam ra  kamāyātam tasmātsa iti patitam ra  cetasi sādhanārthamiti patitam ra  yathā ra  saundaryaniṣedhora cakāro nāsti rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalobādhaneatha bandhyāsutādīnāṃ vikalpanīyād rūpād rūpāntaravirahāt tanmātrasya cavikalpena viṣayīkaraṇe tadanurūpavyavahārasya na kṣatiḥ  evaṃ sati virodhavyavahārasyāpitadanurūpasya kā kṣatiḥ  yathā ca vastutayā bandhyāsutasya virodhaḥ evaṃ nityasyāpi yo dharmaḥpratyanīka upapādayituṃ śakyastena kathaṃ na virodha  tat kathamanubhavābhāvamātraṃ virodha sādhanamanabhidhīyamānaṃ sādhu syāt  yadi tu vikalpopi tadviṣayo nasyāt tatpratyanīkākāraparāmarśo vā na syāt a  sahānavasthānābhidhāno vāvirodha sādhayitumiṣṭo bhavet bhaved virodhasiddhiḥ  ekasya hi bhavatonyabhāve abhāvāt sahānavasthānavyavasthā  bhāvaśca pratyakṣagocara iti kathamekasyānyavastutve ghaṭeta parasparaparihāra sthitilakṣaṇatvaṃ tu pratyanīkākāraparāmarśamātrasādhyam vikalpamātreṇaviṣayīkaraṇepi sannidhīyamānavyavasthānimittaṃ nāvaśyaṃ vastvanurodhi kathamanyathā bhāvābhāvayoreva virodhaḥ parasparaparihāralakṣaṇa  tatra ca virodhe pradhānamudāharaṇaṃ tāveva abhāvasya  vastutvasvīkārepi na bhāvasya bhāvobhāvābhidhāne vastuni nāpyabhāvasyabhāvobhāva iti nābhāvavastu paramparāmupagantuṃ śakyamiti svapracyutimātramavastuvyavahartavyai kasvabhāva miṣyamāṇaṃ kathaṃ tadvirodhi vyavasthāpyatām  virodhāvyavasthāne ca tatrasvātmā ca svapracyutiśca tyekameva vastu svātmanaivāsti ca nāsti ceti syāt na caivaṃniyamenetyayameva virodhārtha  kṣaṇikākṣaṇikavad vā  yathā hyekasya nākṣaṇikaṃtathā nānyasya kṣaṇikamiti  tasmād vastvavastunorna parasparaparihāralakṣaṇavirodhabādhetisthitam nanvevaṃ virodhasyāpāramārthikatve taddvāreṇa kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiraṇyavāstavī svātna hyapāramārthikādhāra pāramārthiko bhavitumarhati virodha  yadāha śaṅkaraḥ evaṃ tarhivirodhakalpanayā bādhakamapi kalpitavirodhatvānna vāstavavyatirekasādhanamityavāstavavyatirekatvāt sattāyāḥ tadāyattaṃ kṣaṇikatvamapyavāstavameveti nyāyabhūṣaṇopi tadevamupaskurvannāha saṃvṛtisiddhenākṣaṇikena virodhāsiddhiriticet  saṃvṛtisiddhamapi vāstavaṃ kālpanikaṃ vā syāt  yadi vāstavam tataḥ kathaṃ tasyāsattvam  kathaṃ śvārthakriyāvirodha  arthakriyāṃ kurvaddhi vāstavamucyate  atha tataḥ ra  bodhane a  sādhanamabhi a  tvavikalpā ra  atra patravinyāsavyatikramaḥ śodhitaḥ a   syāvastutve ra  sthiralakṣaṇa a  mātraṃ sādhyam ra  manyabhāvā a  cakāro nāsti ra  bhāvena  abhāvena  abhāvasya ra   sthāpyatā ra  yathāpyekasya a  virodhāviti ra  tasya sattvaṃ ra  cārtha rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥkālpanikam tadvirodhaḥ kiṃ vāstavaḥ kālpaniko vā  na tāvad vāstavaḥ kalpitavirodhivirodhatvād bandhyāputravirodhavat  atha virodhopi kālpanika eva na tarhi paramārthaṃ tokṣaṇikasyārthaṃkriyāyāṃ kramākramābhyāṃ virodha ityatokṣaṇikāt sattvasya vyatirekasiddhirapyapāramārthikītyavāstavavyatirekatvāt sattāyāḥ tadāyattaṃ kṣaṇikatvamapyavāstavameveti abaddhapralapitametat  na hi virodho nāma vastvantaraṃ kiñcidubhayakoṭidattapādaṃsambandhābhidhāna miṣyatesmābhiḥ upapadyate vā yenaikasaṃbandhino vastutvābhāveapāramārthikaḥ syāt  yathā tviṣyate tathā pāramārthika eva  viruddhābhimatayoranyonyasvarūpaparihāramātraṃ virodhārtha  tacca bhāvabhāvayo b pāramārthikameva  na hibhāvobhāvarūpamāviśati nāpyabhāvo bhāvarūpamiti yoyamanayorasaṅkaraniyamaḥ sa evavirodha  sa ca niyamaḥ svātmānaṃ virodhamapi pāramārthika pade niveśayati  evaṃ na nityaṃkramayaugapadyarūpamāviśati nāpi kramayogapadyaṃ nityarūpamāviśatīti yoyaṃ niyamaḥ saeva virodhastayoḥ  na ca kadācidanyatheti pramāṇasiddhireva pāramārthikateti kathamucyatevirodhasyāpāramārthikatayā sattvahetorvyatirekopyatāttvika iti  nityasya punarapāra mārthikatvamaṅgīkṛyaiva sarvamavasthāpitamiti na kaściddoṣaḥ  yacca kalpitavirodhivirodhasyavāstavatvaniṣedhāya kalpitavirodhivirodhatvād bandhyāsutavirodhavadityuktam tatraivaanena tapasvinā kathamāśrayāsiddhitvādidūṣaṇaṃ sthavīyopi nopalabdhamityāstāṃ tāvadasyamarmodghāṭanam etacca cintyate  kalpitavirodhivirodhatvameva vāstavatvena viruddhaṃna vā yadi tāvanna viruddhaṃ tadā kalpitāvirodhiviruddhatvamapi bhavati vāstavatvamapi syāditikathaṃ tadupanyāsastannirākaraṇekāntikaḥ syāt  nāviruddha vidheḥ kasyacit pratiṣedhasiddhiḥ atha viruddham  sa virodho vāstavovāstavo vā  tatrāvāstavo virodha paraparābhavetiprasaṅgāt asamartha iti vāstavapakṣe kalpitavirodhivirodhopi svayaṃ vāstavaiṣṭaḥ na cāsmākamiva svaviruddhaniṣedhāmidhāyīti paśya dhāṣṭaryavijṛmbhitam  yathā hinityakramayaugapadyayorvirodhaḥ kalpita virodhivirodho nityasya kalpitatvāttathā vāstavatva athavā ra  tadāyātaṃ ra  yenaikasambino ra  vastubhāve ra  atra patrakramaḥ śodhitaḥ a nānyabhāvo ra  virodhe ra  niṣedhopa ra  evantu a   virodhavirodhitva ra atha viruddhamiti nāsti ra  paraṃparā ra  ayamartha a  vāndhya rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalīkalpitavirodhe virodhayovirodha kalpitavirodhavirodho vartate kalpitasya virodhinovirodha iti kṛtvā kalpito virodhī tasyeti vā  kalpitasya hi virodhinovirodhopi kalpita eva na vāstava ityeva bhavatpauruṣeṇa sādhyamānamīkṣāmahe  tasmāttasyakalpitastha virodhasya virodhino vāstavatvena saha yo virodha sopi kalpitavirodhivirodha  siddhaḥ  tasya vāstavatve svavacanavirodha  avāstavatve dūṣaṇamuktameva api ca  virodho nāmaikatra dvayoḥ saṃvāsaniṣedhārthamarthyate  na tu dvayorvastutvasiddhirnāma virodhaphalam  yatra tu dvayostutvasiddhistatra sāmarthyādekena vastunāvastvantaratiraskārāt kacid deśe yathā sahānavasthāne yathoktaṃ prāk  prakṛtastu virodhodharmaṃyorekatra dharmaṇi sadbhāvaniṣedhaphalaḥ tatra  yathā dvāvapi dharmo santo niṣidhyete yatra nīlatvaṃ na tatrānīlatvam ato na nīlānīlamekamiti  tathā sadasattvarūpāvapi vipratiṣiddhau dharmāvakatra dharmiṇisamāropitau pratiṣiddhāveva  na hi jananyā a  tanaye bandhyātanayatvamā ropitaṃtattvatosaditi na niṣedhyam  bandhyātanaye vā vikalpaikagocare jananītanayatvamā ropitaṃna niṣedhyam  na hi jananītanayo bandhyātanayo vaikātmā tāvataiva virodhakārya paryavasanāt kimapareṇa virodhanāmnā yo vastudharmāvanapekṣya nātmalābhamāsādayati evaṃ yatra nityatvaṃ na tatra kramayogapadyavattvam yatra kramayogapadyavatvaṃ tatra na nityatvamato na nityaṃ kramayogapadyayogi paramārthataḥ  tataśva sattāyuktamapi naiva niyamena paramārthataḥ  tataḥ kṣaṇika eva viśrāmyat tadāyattasattākameva sattvamiti sattvāt  kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddheravirodhaḥ  yadi caivamapi virodhavyatirekapratisandhānena mātṛmodakakrameṇa gṛhītvāgirikuharakoṇamāviśya ghoṣayitumicchasi ced ghoṣaya  na punarasmadārabdhasiddhipratibandhe kiñcidupayujyase  tadalamabhiniveśaparavaśībhūya vāstavā evaite virodhādayaityeva sādhu  nanu nityatvaṃ kramayogapadyavatvaṃ ca viruddhau dharmo vidhūya nāparo virodhonāma kasya vāstavatvamiti cet  tadapi yatkiñcit  na hi dharmāntarasaṃbhavena virodhasyapāramārthikatvaṃ brūmaḥ  kiṃ tu yato viruddhau dharmo dharmāntarasaṃbhavepi hi yadi na viruddhau virodhi a  virodha ra  kalpitavi ra  veti nāsti ra  hīti nāsti a virodhe virodhayovirodha ra  sandhāsa na   a   ntrāśa  ra  tat a nīlatvaṃ tatrā ra  sadasattāva ra sadasantā    a  ca ra  virodha iti nāsti a pekṣānā  yatra tatra neti nāsti ra  śrāmyatu ra  sattvāditi nāsti ra   rekaa pratibandhānavāstasān  poṣaya ra  sādhananu    ra   mānaparo ra  viruddho dharmo ra na dharmāntarepi rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥna pāramārthikopi virodhaḥ  viruddhau cet  tāvataiva tāttviko virodha iti vyavahāraḥkimapareṇa dharmeṇa  yadapi bandhyāputravirodhavadityuktam tatra kimekādhāra evāyaṃvirodho dṛṣṭāntīkṛtaḥ atha dvitīyāpekṣaḥ  dvitīyopi pratiyogirūponyamātraṃ vā prathamapakṣastāvadayukta   na hi kavidharaṃ virodhaṃ pratijānīte  tato yadi bandhyāputravirodhasyābhinnadharmiṇopāramārthikatvaṃ tadobhayadharmiṇopi pāramārthikena virodhenana bhāvyamiti koyaṃ nyāyaḥ  evamanyamātreṇāpi na virodha kṛtakānityatvavat pratiyoginā tu tatrāpīṣyata eva  bandhyāputrasya hi abandhyāputratvena virodhostyeva ekātma niṣedhaścābhimata eva dharmavirodha dharmiṇoraikātmyaniṣedha iti yukta banyāputrasyābandhyāputratvena virodho dharmidharmayorvartate naiṣa doṣaḥ  dharmiṇopi dharmadvāreṇaivavyavahayante evaṃ dharmiṇorapi kadācidbhāvapradhāno vā nirdeśa iti  yaśca vaidharmyeṇadahanatuhinayorupanyāsaḥ sopyayuktaḥ parasparaparihārasya vivakṣitatvāt  yo catadviṣayatayā sāpekṣadhruvabhāvāvuktau tatrāpi sāpekṣatayā kādācitkatvamanityatvamuktam  dhruvabhāvopyavaśyambhāva iti yadi bhāvaniyamatvam tadā nityatvameva  tatonityānityayoriya virodhasthitiḥ kathamanubhavapūrvakatayopadarśayantaṃ nopahāsayati nityena kathaṃ virodhapratītirityeva hi prakṛtam  athāvaśyaṃ bhaviṣyattā dhruvabhāva bsāpi na  kasyacidanubhavaviṣaya iti nityavadeva doṣaḥ syādetat  yacca kadācidavaśyambhūtamupalabdhaṃ tadapekṣayedamucyata iti  tadapekṣayārtāha virodha eva nāsti taddhi sāpekṣaṃ ca dhruvabhūtaṃ ca  atha tadā sāpekṣatvaṃ nāstisiddhatvāt anyadā tadā sutarāṃ nāsti asiddhatvādeva  asiddhadhamaṃ evāpekṣetiasiddhasyaivacet  ananubhūte rtāha na virodhavyavastheti sa eva doṣaḥ  siddhikālāpekṣayā anubhūtenaiva virodha iti cet  siddhikālāpekṣāsvīkāre tarhivirodha eva nāstītyeva sādhuetenānubhavābhāvād virodhavyavasthābhāve sādhye vaidharmyadṛṣṭāntābhimataḥ sādhyāvyatirekī asatā virodhaprasañjane tu sādhanāvyatirekī  dhruvabhāvasya nityatārthapakṣe tu apīti nāsti ra  yuktaṃ ra  dharmiṇāpi ra  nakāro nāsti ra  ityuktaṃ ra dharmi iti nāsti ra  doṣo dharmiṇo a  vyāhiyate a vyavahriyate ra  veti nāstira  tayeti nāsti a  bubhau a   manityamuktaṃ ra  ninityayo ra  nakāronāsti a  tarhi ra  pekṣi   kṣya  te ra  vyavasthitiḥ ra  siddhakālā rajñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalausādhyakoṭinikṣepa eveti  bhedābhedādikaṃ tu bhavatu vaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ  na ca tāvatāpivastunoreva nākṣaṇiko virodha iti niyamaḥ anyathāpi samarthitatvāditi  yadapināsiddhe bhāvadharmostītipra vā vācyam tadapyāśrayāsiddhicodyasya dūrīkṛtatvānnirākṛtam  asatopi dharmitvasādhanāt avastuni vikalpasya pratītivyavasthāsiddheśca vyomādisvarūpāpratītirapiparihṛtā syādetat yadi vikalparūpāṃ pratītimāśrityāśrayāsiddhiparihāraḥ sattāsādhanepisamānam tataḥ kathamucyate nāsiddhe bhāvadharmostotyādi  kathaṃ cātmano vibhutvasādhanaṃsarvatropalabhyamānaguṇatvamāśrayāsiddhāvudāhiyata iti cet  sādhanānurodhādubhayatrāpihi bhāvadharma eva heturupātta āśaṅkitaśca  na ca bhāvadharmasthāvastu dharmī bhavitumarhati na hi dhūmaśaṃśapātvādayovastuni vasanti  tasmād yatra bhāvadharmaḥ sādhanaṃ tatraniyamena vastveva dharmī  na ca vikalpamātra viṣayasya vastutāśvāsaḥ avastunyapivikalpamātrānapāyāt  tato vastu dharmīkurvatā pratyakṣānumānarūpe ca siddhirabhidhā tavyā  tadanabhidhāne tu vikalpamātragocaritoyaṃ  sandigdhasattāko nirastasattākovā dharmīkriyamāṇaḥ kathaṃ vastutayā niścitaḥ kṛtaḥ syāt  tathā ca sati yāvān vastudharmo hetuḥ sarvosau nāśrayāsiddhimatikrāmati ekatra sandehādanyatra viparyayāt  tataḥpratyakṣānumānābhyāṃ vastuviṣayābhyāmasiddhe bhāvadharmo na heturastyāśrayāsiddhatvāditiyuktametat sattāsādhane  asattāsādhane tvavastudharmo heturavastuni vikalpamātra siddhaeva nāśrayāsiddhidoṣeṇa dūṣayituṃ śakyaḥ  na hi tasya vastvāśrayāpekṣā avastudharmādeva na ca tadādhārasya pratyakṣānumānāpekṣā avastutvādeva  bhāvadharme tu sādhanevastvevāśrayo a vastudharmatvāt  vastunaśca niścayaḥ pratyakṣānumānābhyāmevatatastayorabhāve niyamenāśrayāsiddhiriti sadasattāsādhanayoḥ kathaṃ samāno doṣa yattu trilocanena pramāṇāntaraṃ nityānāmasattāsiddhau kramādivirahasyābhāvadharmatā na sidhyatītyuktam tad bālasyāpi durabhidhānam  nityā hi dharmiṇa  asattvaṃ ki tu ra  lākṣaṇiko a  tat ra  dharmā ra  santi ra  dharmā ra  kurvatu ra kurvataiva ra  arthaṃ ra  yāvānavastu ra danyavipa ra mātrāsiddha ra  devābhāva ra  niyamo nā ra  pramāṇāntarānni ra bhyāṃ si ra   trayādi rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥsādhyam  kramādiviraho hetuḥ  asya cābhāvadharmatvaṃ nāma svasādhyāvinābhāvitvamucyate abhāvānāṃ śaśaśṛṅgādīnāṃ dharmo na bhāvānāmiti kṛtvā  tadanena vacasāyāvat pramāṇāntareṇa pakṣe sādhyaṃ na sidhyati na tāvaddhetorvyāptirityuktaṃ bhavati tacca kutra hetāvupalabdhamaneneti na vidmaḥ  yathā cānyatra sādhyanāntarīyakatā anyadāpravṛtta pramāṇāntarasiddhā dṛṣṭāntena smāritā pakṣīkṛte sādhyasiddhayarthamupayujyate nānyataḥsādhyasiddhimapekṣate tathā kramādyabhāvebhāvadharmatā vyāptisvabhāvānyadaiva kramākrameṇasiddhatvasya  vyāptigrahaṇakāle pravṛttapramāṇasiddhākāśakamaladṛṣṭāntena smāritāsādhyasiddhāvupayujyate nānyataḥ sādhyasiddhimapekṣate  anyathā sarvānumānavaiyarthyāt kramayaugapadyena hi sattvasya vyāptisiddhau sattvasya vyāpyasyābhāvena kramayogapadyasyavyāpakasya viraho vyāptaḥ sidhyatītyabhāvadharmatvaṃ kramayogapadyaviṣayaḥ vyāptirūpaṃ tathā pūrvameva niścitaṃ sadabhāvadharmatvaṃ na pakṣe pramāṇāntareṇa sādhyasiddhayāvyavasthāpyate tathā kramākramābhāvābhāvenāpi sādhyaṃ prasādhya vyavasthāpyata iti naḥpakṣaḥ pūrvameva vyavasthāpitatvāt  tat kuta itaretarāśrayatvam yathā cakiṃ caitaretarāśrayatvamapyevaṃ yujyate  kramādivirahasyābhāvadhamaṃtvasiddhauteṣāmasattvasiddhiḥ asattvasiddhau cābhāvadharmatvasiddhiriti  viṣamadṛṣṭinā punarabhāvadharmasiddherasattvāsiddhauna prayojakatvamuktaṃ kiṃtu pakṣadharmatāsiddheḥ  tat kīdṛśamitaretarāśrayatvam  naca pakṣadharmataivābhāvadharmatā sādhyāvinābhāvarūpatvādabhāvadharmatāyāḥ atha yadyabhāvadharmatvaṃ kramādyabhāvasya syāt tadā pakṣīkṛtānāmasatāṃ nityānāṃ dharmaḥsyādityabhiprāyāt pakṣadharmatāvyāpāradvāreṇa tadavyāpāro darśitaḥ tathāpi cakrakaṃvaktumucitam  tadapi prācīnacarcayā carcitameva kiṃ ca abhāvadharmatve vyāptirūpe sati pakṣadharmatvamiti nāyaṃ hetvantarasādhāraṇonyāyaḥ  na cāsyāpi hetorevam abhāvadharmatvaṃ hi vyāptirbhavatu mā vā kramādivirahastukena nityānāṃ niṣidhyate  na caitepyasattārūpeṇa dharmiṇaḥ kiṃ tu sadasatvasandehavattveneti yatkiñcidetat bhāvadharmaṃtvamub bhayadharmatvaṃ ca neṣṭamasya kramādivirahasyahetoriti na prathamavikalpe doṣaḥ  nāpi dvitīye vyatirekasyābhāvarūpatvepi siddhau teṣāmasattvamiti nāsti ra  prayojakamuktam a pekṣa ra  vyasatā a  vattveti rajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauṃpratīteḥ samarthitatvāt  na hyabhāvarūpāṇāṃ vikalpādanyā pratītirapratītirvā ubhayathāpyabhāvavyavahārahāniprasaṅgāt  tatonubhavāpekṣāvirahānna tajjananaprasaṅge doṣāvakāśaḥ anāśvāsastu śāsitumucitaḥ sopi kramayogapadyavirahulakṣaṇavyāpakānupalambhasaṃbhavālliṅgajatvena dūrīkṛtaḥ tathā hi tathaiva trairūpyapariśodhanametadārabdham siddhaṃ ca kimiti vismayate yatoliṅgābhāvādityucyate  tasmāt kramādivyāpyasattāvyatirekavikalpe kathamanāśvāsaḥ avyatirekaśaṅkā hyanāśvāsasyārthaḥ  vyāpyavyāpakabhāvaniścaye cāsthānametaditinityānniyamena vyatiricyamānaṃ sattvaṃ kṣaṇikatvena vyāptaṃ siddhamiti na doṣaḥ tṛtīyepi vikalpe vyatirekaniścayastha dṛḍhīkṛtatvāt soyaṃ vyāpakānupalambhonitye svāśraye kramādyabhāva sādhayanneva sattāyāstato niyamena vyatirekaṃ kṣaṇikatāyāṃca pratibandhamasyā sādhayatīti trayosya vyāpārā ekavyāpāra saṃgṛhītāśca  na cadoṣaleśena lipyante  tritvaṃ cārthaśakteḥ sattālakṣaṇatve hetumātratve tu vyatirekamātrasādhanamasattāsādhanārtha iti vyāpāradvaitameveti sthitam nanu vyāpakābhāvasyābhāvarūpatvena vastudharmatayā āśrayāsiddhiparihārepi sakathamabhāvaḥ kasyacit pratipattiḥ pratipattiheturvā tasyāpi vā kathaṃ pratipattiriti kiṃ nadṛśyate  talliṅgajanmā ca saṃpratyeva vyatirekavikalpo na visaṃvādaśaṅkāmaka nidhatta ityuktam  avaśyaṃ ca sādhyabuddhi sādhayatā sādhanena bhāvavyavahāraḥ svīkartavyo nānyathā taccābhāvarūpatve sarvaṃ virudhyate  vyāpakānupalabdhirityapi yadyapyanupalabdhimātraṃ sa evadoṣaḥ na cānyopalabdhirvyāpakānupalabdhirabhidhātuṃ śakyā anyasthāpi kasyacidanupalabdhiriti  tadapi yatkiñcita dharmyapalabdherevānyatrāpyanupalabdhitayā vyavasthāpanāt yathā hi neha śiśapā vṛkṣābhāvādityatra vṛkṣāpekṣayā kevalapradeśasya dharmiṇa upalabdhivṛkṣānupalabdhi śiśapāpekṣayā ca kevalapratītireva śiśapābhāvapratītiriti svabhāvahetuparyavasāyivyāpāro vyāpakānupalambhaḥ  tathā nityasya dharmiṇo vikalpabuddhauparisphurataḥ kramādyapekṣayā kevalasphuraṇameva kramādyanupalambhaḥ arthakriyāpekṣayā ca kevalapratītirevārthakriyāviyogapratītiriti viśeṣaḥ  adhyavasāyāpekṣayā ca yathā neha samanvita ra  pi vyavahāra a  hāri ra  prasaṅga ra  śamitu ra  avyatirikta  śaṅkā a  nityasyāśrayāśa ivābhāvaṃ a  vyāpāraḥ ra  samiti nāsti ra  pratipattiriti nāsti ra  sādhayat ra   tyapi anu ra   hesuravasāyi rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāraḥśiśapā vṛkṣabhāvādityabhāvasya hetupañcamyā nirdeśaḥ tathā bhāvaḥ sādhanamityapivyavahāraḥ na tvabhāvaḥ sādhanameva a kacit  sa ca vyavahāra  avasitārthāvisaṃvādānna parihartuṃ śakyaḥ  yat khalu vyāpakena virahitaṃ tadavaśyaṃ vyāpyenāpītyetāvata evārthasya saṃvādinaḥ tenāpi prakāreṇa pratipādanāt  ayaṃ ca nyāyo yathāsatye dharmiṇi saṃbhāvanayā ekajñānasaṃsargitvamubhayoranivāryam yadi na nityamanādheyātiśayatvādinā dharmāntareṇa saha pratītigocarībhavet yaugapadyāyaugapadyaṃ vāstavadharmiṇā  saha na pratītiviṣayaḥ syādapyevam  na caivam na ca niṣedhyasyasaṃbhāvanāṃ vinā kacidekajñānasaṃsargaḥ tadaiva syālabhyaḥ  tatra yathā hariṇaśirasitenaikajñānasaṃsargi śṛṅgamupalabdham harivarāṅgepi tatsaṃbhāvanayaiva tatsaṃsargānniṣidhyatetathā nīlādāvapariniṣṭhitanityānityabhāve tāvat kramākramī svadharmiṇā sārdhamekajñānasaṃsargiṇī dṛṣṭī nityepi yadi bhavato nityagrāhiṇā jñānena svadharmiṇā nityena sahaivagṛhyeyātāmiti saṃbhāvanayaikajñānasaṃsargadvāraka evaṃ pratiṣedhamāviśataḥ kathaṃ punaretannityajñāne kramāderasphuraṇamiti yāvatā kramākramakroḍīkṛtamevanityaṃ vikalpayāma iti cet  ataeva anantarbhāvācca śuddhanitya vikalpena dūrīkṛtasamāropeṇa kathamullekha kramākramasya  sarvasya ca vikalpamātragocarasya vikalpārūḍharūpāpekṣayā viruddhaniyatāniyata pañcasyā a  dāna a  yat khalvavyā kevalaṃ paramparayā pratyakṣasyāpi janmaiva sākṣāt vyavaharaṇaṃ tu vikalpādivyavadhānenaiva  anumānasya punarubhayamapi paramparayā  vyavahārāṇāmapi smṛtyabhilāṣādinā vyavadhānāt  evaṃ purāpyeṣā samagrā sthitiḥ pūrvārdhana naṣṭaghaṭabuddherjanmasāmagrīmādarśya paścārdhenādhikasya nāśanāmno nānvayona vyatirekastadvivekasāmagra vāstubhayamanukṛtaṃ bhavediti darśitam  tatra nāśākhyaṃ nakiñcidiha sāmagrayāṃ nimittamastītyanvayo nirastaḥ na cāsyāṃ satyāmapi sāmagrayāṃkadācinna syādeṣā buddhiriti vyatirekāvalambanamapāstam  pūrvaṃ tarhi kasmānneyaṃ buddhiritivyatirekapratyayāśātanaṃ śeṣeṇa  yadi purāpyeṣā sāmagrī syāt niyatamiyaṃ bhavantībuddhirarthāntarasāpekṣatāṃ sūcayet  na ceyaṃ sāmagrī purāpyasti vikalakapālapaṃkteḥparighapātādikāraṇābhāvenābhāvāt  tat kuto vyatirekamātramapi  uktasāmagrayāstuna vāsyāmapi syādeṣā na kadāciditi niṣedhadvayenānvayaḥ  śeṣeṇa vyatirekaśca vyaktaḥ tad buddhabhāvakāle sāmagrathā evābhāvapratipādanādasau sāmagraghabhāvo buddhayabhāvavyāpta ityartha  yastu pratyakṣetarasahakārisākalyarūpatayā sarvaiva sāmagrī parīkṣetisamarthayate viṣamadṛṣṭiḥ tataśca parokṣatayā tasyā nānvayavyatirekaniścaya ityucyate hantahutavahendhanādisāmagrī pratibandhopi dhūmāderastamita ityapravṛttinivṛttikaṃ jagat prasajyeta tasmānnādṛṣṭābhyupagamo dṛṣṭasādhanasāmarthya pratirodhenetyalaṃ vistareṇa  tadayaṃ ghaṭāmarśavataḥkapālānubhava evaṃ naṣṭaghaṭāvasāyasādhana iti siddham arthāpattirato gatā kṣayamiyaṃ na dhvaṃsasiddhau prabhuḥna viśeṣabuddhiviśeṣaṇamantareṇeti cet na bhāve  bhinnakālatvād viśeṣaṇatvāsiddhedhvaṃsasya yataḥ ganta ā  danubhāvā ā  prasādhyaprasādhya ā  ndhanāvānatā ā  vinaṣṭi a nakāro nāsti aC ratna niba pṛ   janya ā  nakārastyaktaḥ a  pratyāśāa  miyamabhavantī a  sāmagraghābhāvo ā  taśca ā  sāmarthya  ā  viśeṣamantareneti ā  nābhāve ājñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalausvabuddhayā rajyate yena viśeṣyaṃ tadviśeṣaṇam pūrvāparakālayonaśibhāvayorabhāvāt kena kaḥ syāt  kacit na ca bhāve sthitidharmo dhvaṃsa   kiṃ tu pradeśe  na cānyatra sthitaḥanyasya viśeṣaṇaṃ daṇḍavat  bhedādevamapi syāditi cet  bhede tarhi sarvānyarūpavivekena pratibhāsamānameva viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyaṃ svānuraktapratītiviṣayīkuryāt nasvarūpeṇāpratibhāsamānaṃ daṇḍavadeva  anumānasiddhenāpi daṇḍena  daṇḍipratīterutpādādanekānta iti cet na sarvathā yasya na svarūpāvabhāsa ityabhiprāyāt  daṇḍasyapunaranumānakālepratibhāsanepi niścāyakābhimataliṅgena saha saṃbandhagrahaṇakālestyevasvarūpanirbhāsaḥ  tatastadanusmaraṇādanumānakālepi tadrūpānuraktāṃ buddhimādadhīta daṇḍaḥ na ca sarvathā adṛṣṭadaṇḍasya daṇḍopyanumānabhājanaṃ svarūpānuraktapratītiheturvā dṛṣṭapūrvaḥ evaṃ nāśanāmāpyathaṃḥ kathaṃ tathā sthāt sarvathā adarśanāditi  na ca daṇḍānumānādbhinnādaṇḍipratītiḥ daṇḍotra daṇḍosya daṇḍavānayamiti cānarthāntaratvāt  na ceyaṃliṅgatyāge b na bhavantī pratijñāmātratayānumānaṃ bhavitumarhati yantraṣṭapratītirapināśanāmārthasādhakaṃ niścayamapekṣamāṇā kathaṃ svayameva sādhanatvenābhidhīyeta  nacānyaliṅgamasti sarvathā adṛśyatayā tasmin kasyacit pratibandhāsiddheḥ  ataeva hiseva buddhistatsiddhaye śaraṇamāśrīyate  atonumānasiddhenānekāntaḥ  anumānasthāpiviśeṣaṇasvarūpanirbhāsanāntarīyakatvāda pṛthasiddheścānumāna viśeṣaṇapratītyoritiyasyana svarūpanirbhāsastanna kasyacit svānuraktapratītinimittam yathā karikeśaraḥ  nāstica svarūpapratibhāso dhvaṃsasyeti vyāpakānupalabdhi  svānuraktapratītinimittatvaṃnirbhāsabhaṅge bhavadatiprasaṅghabādhitaṃ pratibhāsavattayaiva vyāptam  na cāsiddhiḥ idantayādarśayitumaśakyasya bāhyavastunaḥ pratibhāsavyavahārābhāvāt idantayā nirdeśanoye cavivādābhāvāt  na hi daṇḍopi daṇḍipratītyā sādhyādhyakṣa siddhatvāt  mūḍhaṃ prativyavahārasādhanepi nedantayā nirdeśaḥ viśeṣato locanagocare kālabhedenapratītiviṣayīkriyateatha sarvaṃ vastu svarūpeṇa pratibhāti na pararūpeṇa yathā bhāva eva nābhāvarūpeṇaevamabhāvopi bhāvarūpeṇāpratibhāsamānopi svarūpeṇa pratibhātyeva  idantayā prati nāśābhāvayo iti nāsti a  svokelita ā  dharmādhvasa ā  pradeśo ā  bhedāditamapi a  pratotirudayā ā  daṇḍetredaṇḍāsya ā  na bhavantoti ā  anupānabhavitu ā  evaṃ a  liṅga a  dhīyate a  ataesaiva ā cet  nave pararūpeṇa pratibhāso mṛgyate tasyābhāvaṃ prati siddhatvāt  svarūpaṃpunarasya kiṃ tatpratibhātīti nibhālayanto na labhāmahe idantayā nirdeśastu bhāveṣvetyapina rājakīyo niyaṃmaḥ  tad yadi bhāveṣvapi keṣucideva netrapātreṣvidantayā nirdeśo nasarveṣviti brūyāt tadā ṭavakādayopi puraḥ pratibhāsina evedantayā paraṃ nirdeṣṭumaśakyā iti kimatra vaktavyam  tasmād yāvaccakṣurgocaracāri vastu tāvadidantayānirdeśapratibhāsameva yatpunaridantayā nirdeśavirahitaṃ tadapratibhāsameva nayanagrāhyamitinyāyaḥ atha viśeṣabuddhayaiva pratibhāsopi sādhyaḥ yathā hi na daṇḍibuddhirdaṇḍabuddhimantareṇa tathā daṇḍapratibhāsamantareṇāpi evaṃ naṣṭabuddhirapi viśeṣabuddhitvānna nāśaṃnāśapratibhāsamantareṇeti kathamapratibhāsaghoṣamiti cet  bhavatyeva vikāro napunaretādṛśaḥ  svasantānavatapratibhāsosmābhirapyanumānena pratipattavya iti ghaṭādipratibhāsepyevamidānīmāyātam  tat kimahaṃ paśyāmi kiñcidityanumānamanāptavatāāptavacanenāpi pratyetavyamityarthamapratikurvāṇopi vaidyaḥ kṛtārtha syāt  antataḥśapathenāpi ttirālambyeta  parokṣe hi viṣayemīṣāṃ prakārāṇāmavakāśa ana jñāne  yatpunarapaśyantamātmānaṃ vedayamāna eva paśyasīti grāhyate vyaktamiyaṃ bhaṇḍavidyāpaśyantamapi vāhyati  yopyapaśyannapi tadvacanena paśyāmīti gṛhṇīta sa khalupaśorapi paśuḥ jñānaparokṣatāvādepi hikasyacitpratibhāsena sādhyatepratibhāsi yat pratibhāsosya nāsyeti sādhyate nopapattibhiḥ  tasmāt pratibhāsopi sādhya ityasaṃbaddhametat  nāśastvapratibhāsamāno yadisādhyate sādhyatām na tu naṣṭaghaṭapratītyeti sthitametatnāśo vāstu na tu pratītijanako yadvaddhaṭe naṣṭadhīḥ abhyupagamyāpi brūmaḥ  astu vā nāśo nāma na punarasyāvaśyaṃ pratītameva janakaṃmudgarādīti śakyam yathā naṣṭaghaṭabuddhereva na pratītaḥ kapālānubhavo heturiṣṭaḥ tathā viśeṣasyāpi ā  vyānirde iti nāsti ā   bhāṣina ā  vaktaṃ ā   buddhau ca a dhikkāro a  asyābhiranu a asyābhirapiranu ā   māyātaḥ ā  gṛhṇāti a ratna niba pū   bhavahetu ajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalonāśasthāpi mudgarādiparihāreṇa eva vastuni vastunāavastunā vā svarūpasaṃkaravyatikaraniṣedhaḥ  tato yathā nīlamanīlaṃ na bhavati ubhayoranyonyasvabhāvatvāt tathā kalasanāśayorapi syāt  na ca tāvateṣṭasiddhiḥ mudgarasannidhimātra nīlānīlayoḥ kathamiti cet  nīlānīlayoḥ parasparaparihāra iti naikatvamanayorityevārthaḥ  tato dharmavirodha evānenāpi prakāreṇaprakāśyate  anyathā tuhinahutabhujoriva nīlānīlavāsasorapi militayoḥ prabandhasthiti  prasajyeta sūkṣmadeśaparihāreṇa virodhasya phalavattvāt  ataeva viruddhopalabdhaukalpikabhāvaḥ sthūla eva deśo dharmī  evaṃ nīlamanīlatvena virudhyata ityapinīlamanīlaṃ na bhavatītyevārthaḥ yadi tu dharmidharmayorapi sākṣādvirodha syāt tadā yatra dharmiṇyanīlatvaṃtatra nīlatvaṃ  na syāt  asti ca yathā ratnāntaraṃ tapanīyamātre tathā nāśasthābhāvarūpadharmamātratvepi bhāvadharmā ghaṭo nāsannabhāvadharmā ca na sannityevārthaḥ tataḥA m sthiti ā  na cātra ā  vadhinaṃ ā  vastuno vastunā a   pātāt a bhavanābhāvana ā  satīti nāsti ā  dharmavidha ā  tādātmye ā
