hetvantaramapekṣata iti hiprakṛtam  dvitīyapakṣepi sutarāṃ na doṣaḥ dravyarūpaṃ hi jātameva prāgapi dravyadhīdhvaniprasava eva sāmānyāt na caitāvatā tadbhāve hetvantaramapekṣitaṃ bhavati  na hi kāryeṇakāraṇasya svaviṣayasāmarthyavyavahāre prāganiṣpanna bmeva tatsāmarthyaṃ tadbhāve vākāraṇam tadeva kāryaṃ hetvantaramapekṣitavat kiṃ ca bhinnena paścāt jāyamānenāpi prakāśaguṇena yadā tāvat prakāśaguṇayuktaḥsaṃpanno dīpaḥ tadā kiṃ punastadbhāve hetvantaramapekṣate yato dṛṣṭāntakṣatiḥ syāt  tannaprakriyāpoṣaṇatrāṇamapramāṇaparāyaṇena  anubhavānurodhena tu yathābhimatameva dṛṣṭāntaḥ na hi prathamadvitīyakṣaṇayoḥ sāmānyayogāyogābhyāṃ viśeṣapratītirasti  nāpi dravyasāmānyayorbhedānubhava iti prakṛtasya tvanyathāpi siddhernātra nirbaṃndhaḥ  tasmānna prakāśasvahetoḥ prakāśarūpaniṣpannastadbhāve hetvantaramapekṣate vaiyarthyāt  andhakārīkaraṇepyasāmarthyāditi siddham  Fdhakaraṇe ra rthakārīkaraṇe a  vaiyarthyasāmarthyastānna a  tathāha ā  siddhāntasya ā iti tada nāsti ā   mutpadyamānaṃ ā  rūpasyamapi ā  jāyate ā  athetiprāntayojanā a  gocarīkurvatīti ra  janayatāṃ a  hīti nāsti ā  hoti nāstiā  ghoṣaṇatrāṇapramāṇa ā   svakāśa ā  arthakārī    ajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaunanu śulkamambaraṃ rāgadravyayogena raktīkriyamāṇamupalabdham tatra raktasvabhāvāsvabhāvatve vastrasya vaiyarthyāsāmarthya codyaṃ rāgadravyasya kiṃ nopakramyata iti cet  nakhalvasya vikalpasya sarvatrāvatāro vivakṣitaḥ kiṃ tu tatsvabhāvātatsvabhāvavikalpadvārakamapi dūṣaṇaṃ hetorasti tāvadityatyantāyoganiṣedha upakrāntaḥ  tato yatretadūṣaṇamupapādayituṃ śakyate tatra dūṣaṇabhāvamāviśati  kimanyacintayā yadi yuktibheda tathā ca vinaśvaratvaṃ nāma kṣaṇikatvaṃ kanīyaḥ kālatvaṃ vā  avinaśvaratvamapi drāghīyasā ukālena sadāsthāyitayā vā  sarvathā yāvatkālāvasthitiko bhāva svahetorudapāditadabhyantare yadi kenacinnāśyeta tadā yāvatkālāvasthitireva notpanna  na hi saṃvatsarasthāyī cāsau divasanāśī ceti svabhāvadvayaṃ parasparaviruddhamasya sādhu nanu vināśakāraṇamantareṇa saṃvatsarasthāyī avāntaraṃ tu vināśakāraṇasamavadhānevāntaranāśīti ko virodha  virodha eva niścaye hi yadyarthānupraveśo nasvabhāve yathā yadyatra patrapāte dhūmaḥ saṃbhavenniyatamiyamaṅgārā anyathā tu guñjāpuñjaiti na svabhāvabhedaḥ  tathā yadi divase vinaśyati tadavadhikameva hetunā janitamsaṃvatsarana śe tu tadavadhikamiti bhavatu  na tu parasparavirodhisvarūpe dvitīyasyaikatrasamuccayaḥ  na hi tatrāni vinaśyanneva saṃvatsarasthāyī ardhārdhena vā tadubhayaṃ bhavitumarhati  vikalpastu saṃśayātmā jñānasyaiva na vastuno dharmaḥ  tasmād vastvekasvabhāvamevana viruddhasvabhāvāntarayogi  etacca divasādisthāyitvaṃ pramāṇena nirūpaṇamarhati satyaṃna veti  abhyupagamya tu cintitametat pramāṇavyāhate hetusāmarthyāśrayaṇasyadurlabhatvāt  tato yadyakṣaṇikatāpi tathāpi yāvānasya kāla sthiteravadhistadabhyantarehetvantarasyāsāmarthya tasya purastādvaiyarthyamiti sthitam  kṣaṇikatvepi na tatkṣaṇenāśakāraṇena kiñcit śakyamiti vyaktam kṣaṇāntare tu svayameva nāstītinārthonarthahetunā  sadātane tvasamartha evāyam tasmād vināśe kartavye na kaścit heturasāmarthyavaiyarthyaṇamatikrāmati yadārthāntare tu karparādau sa eva mudgarastābhyāṃ dūṣaṇābhyāṃ na lipyate tadvyāpārānantarameva janmalābhāt karparasya evaṃ rāgadravyasyāpi tadvyāpārānta ramudayabhāji yogeṇa a ā  tyutpato ā  vyasā ca ā  tayā ca ā  nanva a  a yantrapāte ra  maṅgāryā ā  tadā vādhimeva ā  janitaḥ a  na ca ā dhesvarūpaṃ a  sviti nāsti ā  yadi kṣa a  syasāmarthya ra  taditi nāsti ā vaktavyamiti a  tanatvasamartha  ra  evāsāṃ ā  kapālasya āpatrayātkṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetukavināśādhikāraraktavāsasi na sāmarthya vaiyarthyam  pāṇḍucaṇḍātakanivartane punaḥ kastannivartayati yadāpi daśādvaye ekameva vastravastu tadāpi taddoṣānativṛttireva  na hi raktāvasthāyāmapi śubhrameva taditi nirvahati  tato yadi tadāpi śubhrameva tadvastu naṃ raktatāyāavakāśa ityasamartha rāgadravyaṃ pūrvarakte tu tanmātrarāgāpekṣāyāṃ vyartham  tasmāt sthairyāpekṣayā doṣāvatārāt samayāparādha evaṃvidho na vastunaḥ  pūrvasya svarasanirodhetadupādānāpekṣayā rāgadravyeṇāpūrvaraktavastrotpādane taddoṣasya parihārasiddheḥ  naivaṃvastusthitiriti cet  nanu tadeva cintyate kīdṛśī vastusthitiriti  kimatra kośapānena paraḥ pratyāyanīyaḥ  tat kimakāṇḍenaivaṃ vastusthitiriti ucyate pratyabhijñāprāmāṇyāvalambanasya nirastatvāt nanu samayāparādhopi kathamabhidhīyate vyavasthite dharmaṇi guṇadvayasyatirobhāvāvirbhāvasvīkārāt  yadyevaṃ tadā prācīnaguṇanirākaraṇesāmarthyavaiyarthyaprāptāvapyapūrvaraktatāguṇotpādanenaiva caritārtho rāgadravyavyāpāra iti kathamuktadūṣaṇasparśa  pūrvaniṣpannarūpāpekṣayā hi veyarthyāsāmarthyacintā prakrāntā nāpūrvāpekṣayā na hyapūrvepi kartavye yadyevaṃ rūpaṃ svahetorjātaṃ tadā vaiyarthyam evaṃ jāte tvasāmarthyamitinirṇayāvakāśaḥ  nāśanīyaśca sarva pūrvasiddha eva bhāvaḥ  sa ca vinaśvaretarayoḥ prakārāntaratiraskārādanyatarasvarūpamanativartamāno na vināśahetoḥ kalpitasyāsāmarthyamānarthakyaṃ vā sthātuṃ prabhavati  na caivaṃ hetuvādocchedaprasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ asiddhe hi kārye hetorāśrayaṇam siddhe ceyaṃ cintā  tadaiva ca yadi hetorevaṃrūponiṣpanna iti hetupuraskāreṇaiva vādapravṛttaḥ  na caivamasiddhe śakyamityuktam  tatkathaṃprakṛtāsmadvikalpasya sarvatra saṃbhava  vikalpamātrasya sarvatra hetuphalasaṃmate saṃbhavepināsmadīyayukteraparādhabodhaḥ kṛto bhavati yadi tu siddhepi vastuni vyāpakasvabhāvadvayesāmarthyavaiyarthyāvatārepihetvantaramapekṣamāṇamupadarśayituṃ śakyate syādaparādhaḥ  na caivam  tasmādvikalpamātrasyāparādhepi nāparādhaḥ saviśeṣaṇasya anupalambhavaditi vyarthaḥ tanmātropanyāsaḥ  nāsāmarthya ā  yadi ta iti nāsti ā  pūrvaṃ ā  siddha a  ceditanyayojanā a vastuti ā  naivācaritā ā  pūrvaṃ ni a  nāpūrvākṣayeti prāntayojanā aprakārāntare a   tiraskārasya a  sāmarthasthātuṃ a  dotseda    a ra  reyaṃā  masiddhaḥ śakyāmabhidhātum ā  syeti nāsti ājñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalaub athānupalambhamātrasya svasādhyasādhanasāmarthyaśūnyataivāparādhaḥ vikalpamātrasya punarasāmarthyavaiyarthyollekhaśekharasya na hetuvādāpavādaśaktiśūnyatetiviṣama upanyāsaḥ  aho puruṣakāro bhasmabhūṣaṇasya  evaṃ hi sarvathā hetuphalāpalāpesādhu  sādhitaṃ dhvaṃsasya hetumattvamiti vyaktamayamātmānamātmanaiva viḍambayati  tadayaṃbhavanasvabhāvādivikalpaḥ  saṃkalpaniveśitaśaktirapi viṣaye ca parihāryaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvavyavasthitena anyathā mūlocchedāt prakaraṇapravṛtteḥ  siddhopādhistuvikalpo vināśakaraṇameva kavalayati na kāraṇamātram  atiprasaṅgabhaṅgabhīruṇā tubhavatā nādriyate iti yuktamevaitat  tasmāthantuṃ hetuphale śramoyamaphala saṃsthāpya sāmānyatastattvaṃ kvāpi vimarśa evaviṣaye prārambhasaṃbhāvitaḥ prārambha upakrama prastāvaḥ tena saṃbhāvita ādṛtaḥ  sāmānyena kāryakāraṇabhāvasattāṃvyavasthāpya vināśādau viṣayaviśeṣe kaciddhetusattā kimastu navetyatra vimarśa eṣosmadīyaḥ prastāvānurūpaḥ  hetuphalonmūlanāya tu viphala  prayāsaḥ sāmānyena vyavasthāpyaivaprakaraṇapravṛtteḥ  na cāyaṃ vikalpaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvakṣepāya kṣamaḥ bhavanasvabhāvobhavanasvabhāvo vā hetuto bhavatīti  tathā hi abhavanadharmā tāvad bandhyā prasūtīti bhavanasvabhāvaśca tvanmatena gaganāderabhavanasya kadācidapyabhāvāt tayostāvadasāmarthya vaiyarthyagrasto bhavati hetuvyāpāra  kādācitkaṃ bhāvaṃ bhavanadharmāṇamabhavanadharmakatuvā brūhi na punarayaṃ kiñcidanapekṣamāṇaḥ  kādācitka eva bhavitumarhati yaścāpekṣorthaḥkāladeśasvabhāvaniyamāya sa eva hetuḥ  atha bhavanasvabhāva iti na sattādharmā kiṃutpattidharmeti vivakṣitam tadāpyutpattirityasata ātmalābho na kādācitkatvādanyaiti tadvadevottaram  vināśasya tu kādācitkatvaniṣedha uktaḥ atha hetuto bhavanadharmā yaḥ sa kiṃ bhavatītaro veti vikalpārtha   tadā ādyavikalpa eva viśrānto vādaḥ  tathā hi hetuto bhavati na pūrvamiti na vaiyarthyam sāmarthya ā  punasāmarthya ā  sādhu iti nāsti ā   saṃkalpa iti nāsti ā yamiva ā  kāryeti nāsti ā  pūrṇocchedāt ā  kalayati ā  tu iti nāstiā  nādriyata ā  itoti nāsti ā  hatu ā  vimarṣa ā  prastāva itināsti a  vimarṣa a bhaved ā  tvanmate a  rabhavanasyā ā bhavatu a tke tu a  bhavana dharmānanyabha ā  neti nāsti ā  pekṣaṇa ā  tvodasya ātvādiṣṭa rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetukavināśādhikārabhavati hetuto nānyato bhavatīti kutosāmarthyam  atra ca nirbaṃndho bandhya itidiṅmātramabhidhīyate ubhayoḥ siddhatvāt hetuphalabhāvasya aprastutatvācca  yataścāyaṃsiddhopādhiko vikalpaḥ sannāśasyaiva hetorbādhako nāsadutpādakasya asamānatvātnyāyasya yathoktaṃ prāk  tataśchedadāhādihetavo raktadukūlakāraṇavadupapannā eva mokṣākhyadaśāviśeṣahetuśceti saphala eva tatra prayāsaḥ  tasmānna sato nāśahetuḥ kaścit  svahetutaeva tāvaddeśākā ravat kālatayāpi niṣpattiḥ a kiṃ cadhvaṃso vāstu vidherbalātparighavad yad vā yathā śarkarābhāvosau tadavastha eva tu na yatkiñcitkarāstasya te vyāpārāviratistataḥ kṣaṇinaye dattvādabandhyaṃ kathaṃ deśākāravadasya hetuniyataḥ kālopi yasmānmataḥ yathā hi mudgaraḥ śarkarānikaro vā yastasmātsyānmataḥ nāśahetoranupapattenotpattirnāśasyetyuktam  astu vā nāśābhidhānamarthāntaraṃ kāraṇabalāt  daṇḍavat śarkarā raktatānāśepi koṣāntarakamadhiṣṭhāya tiṣṭhatu santu bhāvāstadavasthā eva nahi te tasya kiñcitkarāḥ  yathā hi mudgaraḥ śarkarānikaro vā tasyākiñcitkaraḥ anyathānāśābhyupagamavairthyaprasaṅgāt tathā  nāśopi sthitimati bhāve svakāraṇādutpadyamānastasya kimaṅga kartumasamartha  yathā hi tasya hetubalabhāvino na sarvathā nāśaḥśakyo vā sāmarthyavaiyarthyābhyām tathānurūpāṃśe nāśopyaśakya eva  tatrāpi svabhāvabhede pūrvavannaśvaretaravikalpasyāvatāravāraṇābhāvāt  niraṃśepi ca vastunikalpanānurodhādetaducyate  tattvatastvaṃśanāśanepi sarvathā nāśa eva sa cāśakya itisādhitam apūrvanirvartanam  vastunastu vāryate  tataḥ yopyapūrva pūrvavat koṣāntaratirohitaḥ kalpamāstāṃ tatkṛto vā punaraparo nāśābhidhānorthastadvadastu  na tu bhāvasyakiñciditi svajñānajananajaladhāraṇādivyāpārānuparamaprasaṅgo dunivāraḥ  hetuto na na bhavatīti ā  nyato iti prāntayojanā a  cakāro nāsti ā  yannāśaka a  tava ra  niṣpatteḥ ā  palidha a  pṛṣṭhamaspaṣṭam ā  aspaṣṭā paṃkti a nāśyepi ra  dupekṣamāṇa ra  kartuṃ samartha ra  śakyatvāt ra  svabhāvābhāvapūrvavannasvabdatasyavi ra  svo pūrvaḥ parvatanakoṣāntara  ra  tatra kuto ra  durvāraḥ ājñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauetena yadavocad vācaspatiḥ nanvasminnutpannepi bhinnamūrtī kimāyātaṃ bhāvasya na kiñcidāyātam astvayamāyuṣmān bhāvaḥ  svakāraṇādhīnajanmanā tadabhāvena tatsva rūpavirahalakṣaṇena svalakṣaṇaśālinārthānurūpavyavahāraṃ pravartayatā nirastasamastārthaṃkriyāki naśchinnamiti tadapahastitam samastārthakriyānirasanasyaiva tadavasthe tasminnaśakyasādhanatvāt tadabhāvenaiva tādavasthyakhaṇḍanamiti cet  nanu bhāve tāvat  tadavastha evasvakāraṇaprabhāvādabhāvo jātastato vyāvṛttya tatkhaṇḍanamanena kartavyamiti samasamayatāprasaṅgaḥ prācīno duṣpariharaḥ  tathā ca sati tatsvarūpavirahalakṣaṇenetyanupapannamna hi tadviraharūpatve tatkālasaṃbhavo nāma  tato mudgarādipadārthāntarasādhāraṇasyaabhāvasaṃjñākaraṇe nābhimatasvalakṣaṇaśālitābhivyaktisiddhiḥ yataḥ tadanurūpavyavahārapravartanamabhidhīyamānaṃ śobheta  tena ca svarūpasyārthakriyāyāṃ tādavasthyasya cākhaṇḍanamiti parasparākarṣī nāśāntarakaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ svayaṃnivṛttirūpatayā na nāśāntarāvakāśa iti cet na samānakālasaṃbhavātnivṛttirūpatāyā pratikṣiptatvāt padārthāntaravat paryudastameva rūpamavaśiṣyate  tena cavināśena niyataṃ parabhūtavināśākhyavastukaraṇaṃ mudgareṇeva ko hi viśeṣosya tatparyu dastarūpatvena mudgarāt yadayaṃ paramanapekṣamāṇa eva nāśayati  mudgarastvenamanapekṣamāṇonāśa iti syāt  vināśasaṃjñākaraṇapratilambhastu bhavet  tāmantareṇa tasyāpimudgarādaviśeṣāt ākārabhedamātrasya maṇimantrādiṣvapi bhāvāt yadi tu  pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ śaktisādhanamekaniyataṃ bhaved bhaved viśeṣatacca nāstīti pratipāditam tasmātprasajyapakṣesti na tulyakālatāna paryudāse paranāśavarjanam   rūpaparivahanakṣa  a  nāśinā ra  nanu tāvatā ra  stato  khaṇḍanana itityaktam ra  tatonurūpādi ra  padārthā saṃjñā iti tyaktam ra  hāraḥ ra  vināśane ā  niyatasyara    mapekṣamāṇameva ā   mapekṣamāṇa ā  vināśakāraṇaprati a  yadi pratyākhyā ā  vikalpāśeṣa ra  tulakā aiti saṃgrahaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetuka vināśādhikāraḥsthitenyadanyatrabhavad bhavet sakṛniyogatonyakṣaṇatānurodhini sthitepi hetau bhavadekadā na cetprayojanaṃ tatkṣaṇabhaṅgasaṃbhavāt sthitena ki vyomni samakṣaṇaṃ phalaṃphalena nāśopi yathaiva lakṣayet  ityantaraślokaḥ yadi tu nāśākhyaṃ kāryaṃ na tasya nivartakaṃ ki tvanyadeva daṇḍādi tadā bhāvaścanivartate abhāvaśca pravartata iti bhavati kālabhedaḥ kiṃtu nopayogo nāśasya  nāpitadabhāvena nirastasamastārthakriya iti vācyam  asāmarthyavaiyarthyaṃ ca prastutam  tatopirikteyaṃ vācoyuktiḥ yatpunaratra tenotprekṣitam  yathoktaṃ svahetuto bhāvo naśvaronaśvaro vā  jāyateiti tatrocyate  na vayaṃ vinaśvaramavinaśvaraṃ vā jānīmaḥ kiṃtu santaḥ svahetubhyojāyante dhvaṃsante ca hetvantarebhya svapratyayādhīnasannidhānebhyaḥ dhvaṃsaśca dhvaṃsamānādbhinnohetubhedataḥ svabhāvabhedācceti tatrāpyucyate  yadi naśvarānaśvarasvarūpamavidvāneva bhavānevamāha tadā ka nāśo nāma padārtha   kuto vā vyāvṛttyā bhavati vyavasthāpyo yodhvaṃsamānād bhinnaḥ saṃpratyeva pratijñātaḥ sa idānīṃ vinaśvarāvinaśvarasvarūpāparijñānenavyavasthāpyamāna ākāśādiṣvapi ki na vyavasthāpyate  teṣu nāśādarśanāditi cet nanvanyatrāpi nāśo nāma dṛśyata iti śapathagamyametat  tato vinaśvaretarasvabhāvāviṣkaraṇaṃ bhavataḥ prasahyāyātaṃ kimatra śa  thena  tathā ca sati svahetoreva tadatadrūpa janmani niyatāvatāramasāmarthyavaiyarthyadūṣaṇaṃ paśyatopi tatra hetvantarapratijñānaṃ kathamitivayamapi na jānīmaḥ  athedamākūtaṃ vaidarbhyagarbhayā girā pratyakṣata eva kutaścidutpādaḥkutaścinnāśa upalabhyamāno vinaśvaretaravikalpena kathamapohituṃ śakyaḥ  na hi pratyakṣa lpalakṣaṇatānu ā nyakṣaṇatastu a  ityarthāntara a  vāpi ā  likhitaṃ ā  naśvarātā a  atro ā  sveti nāsti ā     khararūpamviddhā ra   tivyava itināsti ā   mvivinaśvarā a mviśvarā ā  natvanyatrāpi a  pātipratyakṣameva ā tarāvi ājñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalausiddhaṃ vikalpaśatenāpi śātayituṃ śakyam sarvapramāṇavyāpārasya pratyakṣa evaviśrāmāditi tatrāpi nāśa iti yadi padārthāntaraṃ svasamayaprasiddhamucyate yo mudgarādijanmāghaṭādipadārthamarthaḥ kadarthayati tasya janmavyāpārī pratyakṣagocarāviti mahatsāhasamityupapāditaṃ prāk  tat kathaṃ na vikalpāvakāśaḥ atha naśyataḥ svayameva rūpaṃ bhedāntarapratikṣepeṇa tanmātrajijñāsāyāṃ pṛthagivādarśyamāno nāśobhipretaḥ tathā ca dhvaṃsante hetvantarebhyaḥ ityabhītvaivoktam  evaṃtarhi daṇḍādibhyaḥ kuṇḍādayo vinaśyanti na svayamiti siddhāntaniṣṭhāyāṃ dhvaṃsaścanirastasamastārthakriya ityapi suptavilapitameva  tat kimanayā vācaspati aabhipretīti na vidmaḥ  evaṃ tarhi yāvati pratyakṣavyāpāra  tāvatopi kathamapahnavaḥ kiyati cāsau  pratyakṣavyāpāra  utpadyamāne ca hetvantarāddhetvantarānnirudhyamāne cabhāve tadutpattihetovināśa heturanya iti siddham na ca nāśo nāmānyo yataḥ pratyakṣagocaracodyāvakāśa iti  dhigetat vināśasya bhāvādananyatve tadvetarbhāvahetureva bhāvahetureva na bhāvotpattihetuḥ tatkathamutpattihetoranyo vināśahetu  kathaṃ ca pūrvaniṣpannasya paścāttano hetuḥ  pūrvaparabhāvaścāyamadhyakṣasiddha eva kiṃ cotpadyamānaṃ  nirudhyamānaṃ ca vastvekamanekaṃ vā  ekatvaṃ tāvadviruddhadharmādhyāsādayuktam  atha pratyakṣeṇa tathā vyavasthānāt kiṃ kurmaṃ iti cet  ekapratyakṣeṇaekadekādhārayorupalabdhī sādhuravirodhaḥ nīlacaturasratāvat  yadā tu bhinnakālamadhyakṣadvayamekaikarūpagrāhi tadā pratyabhijñānamātrameva miśrayati  taccāpramāṇamityuktam tato viddhadharmādhyāsād bheda eva  ekatra tu kṣaṇe vibhāgābhāvānna virodho vyāvṛttibhedamātreṇaikatra bhāvāt  tathā hi sa eva bhāvakṣaṇa prāgabhāvādutpadyamāna ucyatepaścādbhāvānnirudhyamāna ucyate  kṣaṇaparamparāvyāpinyapi vastunyevamastīti cet  mahatmāhatasāhasa ā  prāgiti nāsti ā  rūpabhedā a  māno iti nāsti a tāvatopi  pratyakṣavyāpāra iti nāsti ā  bhāvye ā  tata utpatti ā siddhiḥ a  pratyakṣā a  bhāvādina ā  bhāvahetureveti prāntayojanā a  ca a tpadyamānani a  virudhya ā  mātra iti nāsti ā  ato a  dyavirodhoa  bhāvanirudhya akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetuka vināśādhikāraḥna vyāpakadvāreṇa  virodhasyaiva siddheḥ  prathamakṣaṇepyutpadyamāno bhāvo vā bhāvikṣaṇāntarāvasthānena vyāpto na prācīnāvasthiti kṣaṇamapi spṛśati nirudhyamānaścāsaucaramakṣaṇe prācyakṣaṇāntarāvasthānena vyāpto na ca bhāvinīmavasthiti kṣaṇamapispṛśatīti virodha eva  kṣaṇe punarekasminneṣa vibhāga iti vyāvṛttimātrabhedo navirodha  tasmāt kṣaṇadvayamapi sthitivivakṣāyāmudayanidhanadharmayovirodhānnaikatvam anekatvapakṣe ca prācīnaṃ vastu mudgarādiparigaṇita vināśa hetu vyatirekeṇāpi nirudhyamānaṃ svahetoreva niyatakālasthitidānasāmarthyamuddopayatīti na vināśahetuḥ kaścit  athāparigaṇitā eva vināśahetavaḥ tatra durupalakṣaḥ kaściddheturanirjñāyamānaḥsvanibandhanaṃ nidhanamādadhīteti kimayuktam  evaṃ tahi pratikṣaṇamapi vināśasaṃbhāvanāyā na pracyutiriti vyathaṃ vināśahetuvyavasthāpanam  parigaṇitasya hi bhūyolakṣaṇasya hetoḥ prasiddhapradhvaṃsalakṣaṇāt prāgabhāvaniścayena vināśavyavasthā mābhūditisahetukatvaṃ vināśasya sādhayitumārabdham  sūkṣmatayā tu durupalakṣaṇasyāpi hetoḥ svīkāre prayatnaveyarthyamāyātamityalaṃ mithyāvikalpena  tasmāt sthitimati vastunisarvasyākiñcitkaratva pratipādanāt santaḥ svahetubhyo jāyante dhvaṃsante ca hetvantarebhyaityarthapadametat  tat kutaḥ idaṃ maṇimantrauṣadhamindrajālaṃ bhāvena śikṣitaṃ yadayamavikalānyadarśana pratyayastadavastha eva kadācidadhyakṣaḥ b atyakṣaśceti nanu kṣaṇikanītāvevāyaṃ doṣa ukto yuktaśca  yadāha śaṅkaraḥ  na hi bhāvasyanivṛtterutpattimantareṇa prāgiva paścādapi svarūpahāniḥ yenāyaṃ tadaivānupalambhaviṣayona pūrva hānau vā paścāt saivāsya nivṛtterutpattiriti  tadayuktam kṣaṇikapakṣe hiprāgiva paścādapi na svarūpahāniriti sāhasametat  nivṛtterutpattimantareṇa svīkriyamāṇāpi svarūpahānirasaṅgataiveti cet  nivṛttyādināmnaḥ padārthāntarasyotpattiḥbhavatu mā vā bhūt yata evāsau kṣaṇasthitiniyatorthaḥ tata eva kṣaṇāntaramavyāpnuvankṣaṇāntare nāstītyucyate sa evārtho bhāvasya kṣaṇāntare nāśo jāta ityanena vacasocyate  nāpūrvavastūtpādo vidhīyate  chandato hi vacasā pravṛttiḥ  arthastu nirūpaṇīyaḥ tatra yadyekakṣaṇādhīnatayā kṣaṇāntare niyatasattāvasāyasiddhiḥ tāvataiva caritārtho neti nāsti ā  dvāreṇaiva virodha a  veti nāsti a  darśayati ā  vyāptau a nneva ā nnaiṣa a   viśāśa a  tathā a  kimaprayuktaṃ a  nakārī nāsti ra preti nāsti ā  svīkārapra ā  nadhyakṣaśceti a  prāgeva ā  vinayo ā nakārastyaktaḥ a   rasaugataiveti a  nārtha  a  kṣaṇe   ṇi ā vacasā ā yatra ra  śattāva ājñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauvināśavādaḥ kimatra kasyacidutpattiparyeṣaṇayā  na hi gṛhe eva devadattostīti sarvatrānyatravastvantaramabhidhānanirodhabodhanamiti nyāyaḥ tatrāpi pradeśāntarebhāvavidhirastīti cet  astu tadarthameva niyama nibandhananipātaprayogāt  kevalaṃ kiñcid vastu vidyamānamutpadyamānaṃ vāna pratītipathaprasthāyiniṣedhamātrasyaiva pratīteḥ  tāvataiva ca devadattamanusarataḥ pravṛtinivṛttipāṭavamāpanīpadyate vastvantarapratītāvapi hi vihitāyāṃ gṛhādanyatra yāvanna niyamānusāreṇadevadattasya prasajyātmānaṃ niṣedhamavasthāpayati tāvanna susthaḥ  tasmādaspṛṣṭavasturūpamabhāvamātramavaśyapratipādyam na cānyatra nāstītyanena vasturūpaṃ kiñcid vidhāya tadeva paramasti na devadattaiti kramavatī pratītiranubhavaviṣayaḥ yathā gṛha evāstītyanena nānyatreti  bhavatucaivam tathāpi paścādabhāvamātrapratītyaiva viśrāmaḥ  anyathā parāparavasturūpapratipattāveva puruṣāyuṣamupayujyet na prakṛtaniṣedhabodhasiddhiḥ  tasmād yathātra niṣedhamātraṃmandirādanyatra devadattasya vyavahriyate tanmātrameva ca devadattasyānyatrābhāva pratītigocara ityādi vyavahārasyāpyarthaḥ tathā ekatreva kṣaṇesti bhāvaḥ kṣaṇāntare nāsti kṣaṇāntare tasyābhāvaḥ pratīyata iti niṣedhamātramanyatra kṣaṇe khyāpyate  na vasturūpasaṃsparśaḥ nāpi tadapekṣāniṣedhasiddhayepi  evaṃ svarūpahānirityapi niṣedhamātravyavahāra eva tatra ca na kasyacidutpatyā sattayā vopayoga iti kathamucyate nivṛtteḥ utpattimantareṇasvarūpahāniriti  ataeva hānau vā paścāt saivāsya nivṛtterutpattiḥ ityapi pravāhāpātaḥpātakavatparihāryaḥ  paścāt svarūpahānirityapi hi paścānniṣedhavyavahāramātram na tuakasyacid vasturūpasyotpattiriti  sa ca niṣedhavyavahāro devadattasyaivānyatra kacitsattāniyamapratibandhādavyavasthitasaṃvādī  etena yat nyāyabhūṣaṇopyāha ko hyevaṃ śraddadhīta pratyutpannāvasthāyāmeva sanbhāvaḥ paścāttvasan na ca paścānnaśyatīti  tatrāpi kaḥ punarevamāha na paścātnaśyatīti  yadi paścānnaśyati tadā paścānnāśotpattiḥ svīkṛteti cet  yadi tvamevavacasāmartheṣu svāmī  dhāya na niṣedha a   mutpadyamāna iti nāsti ā  cakāro nāsti ra  yāvanniyamāā  mātreti nāsti a  pratītaiva a  puruṣāpuruṣamupayudyeta a puruṣāyuṣamuhyeta ā vyāpyate a  syotpattividheḥ a  sattāniṣedha dadhyavasita a  va paścāt tva āvaḥ paścātve akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetukavināśādhikāraḥsyādetat  dvidhā tvarthasthitiḥ pramāṇānusāriṇī samayānusāriṇī ca  prathamāyāṃ paścānnaśyatīti paścādasanniti vyavahiyata ityevārtha samarthitaḥ  aṃtaḥ pramāṇaparāyaṇena kathamabhidhātuṃ śakyaṃ paścādasanna ca paścānnaśyatīti  dvitīyāyāṃ tu navirodha  yasya hi paścānnaśyatīti paścānnāśotpattiriṣṭā taṃ prati paścādasan  na sanvyavahartavyo na ca paścānnaśyati  na cāsya paścānnāśavastutpattiriti kathamaśraddhāviṣayaḥ   tadapariniṣṭhitārthatattvavacanavibhramamātreṇa grāmyajanamanohareṇa samayanirvāhamanoratha iti kaṣṭam rūpeṇa kāryamutpādayan kṣaṇamātrasthāyināpi rūpeṇa ki notpādayet  sarvaṃ tu rūpamaspṛśan kāryaṃ kuryāddheturiti kasyaśraddhāviṣayaḥ  tato yathāyaṃ bhāvo niyatadeśo niyatavastusaṃsthānādyāṃkāra svahetorevasamutpadyate tathā niyatakālopīti kimasaṃbhāvyamatra  na ca deśādiniyamena svarūpasaṃkocamabhāva eva bhāvasya bhāvayatīti vācyam  na hyabhāvo bhāvamutpannaṃ vāsaṅkocayet  kāraṇena saha saṃbhūya saṅkacitameva cotpādayet  atra pakṣe pṛthak pauruṣarahitaḥ  kāraṇasāmagrayantarbhūtobhāvopi nāma yadi bhāvasādhakaḥ kaścidupapādayituṃśakyaḥ kiṃ naśchinnam  yādṛśī tādṛśī vā kāraṇasāmagrī kāryaṃ kuryāt  yathā tuniyatadeśākāraṃ kurute tathā  niyatakālamapi kartuṃ kastasyāḥ śaktivighāta iti brūmaḥyatastadarthamarthyate parotpattiḥ paścāt  prathamapakṣepi kiṃ tāvat sa bhāvaḥ svahetoviśva rūpa utpanno niyataḥ kriyatebhāvena  na vā kenāpi rūpeṇa niṣpanna kenacid vāniṣpanna eva na tu deśākārakālairiti vikalpāḥ antyastāvadayuktaḥ  yena hi rūpeṇa niṣpannaḥ sa eva tasyākāraḥ sa ca na vyāpārabhāvamanubhavaḥ kṣamate  tasmāt svakāraṇādeva deśādiniyata iva kālaniyatopi jāta iti na sthirapakṣavat kṣaṇikapakṣepi vīkṣaṇādiprasaṅgaḥ bhāvasyaivābhāvāt sthirapakṣe tu sa cāsti tadavasthaśceti na nivartate prasaṅgaḥ padārthāntarotpattāvapi tasyatatrākiñcitkaratvāt  aprastutābhidhānaṃ ca bhāvanivṛttau prastutāyāṃ vastvantarodayavarjanāt na nu bhāvanivṛttau prastutāyāṃ nivṛtterudayopadiśyate iti kimaprastutamatra na tu tāvadetra nivṛttiḥ prasajyātmā yāvannodayopadeśaḥ  udaye tu tatparyudastavastvantaravidhānāt punararthāpattyā nivṛttyākṛṣṭiḥ na tu saiva nivṛtirvastutvādeva anyathātiprasaṅgāt yattu śaṅkaraḥ bhāvādbhāvāntaravadarthāntaratvāviśeṣe kathaṃ sa eva tasyaiva nivṛttiriticet  atra vastusvabhāvairuttaraṃ vācyaṃ yeṣāṃ svahetubhyaḥ kaścidarthāntaratathā anyeṣāmaheturevaṃ svakāryasthāpi mābhūt tādṛgetadapīti etadeva nyāyabhūṣaṇopi tadapi dvividhasthāpi virodhasya ghaṭanādapāstam yadi ca virodhādarthāntarasyāpi nivṛttibhāvo varaṃ mudgarasyaivāstvityapi darśitam  na capratyakṣamanumānaṃ vā nivṛttau pravṛttam  tadvirodhaśca pramāṇasiddhovaśyavaktavya iti sundaram  anyepi ā  vasthiti ā  mātreṇa ā kāriṇeva ā  pekṣa e   va  ra  siddhopasthāyī ra  pratyakṣa  ā  karma a  prasā ra  vartanāt ā  nanvabhāvaa  padeśyate a  nodayāpa a  sahyarthā a  bhāvena ra  sahasthiti a  syādyaghaṭanā tasya  kiñcidbhavati na bhavatyeva kevalam pra vā  iti duratikramo nyāyaḥ yattu nyāyabhūṣaṇaḥ yadi tasya na kiñcid bhavati tataḥ pratiṣedhopi na tasyabhavatītyapratiṣiddhasvarūpastadavasthatvāt prāgivopalabhyeteti prāgeva prarihṛtametat  tathāhi pratiṣedhopi na tasya bhavatīti yadi pratiṣedhākhyopi padārtho notpadyata ityarthaḥtadā satyametat na tu tāvataivāpratiṣiddhasvarūpatvamarthasya svahetutaiva kṣaṇāntare pratiṣiddhatāpratipādanāt a atha vācanikapratiṣedho vivakṣitastadā kastamapahastayati kevalamatra pakṣe prāgivopalabhyetetyasaṃbaddham na yo yadā nāsti sa tadopalabhyaḥ  anyathākānyakubjasthitopi pāṭaliputre dṛśyeta  māndhātāpi vādyopalabhyeta nanvadya māndhāturabhāvastena nopalambhaḥ  ko vai anyathā prāha  kevalaṣaṣṭhīnirdeśādbhedāvasāyepi na tato bhinnaḥ padārtho vidhīyate yāvānevārthī māndhātādya nāstitatkālaniyatasattākatvāt tāvāneva māndhāturadyābhāva iti   na tu samānametadapiyāvānevārtho māndhāturadyābhāva iti tāvāneva māndhātādya nāstīti yadapyucyate  tatkālaniyatasattākatvāditi tatrāpi tatkāla evāstīti kālāntareabhāva eva pratipādyata iti kimatrādhikamabhihitam  uktamevaitat  tathāpyucyatebhedābheda nideśayoreka evārthastattvataḥ kevalaṃ yadi bhinnavastusiddhi pramāṇabalāvalambinītadādya nāstītyasyāpi vākyasyādyābhāvostītyayamevārthaḥ atha bhinnavastubādhaiva pramāṇānvayinī tadābhāvostīti tāvadastu  adyābhāvojāta ityasyāpi vākyasyādya nāstītyevārtho veditavyaḥ  pramāṇānveṣaṇe ca dṛśyatayāsvīkṛtasyādarśanameva bādhakamuktaṃ ca sādhakaṃ ca kiñcinnetyapi  adyānupalambhepiA svopajñavṛttyanusārī pāṭhaḥ  darśanam  na tasyeti nāsti ā  sveti nāsti a  pratiṣiddhateti nāsti ā  nanvasa a  tatkāpyu  ajñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalautatkālavartinaḥ kālāntare vastvantararūpamaspṛśatā virahamātreṇa siddha tvamityupapāditam  na ca virahamātreṇeti karaṇaśaktinirdeśād vastutva pratyāśā vivakṣāparatantratvātkriyākārakavyavahārasyayāti gandharvanagarādeṣa bandhyāsutaḥ padāre mṛgatṛṣṇāmbhasi snātvā pitre dātuṃ jalāñjalim iti  sakalakārakaśaktiyogepi vastutvābhāvāt sarvathā mithyedamiti cet  vivakṣāparatantratāmātreṇa dṛṣṭāntīkṛtatvāt ka evaṃ sādhurabhidadhīteti cet  na kopyabhidhattāṃ prakṛtasiddhevirodhāt  naca sādhorapyetatpāṭhosaṃbhavī sarvathā ki tat sādhurnābhidadhīteti tadaśrutavataḥ praśnetatpāṭhamātreṇa sādhutākṣaterabhāvāt  kūrmaromṇāṃ tu mithyātvaṃ svīkṛtamityapi kimasādhunaiva vaktavyam  nāpi sarvathā mithyaivedam  tathā māndhātā nāstīti nādya sthīyatemāndhātreti vā vyaktā kartṛśaktirna vastutāṃ pratyujjīvayati niṣedha eva tasyā vartata iti cet  ata eva vivakṣāpāratantryamapetasandeham vastvantarotpattireva hi niṣidhyate kālāntareb na ca prasajyapratiṣedhavyavahāramātraṃ pratiṣidhyate  tadasya bādhavidhānapratipādanepi na paramārthasat padārthāntarasiddhiḥ tena yadu vārtikaślokasya nyāyabhūṣaṇaścakāra kāvyamabhāvo yadi paścātra bhāvastasya kimiṣyate sopi na  pratiṣedhoyamabhāvasya kimiṣyate   rūpaspṛśatā ā  suto ya a   rontumi a romnāmi ra  kāraṇa ā padavataraṇa ā  evārthā ā paścādabhāvavyavahārapravartanamātrasyeṣṭhatvādvastutpattereva pratiṣiddhitvāt nanu keyaṃ vācoyuktiḥ abhāvavyavahāramātramiṣyate paścānnābhāva iti  evaṃhi sati visaṃvāditāprasaṅgobhāvavyavahārasya abhāvaśca mithyeti bhāva eva pratiṣedhyasyasyāt pratiṣedhaniṣedhaśca vidhānāt kīdṛśoparaḥ pra vā  iti nyāyasya svayaṃ pratijñānāt  sa cābhāvo bhavan paścādeveti sphuṭataramasyakādācitkatvāt sahetutvaṃ vastutvaṃ ceti  tathā ca saha evāha yasya bhāvasya paścādabhāvasa eva nāśa ityucyate  kathaṃ bhāvasya vināśonyo vā kaścinnopalabhyate  atha bhāvasyavināśa ucyate kiṃ tu sa bhavatīti nocyate bhavatītyabhidhāne ko doṣaḥ  bhāva evasyāditi cet  tatkimidānīmabhidhānādevārthasya rūpaparivarto bhavati  yadi cabhavet tato jāyata ityucyatām  janmāpyabhāvasya kuta iti cet  kādācitkatvāt akādācitkatve tu pratyutpannāvasthāyāmapyabhāvaḥ syāditi atrocyate vyavahāraśabdena tāvadasmākaṃ niścayavacasī abhimate vacanaṃ cavikalpena sahaika viṣayameva  vikalpasya ca grāhyādhyavasāyabhedena dvividho viṣayaḥ tatra yatpratibhāsaṃ vikalpajñānamājāyate tad grāhyamucyate  yadāśraye tu pravṛttinivṛttītadadhyavaseyam yathā paścādabhāvo bhāvasyaiva jāta ityasyaiva vikalpasyārthāntarotpattiḥsākṣānnirbhāsamānā grāhya tadbhāvārthakriyārthino nivṛtterāśrayabhūtā ca tadviviktatatkāladeśasvabhāvavastvavasthādhyavasevā yatastadvikalpodaye vināśākhyavastūtpattiparāmarśavimukhaḥ pratiṣedhyabhāvārthaṃkriyārthī taddeśakālātmani vastuni na pravartate api tunivartate  tatastaddeśakālavastvavasthādhyavaseya ucyate  tatra pratibhāsamānavastvantarāpekṣayāvyavahāramātramucyate yatnena nirūpatayā nayanasahasreṇāpyudīyamānapadārthāntarasyānupalabdheḥ tatastadvisaṃvādepi yatra pravṛttinivṛttibhyāṃ pariniṣṭhitavyāpāro vikalpa saṃpadyatetamadhyavaseyaṃ viṣayamapekṣya na visaṃvādasaṃvādaḥ  adhyavaseye ca saṃvādetaracintā na vācāni a bādhāni ā  cābhavan a  bhāvāt ra  sadaika ā  paścādbhāvosyajāta a  nirbhāsaṃ mano a  nivṛtti a   samvāsa  ājñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaupratibhāsini  tadayamavyāpakopi yadi nyāya prakṛte tāvadavaseyasaṃvādenaiva saṃvāda manuśiṣmaḥ  pratibhāsinī tu visaṃvāda sādhya eva yadi sidhyati prasannāḥ devatāḥkimatrabhavata a kopena tasmādabhāvavikalpapratibhāsinaḥ kāryarūpasya mithyātvepi nābhāvavyavahārasyavisaṃvāditā adhyavasitārthayāthātmyasya sattvāt  tasya ca kalpitarūpasya mithyātvepibhāvavirodhinaḥ pracyutimātrasya vyavahataṃvyaikarūpasya mithyātvamiti na vastuniṣedhebhāvaprasaṅgaḥ tasya tu pracyutimātrasya niṣedhe syāt  na cā sā tena rūpeṇa pracyutimātrātmanā pratiṣidhyate  kiṃ tu vasturūpatayā kalpitayā nanu vastu na bhavatītyayameva pratiṣedhaḥ tathā ca sā pratyutirasti na veti praśneyadyasti kathaṃ na vastu  nāsti cet kathamapratiṣedhaḥ  ucyate vastuvirahamātrasya vastutvāropa eva niṣedhaḥ  na vastutvaniṣedhastanniṣedhaḥ  tataḥ pracyutirastīti na pracyutirūpātpravyavata ityayamevārtha  ghaṭostītyapi hi ghaṭarūpāpracyutimātramāpadyate  natvasti prayogamātreṇa kalpitasthāpi traiguṇyamayatvādevidhiḥ  yathā ca pratiṣiddhaghaṭarūpādatiriktarūpāpekṣaiva nāsti ghaṭo nityatayā kṣaṇikatayā veti sādhu tathā nāstipracyutirityapi vastutvenetyapekṣaiva sādhu  nirupādhistvasti pracyutiriti tatsvarūpāpracyutau na duṣyati  yāvañca na pratiṣedhyabhāvastāvatpracyutiḥ svarūpāpracyutiḥ parasparābhāvarūpatvādanayoḥ  ataevanivṛttiryadi tasminna hetorvṛttiḥ kimiṣyate sāpi na pratiṣedhoyaṃ nivṛttiḥ kiṃ niṣidhyate iti durlaṅgoyaṃ nyāyaḥ  evamabhāvo yadi paścānnaityanena paścādabhāvākhyavirahamāśaya pra vā   bhāvastasya kimiṣyate satini ā  tviti nāsti  matrabhavaḥ a ā  syāttena raā  pracyava i ā   māpādyate ā  vidhe a  ṣiddha  ā mātreti nāsti dabhāvavi akṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetukavināśādhikāraḥityucyate yadi tadā na doṣa    yasya hi yadāstītyasya pratyanīkaṃ nāstīti virahamātrama vasturūpaṃ kalpanā viparivarti pratiṣidhyate tasya tadā niyamenāstītyevaṃ rūpamantarmātrāyāmupasthānamāsādayati  yadā tu paścādvirahamātramapratikṣipya paścād bhavati jāyateceti vikalpavivartavaśād vāsanāvaśagādvasturūpasya kalpitasya niṣedhaḥ tadā kathaṃvirahamātrapratikṣepaprabhavo bhāvaprasaṅgaḥ yatobhāvastasya kimiṣyateityucyate  na hi ghaṭaḥ kalpitarūpaniṣedhe svarūpāta pracyavamāsādayati udakadhāraṇādyartha kriyāvirahaprasaṅgāt  na ca pracyute svarūpollekho vastutvapratyāśāyā pūrakaḥasatsvabhāvo bandhyāsuta ityādivat svabhāvāvasthānaniveśanepi tadayogāt asiddho heturityādivad vā tasmāt nāśaḥ paścād bhavati jāyate mudgarādibhya iti bālavyavahāramātramapalapyate  tatu pratibhāṣitaṃ tu kādācitkatvādi vasturūpaṃ nāstīti brūmaḥ na ca vastu yāvad vyavahāropasthāpitaṃ tatsarvaṃ vastutattvamiti śakyamśāstrapraṇayanānarthakyaprasaṅgāt  vyavahāraṃ tu vitathamupadarśayannapi mūlabalābalābhyāṃkaścidupādeyo heyaśca etadbhāveyamasyabhedaḥ tadabhāve cātra nāsti svayaṃ cānena rūpeṇa bhidyamāno nānyamapekṣata iti  tatkathaṃ pradīpena sāmyam  kiṃ capradīpavaccedayamapyabhāvobhinatti bhāvaṃ ca vibhidyate ca sa eva vibhāgaḥ agṛhītamapi kila vilocanaṃ grāhayati rūpamiti tadviśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇamagṛhītamapiviśeṣaṇaṃ grāhayatīti manyamānasya prathamamapi viśeṣaṇamagṛhītameva grāhayiṣyativiśeṣyamiti kṛtaṃ tadgrahaṇenāpi saṅkīrṇagrahaṇabhītiḥ tathā sopyupādhirasaṅkīrṇogṛhyamāṇaḥ kathaṃ parabhedako nāma svayaṃ viṣṭambhidravyavat  evaṃparamparāpekṣāyāṃ vyāvṛttavastunaḥ kalperapi grahaṇābhāvādastamayo durvāraḥ yadi ca viśeṣaṇamabhāvaḥ tadā svahetoreva bhinnabhāvasaṃbhave bhinnadarśana vikalpanayorarthāpattyā siddheḥ kimabhāvena  na hi bhinnamabhinna manubhavitavyamabhrāntapratyayena anāpi bhinnamanubhūtaṃ yaccāha  athavā nirvikalpakajñānena vyāvṛttivyāvṛttyānantyamapi gṛhītamititatrāpi yattāvad a  viśeṣaṇa iti nāsti ā  viṇānāmapi a  satyantu a  stanāteḥa  viśeṣaṇa iti nāsti ā  viśeṣaṃ grāhamiṣyatīti ā vyāvṛttivyatiriktena rūpeṇa vyāvṛtti vineti na yuktam vyāvṛttenityadharmatvāt  yo hi dharma kadācid bhavatitena dharmeṇa vināpi dharmī vyapadiśyate yathā kuṇḍalena vinā puruṣokuṇḍalī nāśātprāganaṣṭa iti  na ca vastvantarād vyāvṛttivihīnaṃ vastu kadācit yathā na gotvavihīnosti gauḥ nauṣṇyavihīnogniḥ atha vyāvṛttivyatiriktena rūpeṇa vyāvṛttamityabhipretam  tadiṣṭamevāsmākambhedābhyupagamāt  na caivaṃ vyāvṛttiranathikā  yadi vyatiriktena dhanena dhanī puruṣaḥkimetāvatā dhanaṃ vyarthaṃ bhavet  tasmāditaretarābhāvopi bhāvādarthāntarameveti tadapividhūtam  yasmāt na khalu vastusatīṃ tadvidhūyasiddhāntamātrakathayā kimatra na ca vināśāt prāganaṣṭa ityudāhatuṃ yuktam vināśasya bhedāsiddheḥ  na vyāvṛttivihīnaṃ vastvityapi vyāvṛttestāttvikābhede siddhasādhanam bhedāsiddhiḥ svakālaniyatastu sa nānyadāsti  vyāvṛttamupra a   tyasamarthā ra  kathyate ā  kiṅkonasaṃhṛtaṃ ā   sthānavasaraḥ ā vyāvṛtte tā ā  siddha sādhanaṃ a  bhede asi ā  svarūpeṇe ā  dhvanivad vāā  tadanya ā prasajyaparyudāsayorbhedasādhanārthamabhāvabhāvavyavahāraviṣayatvena vibhāgapratyapīpadat tad bhavato bhāṣaiva bhāvānyatetyatrāntare tiraskṛtam  na hi nyāyasiddhasyasamayamātreṇa bādhanaṃ sādhu  tathā hiyajjāyamānamupalakṣitamarthakāribhāvātmanā vyavaharanti tadeva santaḥ soyaṃ na yaḥ samayato yadi bhaṅgabhāgībhāvānavasthitiriyaṃ na ca paryudāsaḥ yadā hi mūrtāmūrtasapratighāpratighasanidarśanānidarśanadū rāsanna sthūlasūkṣmādiprakāreṣukaścid bhāvamabhāvaṃ vā kaścit svecchāvaśādabhidadhīta  vindhyavandhyāsutādikamabhāvabhāvaṃ vā tadāyātamavyavasthānaṃ bhāvasya  na caivaṃ kṣatiḥ  svasamayānurodhātabhidhānabhedasaṃbhavāt  b kevalaṃ kimidānīṃ paryudastaṃ vastu vyavahriyatām tasmāt samayānurodhādabhāvaśabdāpravṛttāvapi ekasya kāraṇāpekṣasaṃbhavasyopālambhabhājovā anyastādṛgeva padārtha paryudasto vaktavya  tatkathamabhāvaśabdasaṅkatamātreṇaparyudāsavyudāsaḥ  yadi punarupalambhasaṃbhavāvapyabhāvābhimatasya samayamātratantrāvityucyatetadā vāstavaḥ prasajyapratiṣedha evāyaṃ na paryudāsa iti na doṣaḥ  anena tu nyāyavinmāninānyāyāgataṃ tameva prakāramullaṅghaya saṃbhavopalambhārthakriyāśaktayaścābhāvasya bhāvikyaabhyupagantavyāḥ  paryudāsapratyanīka prasajyapratiṣedhatā ceti kimatopi vyasanamanavasānamanyat  yaccāyamāha na hyutpattirbhāvasya lakṣaṇaṃ yena nivṛttirbhavantī bhāvaḥ syādanutpattimatāmaṇyākāśādīnāṃ  bhāvatvāditi  tatrāpipāṇinena nadī gaṅgā yamunā ca sthalī nadī abhavannapi bhāvosya na bhāvosya bhavannapi  dityapi a  prajya ā  bhaṅgabhaṅga a   mapratiṣṭhāpratigha ā  kañcitkañcita a kaścitkaścit a mabhāvamabhāvamvā a  paryudasto vaktavyaḥ iti nāsti ra  pālambhaa  mattā ra  prāṇi a rakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetukavināśādhikāranaraḥ svātantryamāpanno yadicchati karoti tat ubhayatra samānoyaṃ nyāyo nyāyavidāṃ mataḥ nadīsaṃjñāniṣedhepi nāvagāhasya bādhanam   bhāvasaṃjñāniṣedhepi paryudāso na bādhyate upalambhārthaśaktasya kāraṇāpekṣajanmanaḥ sarvasya paryudastatvaṃ vastvantaramapekṣya hi abhāvasaṃjñāvirahe paryudāsavyavasthitiḥ na kāpi sidhyet sarvatra saṃjñāyā  sulabhatvataḥ yaccedaṃ svarūpanivṛttilakṣaṇā cotpattiḥ pradhvaṃsasyeṣyate na tu prāgasataḥ sattāsaṃbandhalakṣaṇā kāraṇasamavāyalakṣaṇā veti tatrāpisvarūpasyaiva nirvṛttiḥ sarvatrotpattirucyate prakṣipya samavāyaṃ tu vimūḍhaiḥ sāpi hāritā samavāyasyaivābhāvāt ka sattāsaṃbandhādiḥ  astu vā sopitathāpyapūrvātmalāevotpatti dharmādharmāntarāṇāṃ tu bhāvābhāvau na sādhakabādhako  kiṃ ca kāryasyāpyabhāvasya na prāgasataḥ sattāsaṃbandha iti korthaḥ  kiṃ prāgasanneva na bhavati  athapaścādapi na sattvamasya  ubhayathāpi kutaḥ kāryatvamākāśākāśa kuśeśayavat  prāgasataḥsattvamastu paścānna tu sattāyogaḥ nanu sattvaṃ sattetyanarthāntarametat  yogaśca sambandhaḥ  tatra sattvayogosti nasattāyoga iti kopyayaṃ nyāya  atha sattā mahāsāmānyamucyate tadabhāvepisvarūpasattvamātreṇa paścāt sannityucyata iti cet  tattarhi svarūpasattvaṃ yadi tāttvikamtāvataiva kāryatvaṃ kimapareṇa kartavyamanyasyāpi kāryasya  athaupacārikam tadānāśasyāpi kutaḥ kāryatā  na hi bandhyātanayasya paścādbhāvopacāre kāryatā vāstavīnāma  abhāva ā  saṃjñayāḥ ā  nivṛttilaṃkṣaṇā ā  prakṣepya a  dharmā iti nāstia  sādhakāsā a  nakāro nāsti ā  mākāśākuśe ājñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalauyaccedaṃ nivṛtterapyādimattvamityucyata iti tadāpi nādhikaṃ kiñcit  sā ca nivṛttira bhāvarūpeṇaiva b ādimatīti punarna sahāmahe kāryāntarasādhāraṇatāyā pratipādanāt  ādeśamātrametat bhūbhujāmeva śobhate  bhāvopalambhakāle tadrūpānupalambhādityapi paścādrūpopalambhe śobhāmābhajati  sa ca nāsti kumbhāsaṃbhavavikalpamātraṃ tu saṅke tānurodheneti darśitam arthī paṭārthakriyayā ghaṭasyānupalambhane na prāvataṃta ityasti nānyadṛk pratiyoginaḥ tadalamasya prakriyāmātramavakaraṃ nirūpya svayamūhyadoṣatvāt yaccāha nāpyarthaṃkriyāhetutvamātreṇa bhāvatvaprasaktiḥ tvaduktabhāvalakṣaṇānabhyupagamāditi tatrāpi paryudāsatvānatikramādityuktam  tasmānna bhāvādarthāntaramabhāvaḥ yatpunarāha tvayāpi bhāvābhāvayolaṃkṣaṇabhedobhihitaḥ  tat kathamekatvam sarvārthānāṃ lakṣaṇabhedādeva bhedavyavasthā tatopi cenna bhedavyavasthitirna kasyacitkutaścid bhedasiddhirityadvaitaprasaṅga iti  tadapyaparyālocanaphalam  yo hi naśvarasvabhāvaeva nāśo nāśyatīti bahulādhikārāt kartari ghan taddharmatākalpanayā vā tadvācakenābhidhānāt  tannāśaṃ bhāvasvabhāvamicchāmaḥ  tamevāśrityasattāmātrānubandhitvānnāśasyānityatādhvaneḥpra vā  ityuktam tathā cānenaivotthāpitam bhāva eva kṣaṇasthitidharmā nāśa iti tasyābhedamevabrūmaḥ  naśanaṃ nāśa iti prasajyātmā dvidhā vyākartavyaḥ tattvatastāvad vastutvavirahāttattvānyatvaśūnya evāsau bhāvo na bhavatīti tadbhāvaniṣedhamātrapātraṃ tu kharaśṛṅgādivat saṃvṛttau tu yathā kālabhedena vikalpyamānaḥ kādācitka iti pratibhāti tathāsarvopākhyāviraharūpatayā bhāvādbhinna iva pratibhātīti nāvastutvepi lakṣaṇa  mityukta ā  bhāvasvarūpe a   matībhirnapuna ā  vāle ā  pā sū    tadavācake ā  svarūpa a   nāśasyā  sāraśṛṅgā ā  saṃvṛto yathā ā ivābhāti ā  sarvopakṣo ra  kṣaṇabhede ākṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetuka vināśādhikārabhedākhyānavirodhaḥ  evaṃ ca sati saṃvṛttyā lakṣaṇabhede bhāvābhāvayorbhedasyeṣṭatvāt tattvena ca lakṣaṇaikatāvirahe bhāvasya tenaikyaniṣedhāt kathamadvaitaprasaṅgopālambhaḥ  naśyatītitu nāśo naśvarasvabhāvaḥ kathaṃ bhāvātmatāṃ pariharet  sa ca sahetuko bhāvahetunaiva na tuparastasya heturbhāvasvabhāvatvāt  tadayaṃ yatbhāve hyeṣa vikalpaḥ syād vidhervastvanurodhataḥ pra vā  ityata āha tadapi svavacanavirodhādayuktam  tvayā hi bhāvābhāvayostādātmyamuktamtacca tattvānabhyupagame virudhyate  tattvābhyupagamepi lakṣaṇabhedo virudhyate  yasya hilakṣaṇabhedena bheda ucyate tasya kathaṃ tattvātattva nirvacanīyatvamiti  tatsukhaidhita krīḍanaśīlatayā kṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ punaḥ kārayati  na khalu bhāvapracyutisvabhāvenābhāvenabhāvasya tādātmyaṃ brūmaḥ  yastu na bhavatītyabhāva  uttarakṣaṇāpekṣayā tena kastādātmya virodha iti nāśavimarśena gatametat  a evamanyadapyanadhikamavadhīritamasyaveditavyam yadapyāh nanvabhāvasya sarvadharmavivekalakṣaṇatvādutpattirna yuktā  sāhi bhāvadharma eveti na jñeyatvāderbhāvadharmasyābhāvepi sadbhāvādityādi tadapyasāram  na hi sādhāraṇadharmaṃyogamātreṇa virodhapratiniyatānāmapi dharmāṇāmavakāśaḥhutāśanasyāpi śaityaprasaṅgāt abhāvasyaiva vā sarvatra sadbhāvaprasaṅgāt jñeyatvādīnāmapiniṣedhāt  utpattiścābhūtvā bhavanarūpatayā bhāvadharma evetyāpāditameva yattu svayaṃ na bhavatīti kortha  kiṃ svayamevāyamabhāvaḥ  kiṃ vā svayamabhavanaṃkaroti  uta bhavanaṃ  na karoti  atha kiñcinna karoti  svayaṃ vā na kiñcit  kiṃvā svayamabhāvībhavatīti ra vikalpya dūṣaṇamārabdham tadapi mamaṃcchedikājanitārtaravaprāyam tatra hi svayamiti hetvantaramanapekṣya svahetunā kṣaṇaniyatasthitirjanita itikṣaṇāntareṇa na kiñciditi prakaṭita evārtha  tatotatsvabhāvaḥ paścādasau kuto śyatī tu ā  naśvaraḥ a  tvayā tādātmyamuktamiti prāntayojanā a  sukhoditaḥ ra bhāva iti nāsti ā  svabhāvo ā  uttama ā  nanu a  yuktaṃ ā  sahiā  apīti nāsti ā  udbhavanaṃ ā  vikalpadūṣaṇa ā  ntare ājñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaujātaḥ  svahetorhi tatsvabhāvotatsvabhāvād vyāvṛtta utpannaḥ  sa kathaṃ paścāṃdapyatatsvabhāvaḥsyāt  na hi laghusvabhāvād vyāvṛttaḥ pāṣāṇaḥ kadācillaghu syāditi  tadapi plaeva  yathā hi deśāntarasthitivyāvṛtta utpannaḥ tathā kṣaṇāntarasthitivyāvṛttopi kathaṃkṣaṇāntarasthiteravakāśa ityuktaprāyam nanvasaditi na tadeva vastvabhidhīyate vidhiviṣayatvāt anyaccābhāvaśabdābhidheyaṃ pratītigocarāpannaṃ tvayā neṣṭam tato nirviṣayaḥ pratiṣedho visaṃvādītyapratiṣiddhaṃvastu syāt  naivam pracyuterapi pratipādyatvāt kuto nirviṣayatvam  nāpi visaṃvādaḥbhāvasthitau hi pratiṣedhasya visaṃvādaḥ syāt  sa ca nāsti pracyuteḥ pratipāditatvāt na cāvastunaḥ saṅkalpaviṣayatāyā apyanupapattirityuktameva yatpunararthāntaraviṣayopi pratiṣedhaḥ kathaṃ vastupratiṣedhaka iti cet  tadabhāvābhidhāyī kathaṃ na pratiṣedhaka ityuktam tadapi pratyuktaprāyam  tadabhāvo hi na prasajyātmakorthāntarasvīkārāt paryudāsamātratve tu nārthāntaranivṛttiravaśyamarthāntarabhāvena vibhāvitābhavati  virodhastu nāstīti pratipāditam  satyapi vā virodhe   kiṃ viruddhadvārāśrayaṇena sākṣādevābhāvapratipādanamastu syādetat vacasābhāvapratipādane kṛte saṃśayāvakāśaḥ viruddhadvāreṇa tu niścayaityasat  viruddhapratipādanamapi hi vacasaiva vartate  tad yathā vacanamātrapratipādye hutabhujineha śītamityeva sādhu na tu nātra śītaṃ variti tadvadetadapi athānyaccintyateatrottaraṃnālaṃ niṣedhavidhaye b yadi paryudastamanyopalabdhiritarasya kathaṃ niṣeddhī naṣṭo ghaṭaḥ sa iti vā bhavato vikalpākāraḥ kathaṃ ghaṭaniṣedhanamādadhāti nehāstyasāviti vikalpamabhiprasūteranyo niṣedhavidhiranyadhiyo na tāvat pūrvavat ā  anyathā ā  prastuterapi ā   viṣayepi a   dabhāvobhi ā kiruddhatvārā ā   ritasya a   viti iti nāsti a  na bhavet ākṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetuka vināśādhikāraḥnābhāvakalpanadhiyopyaviśaṅkitāyāmānāṅgabhāvamavadhūya niṣedhakatvam sato vināśanaṃ nāma nopapannamitīritam nāsata   karaṇe śaktiraniṣṭā vastunaḥ sataḥ tataḥ  pratiyogyanubhavaḥ pratiyogyantaraviraha vikalpamutpādayediti nehānupapattiḥ na ca tanmātrādanyopyanubhavasya pariniṣedhanavyāpāraḥ  yasyāpi vikalpasya naṣṭo ghaṭaityevamākārasya vā niḥśaṅkagamanādau tadarthakriyānvitatayā pravṛttivyāvṛtyavasthāyāṃvā nimittabhāvānnānyaniṣedhakāritvam  evaṃ vacanasyāpi tadvikalpotpādanadvārakamevaniṣedhasādhanatvaṃ draṣṭavyam etena atha nāstīti jñānamevānupalambhaḥ tadapi vastusat kathaṃ vastvantarapratiṣedhasyaviṣayaḥ syādityādyavakaraparihāra siddhaḥ naca nāstīti jñānamanupalambhosmākaṃ ki tu pratiyogyupalambhonirvikalpa eva nāstoti jñānaṃ tu manovyavahārarūpaṃ tat phalameva  kiṃ caivaṃvidhanirbaṃndhena vastucintāyāmanupayogāt   yadapyasya nāstīti jñānaviṣayanirūpaṇamtadapyasaditi nirūpaṇena gatārtham  yattu  tadviviktabhūtalādeviṣayatvamāśaṅkayoktam nabhūtalādervastvantaratvāt na ca vastvantare pratipādite pratīte vādyaghaṭādivastvantaramabhūtamiti pratipāditaṃ pratītaṃ vā bhavati  evaṃ hi vastvantaraṃ hi nāśa ityetasminmate yadūṣaṇamuktaṃ tattu svayameva parihṛtaṃ syāditi  tadapyasaṃbaddham kevalaṃ hi bhūtalamasyaviṣaya iti kathaṃ na ghaṭāderabhūtatvabodhaḥ yaiva hi ghaṭādyapekṣayā kaivalyāvasthā pradeśasyasa eva ghaṭavirahaḥ  vacanādināpyevaṃ kevalaṃ pradeśapratipādane kathamiva na prakṛtaghaṭādyapekṣya bhāvapratipādanam  evaṃ yadi karpūrādivat kevalasya nāśasyāpyupalambhaḥsyāt bhavatu ghaṭo niṣedhapratītiḥ ghaṭaniṣedhastu kena kṛtaḥ  pūrvaṃ sanneva hi ghaṭābhāvaḥtaddvāreṇa pratipattavyaḥ na hi pradeśena ghaṭābhāvo janyante kiṃ tu sanneva ghaṭābhāvatadvāreṇa niścetavyaḥ yadi hi ghaṭopi na syānna pradeśakarūpaniyatā pratītiriti  evaṃ kalpā ā   śakacayānā a nādbhṛtabhāva ā  sattā a  nāśataḥ a  tatā  sakārasya ā  thitayā ā  vyāvṛttā ā  bhāvānya a  vacanamapi vastvantarapra a  pratīte vādyaā  mānā ā  yadya ā   vibhakta ānāsti ā  ntara iti nāsti ā  dyupekṣayā a  kai vasthā ā  kevala mitiyojitam a  paṭādyabhāva ā  karpūrṇa rādivat a karparavat ā  hṛtaḥ a  nakāro nāsti ajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauṃyathā yadi ghaṭodyāpi syānna karpūraikarūpaniyatā pratipattistathā na nāraukarūpaniyatāpratipattiriti balād ghaṭābhāvaniścayo bhavatu yadi pūrvaṃ ghaṭābhāvaḥ syāt saca nāsti tadbhāvepi ki nāśena kapālenaiva pratiyogitā gatārthatvāt  na ca  nāśapratītirapyastītyuktam tasmāt sata a pradhvaṃsane sadrūpeṇāsadrūpeṇa vā dūṣaṇamuktaṃ kathaṃsadrūpeṇa satosato vā niścaye kartavye syāditi na samānaḥ parihāraḥ yattvāha na ca tadvivekāpratītau tadviviktagrahaṇaṃ bhavati  tadvivekaśca na bhūtalādisvarūpameva viśeṣaṇatvāditi tat nyāyabahiṣkṛtam  viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvopi saṅkalpārūḍhe rūpe  sacabhinnaṃ bhāvamabhinnamākalayati vyaktaṃ tadanyātmanājiṣṇu sphārakadambaḍambaramiva svāṃśairanaṃśa jagat ki ca svākṛtimātra eva ra viṣayavyāmohadohakṣamaḥsaṅkalpaḥ paramaindrajālika iva dhūbhūtasthitiḥ yathā hi bhinnaṃ bhāvamekīkurvannutpadyate tathābhinnaṃ bhāva bhinnamākalayatītyapyarthaḥ yathāśilāputrakasya śarīram śarīre karacaraṇādayaḥ lambakarṇo devadatta ityādi  tasmātkalpanādhīno viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇabhāvobhinnopi bhāve bhedavivakṣāpekṣavyavahāraḥ kathaṃbhedaniyatamātmānamātanoti  skhaladgatirayaṃ rāhoḥ śira ityādinirdeśa iti cetu yadi satyametattadā bhinnasya sākṣādanupalambhādeva  iyaṃ ca gatirghaṭavivekākhyapadārthāntarāpekṣayāpyasti tathāpi neti koṣapānaṃ pramāṇam  tasmāt sa ghaṭābhapradeśa evaayamanyo ghaṭavivikto na tu ghaṭavivekena bhintena viśeṣita iti tasmād yadyapi kiñcid viśeṣaṇaṃ bhinnameva dṛṣṭaṃ vāhādi tathāpi nāyaṃ niyamaḥviparyayasyāpi darśanāt saṃbhāvanācca bādhakādarśanāt  vivakṣāparatantratā tu dṛṣṭāntasaṃbhāvanābījam  tadevaṃ na vācyaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyādarthāntaratvād vāhādivaditi ki cavyāptaṃ bhidā yadi viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇatvaṃbhedātyayānnanu tadā tadabhāva eva  ghaṭādyapi a  nāśayatīti ā  niścayāya ā   pratīto ā  dāha ra  bhūta iti nāsti ā   mākramati ā  śarīrakara a   niyamā ā  ghaṭāt a  dṛṣṭānta iti nāsti ā  tyāyā āśaireśaṃ ā pekṣya ākṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetuka vināśādhikāradeśo viśiṣṭa iti nāsti yathā tathedamapyasti dṛśyamatabhedadgasti neti na ca dṛśyānupalabdheḥ pramāṇātmano viśiṣṭavyavahāramātreṇa sa ghaṭādanya ityarthaniṣṭhenabādha kiṃ tu tathaivāsyeti yaccāha abhedepi na pramāṇaṃ kiñcidastīti tadanunmīlitākṣasyaiva sāmpratamanyathā pratyakṣodayasya nivārayitumaśakyatvāt kimiha kalasadhvaṃso dṛśyo na vetyudito janovadatu samayasmṛtyā dṛṣṭi vimarśaparāṅamukhaḥ kalayasi punaḥ kāṃskānarthāniheti para yadipradiśati dharādibhyaḥ sabhyastvameva vayaṃ na tu yaccedam yadi ca ghaṭo nāstītyasya saṃjñānasyābhidhānasya ca bhūtalameva viṣayona ca tatonyo ghaṭābhāvaḥ tadātra ghaṭostītyasyāpi bhūtalameva viṣaya syāt  ghaṭopina tatonyaḥ kalpanīyaḥ tathotpādena viśiṣṭaṃ bhūtalamevobhayatrāpyastu  na caitadyuktam yasmād ghaṭasadbhāvavaddhaṭāsadbhāvepi bhūtalatonyaḥ pratibhāti evaṃ hi vidhipratiṣedhayoḥprayogopyarthavāneva bhavediti tadvaraṃ januṣāndho na punarayaṃ durnītidagdhabuddhiḥ  abhāvavat kila kalasopi kalpanāmātra viṣayoṃ na locanagocara iti kimatra brūma  sakumbhamudbhūtaṃ bhūtalam b ityapi sahitotpattirāpadyate na rūpasaṅkaraḥ bhedopalambhasyabhinnārthakriyāniyogasya catvāt  tadvannābhāvopi bhūtalakapālādibhyobhinna pratibhātīti cintitameva  kiṃ catato vidhipratiṣedhaprayogayorapi kānupapattiḥ avasthādvayapratipādanāt  tathā cajālāntareṇa praviṣṭālokasyābhāvo bhinnadeśo bhāsamāna kimapotuṃ śakyaḥ  kevalamvicchinnaḥ sphuṭanīlakāntikalita tāvatpradeśasthiti bhinnārthatvaviniścayāttu sa iti prakhyātināmāntaraḥ neti dṛśyasat ra  miṣṭena ā  kintvanayevā ā  tārthasyai a  jñāna ā nāsti ā  sadbhāvavad ghaṭā iti yojitam a   va bha nāsti ā  durṇīti ā śaṅkaraḥ ā  kriyādi ā  cakāro nāsti ā  vimarṣa a   niheparaṃ ā tathāta ā  prakhyāta ājñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalīālokasya yathā tathānyavirahopyātmasvarūpasphuṭīkāre kiṃ kalasaḥ kimātapabhidādhyakṣeti citraṃ mahat na hi sūkṣmamīkṣamāṇepyatyanta vicitrasya bhāvarāśerabhāvānāṃ saṃbandhibhedādbhedopacāramantareṇa sūkṣmopi svabhāvabhedastama ivopalambhagocaraḥ  tavaramālokavivekopi sakalānyavivekavadanālokya evāstu  tamastu vastveveti gṛhāṇa  kimaṅgakaṣṭasaṃkaṭe sukhinamātmānamāveśayasi nanu nimīlitākṣasyāpi tādṛṅa nīlapratibhāsaḥ saṃbhavī na ca nīlamarthamupasthāpayatīti  tadayuktam kṛṣṇavarṇāntarasya sarvasyāpyabhāvaprasaṅgāt  anyādṛśametatkṛṣṇāntaraṃ kalayāpi nimīlitākṣapratibhāsāditi cet  andhakāropi tarhi punaḥparimitadeśo vicitrasaṃsthāna pratibhāsamānaḥ sphuṭataraṃ nimīlitākṣapratibhāsādbhinna rūpaevānubhūyate ekarasaśca nimīlitākṣapratibhāsaḥ andhakārastu kadācit kiraṇaparamāṇunikarasaṅa karakāle viralarūpaḥ anyadā ghano ghanataro veti kathaṃ sāmyam  kṛṣṇatāmātraṃpunaranyatrāpi sādhāraṇam anyatra nīlavarṇe vastuni sparśāntarasahacāra avaśyambhāvīti cet  naindranolādimaṇikiraṇajālake tadabhāvāt   anupalakṣyastatra sparśa iti kalpanaṃnāndhakārādvibheti  tasmādrupamātramubhayamastu  na hi dṛṣṭenupapannaṃ nāma  yadicāśrayovaśyamugya  maṇikuḍyādikamastyeva  na ca vastuvyavasthāyāṃ pratyakṣapratibhāsamāśrayata  pratibhāsaviplavena vyabhicārābhidhānaṃ dhīmato dhinoti  anyathā vātapittakṣobhādinā jvalitastambhādisaṃdarśanāt satyamapi jvalitastambhādikamasatyaṃ syāt prakṛtipratyāpattau tu yathā tatpratibhāsābhāvaḥ tathā nayanonmīlanakāle nīlābhāvaviplavasthāpi  andhakārādarśanaṃ tu svasthāvasthāpekṣameva yathopavarṇitaviśeṣam  tatpratibhāsasya ca pratyakṣa saṃbhavasāmagrīvidha ṭa ne vighaṭanaṃ guṇa eva nāparādhaḥ pratyakṣasvabhāvatāyā iṣṭatvāt  mātape ā  vipadakṣeti a  sa  su   sūkṣma a  māṇopyante a   lokavāstuā   śayati a  dṛśaśīla ā  kalāyāpi ā  tahīti nāsti a  varṇaā  caro ā  jātake a   labhya    a  nārthakarotarṣiteti ā  ca ayovaśyamṛtaḥ ā vāśrayo a  bhāsanā a  ghīnoti a  darśanāt ā  kāra a vighane vighaṭanaṃ ākṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetukavināśādhikāraa  yatpunaruktam kṛṣṇarūpasyālokena vinā grahītumaśakyatvāditi  nanupītāvadātādayopi nālokanirapekṣavīkṣaṇā iti pradīpacandrātapādayopi   prakāśāntaramapekṣeran  vicitrāstu bhāvaprakṛtayaḥ pramāṇasamadhigatā na paryaṃnuyogamarhanti yaccālokavat tadabhāvasyāpi grahaṇe cakṣurālokāntaranirapekṣamācakṣāte śaṅkaranyāyabhūṣaṇo tadapi na kiñcit  niścāyakaṃ hi cakṣurvijñānamabhāvasya na grāhakamavastutvāt ālokāntarānapekṣamiti tu siddhameva  na caitat vācyam  yo hi bhāvoyāvatyā sāmagrayā gṛhyate tadabhāvopi tāvatyaivetyālokagrahaṇasāmagrathā gṛhyamāṇaṃtamastadabhāva evetieveti tamograhaṇasāmagrathā gṛhyamāṇasyālokasyaiva tadabhāvatāprasaṅgenānaikāntikatvāt  ghaṭapaṭayorvā samānagrahaṇasāmagrīkatayā paramparābhāvatvaprasaṅgaḥ tasmāt padārthāntare  rūpavivekena pratibhāsamānamadhyakṣe andhakāramālokavirodhi vastveva  virodhitve  tarhi kadācidālokamapyandhakāra  paribhavediti nacodyam adyāpi prakṛtivādasyopasthāpanāt tūlānalādivat etena tamasa evaṃ pratiyogivastuna upalabdhirabhāvaṃ sahasā vyavahārayituṃ prabhavati tamasyālokanivṛttāvapīti siddhe yathehālokasyābhāvopalabdhistathā sarvatreti śaṅkarādīnāṃ pratyāśāpratyādeśo veditavyaḥ  anupalabdhiniṣṭhāyāṃ tu jñānākārepi pratiyoginyabhāvasiddhirśitā  na ca kaścid doṣa ityāstāṃ tāvat  tasmānnābhāvo nāma kiñcidyatra kāraṇavyāpāra iti sthitam etena trilocanopi nirastaḥ yadāha  bhāvasya vyatirikta nivṛttimanicchadbhiraśakyā  svarūpanivṛttiravasthāpayitum yā hi tasya prāktanī kācidavasthā bhavadbhirarthakriyānirvartanayogyā dṛṣṭā seva yadyuttarakālamapyanuvarteta tarhi svarūpeṇaiva nivṛttaubhāvaḥ kathamavasthāpyeta  tadānīmayaṃ naṣṭo bhāvo  na sapadi svahetupratilabdhasvarūpātirekiṇī tasya kācidavasthotpadyeta  gṛhītu ā  vīkṣaṇāt a  candropādayopi ā   cakṣate ā  pekṣya a māṇasyaivālo a  parasparatvā a  padārthāntararūpa a  mityadhyakṣa ra  virodhea  sthānāt a  mahatsādhya    a  vivṛttāva ā   chāyajjñānā ā  ktāvyaniā  raśakyasva ā   nivartana ā  vartate ā  nivṛtto bhāva a  mupasthāpyate ra naṣṭo nāma yadi ajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauutpattau saiva tasyātmāntaraṃ jātamityatāvasthyas   atādavasthyamevāsya vināśaṃbrūmaḥ  tādavasthye tādātmyameva svarūpeṇa nivṛtto bhāva ityasya śabdasya satyamarthaṃ navidmaḥ  svarūpanivṛttiḥ khalviyaṃ bhavantī bhāva eva syāt bhāvādanyā vā  tattvesvakāraṇebhyo niṣpannasyānyathānutpattāvṛttapatterārabhya sattvānnityatvaṃ prasajyate anyathātveca tadeva nivṛtteranyatvamiti priyamanuṣṭhitaṃ priyeṇa  tasmādutsṛjya vibhramaṃ nāśotpattirevanaṣṭatvamabhyupagantavyam tat kimucyate naṣṭasyādarśanam na ca tasya kiñcid bhavatīti  adarśanaṃ naṣṭasyapunarabhāvadarśanameva  ātmahānamabhāvotpattimeva vayamaṅgīkurmaṃ iti sarvamanavadyam akṣaṇikāḥ santaḥ kāraṇavattvāt  yatkāraṇavattadakṣaṇikam yathā bhāvavināśaḥ  kāraṇavantaśceme santaḥ  tasmādakṣaṇikā iti  kāraṇavattvasya bsādhyaviṣayaye vṛttiśaṅkā vināśa hetumattvameva nivartayatīti  prasiddhavyāptikātkāraṇavattvādakṣaṇikatvasiddhiriti vyatiriktanivṛttimantareṇāpi svarūpanivṛtterupapāditattvāt tataśca kṣaṇādūrdhvaṃ kutaḥ prāktanaśaktāvasthāsthitiḥ  vyatiriktotpādepi kathaṃ naṣṭo nāma atādavasthyamatādātmyaṃ ca jātamityasyātyakṣarasya svahetorevāvasthāsvabhāvāntaravirahitoyaṃjāta ityevārtha uktaḥ  tanmūlaka atādavasthyā divyavahāra eva paścādbhāvī natadvikalpapratibhāsi bhāvāntara miti na tattvānyavavikalpāvakāśaḥ  tasmādutsṛjya vibhramaṃ naṣṭavyavahārostu na tu tasyānyat kiñcit jāyata iti  adarśanaṃ cābhāvadarśana mevetisaṃpratyeva pratyākhyātamiti sarvamanavadyam xtasmāt prasajyātmanobhāvasya nāśākhyasya hetureva na kaścit  vinaśvarasvabhāvetu hetvantaraśaktimapākṛtya svahetoreva sāmarthyasamarthanād jātamātrameva vinaśyatīti nakṣaṇāntaramanvetīti siddheḥ  kāraṇavattvasyākṣaṇikatvena vyāptyasiddheranekāntaḥ kṛtakānāmavaśyamantepi nāśābhyupagame ca virodhaḥ  pramāṇagocarasya pakṣīkaraṇe pratijñāyāanumānabādhā  agocare cāśrayasvarūpayorasiddhiriti sthitam yat punarayaṃ bhagavato bhāṣyakārasya pratyakṣataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhimanavagāhamānaḥ anurūpavikalpābhāvodbhāvanamātrasāreṇa vistareṇa dūṣaṇamabhilaṣannapabhāṣaṇapramādamācarati tāvadava ā  tādātmye vā a  bhāvādanya vā ā  tatvebhyalaṇaṇebhyo ātathetyalakṣaṇebhyo ra  ranyartha ā   hānima a  vṛtti śaṅkāṃ ā   sattva ā pratisiddha ā  tpāde tu a  hāraya a  tāvā a  sṛṣṭa a  jāyateti ā kiñcit ā  siddha iti nāsti a  mantevi atadasya caṭulavaṭubhāvasulabhamanātmajñatāviṣkaraṇamātramiti mantavyam  tathā hi pratyakṣasiddhaṃ kṣaṇikatvamiti na pratyakṣavyavahṛtam anurūpavikalpānudayāt  kiṃ tu pratyakṣagṛhītam vyavahāratvānumānāt  taccānumānaṃ yadi svayaṃ kutaścilliṅgāt prasādhyapratyakṣeṇa kṣaṇabhaṅgagrahaṇavyavahāramādadhīta sāmarthyāt tadā na viśeṣaḥ sattvādyanumānavat  arthato hi tadā pratyakṣeṇa kṣaṇabhaṅgagrahaṇamavasthāpyamānaṃ svapauruṣasparśābhāvāt na pratyakṣataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiprasiddhi puṣṇāti  yadā tu pramāṇāntarasiddhamadhyakṣasya kṣaṇamātra sthitigrahaṇamāśritya vyavahāramātrasādhanamanumānaṃ pṛṣṭhajavikalpa nirviśeṣaṃ tatpauruṣameva dīpayadutpadyate tadā pratyakṣataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiriti mukhyamākhyāyate  tadayamathaṃḥkṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetukavināśādhikāratathā hikṣaṇitvamadhyakṣa dhiyādhipātaṃpātaṃ punarna vyavahārametat ataḥ samakṣagrahasādhanenaprasādhyate tadvyavahāra eva kṣaṇabhaṅgenyadāsiddhe pratyakṣeṇa grahasthitiḥ pratyakṣeṇa grahādasya kṣaṇabhaṅgavyavasthitiḥ yannirbhāti yathā tathā tadakhilaṃ gaṅgāmbu gauraṃ yathānocenna prativastu śaktiniyamaḥ saṅkīrṇabhāve bhavet saṃskārā  pratibhānti cendriyamatiṣvekakṣaṇasthāyinaḥsyādekakṣaṇavīkṣaṇāditarathā la dṛṣṭastrikālī kalaḥ liṅgarūpopapattivya vakīrṇoyaṃ svabhāvahetuprayogaḥ  atra ca sapakṣe sadbhāvānnavirodhadoṣaḥ  dvitīyapādena cānekāntaparihāraḥ  tathā hi nirbhānaṃ pratyakṣa pratibhānamuktam tato yāvatā viśeṣeṇa padārtha pratyakṣe pratibhāsamāsādayati tanniyamaparihāreṇayadi svarūpasthitimābhajeta tadā sarvasaṅkīrṇamasya rūpamiti sarvatra sarvopayogādiprasaṅgaḥ  ataḥ svarūpaniyame pramāṇāpekṣāyāṃ pravṛttinivṛttikāmasya yad yathā pratyakṣe nātmya a  hṛtam ā  sāmarthyate ra  tattvādya a  bhaṅgi ra  pratyakṣabhataḥa   sthita ra  vipātaṃ ā  noce pra raā  pekṣayā ā svakārā   nāne a  yāvatojñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaupratibhātaṃ tattathaiva san nānyatheti  tadanena avaitathyavyāpto hi pratyakṣa pratibhāsorthasyānyathāvasthāne vipakṣe vyāpakābhāvādabhavaṃstathāvasthānena vyāpyata iti darśitam tṛtīyapādena pakṣadharmopasaṃhāraḥ  tadasiddhiparihāraścaturthena  pūrvāparakālayorekatve hipadārthasya dṛṣṭādrūpādrūpāntaravirahāt sakalakālakalākalitasya deśāntarayuṣopi rūpasyāvaśyaṃ pratibhāsa iti na deśakālāntarāvasthāpratipattaye pramāṇāntaraparyeṣaṇāvakāśaḥ asti ca paryeṣaṇā idānīmanyadeśe kāle vā tadvastu kathamasti kiṃsvinnopanipātinārāgarasena siktamiti tadupanipātasaṃbhavinyavasare vimarśadarśanāt  na ca darśanaviṣayīkṛte tathā saṃbhavaḥ  na ca dṛṣṭepyanavasāyaḥ śakyobhidhātum tādṛśi jijñāsiteraktādau rūpe kṣaṇikatāvadanabhyāsābhāvāt  anyathā paścād darśanepi nāvasāyodayaḥsyāt  tasmāttadanavasāyastu tadapratibhāsādeva nanu vastunastrekālyavyāptipratibhāsepi svasaṃbandhiviśeṣāṇāṃ kāladeśadaśāntarāṇāmapratibhāso na bādhakaḥ kṣaṇikagrahaṇepi tatsaṃbandhihetuphalasaṃyogyādivastvantarāṇām apratibhāsasya samānatvāt ataḥ saṃbandhyantarāpekṣayā pramāṇāntaraparyeṣaṇamapi yuktameveti cet  naivam deśakālakriyāguṇādīnāṃ bhāvād bhedāsiddheḥ bhinnasya tu saṃbandhinopi pratibhāsastatpratibhāse mābhūt  tasmāt kṣaṇāntaradaśāḥsarvā nirvāsya kṣaṇaparigatenaiva rūpeṇa pratibhāsanaṃ samastavastunaḥ siddham yāvartāhi raktādirūpā visadṛśī daśā na sannidhīyate tāvatkālamekīkṛtauca grahaṇamastu  tadapi nāsti darśanalakṣaṇānantaraṃ jhaṭiti vicalane vilocanasyasadṛśeṣvapi tattvataḥ kṣaṇāntareṣu viparyayaśaṅkāvatārāt sākṣātkṛteṣu ca tadayogāt yadanantaraṃ tarhi locanacalanaṃ tadarśanaṃ naikakṣaṇikamavasāyaviparyayaśaṅka pṛthagjanasyasaṃbandhamutthāpayitum avaśyaṃ hi dvitrānapi kṣaṇānudīyamānameva tadarśanaṃ tadupayogi tato dvitrikṣaṇasthāyino rūpasya kathaṃ prathamakṣaṇe pratibhāsabhraṃśa  yena dvitīyādikṣaṇasya bhedasiddhiriti cet  yasya tāvatprathamakṣaṇa b vīkṣaṇakṣaṇāntaramevacalati cakṣuṣi viṣayavikalpodayaḥ tasya durvāra sarvāparakṣaṇaviparyaya vimaśavikāśaḥ  bhānaṃ ā  nyasyā a  vyāvasthā ā  kāla iti nāsti ā  kāleiti nāsti ā  kiñcinno a  vāsanāsakta ā  vyastada ā  sveti nāsti a  śada iti nāsti ā  hetuphalaṃ ā  yogādi a   disadṛśī a  vacanaṃ a kṣaṇamava ā   samartha a bhraṃsa ā  kṣaṇa iti nāsti ā vyāpino ā  bhāvasya ā  pratha iti nāsti tasmād ākṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyehetukavināśādhikāranaivaṃ kasyacit saṃbhavatīti cet  kimatra bādhakam  sādhakamapi kimatreticait  ucyate  yadi tāvadīkṣaṇakṣaṇamātrānantaramavasāyodaye sādhakānveṣaṇamtadā dvividhaḥ pratyakṣapṛṣṭhajo vikalpaḥ dṛṣṭamātra vikalpaśca  dṛṣṭamidaṃ vastraṃ vetyeva svarūpa viśeṣavikalpaśca kṛtrimetaramaṇimuktādau  tatrāsya viṣaye sādṛśyāpahāyaṃmandadhiyaḥ pṛthagjanasya  bhrāntirutsargasiddhābhyāsaprakarṣasaṃbhavināpohyate prakarṣatāratamyenodayasya kālasya lāghavatāratamyaniṣṭhāyāṃ darśanakṣaṇānantaramapyayamudayamāsādayannaśakyasaṃbhāvananiṣedhaḥ  dṛṣṭamātrasya vikalpasya tu darśanānantarameva janmotsava siddhaṃ sāmagrībhedenāpohyate  tathā hi prakṛtyā anādisaṃsārasantatisātmībhūtavikalpāstvanubhūtapratyakṣepi ca vastuni vikalpāpekṣapravṛttinivṛttayo viśeṣataḥ sukhaduḥkhaprāptiparihārārthinaḥ sarve sarvadā tatsādhanavimarśābhyāsavāsitasantatayaḥ kathaṃ tadviṣayānubhavepi samathahetau samupasthite vilambitavikalpabhāvānanubhavitumarhanti  kevalaṃkadācit saṃhṛtāḥ yato na vikalpasaṃhārābhyāsaḥ kadācidanyāsaktiḥ kadācidātyantikamohādāmukhībhāva ityevaṃprakārasāmagrathā vilambasaṃvāhitavikalpajanmāno bhaveyuḥ tadabhāve tu siddha eva pratyakṣakṣaṇānantaramudayo vikalpasya  tatastadarśanavinākṛteṣusarveṣveva viṣayakṣaṇeṣu raktatādisandehṛdolāndolanaṃ manaso viprakṛṣṭakṣaṇaparamparāstrivadvitīyakṣaṇepi vimarśaviṣayīkṛte kathamanavakāśaḥ  na ca pratyakṣa pratibhāsepyevam tasmāt kṣaṇaparigateneva padārtharāśiradhyakṣapratibhāsamāviśati ataḥsyādetat  pratyakṣasya kṣaṇikatve satyupapannametat yādatā pratyakṣamanekakṣaṇavyāpi tatonekṣaṇavyāpini pratibhāsite vikalpāvakāśaḥ   sāya    tat kathamekakṣaṇagrahaṇasiddhiḥ  ucyate ki tāvat svarūpaniṣpattāvupayogādane kakṣaṇasya vyāpakamadhyakṣam atha kṣaṇaniṣpannasyaiva sthairyāt  tatrādyakalpastāvadasaṃbhavī jñānasyāvayavirūpatāviyogena khaṇḍaśa utpattarayogāt  kṣaṇabhedinaśca tevayavā pratyakṣasya yadiparicchittisvabhāvāḥ tadā tāvantyeva pratyakṣāṇoti prathamapratyakṣāpekṣayā saiva cintā aparicchittisvabhāve tu samuditamapi na pratyakṣam  akhaṇḍaśaḥ paricchittiḥsamudāyena sakalātmavastuparicchedaḥ  tadāpyādyakṣaṇaparicchinnaḥ khaṇḍa eva sakalātmavastu tadapraviṣṭasya tato bhinnatvāt  anyathā krameṇa pratīyamānaṃ viśvamekameva vastusyāt sakalaṃ ca pratyakṣamekameva pratyakṣamiti  ucyata iti nāsti ā  vetyevaṃ a   viśeṣa iti nāsti ā  atra  patraṃ bhraṣṭamā  sāya ajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaudvitīye pakṣepi niṣpannavyāpārasya vā  a kṣaṇāntaravyāptiniṣpannavyāpārasyaiva vā  prathamapakṣe viṣayagrahaṇamevāsya vyāpāra iti tāvataiva vikalpajanmāvakāśaḥ svayaṃ kṣaṇāntaramastu mā vā  tathā ca sati calati cakṣuṣi viṣaye vātadviṣayagrahaṇapravaṇamadhyakṣamavatiṣṭhata iti apūrvoyaṃ nayaḥ  agrahaṇāvakṣaṇāvasthānetu na tāvataiva vikalpajanmāvakāśānmuktiḥ  na ca pūrvagrāhiṇa paścādagrahaṇe sthairyapakṣasthitiriti indriyaviṣayavidhāne vāgṛhṇatopi tasya sthitiriti śraddhāvadheyameva evamaniṣpannavyāpārasthitirityapi duḥśraddhānam  na hi kāryāntaravajjanmātirekeṇajñānasyāpi vyāpāraḥ astu caivam  tathāpīndriyaviṣayopanidhau labdhodayamadhyakṣamanadhigatagocaramubhayavicālakāle kalayat kilāstīti subhāṣitaṃ pūrvavat tadalamatipratiṣṭhamithyāvikalpairiti caturthapādena prāk paścād vā citraraktādirūpasya tadaiva nirbhāse sūcitapramāṇāntarāvṛttiviparyayeṇa yad yad rūpaṃ vyavasitisahaṃ kāpi nirbhāsamānemānaṃ bhinnaṃ spṛhayati na tat tatra nirbhāsayogi rūpābhāse rasa iva tathā tatkṣaṇe bhāsamānepūrvāvasthā vyavasitisahāpekṣyate mānamanyat iti   viruddhavyāptopalabdheḥ sthitametat ekakṣaṇasthāyinameva bhāvasvabhāvamāmukhayatipratyakṣapratibhāsa iti  na ca tatpratibhāsabahibhūtopi svabhāvastasyeti niveditaprāyaṃvyāptisamarthanaprastāve tatsiddhisiddha neti tasmāt siddhamadhyakṣeṇa bhaṅgaratvam vyavahṛtaṃ cānumānena mānāntaropapāditaṃpratyakṣeṇa kṣaṇikakalane nyāyadiksūcanātaḥ sāmarthyāptavyavahṛtividhau dhomato na prabandhaḥ sopyācāryapravararaviṇākāri ki tvalpamedhā statvābodhāt prakṛtimukharosatyamabhyujjagāra  vakṣaṇā ā  sthiti ā  vadhi ā  metat ā  kaivaṃ ā  śubhāṣitaṃ ā  dalamaprati ā  senucita a  vattantri a  ūrdhvā ā  rudra ā  svabhāvanāsu ra  sāmarthyanta a  virodhī ā  ki tulyamedhā ā  stvattvā ā svattvābhāvāt punarupalabdhiraindriyī  asti ca tatkṛtasaṃskārajanmā vimarśa ayametatsahita evopalabhyate tat kimanayoḥ sadātanoyaṃsahacāraḥ atha suhṛdayasyeva sātyaya iti  parāmarśadurbalasya hetunāntarīyakapratītirapibhavati  tadanurūpaṃ cānuṣṭhānam  na punaratrāparo jñānavivataḥ saṃvedyate  tatobhūyodarśanaṃ tāvat saṃskāradvāreṇa sahāyameva kṛtam na tatprastutamabhidhātuṃ śakyamtadantimamekajātikāśeṣavyaktiviṣayaka ityapi manorathamātram tadvayaktīnāṃ nirbhāsābhāvāt  saṃśayopi tadanantaraḥ saṃśayatvādeva na niścāyaka sambandhasya  paścimaścaniścayākāratvepi parāmarśaśūnyasyaiveti pratyakṣābhikhyayāpi tadupasthāpite prameye kaāśvāsa  aliṅgajasya hi vikalpasya pūrvapravṛttadarśanavyāpārānusārādevārthaṃtathābhāvasambhavo na svātantryāt b atiprasaṅgāt pūrvapravṛttāni ca darśanāni sahacāramātrasākṣīṇi vātātapādisahacāravat kañcid viśeṣamanāviśanti kathamasya yathārthatāṃsamarthayitumīśate  tathābhāvepi tānyeva tatra pramāṇam idaṃ tu smaraṇaṃ pramāṇatvenanirdiśyata iti sādhu  vātātapayoḥ paścāt sahacāravighaṭanāsti viśeṣa iti na vācyamvyabhicārādarśanakālāpekṣayābhedasya vivakṣitatvāt atrāpi avighaṭananaścayānupapatteścokkatvāt  yāvadeva vahivyāpārāt pūrvaṃ dhūmānudayo hṛdayasaṃvāsī tāvadeva hisahacārāntarād bhedavimarśaḥ tata eva tadvyabhicāre dhūma upādhirahitaṃ sambandhamati krāmediti śobhate  anyathā pūrvaṃ sahacāramātropalabdhau yathā dhūmamantareṇānala vilokaneanalasya dhūmena sambandhe upādhikalpanaṃ sāmānyena tathā dhūmasyāpi vahnimantareṇabhāvasaṃbhāvanāyāmupādhyantarakalpanaṃ bhaviṣyati ataḥ kasya kenaupādhikaḥ svābhāvikojñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalīvā sambandha syāt  na hi suhṛdorekavyatirekeṇānyadarśanevyatirekeṇāpi taddarśanasaṃbhāvanā na bhavati  kevalaṃ caitramantareṇāpi maitrasya bhāvāvirodhād bhūdharavivarapraviṣṭasyāpi na darśanayogyatā vigalati dhūmasya tu niyataṃ vinā vahnimudaya eva nāstītina saṃbhāvanā tāvatā ca tadutpattireva śaraṇīkṛtā bhavati  sā ca na bhūyodarśanādityuktameva ata eva gogotvayorapi na svābhāvikaḥ sambandhobhidhātuṃ śakyaḥtadutpattipratītivirahenyasmāt sahacāriṇo viśeṣābhāvāt  na ca sahacāradarśanamapyasti pratyakṣeṇobhayabhāgānullekhāt  tat kimatra svābhāvikopādhikavādaprakṣepeṇavibhāgena  gamakatvaṃ ca sāmagrayāḥ kāraṇatvādekaṃ kāraṇamanyāpekṣameva janakamityaniyamaḥ kāryaṃ tu sāmagrīniyatatvena pratyekaṃ niyatamiti tadeva liṅgaṃ na kāraṇamiti siddham aāgnerindhanasannidhau dhūmadarśanād viśeṣoddeśenaiva siddha upādhirindhanam  dhūmasyapunaragninā sambandhe tadupādhirbhavan dṛśya eva bhavet anupalabdhastu nāstītyucyate tat kimindhanameva paramupādhiryena dṛśyatāniyamaḥ sambandhe hi vivakṣyate apekṣaṇīyamarthāntaraṃ svabhāvaviśeṣa eva copādhirabhidheyaḥ  na cārthāntaraṃ dṛśyatāniyatam  tataścadhūmasyāpi hutāśena saha sambandhe syādupādhiḥ na copalakṣyata iti kathamadarśanānnāstyevayataḥ svābhāvikasambandhasiddhi atha yadyapekṣaṇīyamarthāntaraṃ syāt kathaṃ dhūma ityeva pāvakasya sattāniyama iticet  nanvidameva cintyate kiṃ dhūme sati avaśyamagniḥ sambhavī na veti kadācidarthāntaramupādhimapekṣya dhūmopi syāt nāgniriti kimatra niṣṭaṅkakāraṇam tasmāt pāvakaparādhīnodayo dhūmaḥ pariniṣṭhataḥ kathaṃ tadabhāvepi bhāvaṃ svīkuryādityevasādhu  asiddhā a ceyamupādhyanupalabdhiḥ yathā hi dahano nendhanena vinā dhūmenasaṃbadhyate tathā dhūmopi na tena vināgniā saṃbadhyata iti samānamupādhitvaatha siddhasyāgnerindhanasāhityena dhūmalābha ityupādhivyavasthāasiddhasya tu dhūmasya tannimittātmalābhatayā tadavyabhicārāt svābhāvikaḥ sthāpyata iticet  evamapi saiva tadutpattirāyātā saiva ca svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ  na ca yathoktamānasādigrāhyaḥ  na copādhidṛśyānupalabdhibādhya ityaupādhikaśaṅkāyāṃ na vipakṣānnivṛttirdhūmasyeti sthitam mindhanasyobhayatra vyāpticarcāvācaspatye tu prabandhegnerdhūmena saṃbandhe indhanamupādhidṛśya ukta eva  dhūmasya tuvahninā sambandhe svābhāvikatvamupādheranupalabdhimātreṇa ca bādhaḥ  tatra ca kacidvyabhicārasyādarśanāditi hetuḥ  tatredamālocyate kimayaṃ heturupādhyanupalabdhisādhakaḥatha saivāsya sādhikāyaṃ svābhāvikatvasya bhūtānupalabdheradāṭhyaṃśaṅkayopādhereva bādhakaḥ prathame nirupayogaḥ na hi buddherbhāvābhāvī hetvantarasādhyau svasaṃvedyavedanāntarasvabhāvatvāt  nāsti copādherupalabdhiriti siddhevānupalabdhiḥ  evaṃ vyabhicārādarśanepihetvanupayogo vācyaḥ  vyavahārasādhanamupayoga iti cet na vimaterabhāvātapratītimātrasya siddhatvāt  tṛtīyopi na yuktaḥ  ekasthā dṛśyaviśeṣaṇarahitāyāniṣedhasādhanāśaktau dvitīyasyāḥ kīdṛśī śakti  vyabhicāro dṛśya eva vivakṣita iticet  tarhi na sarvatra sarvadā vā  tataśca na kacid vyabhicāra ityataḥ svābhāvikatvamayuktam  kacit tu na dṛṣṭo vyabhicāra ityevaṃ tatkalpanamanalasyāpi dhūmena prasajyeta caitramaitrādīnāṃ vā parasparam  sati caivaṃ svābhāvikasambandhepyanāśvāsa ityāyātam tasmāt sarvatraivāvyabhicāra paryeṣaṇīyaḥ  tatonumānaviṣayepi yāvanna sādhyaṃpratyakṣeṇopasthāpayati tāvannāvyabhicāraṃ pratīyāditi kṛtamanumānena  kiṃ ca tadutpattivādeṣyaṃyā dhūmasyānekāntaparihārāya svābhāvikavāda āśritaḥ anekāntaśca vyabhicārāśaṅkayā  tataḥ svābhāvikatvāvyabhicāraḥ sarvatra  sarvatrāvyabhicārāca svābhāvikatvamitītaretarāśrayaḥ  yasya tu sakṛdekajāteranyajātyadhīnotpattipratītireva sarvatrāvyabhicārapratītiḥ tasya nāyaṃ prasaṅgaḥ bhūyodarśanāpekṣāyāmeva tadavatārasya nyāyaprāptatvāt  yathā hyekadā darśane śaṅkāyāmanyāpekṣā tathānyadāpi śaṅkāpekṣā  parasparākṛṣṭaeva sarvatra darśanākṣepaḥ  yadi tu tatrāpi vārasaṃkhyāniyamaṃ darśayet yathāsmākam prāgadṛṣṭī kramāt paśyan vetti hetuphalasthitim b dṛṣṭau vā kramaśopaśyannanyathātvena ca sthitiḥ iti pratyakṣānupalambhayorvāratrayaniyamovayave samudāye tvekavārasya tadā tāvataivasustho bhavet  bhūya iti tvapariniṣṭhitasaṃkhyaḥ kiyatā nirvṛttimāsādayet lakṣyānusārī tadaśakyatve ca na kacidanumānamayaṃ kuryāditi lakṣaṇaśāstramanarthakam  smaraṇe tucittapāṭavādhānāya kiyadapi darśanaṃ pravatrtsyati  na tatra parimāṇaniyamamantareṇa kiñcitkṣīyate bījeḍakarajananāya kālaparimāṇaniyamavat  evamabhijātamaṇitasvasphuṭī bhāvepi na darśanānāṃ parimāṇaniyamaḥ sūkṣmarūpabhedodbhedamātrasya vivakṣitatvātjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvaloprabhāsvarādivāvarakapraviṣṭasya  yamalakavad vā  dhūmādau tu na rūpasya bhedo vivakṣitaḥkiṃ tu svarūpastha  yathā hi nīletararūpayo prāk paṭīyasopi koṭirapi darśanāni nabhedāvadhāraṇapaṭūni tathā vyabhicāradarśanāt prāk vyabhicārāvyabhicāravatorarthāntaresannidhīyamānayonaṃ kiñcid rūpabhedāvadhāraṇam  dhūme tu na rūpādviśeṣollekhi hṛdayamapita pāvakādhīnasaṃbhavatayetyuktam  ata eva ca satpravṛttapratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ nirvṛttiḥ turūpāpekṣayā tu dhūmepi yādṛgeva darśanamādyaṃ tādṛgeva koṭitamamapi na maṇivadviśeṣabhāk tādṛgeva darśane yadi vyabhicāraśaṅkārahitaḥ pratipattā tadā na dvitīyasyāpi darśanasyaapekṣā  śaṅkamānastu śatenāpi darśanairapratyaya eveti bhūya iti bhavadīyamantrākṣarajāpinaḥ kā gatiḥ  ataśca śatadhāpyavyabhicāradarśī purastāt sandehavāneva yat tvanupalabhyamānasyāpi kalpanānupapatteriti supteneva vilapitam tadbālasyāpyasāmpratam  anupalabhyamānasyaiva hi kalpanā bhavati prakṛtīśvarādivat kalpitaṃ tu kiñcit pramāṇamanveti kiñcinneti viśeṣaḥ  na hi dṛśyamāno ghaṭa kalpitaucyate  tasmādanupalabhyamāneṣveva kalpanāvyavahāraḥ kevalaṃ kacidāptavacanādinābādhakādarśanā d dṛḍhaḥ sattāvasāya vimarśakasya tu pākṣikaḥ  tato dhūmasyāpi yadivyabhicāro dṛṣṭo dṛṣṭa eva  kastatra saṃśayaḥ  yadā tu na dṛṣṭastadā sattekāṃśāvasāyo mābhūt prāmāṇikādhikārāt pākṣikastu sattollekhaḥ kathaṃ vāryaḥ  athaivamabhiprāyaḥ natatraivānupalabdhivivakṣitā kiṃ tvanyatrāpi yannopalabhyaṃ tasya na śaṅkati cet  nanvagnivyabhicāraścāmīkarādau dṛṣṭa evetyastu santoṣaḥ  atha dhūme na dṛṣṭaḥ tat kiṃ sthāṇaupuruṣatvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yena sthāṇau śaṅkayate  ūrdhvatāliṅgite dṛṣṭamiti cet  ihāpi bhūyaḥsahacāriṇi dṛṣṭa evānyatra  ata eva na cādṛśyamānopītyādi viplatam  yatraiva tuyat saṃśayyate tatraiva tasya darśanamapekṣyata ityalaukikam  ato dhūmajātāvadṛśyamānopivyabhicāra upādhirvā darśanāyogyatayā maśakya  sa a idānīṃ saṃśaya svābhāvikatvasaṃśayasvabhāvaḥ svābhāvikatvaniścayaṃ tāvadavaśyaṃ pratibadhnāti  svābhāvikasaṃbandhabalena ca dhūmo gamakaḥ kathaṃ tadaniścaye gamakatvena gṛhyeta  na hi dharmaṇi sattvenaheturgamakaḥ sattvasandehepi gamako bhavitumarhati  yaśca yatsandehe pravartate satadasambhavepi pravartata eveti svābhāvikasaṃbandhaṃ vidhūyāpi dhūmasyevānyasyāpigamakatvaprasaṅgaḥ  tasmānniścayapratibandhaḥ svābhāvikatva pratibandha evārthataḥ niścayamantareṇa gamakāṅgasya svayamakiñcitkaratvāt  tasmānniragnau dhūmasyavyāpticarcāavaśyaṃ śaṅkhyā bhāvyaṃ niyāmakamapaśyatāmpra vā  iti durlaṅghayametattadutpattyanāśrayaṇe  na caivaṃ prāmāṇikalokamaryādātikramopālambhaḥ  na hipramāṇagocare kaścidaniścayamācaṣṭe pramāṇābhāve vā niścayam yathā bhavānupādherbādhikapramāṇābhāvepyabhāvaniścayam  ata eva na saṃśayapiśācasya sarvatrāvakāśa pramāṇābhāvaevānumatatvāt  pramāṇaviṣayepi kiñcivaktuṃ śakyata iti cet  yadi mukhamastītivaktavyamucyatām  kevalaṃ yadi svīkṛtapramāṇadharmo vakti tadā sudānamuttaram  athetaraḥtadetareṇaiva vaktavyam nāsmākamavasaraḥ  svīkṛtapramāṇasya hi niścayaphalatvātpramāṇasyāvipratipannapramāṇaviṣaye niścayasvīkāranāntarīyaka eva tatsvīkāraḥ kathaṃ sarvatraśaṅkāpiśācī labdhāvakāśā bhavet  kevalaṃ tvatpraṇītalakṣaṇaṃ na pramāṇamiti brūhi tacca vicāryamāṇameva vartate  athādṛśyamānopyupādhidhūme śamayata iti prāmāṇikalokayātrātikrama iti cet na prāmāṇikairevāyogyānupalabdherbādhādhikārapratiṣedhāt anyatheśvarasvargasādhanāderdatto jalāñjaliḥ  anumānāgamapramāṇasiddhernāyaṃ doṣa iticet na pūrvamanupalabdhyā bādhitenumānāde sādhakasyāpravṛtteḥ sarvajñasiddhī prasādhita tvāt tasmāt pūrvāparaparāmarśavivekaphalame tadanupalabdhimātraṃ niścayasādhanamiti tataḥ pramāṇaviṣaye saṃśayānavakāśāntrāyaṃ kacitpravartetetyasaṃbaddham  na ca śaṅkatyeva napravṛttiḥ arthasaṃśayena pravṛtteranivāryatvāt snigdhānnapānavat  etat tvanarthaka saṃśayenodāharatorthānarthaṃ saṃśayaviṣayopyajñāta iti kimataḥ paraṃ vācyam  na caitat prakṛtampramāṇavṛttau saṃśayostu na vetyasya prakṛtatvāt tatra coktameva  athedamākūtamanekadhādhūmasya dhāmanyavyabhicāradarśanāt kadācit tadantareṇa dhūmo bhaveditīyamanarthaśaṅkā sā ca nivṛtyaṅgamiti tāmavadhūya svābhāvikasambandhabodha eva vidhīyatāmityarthaḥ yathānnapāne maraṇaśaṅkāṃ nirasya pravṛttireveti  yadyevamarthasaṃśayopi pravṛttyaṅgamiti yuktam bhūyaḥ sāhityadarśanādavyabhicāra eva b hi prāyika annapāne jīvanavat  athedṛśamanarthasaṃśayameva brūma iti cet  sa tarhi pravartaka eva  tat kathaṃ nāyaṃ kacit pravartetaityucyate  kathaṃ vānarthakasaṃśayopi nivṛtyaṅgam  etacca kadācid vyabhicārepisamānam kādācitkādānamānavayācanavaditi sādhvī dhūmasya svābhāvikasambandhasiddhiḥ  yathādṛṣṭāśaṅkanaṃ ca prāgeva pratipāditam  ataeva viśeṣetyādi siddhasādhanam jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalītaduktamityādinā khāturamādāya dahanapraveśa eṣaḥ  tathā hibādhājñāne tvanutpanne nāśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikātula lo vā iti  yadhulikhyamānasyārthasya bādhajñānamutpannaṃ sādhakaṃ vā pramāṇam tadā śaṅkāyāḥkāvakāśa  tasyāḥ saṃśayarūpatvāt sādhakabādhakasya caikāntāvasāyasādhanatvāt athendriyeṣu timirādibādhajñānānutpattirvivakṣitā tadaprastutam  na hi dhūmādī svarūpasyāsiddhirāśaṅkitā kiṃtu vyāpteriti ko vārtho niṣpramāṇikā iti yadi sādhakapramāṇaviraha iṣṭaḥ tat kiṃ śaṅkāyāḥ yad vā śaṅkayollikhyamānasyārthasya tasyāpi tatraivānyatra vā  anyatrāpi sajātīyeanyamātre vā  prathamapakṣastāvanna prastāvānurūpaḥ  bhavatu vā tathāpi tadanyajñānesādhanamekārdhasamavetaṃ mānasamarthāpattiḥ svasaṃvedanaṃ vā tanna kṣīṇamasyā  śaṅkitasyaprastute sādhakapramāṇābhāvastu śaṅkāsādhaka evetyuktam  anyatra sajātīyena pramāṇābhāvasya tvayamarthaḥ yad dhūme vahnayanāyattatvaṃ śaṅkayate tat tajjātīye pramāṇenanāvagatam tatra vyaktyapekṣayā tajjātīyatvam jātyapekṣayā vā  vyaktyapekṣayātāvad dhūmāntarameva tajjātīyam  yadi ca tatra citrabhānunānāyattiḥ pramitā tadāvyabhicārādeva vyāptibahiṣkṛto dhūmaḥ sādhāraṇānaikānto zāta iti kimatra sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvārthaṃ śaṅkāvatāraṇena  apramitāyāmapi vahnayanāyattāvavyabhicārādevaki śaṅkayeti cet  adarśanamātreṇa vyabhicārasyābhāvāsiddheḥ yogyānupalabdherevābhāvasādhanedhikārāt  tato bahulaṃ sahacāramātre vyabhicārī nāvyabhicārī niścita itiśaṅkāvakāśaḥ  jātyapekṣayā tu dhūmajāteranyaiva jāti kayācid dravyādipratyāsattyāsajātīyā tatobhimatapakṣopanipāte jalādau vyabhicāradaśaṃna muktameva  yuktaścāyamevapakṣaḥ  dhūme vyāpticintāyāṃ deśakālāntaraviprakṛṣṭaṃ dhūmamekīkṛtyaiva nirṇayaprakramātjātyantara eva śaṅkaṣamānadarśanamanurūpam tāvatāpi smṛteranubhavapūrvatvāpracyuteriti prathamapakṣādanyatrāvācakaṃ cedamakṣaraṃ tatra cānupayuktamiti yatkiñcidetat ajātabādhakotprekṣiṇa saṃśayātmatvamapi bālavilapitameva  bādhotprekṣaṇaṃhi niścayātmatayā saṃśaya viruddhamityuktam na hyaniścayaphalaṃ bādhakaṃ vā  tato yatrasadabhāvaḥ
