caitad ghaṭādau dṛṣṭāntadharmaṇi dṛṣṭam  tā ṭī pṛ īśvaravāde pūrvapakṣasaṃkṣepaḥnanvevaṃ rūpādyupalabdheḥ kriyātvena cakṣurādisādhanānumānamapi katham  na hicchidādaya kriyā indriyasādhanā dṛṣṭāḥ tāsāṃ kuṭhārādisādhanatvāt  atha dṛṣṭāntadharmiṇyadṛṣṭamapi indriyasādhanatvaṃ pakṣadhamaṃtābalāt sidhyati rūpādyupalabdhigataṃ hikriyātvaṃ tadeva karaṇaṃ gamayet yat tadupalabdhinirvartanasamartham na ca kuṭhārādayaḥsamarthā iti pakṣadharmatābalāt kuṭhārādivilakṣaṇamadṛṣṭacaramapi cakṣurādi upasthāpayatīti tadatrāpi samānam  na hyaparimeyāniyatadigdeśaindriyakātīndriyakatrasasthāvarādilakṣaṇakāryotpādayogapadyamasati sarvaviṣaye jñāne nitye vā seddhumarhati  no khalvīdṛśaṃpārameśvaraṃ jñānaṃ kāryaśarīrendriyādikāryaṃ saṃbhavati śarīrādyutpatteḥ prāgasyācaitanyenatatprākkālakāryotpādāya parameśvarāntarakalpanāprasaṅgāt  evaṃ ca tataḥ prāk tataḥ prāgitianekālaukikakalpanāyāṃ varamekamevālaukikaṃ buddhinityatvaṃ kalpitam  etenaiva śarīrendriyanityatvakalpanā prativyūḍhā  etena yadeke bruvatesanniveśādimatsarvaṃ buddhimaddhetu yadyapi prasiddhayet sanniveśāderekakartṛkatā kutaḥ vidhiviveke pṛ iti tadapi parākṛtam  teṣāṃ sidhyet sarvajñanirākriyāmanoratho yadi piśitacakṣuṣaḥparamāṇūn kṣetrajñān tatsamavetān vā karmāśayān draṣṭumīśate  na caitadasti  tasmātatīndriyārthaṃdarśinosmadādivilakṣaṇā bahavaḥ kalpanīyāḥ  tad varamastveka eva tādṛśaḥkalpanālāghavāyeti  tadeva kāryatvādeva pakṣadharmaṃtāsahāyādevambhūteśvarasiddhiritisthitam bhavatu vāsmādupādānādyabhijñakartṛmātrasiddhiḥ  pāriśeṣyānumānāt tu vyatirekidvitīyanāmno viśeṣasiddhiḥ  tathā hi tanubhuvanādyabhijñaḥ kartā nānityāsarvaviṣayabuddhimānu tatkartustadupādānādyanabhijñatvaprasaṅgāt  na hyevaṃvidhastadupādānādyabhijñodṛṣṭo yathāsmadādiḥ tadupādānādyabhijñaścāyam  tasmāt tatheti  no khalu paramāṇubhedān pratikṣetrajñasamavāyinaśca karmāśayabhedānaparimeyānanyaḥ śakto jñātumṛte tādṛśādīśvarāditi jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalovittokastu yathā dhūmadarśanena pakṣadharmatābalāt nikuñjavatitvaṃ vaviśeṣovyāpakopi pratīyate tathā karturapītyadoṣa iti tādṛgeva puruṣaviśeṣa īśvara b pramāṇasiddha iti kathamanīśajagadvādino bhagavataḥ pramāṇenāvyāhataśāsanatvamiti  īśvaravādādhikāre pūrvapakṣasaṃkṣepa samāptaḥ  īśvaravādādhikārai saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyāpekṣaprabandhabhīrūṇām īśvaravāde dūṣaṇamātrakatheyaṃ samāsena iha yadyapi bahulaṃ sahacāramātraṃ kāryasya prayatnavatā darśitam darśitaśca tadabhāvekacidabhāvaḥ tathāpi pratibandhāsiddheḥ kāryamapi syāt naca buddhimatkartṛpūrvaka mityāśaṅkā bādhavaidhuryāt kāryaṃ buddhimati sādhye sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttiko hetvābhāsaḥ  naca sapakṣavipakṣayodarśanādarśanamātreṇa sādhanasya bhāve sādhyasyāvaśyambhāvaḥ sādhyābhāve vā tadabhāva ityevaṃ rūpāyā vyāpteḥ pratibandhaśabdavācyāyā  sādhanaṃ bhavitumarhati bhāvivyabhicāradarśaneṣvapi tathopalabdheḥ  kimidamidānīmadarśanamabhāvādeva vyabhicārasyaatha darśanasāmagrīsamavadhānavirahāditi nirṇetumaśakyameva sahacāramātradarśinovimarśaśīlasya ata eva vācaspateḥ svābhāvikasambandhaghoṣaṇamapi śabdapuṣṭimātram tadatiriktārthāpoṣaṇāt  bhūyodarśane hi vyabhicārādarśane svābhāvikavyavasthā  vyabhicārādarśanaṃ cavipakṣedarśanamātramuktaṃ bhavati  yat punaretadupāgheranupalambhena vyabhicārāsiddhiriti tatranopādhirnāma dṛśyacihnasthānīyaṃ kiñcidasti yadanupalambhovyabhicāraṃ vyavahārayet  kiṃtuvyabhicāradarśanamātreṇaiva tatparikalpaḥ  tadadarśanāt ca svābhāvikatvamiti viśeṣābhāvātna svābhāvikavādena kiñcit sādhyena saha bhūyo dṛṣṭo heturvyabhicāre ca na heturitīyataivaparyāptatvāt  etacca sarva vyāpticarcāyāṃ vivicya kacidarthāntarasya pratibandho nāmatadutpattimantareṇa sā ca pratyakṣānupalambhasādhanaiveti vyavasthāpitamiti tata evāvadhāryam etena śaṅkaravācaspatimatāvalambina pratyuktāḥ astu tarhi prayatnavatāpi kāryasya tadutpattilakṣaṇa evaṃ pratibandho dhūmasyevavahninā  yathoktaṃ vittokena  tathā hi kumbhakāravyāpārāt prāk mṛtpiṇḍadaṇḍacakrādiṣu satsvapi kāryaṃ kumbhākhyamupalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptamanupalabdhaṃ tadvyāpārānantaramupalabhyata iti hetuphalabhāvasiddhau kuto vipakṣavyāvṛttisandehaḥ  satyamatra pakṣavipakṣavṛttireva na sandehaḥ atra hi pratyakṣānupalambhayogyasvarūpasvīkārādabhivyaktonupalabdhapuruṣavyāpārairvṛkṣavīraṇādibhirvyabhicāraḥ  pakṣīkṛtāstṛṇādayaḥ na ca pakṣīkṛtenaivajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauvyabhicāra iti cet na pratikṣiptasya pakṣīkaraṇe nyāyābhāvāt  anyathā anuṣṇogniḥprameyatvādityādāvapi pakṣīkaraṇameva śaraṇaṃ syāt  tathā hisandigdhe hetuvacanād vyasto hetoranāśrayaḥ pra vā  iti nyāya  adhyakṣameva pratiyoginaḥ pratiyogyantarāpekṣayānupalabdhirucyate  atatonupalabdhibādhitamapi pratyakṣabādhitameva  vyavahārasādhanāpekṣayā tu sānumānam na cānumāna bādhitepyanyāvakāśaḥ  sā tarhi dṛśyaviśeṣaṇāpannasyaivābhāvaṃ vyavahārayatidṛśyādṛśyaśarīretarasādhāraṇaṃ ca buddhimattvamiti dṛśyatāniyamānupapatterbuddhimataḥ kathamanupalabdhimātreṇa tṛṇādijanmani niṣedhaḥ  tataḥ sandehāta pakṣīkaraṇaṃ nyāyyamiticet  tadetad vikrotagavīrakṣaṇam  vyāptisādhanāyādhyakṣānupalabdhyoravakāśadānādevadṛśyaviṣayatāsvīkārasya prasahyāyātatvāt  na hyadṛśye pratyakṣamanvayasādhanamanupalabdhirvāvyatirekasādhanī bhavitumarhati  tadayaṃ bhede satyanvayavyatirekarūpamadhyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃhetuphalabhāvamavataranna dṛśyatāmativartituṃ sādhyasya śaktaḥ  dṛśyatve ca niyatatṛṇādināvyabhicāra iti sādhāraṇānekāntaḥ atha vyabhicāracamatkārādadhyakṣāgocareṇaprayatnavatā vyāpti gṛhṇīyāt gṛhṇātu na tu pratyakṣānupalambhāśrayaḥ śreyānasya  nanu dṛśyādṛśya viśeṣaṇamanapekṣya prekṣāvanmātreṇa vyāptigrahaḥ  naivam tāvatāpi hi pratyakṣakṛtāyā vyāpteranavakāśa eva dṛśyaikasvabhāvaniyatā hi sā kathaṃ dṛśyāvṛśyaviṣavā bhavet  taddhi dṛśyamadṛśyaṃ carūpame kabuddhimatvādidharmānuvṛttāvapi svabhāvaviprakarṣetarābhyāmatyantaṃ bhinnajātiḥ  tataḥpratyakṣaṃ dṛśyekajātisvīkāreṇa pravṛttamitaravārtānabhijñaṃ tadviśiṣṭameva sādhāraṇamapi dharmaṃvyāpakamādarśayati VIyadyapi deśakāla viprakṛṣṭamapi na dṛśyam tathāpi ta da darśanayogyatayaikajātyeveti svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭasyaiva pratyakṣeṇa parihāraḥ  sarvānyavarjane hi svalakṣaṇaikaparyavasānād vyāptireva na syāt dhūmāgnivat kampamārutavañca  yathā hi svapravṛttiyogyajvaladbhāsurākārapuraskāreṇa pravartamānādhyakṣakṛtā vyāptiḥ saptāciṣi na jaṭharānalasādhāraṇarūpaparyavasāyinī anyathā tārṇādibhedavadabhimatepi rūpe sandihāno na tatsādhyārthakriyālābhaikāgrabuddhiḥ pravarteta  pratibandhavaikalyavad vāsati jaṭharyatva ityāmṛśataḥīśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇampravṛttiḥ syāt  yathā vā pallavollāsane samīraṇena vyāptiradhyakṣajakṛtāspṛśyarūpapuraskārānnastimitamārutasādhāraṇarūpaparyavasāyinī anyathādyāpi kisalayakampena mātariśvānamanumāpayan spṛśyaprabhañjanānurūpapravṛttinivṛttī niścayenācaret tathā puruṣepipratyakṣakṛtā vyāpitāgṛhītiradṛśyarūpaparihāreṇaiva  tasmāt pratyakṣāvyājena yadiparamiṣṭamātrameva sādhanaṃ nādhyakṣaṃ dṛśyādṛśyasāmānyepīti vyāpterabhāvāt sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvameva prayogaḥ yo yaḥ pratyakṣakṛtaḥ b kāraṇatvaniścayaḥ nāsau dṛśyādṛśyarūpaparyavasāyī yathāgnau jaṭharajātajātavedaḥsādhāraṇarūpaṃ pariharan  pratyakṣakṛtaścāsau buddhimatītivyāpakaviruddhavyāptopalabdhiḥ  pratyakṣakṛtatvaṃ hi dṛśya viṣayatvena vyāptamadṛśye tasyāpravṛtteḥ taduviruddhaṃ dṛśyādṛśyaviṣayatvam tadvyāptaṃ dṛśyādṛśyarūpaparyavasāyitvam ki ca yadi dṛśyādṛśyaviśeṣaṇamavadhūya dhīmanmātreṇa vyāpti vivakṣitā evaṃ sati yadābuddhimadabhāve kumbhakāryasyābhāvamupadarśayed vyatirekapratipādanāya tadā dṛśyādṛśyaviśeṣaṇarahitacetanamātrasyābhāva kena pramāṇena siddhaḥ dṛśyānupalabdheśyasyaivapratiṣedhedhikārāt  anyathā tṛṇādinā vyabhicārasyāśakyaparihāratvācca naca dṛśyapuruṣaviṣayaivānupalabdhirbuddhimanmātrasya vyatirekabodhasādhanībhavitumarhati ātyantikaviṣayabhedasya vyaktatvāt  anyathā tṛṇādijanmanyapi dṛśyapuruṣaviṣayaivānupalabdhistadvayabhicāra sthirīkaraṇakāraṇaṃ syāt  na hi lābhe praveśaśchedeniḥsaraṇamiti nyāyyam  tasmād dṛśyaviśeṣaṇāpoḍhapakṣe vyāptigrahaṇakāle vyatirekagrahaṇopāyābhāvād avyāpteḥ punarapi vipakṣavyāvṛttisandehaḥ  na ca nabhasyubhayābhāvavibhāvanamupāyo vyatirekagrahaṇasya kāryābhāvasya buddhimadvayāpārābhāvaprayuktatvaniścayānupapatteḥ  tadaparakāraṇasākalye hi tanmātrābhāvebhāvaḥ kāryasya tadabhāvaprayuktaḥpratyetuṃ śakyaḥ  yathā trikapañcaka cintāyāṃ cintitam  dvayostu kacinnivṛttimātramakāryakāraṇabhūtayorapi sulabham kiṃ ca buddhimatkāraṇavyāpāravirahāt vihāyasi kāryatvābhāva uta kāraṇamātraviprayogāditi ko niṣṭaṅkaḥ  tathā ca sati viphala  sakalo yatnaḥ  anvayopi hikāraṇamātreṇa kāryamātrasya gṛhyatāmutasvit puruṣaviśeṣaṇena kāraṇeneti sandeha eva atha dṛṣṭa evāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ kathaṃ parihartuṃ śakyaḥ dhūme dahanātmavatu  yadyevaṃ dṛśyaśarīrajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaurūpopi viśeṣaḥ pratīta eva kathaṃ parihartuṃ śakyaḥ citrabhānorbhāsurākāravat  sa tarhiviśeṣaḥ kāryeṇa vyabhicaryaṃta iti cet  vyabhicayaṃtām  kāryepi kāraṇavad yathāparidṛṣṭaviśeṣaniṣṭha evānvayo bhavatu ghaṭavat saudhādāvapi dṛṣṭatvāditi kiṃ naśchinnam etaccānvayamātraṃ gajanimolitena dūṣaṇamavadhīryābhidhoyate  vastutastu pratyakṣānupalambhayorekasyāpi vyāpārāyogānnānvayo na vyatirekaḥ  asti ca kāryatva murvīdharādauna ca darśanātikrānte kartaryanvayavyatireko spṛśati  tādṛkcetanakṛtetaratvābhyāṃ carāśyantarābhāvād gandhādivadasādhāraṇānekānta eva  tasmānna pratyakṣeṇa kāryamātrasyavyāptigrahaṇamiti siddham a yātāścaivaṃ yadamī pratyakṣānupalambhāviśiṣṭakāryaṃ jātyullekhenaiva kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇapravṛttayo na kāryamātrollekhena  tathā hi pratyakṣānupalambhapravṛttisamanantaramīdṛśāt jvaladbhāsurasvarūpavastuviśeṣādīdṛśaṃ dhavalimaliptakaṇṭhāmbakavikārakārivastu jāyata ityanenākāreṇa hetuphalabhāvavyavahāraḥ sarvāparakāryakāraṇajātivyudāsenaviśiṣṭameva jātiyugmamullikhan pravartate  iyameva gatiḥ sarvatra hetuphalabhāvavyavahṛtauīśvarānurodhāt tu prasiddhanyāyollaṅghanametat  iti paśyāmaḥ kaḥ punaratrāparādho yadi tārṇādibhedamudasya vahninā dhūmamātrasyeva bhūdharādibhedamapyudasya kāryamātrasya buddhimatā vyāpti pratīyāt pratyakṣam  yathaiva tarhi varhiṣākāryajātiviśeṣasya dhūmasyāvāntarasūkṣmajātimātramantarbhāvya vyāptigraho na tu tadvijātīyasparśa tathā buddhimatāpyastu vastrādeḥ  yathā vātyantavisadṛśorapi kāryajātīantarbhāvya bhūtimanmātrasya cetanena vyāpti jighṛkṣasi tathā vahnināpi gṛhṇīyāḥ indriyapratyakṣasyaiva hi vyāpāra ubhayatra kathaṃ bhinnāṃ vṛttimāśrayeta  vyabhicāradarśanādarśanakṛtoyaṃ vibhāga iti cet  tatrttārha darśanādarśanaṃ saṅkalpamanārūḍhaṃ gacchattṛṇasparśavadakiñcitkaramiti tadanurūpavimarśenāvaśyabhāvyam  na cāsti na hi kaścidagnidhūmādiṣvanvayavyatirekagrāhipratyakṣānupalambhapravṛttau kāryajātiḥakhilānalādutpadyata iti saṅkalpamanubhūya bhūyo vyabhicāradarśanāt yato vā kāryāntarāṇivahnimantareṇāpyupalabdhānyupalabhyante vā tato dhūma evānena janyata iti niścayaṃ paricinoti kiṃtu jhagityeva pratyakṣānupalambhāntaramasmādagnyāderidaṃ dhūmādīti jātiviśeṣadvayaṃ hetuphalabhāvavyavahārabhājanī kurvannanubhūyatenusandhānapratyayaḥ  pratyakṣagocareīśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇamanvayavyatirekayorna kaścid viśeṣaḥ  yadā ca vikalpāntarasthitasya jhagiti kaṇṭakādvyathetyanupalambhapūrvikādhyakṣa vihitā hetuphalabhāvagrāhiṇī matiḥ tadābhivyakto vyabhicāradarśana vimarśavirahaḥ samasamayāsambhavād vikalpānām  tadihāpyasmāt śilpinaidaṃ pṛthubudhnodarādyākā kāryamityavāntarasūkṣmabhedamudasya vyavahāraḥ  yadā tu paṭaśakaṭādikamapi puruṣādutpadyamānaṃ paśyati tadedamapīdamapi puruṣeṇa janyata itimatiravisaṃvādinī samudeti kiṃ ca vyabhicāro nāma ki siddhāyāmeva vyāptāvanumānamātraṃ khaṇḍayati atha vyāptireva mithyeti vyavasthāpayati  atrāpi pakṣe svasāmarthyena sphuratyeva vyāptigrāhiṇa pramāṇe  yad vā tasyaiva prāmāṇyakṣayamādadhānaḥ adyāpi sarvatra viṣaye niyate vā niyatepi kimiṣṭivaśāt atha pratyakṣasya tatraiva pravṛtteḥ  prathamaḥ pakṣastāvanna yuktovirodhāt  na hi b sādhyāvinābhāvalakṣaṇā ca vyāptirhetoḥ sādhyābhāva saṃbhavakṛtaśvānumānābhāvaḥ saṅgacchate anyatrāpi vyāptāvanāśvāsācca evaṃ vyāptigrāhiṇi pramāṇe prāmāṇyādapracyutibhṛti vyāptimṛṣātvabodhanamapyasambaddhaṃ boddhavyam  sarvatra ca vyāptigrāhiṇa prāmāṇyakṣaye dhūmādagnirapi nānumātavyaḥanyasya vyāptigrāhiṇobhāvāt  kimidānīṃ śaraṇamīśvarānumānasya bhaviṣyati svecchayā ca niyate viṣaye vyāptivihitau pramāṇaṃ varākamudāsīna miti na kaścitheturaheturvā tattvataḥ dhūmepi svecchayā vyāptikhaṇḍanaprasaṅgāt  niyata viṣayatvaṃ tuvyabhicāragocarasyāpi pratyakṣasya katham yāvatā yathā niyatajātipravṛttaṃ vyāptigrāhisarvaviṣayamiṣṭam tathā vyabhicāragocaramapi sarvaviṣayamevānyūnānatiriktaśaktitvādubhayo  tadekaviṣaya eva vyāptigraho vyabhicāravedanaṃ ceti kimadhunā sādhanamasādhanaṃvā syāt  bhavatu vā bhavaduparodhād bādhabodhina pramāṇasya niyataviṣayatvam tathāpi na khalu sakṛdeva vyabhicāravatāṃ bādhabodhaḥ kiṃ tu krameṇa  tadā ca vyabhicāriṇāmapi vyabhicāradarśanamāhatya nāstīti dhūmasya tato viśeṣābhāvāt punarahetutvam hetutvaṃvānyasyāpi na ca sarvasyānyasya vyabhicāradarśanairdhūme vyāptiviśvāsa iti vācyam  evaṃ hipurastāda dhūme vyāptigrahaṇānantarameva parvatanitambe dhūmād dahanānumānaṃ na śārdūlāditina syāt vyabhicāradarśana vilambāpekṣaṇāt  aśakyaṃ caitadanyatra vyabhicāradarśanairabhi jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaumate vyāptiviśrāma iti  vyabhicāraviṣayāṇāmadhyanantatvād deśādiviprakarṣavatāṃgocarīkaraṇakālāpekṣayā puruṣāyuṣasya kanīyastvāt  tasmād vyabhicāradarśanavanniyataviṣaya eva vyāptigraho nirapavādaḥ śuddhekādhyavasāyasya vibhāgena pravṛtteḥ  ataeva casvābhāvi kavikalpasyaiva kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇedhikāro naupādhikasya asti hi śuddhaviṣayajanitālocanājñānamātrāpekṣo bālatiryaksādhāraṇo vikalpaḥ sa śuddhaḥ svābhāvika iti cocyate yadvaśāt paśavopi kṣutpipāsāpraśamādisādhanāni tatraivasamarthānyavadhārayantaḥ punastadanvitayā tathaiva tatastatra pravartante nivartante vānanvitayā asti ca saṅketasmaraṇasacivālocanājñānajanito vikalpa yathā dīpāt kajjalamālokayato nīlamidaṃ rañjanādyapayogītyeva vikalpa pūrvadṛṣṭārthakriyāsmaraṇasahāyānubhavabhāvitastādṛgaupādhika ucyate  na ca tadā nīlavikalpa ityeva pradīpādakhilaṃ nīlamutpadyataiti prekṣaḥ kaścinniścinoti  kiṃ tu yadeva kajjalāvalokanamātrānurūpavikalpapuraskṛtaṃ a vastu kajjalaśabdasaka tayogya jātiyogāt svarūpaviśeṣād vā tadeva pradīpakāryaṃvyabhicārālambane coktam evaṃ dhūmepi dhavalamidaṃ vastu varjāyata iti saṅketānusārī vikalpa aupādhikaevākṣipati kāryatvena tuhinādikam  śuddhe tu vikalpe dhūmajātireva vyabhicārapratyayo vā bhinnaviṣayaeveti siddham evaṃ tarhi vyabhicāradarśanena sādhāraṇānekāntavyavasthā duḥstheti cet  evametad yadi buddhipāṭavaniyamaḥ sarveṣām  mandabuddhistu sādṛśyādinā yadā tu kāryajātau sarvatravyāptigrahaḥ tadā kiṃ sādṛśyāpekṣayeti  yadi tarhi jātiviśeṣapratibaddha evādhyakṣeṇa pratibandhabodhaḥ kathamatyantavijātīyopi tīyā api ghaṭakuṭakuḍyādayaḥ dharmāntarotpattivyavasāya tadā dharmavyāptirucyate payasi auṣṇyādivat tadā ca auṣṇyāntara meva sajātīyo dharmaḥ nādhunā dharmijāterapekṣā evaṃ rāgopi ghaṭakuṭādidravyavejātyamavamatya svayaṃ iti tu viplavaḥ pareṣām  ayamevārtho yādṛk kāryatvaṃdevakulādau puruṣavyāptaṃ pratītam na tādṛg yugandharādāvityanayā diśopadiśyate yajjātīyaṃ devakulādi puruṣavyāptaṃ na tajjātīyaṃ yugandharādītyarthaḥ  atyantavejātyāccakāryaśabdamātrasāmyamucyate na punarakāryavyāvṛtteḥ kacit nyūnabhāvaḥ  vyāptau tu kāryatvāderanantarbhāvaṃ brūmaḥ  ataeva sanmātreṇa sāmyaṃ nopayogi mūrtatvādineva dahanānumāne īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇammañjaryāstu paryanuyogosthānapatitaḥ  ghaṭādijātireva puruṣavyāptā siddhetivadatānyatra saṃśayamātrasya vivakṣitatvāt  kulālādimanuṣyakṛtabuddhiśca kṛtabuddhiruktā tadabhāvaśca jātibhede uttarīkṛtaḥ  sa cobhayasiddhatayā na visarjanānyavakāśayati na cātyantikajātibhedamantareṇopapadyata iti niveditam evaṃ vācaspaterapi viśeṣagaveṣaṇaṃ kṛtabuddhivaidhuryasyābhidheyaprayojanayoraparijñānaprayuktamiti veditavyam  yadi hi kṛtabuddhirnāstīti prakṛtasādhyabuddhirnāstīti vivakṣitam tadā pratītikalahemuṣmin kuto viśeṣādanyatra sā bhavati parvatādau tadabhāvānneticintyate  yadā tu kṛtabuddhirnāstīti a  samāna śilpikṛtabuddhirnāstītyabhidheyamtatra ca na vivāda  prayojanaṃ ca kumbhādibhyombhodharāderatyanta vaijātyakhyāpanam tadavyaśakyaparihāram  tato gṛhītavyāptikebhyotyanta vilakṣaṇāt kathaṃ prakṛtasādhyabuddhirityabhipretam  tadā plavata eva sakalamevaṃvidham  utpattimanmātre ca vyāptinirasanāt hantotpattimadityādyuttara kāladaṇḍakhaṇḍitameva  tena ghaṭe dṛṣṭavyāptikasyaghaṭasajātīyameva buddhimatpūrvakam  yadā tu prāsādādāvapi vyāptigrahastadā tajjāterapitatpūrvakatva siddhirityapyuktam yaccātha yajjātīyamityāśaṅkaya ki kāryajātīyam  tathā na dṛṣṭamityuttaramtadapi svābhāvika vikalpāvabhāsina  sāmānyasya pratyakṣeṇa vyāptigrahaṇayogyatāsamarthanāt karthitam  tasmād yadapi aupādhikavikalpapratibhāsināpi rūpeṇa tajjātīyavyavahāro duṣpariharaḥ vyāptigrahaṇe tu pratikṣiptatvānmahān viśeṣa iti ata eva vittokavikalpā api na kiñcit  tathā hi yadyasmadabhiprāyapraśnaḥtadā viśiṣṭeva kāryajātirdevakulakalasādilakṣaṇā buddhimāptā yaduṣṭehi parokṣakriyasyāpyanubhūtasajātīyaśilpyanumānam sā na siddhā sindhubhūdharādau  kāryatvamātraṃ tuna vyāptamityuccaistarāṃ tanvanta evāsmahe  tatra kimebhirvikalpairiti cintaya  yadviśeṣādviśiṣṭā kāryajāti sa viśeṣa kimanirūpitarūpa evetyapi pāpīya pratyakṣasiddhānāṃkāryajātīnāṃ parasparavesadṛśyasyāpahrotumaśakyatvāt  vyāptistu viśiṣṭāyāṃ jātībhavatu kāryamātre vetyatra paramāpātato vimantumarhati  kathamanyathā svayamapi vastutvasyāgnikāryatvāsaṃjananaṃ vyabhicāramālambya parihṛtam  vyabhicārabuddhīnāṃ niyatajātiviṣayatve vivādābhāvādityāvirbhāvitameva  tasmādākārārthakriyāsāmarthyādivedanātcitrākāre jagatijyāyasī jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalauniyatamīśvaraprasādādevālaukikamekākāramālokitamasyetyupekṣaivayadapi prācīnamupādānodāharaṇamasya kāryamātre vyāptisamohayā tadapi naupayikam tatrāpi pratyakṣavyāpārasyāśakyasādhanatvātnaisargikavikalpaviṣayatvātupādānasya dṛśyādṛśyasvabhāvatvācca  tat kimidānīmupādānena kārya rāśervyāptirevanāsti  āhosvit pramāṇāntaragamyā bhavatviti cet  ubhayatra saṃśayaḥ satopivyabhicārasya viparyayabādhakānumānasya vānullekhasaṃbhavādidānīmekāntahetorabhāvāt tadayaṃ sopādānaṃ sarvotpattiriti sarvatantra siddhāntovirodhādanuvṛttaḥ yāvacca kāryamālokayāmastāvadupādānavadevetyavigānena vyavahāropi  na ca kāryaparyantabodhaḥpṛthagjanasyeti tanīyasāpi viparītāṃśena saṃśayo durvāra  buddheśca buddhirupādānaṃ niścitāiti vijñānasya vijñānā nyānupādānācca sidhyatīti na virudhyate tato yadi siddhāntādapi b tadvyāptivyavasāyo na kācit kṣatiḥ  pratyakṣāt tu mā bhūt kevalamatrapakṣecetanopādānatvaheturekadeśasiddhaḥ śaṅkayeteti vyavasthā  sā cāyātaiva ki kriyatām  viparyayabādhakapramāṇalābhe tu sāpi na syāt  kevalaṃ pratyakṣeṇa kṛtsnakārya vyāptivādenudāharaṇamevedam  ataḥ pratyakṣasya jātiviśeṣe vyāpāraniyamaprasādhanādviśeṣahetvabhāvādityādyapi dhvastam yatpunaraparasya viparyayabādhakapramāṇopanyāsapauruṣam tatrāpi prathamadvitayaṃtāvad bādhakaṃ dhūmasyeva siddhāyāmeva tadutpattau tatsādhakapratyakṣānupalambhasya viśiṣṭajātyadhikāreṇa pravṛttisādhanād viśiṣṭameva ghaṭādikāryaṃ prati śakyam  evaṃ ca yadibuddhimantamantareṇa jāyeta sakṛdapi tato na bhavet aniyatahetutve vāhetutvamiti nakāryamātraṃ prati tasya puruṣādutpattiprasādhanābhāvāt  tataśca tat kāryaṃ yat puruṣapūrvamityapi niravakāśam nāpi kāryāvirāmaprasaṅgasaṅgatiḥ svakāraṇāyattasannidheradṛṣṭapariṇāmasahakāriṇaḥkāraṇāvasthāviśeṣasya satatamabhāvepi kāryāṇāṃ kādācitkatopapatteḥ yadapekṣayā nityaśakterapi īśvarasya śaśtranna karaṇa tvam  ekāvasthāniyame hi kāraṇāntarāṇāṃ pravṛttinivṛttisādhanīcchā prārthyeta  sa ca nāsti bījasyocchūnataratamādibhāvavat pariṇāma śatānandasyeti prāntalekhaḥ īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇamparamparāparicayasya teṣāmapotumaśakyatvāt  astu vā ekāvasthāniyama īśvarasyaicchāyā api nityatvāt tadavastha kāryāvirāmaḥ anitye tu yadapekṣosyā kadācidbhāvaḥ tadapekṣayā kāryagrāmasya yadi syāt kīdṛśo doṣa  kumbhādikāryakramepi tarhiki puruṣecchayā yadapekṣosyāḥ kramaḥ tadapekṣa eva kumbhāderapyastīti vaktuṃ śakteḥ tadayuktam pramāṇena dṛṣṭasāmarthyasya hetorapohitumaśakyatvāt  prastute tu pramāṇābhāvāt kāryakādācitkatāmātramāśritaṃ tadanyathāpyupapatsthata iti kutaḥ puruṣāpattiniyamaḥ kāryasya atha kumbhāde kadācidbhāva puruṣādhīno dṛṣṭa iti kāryāntarasyāpi tatheticet  evaṃ tarhi tadeva darśanādarśanamātraṃ vyāptisādhanamāyātam kimatra viparyayabādhakopanyāsaśauṭīryeṇeti tṛtīyamapi nirastam yaccocyate kāraṇasannidherdhīdhanādhīno niścita iti tatrāpi tathā darśanamātrā śraye etadeva vācyam  viparyayabādhakaṃ ca na kiñciduktam  pratyakṣānupalambhaśaraṇīkaraṇeca vātopaghātādimilajjambālabījādisāmagrathā anaikāntikatvādi sarvamākṣepaparihārasametaṃ kāryavadavagantavyaṃ sāmagrī viśeṣa eva vyāptiyogya ityetatparyantam  tanna kāraṇasāmagrayā puruṣeṇa vyāptisiddhiḥ yato vipakṣe vyāpakānupalambhādasambhava iti caturthamapi karthitam tāva taiva vācaspaterapi a hṛdayaśūnya pralāpopahastitaḥ  yathā hi vitatānāṃ tāvadajananabījamuktamavasthāviśeṣābhāvo nāma  yadyapi daṇḍacakrādīnāṃ puruṣādeva milanamupalabdhaṃ tatprayatnasacivānāṃ ca kāryārambhaḥ tathāpi sarvatra sarvadā vātathaiveti niyamayituḥ pramāṇasyābhāvāt kāryotpādavyāpakasyāpi kāraṇasamavadhānasyabuddhimadadhīnatvena vyāptaya siddhestadavastho doṣaḥ  yathā ca kāraṇāntaradaśāviśeṣāśraye ṇaiva kāryāṇāṃ kadācid bhāvastathā prakṛtaviśeṣopīti pañcamaṃ ca pañcatāmañcitam kāraṇamātrāpattisādhanaṃ punaretaditi darśitaṃ śāstre etenaiva śaṅkaroktamapi nāpi kaścid viśeṣa ityādi kāvyaracanāmātramāpāditam pratibandhasādhakapramāṇaparyādānāt  yadyapi ca nirabhiprāyavyāpāratvena prāsādādihetubhyo bhūbhūdharādihetūnāṃ na viśeṣastathāpi prayatnavadapekṣānapekṣābhyāṃ yadi syātko doṣaḥ  yathā pārthivatvā viśeṣepi lohalekhyatvālohalekhyatve  avaśyaṃ ca nirabhijñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalīprāyatvāviśeṣepi viśeṣa eṣāmeṣitavyaḥ śakteḥ kathamanyathā kāryavaijātyamātyantikam tadasau śakti prayatnavadapekṣāve mukhyamapi yadi kṣameta kā kṣatiḥ  kiṃ ca karturapikarādivyāpāramantareṇa samīhāmātrāt na mūrtakāryasiddhirupalabdhā tamativartamānānāṃbhūdharādīnāṃ kā gaṇanā samīhāmātre karādayopi samīyā pravartyanta iti cet  samīhāpi sanniveśini śayādivyāpāravirahe na kiñcitkarītyuktam  tato yayā śaktayā karādivyāpārapāravaśyamapāsyamahīdharādihetavo nirabhiprāyatve satyapi na kāryakarmaṇi pratihanyante tayā samīhāmapinātikrameyuriti ka evaṃ śraddadhīta  na hi dhūmodayakāle ucchaladbahalarūpa vastu vahnīndhanajanyatayā sambhāvitamekābhāvaniścaye niścīyamānamanyābhāvepi na bhāvaśaṅkāyāṃniveśayati tādṛgetadapi śarīrasvīkāre tu prādeśika kāryānityāne kāsarvajñatvāt sādhu sādhita sudhībhirīśvaraḥ  etenaiva vā vyabhicāra  kāryatvādeḥ  na hyanadhiṣṭhitānāmityādivacanāddarśanādarśanamātrādanyamupāyamasya vyāptisādhanāya spṛśati tacca kṛtottaram  yadi cadarśanādarśanameva śaraṇam tadā yathā samīhāvataḥ kāryakriyā dṛṣṭeti kārye sati samīhāvatonumānamiṣṭam tathā karādimata eva mūrtakriyā dṛṣṭeti karādivyāpārānupapattaupuruṣasyākriyaiva kasmāt na niścīyate  na khalu kāryahetuvyāpakānupalambhayoḥ prāmāṇyekaścid viśeṣaḥ  yadi tu darśanādarśanamātramanāsthāya pramāṇāntaramekaniyataṃ syātsyādekasādhyabuddhiḥ tadabhāve tu pratibandha b eva tayoḥ parasparam na bādhā tulyakakṣatvāditi prakaraṇasamaḥ parābhiprāyāt prayogaḥ yo na svāṅgavyāpāravān nāsau mūrtanirvartanasamartho dṛṣṭaḥ yathā kulālaeva saṃhṛtakarā divyāpāradaśāyām  nāsti ca svāṅgavyāpāraḥ prakṛte puṃsīti vyāpakānupalabdhi  nāśrayāsiddhiḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyanyāyeneti vastutastarhi dūṣaṇāntarameva yuktaṃkaḥ pratihetoravakāśa iti cet na bhūyodarśanasya vyāptisiddhāvana ṅgatvapratipādanārthamasyopanyāsāt  yadi bhūyodarśanamupāya tadaivamapi syādityutteriti vyāptigrahaprakārāṇāmayogādanekānta iti sthitam astu vā vyāptigrahaḥ kathañcit tathāpi neśvarasiddhipratyāśā phalavatī buddhimataḥ sādhyasyaikatvaniyamaniścayābhāvāt  ekatve hi tasya siddhe nityavibhusavaṃjñatvaīśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇamsiddhirīśvaravyavahāramāropayet  yadā tu bhinnadeśakālakalitaṃ kāryajātamanekena saṃkhyātikrāntena kartrā kṛtaṃ sambhāvyeta na tadā vibhutvanityatve svasvaviṣayopādānādimātravedanasiddhau ca ka sarvajñatvam atha bahūnāṃ vyāhṛtamanasāṃ vyāpāre kāryasyānutpattirupanyasya vilopādiprasaṅgaścasyāditi cet  pratyekaṃ vaibhavādiguṇayogādīśvarāṇāṃ vyāpāre syādapīyamāśaṅkā adyapunarekopi tādṛ na sidhyatītyucyate  arvācīnaśaktayaśca bhūyāṃsa ekamanekaṃ ca kāryamārabhya niṣpādayanto dṛśyanta eva  nanvanekatrāpi pradhānabhūtenaikena bhāvyam balīyasāvā sūtradhāravat senānīvad vā  atastasyaiva kartṛtvamitareṣāṃ tadanuvṛttitvāditi cet natatrāpi niyamābhāvāt svasvaprayojanānurodhena svatantrāṇāmapi keṣāñcidekasattvādighaṭanādarśanāt  tatrāpi kaścideva prathamaḥ prayojaka ityapi nāsti anekasya tathā hṛdayotkalikāyāanivāraṇāt nīcasthāpi prayojakatvasambhavāt tasmād bhramaramadhumakṣikāvalmīkajantuvat kṣudraprāṇibhirapaye ke kamainākādikaraṇasambhāvanāyāṃ kā vārtā viśvasyaikena kriyāyāḥ  tatrādṛṣṭajanmānastāvat tāvataivakṛtārthīkṛtacetanānumitayaḥ kṣitidharādayaḥ  te ca kṣudrajantava upādānamatikṣudraṃ pṛthivyādidravyamupakaraṇaṃ sukhādisampradānamātmānaṃ sthitisukhādi ca prayojanaṃ jānanta evavalmīkajantuvat pravarteran  siddhe ca nāvaśyamadhiṣṭhāyakā dṛśyeran vicitraśaktikarmākṣepāt svabhāvaviprakarṣād vā  yepi dṛṣṭajanmāno vṛkṣādayaḥ pauruṣeyāḥ tatracintaiva nāsti  adṛṣṭapuruṣavyāpārāstu ye bindhyayugandha rādiparisaradbhāvāstepi piśācādiprakārairadhiṣṭhātṛbhirasaṃkhyaiḥ kartṛmanta iti kaḥ sarvavedī bhavatu  deśakālayoścabhinnā evepri ka vibhutvanityatve  na caivaṃ śaṅkāyā a bādhakaṃ kiñcidasti vastubalapravṛttamanumānam inanucaivaṃ tāvad bhavadbhirapi na svīkṛtameva  etāvaccātikaṣṭataraṃ kalpayato varamīśvarakalpanaiva lāghavāditi cet  satyam yadi kalpanāmātretaranyāsaḥ tadā bhavadupanyāsameva puraskariṣyāmaḥ  yāvat punaranumānavyājaṃ na varjayasi tāvadavaśyamasmākaṃdṛḍhanirūpaṇābhiyogaḥ  atha kṣudraṃrasaṃkhyanirmitā narmaṃdādaya iti dunoti cetaścet ekenāśarīreṇa nirmitā iti suṣṭhutarām  tasmāt pramāṇameva sarvato balavad yathā sthāpayati tathārthaṃsthitiḥ  ataeva tad dṛḍhaṃ nirūpyate  na ca kṣudreṣvanurodhaḥ kaścit jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalaukṣudrairakṣudrai radṛśyaiḥ samānaśaktibhiradhikaśaktibhiḥ svatantraiḥ pradhānasammataikaikajantusanāthāparimitayūthairvā sthūlāṇukaikāne kasvakāryabhāgopādānādimātravedibhiḥ ṣaḍgatiparyāpannaiḥ kṛtobhavatu bhuvanasanniveśaḥ eka eva tu kartāsya mā bhūt nāpi bauddhastathānupagamāt tato hetuvyāvṛttiḥ ekatopi vyāvṛttiprasaṅgāt na ca vastubalapravṛttenumāne paropagamāpekṣā  upagamamātrasya tyāgenāvirodhāt  tadevaṃbuddhimanmātre sādhye upādānādyabhijñatālakṣaṇaviśeṣanāntarīyakatayā sākṣādupādānādyabhijñakartṛsādhanād vābhimatasiddhinaikāntiko sarvaṃkāryakriyāyā ekakartṛtvāsiddheḥ upādānādyabhijñamātrasādhane ca vaiphalyam bhāratādikathāvat  tataḥ sādhanāntarābhāvādasmādeva sarvajñādiguṇavataḥ siddhiriṭeti tadapekṣayaiva dūṣaṇamabhidhānīyamanekāntalakṣaṇamiti sthitam ato yāvatīmarthaṃgatimityādi durlaṅvayam  sādhyasāmānyapratibandhākṛṣṭatvepiviśeṣasya siddhi sādhanādhīnaiva tadekaparatayā sādhanopanyāsādanyasādhanābhāvācca bauddhasyāpi hi nairātmyasiddhiḥ sādhanādhīnaiva  yadi hi nairātmyatyāgepi kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanaṃ caritārthaṃ bhavet tadā kiṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhane nairātmyasiddhiḥ syāt  bhavatastusārvajñyādisiddhimuddhūyānyathāpyupādānādyabhijñānalakṣaṇo viśeṣa upapāditaḥ nātmopanyāsapūrvakonvayo dṛṣṭānte pradarśyata iti anupayuktam  sākṣāt tadanvayadarśaneapi tannāntarīyakatvaṃ sādhyasāmānyasya darśayitavyameva  taccaikatvena sakalakriyādhārasyavyāpterabhāvādaśakyam ataevaetenaiva vācaspatyopi sārvajñyasādhanābhinayaḥ prativyūḍhaḥ  siddhe tu sarvajñe kartarikarturekatvanirūpaṇaśramosmākamanuyogītyuparamyate  yadapyayaṃ vyatirekiprayogamāhatadapyekatvāniścayādeva dūṣitam anityāsarvaviṣayabuddhitvepyupādānādivedanasambhavasyopapāditatvāt vittokasamādhāne tu dhūmāddharādharāyoga vyavacchedavat agneḥ pañcavarṇaśikhākalāpatāyā apyanumānaprasaṅgaḥ  nātra sāmarthyamiti cet  tatrāpi pakṣāyogavyavaccheda evasāmarthyāt  pṛthvībhṛti prayatnavataḥ siddhāvapyekatvāniścayāt ka sarvavedanasiddhiḥ b  nanu dūdhaṇukasyāpi kāryatvāt kartā tadupādānaparamāṇudarśī niyamenaeṣitavyaḥ  na ca māṃsacakṣuṣastathā bhavitumarhanti  anyathā kimasmadābhiraparāddhaṃ yenaīśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇamtathā na bhavāmaḥ  tadavaśyaṃ kartātīndriyadarśī svīkriyamāṇo neśvarādanyo yuktaḥ  tadapiyatkiñcit  na hi māṃsacakṣuṣpi sarvasādhāraṇaṃ karaṇasāmarthyam asmadatyantamapakṛṣṭānāmapigṛdhrādīnāmindriyapāṭavātiśayadarśanāt  kṣodiṣṭhānāmeva ca keṣāñcit paramāṇudarśanamapisyāt karmaśaktiviśeṣāt yathā pipīlikānāmasmadagocaragandhāṇugrahaṇam  catanmātrasūkṣmamīkṣamāṇairdeśakālaviprakṛṣṭasyāpi sūkṣmāntarasya grahaṇam sakalasthūlasya vā tanna tāvataiveśvarasiddhipratyāśā naevaṃ tarhi bhavatu paramāṇodarśanasambhāvanā sakalakṣetrajñatatsamavetadharmādharmāśayaviśeṣāṇāṃ tu katham  na kathañcit  na hi kāryakriyā kṣetrajñasvarūpādiparijñānenāpi vyāptākulāladṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭā kiṃ tu sampradānopakaraṇavedanadvāreṇa tadākṛṣṭiriṣyate  sā cāśakyāsāmarthyānupapatteḥ uktakrameṇāpi tanmātravedanasya caritārthatvāt  karmaṇi svasyābhipreyamāṇatvena sampradānatāyā durvāratvāt yathā svasmai mandiraṃ karotīti  anyathā tenaivavyabhicāraprasaṅgaḥ sampradānajñānāpekṣāyāḥ anumīyamānastatrāparaḥ sampradānavedī bhaviṣyatīti cet na vyabhicāradarśanenakartuḥ sampradānajñānanāntarīyakatvāsiddheranumānavārtāvirahāt  na cānumīyamānāpekṣayātasyā kartṛtvam  evaṃ hi kulālasyāpyakartṛtvaprasaṅge vyāptigraha virahāt tadavasthonumānānudayaḥ  tasmād yad yadavaśyaṃ sampradānajñānāpekṣaṃ kartṛtve svātmāpi sampradānameṣitavyaḥ na ca paramapi sampradānaṃ vyavahāraprasiddhamuddhūya kṣetrajñarūpamasau jñātumīśaḥ karmāśayabhedārthopakaraṇaśabdasaṃgṛhītānapi  tato yathā kulālastāna vidvān daṇḍacakrādivedanenaivopakaraṇajñaḥtathānumīyamānā api jantavaḥ svakīyakaramukhādijñānenāpyante bhaviṣyanti tat kutastyametat kṣetrajñarūpatadīyadharmādharmāśayabhedaparijñānam  athāśarīrasya kasvāṅgavyāpārasaṅgatiḥ  aśarīrasya siddhisaṅgatirapi kīdṛśī  ekatve hi siddhe śarīrīprādeśiko na sarvakarmaṇi samartha iti sāmarthyādaśarīrisiddhipratyāśā ekatvaṃ ca duḥsādhamityuktam  na cāśarīratvepi daṇḍacakra karamukhādyupakaraṇānupapatteḥ pāriśeṣyāt karmāśayabhedajñānenaivopakaraṇajñānaniṣṭheti sauṣṭhavāya  dikkālasamavāyāderapyupakaraṇasaṃgṛhītasya jñānenatajjñatāmātrasya kṛtārthatvāt kaḥ punarasau viśeṣo yatastadavasthasya digādijñānenaivopakaraṇajñatā  a nadharmādharmādijñāneneti  ubhayajñānenaiva bhavatviti cet  tadayuktam  nahi yāvadupakaraṇaṃjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauṃtāvat kartrāvaśyaṃ jñeyamiti dṛṣṭam  na ca digā dijñānenaivopakaraṇa vittistadavasthasyetiniścayaṃ brūmo yato viśeṣaparyanuyogaḥ kiṃ tūpakaraṇāntarasambhavānna pāriśeṣyaviśrāntiḥatretyucyate  tato yathā parāparakartṛṣu daṇḍacakrāditurīvemādyupakaraṇavirahaparamparāyāmanyānyairupaka raṇairdharmādibāhyai rupakaraṇajñatāsthiti rupalabdhā tathā kimadyāpyastu  utadharmādīnādāyaiveti sandeha eva  yadi punaranyadupakaraṇaṃ na syāt pāriśeṣyavyākhyānaṃśobheta  abhyudayaniḥśreyasamārgādisandehe ca kiṃ tādṛśā tena kartavyamīśvarābhidhānenadhanavirahiṇeva tasmādaśarīritvepi na dharmādijñānākṛṣṭiḥ kiṃ punastadasiddhau  mā bhūdupakaraṇatayādharmādervedayitā niyamena kāryatayā bhaviṣyati yataḥ kartā kāryarūpādivedaka sa ceśvaraityapi niḥsāram  dānahiṃsādikaṃ hi kurvantastad vedayanta eva svarūpamātreṇa na tāvatāta eveśvarāḥ  na cānyaḥ kāryena tadvedī siddhaḥ  dharmādharmatvena tu niścayaḥ tatkāriṇopināvaśmbhāvī kumbhakāravat  tatkāriṇāṃ tarhi tattvena niścayābhāvāt tattvaniścayaḥ kāryatvātkartāramīśvarameva sannidhāpayedityapi nāsti  dharmādharmatvaniścayopi hi samīcīnaḥsandigdhasattāka eva vartate  kathaṃ tataḥ pratyāśā  anirastaviparyayāśaṅkasaṅkalpasvabhāvastubhūyasāmāgamadvāreṇa devajātismarādisvīkārācca teṣām apyasti leśena samyakkarmaphalasambandhabodhaḥ  na ca tāvataivaiśvaryaparyāptiriti tadevamīśvarāsiddheḥ sakalajanmināṃ śubhāśubhakarmāṇi nopakaraṇam kiṃ tu kāraṇānyevalokavaicitryasyeti dhīmatāmupādeyaḥ prathamaślokārtha iti  īśvaradūṣaṇaṃ samāptamiti  vārtikasaptaślokī sthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthānaviśeṣārthakriyādiṣu iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayothavā   siddhaṃ yādgadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvābhāvānuvṛttimat sanniveśādi tadyuktaṃ tasmād yadanumīyate   vastubhede prasiddhasya śabdasāmyādabhedinaḥ na yuktānumitiḥ pāṇḍudravyādivadbhutāśane   anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛdvikārasya kasyacit ghaṭāde karaṇāt sidhyed valmīkasyāpi tatkṛtiḥ   sādhyenānugamāt kārye sāmānyenāpi sādhane sambandhibhedād bhedoktidoṣaḥ kāryasamo mataḥ   jātyantare prasiddhasya śabdasāmānyadarśanāt na yuktaṃ sādhanaṃ gotvād vāgādīnāṃ viṣāṇavat   vivakṣāparatantratvānna śabdāḥ santi kutra vā tadbhāvādarthasiddhau tu sarva sarvasya sidhyati   pramāṇavārtike prathamedhyāye  īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam karmanirmita vaicitryamanīśaṃ yo jagajjagau praṇamāmi pramāṇena tamavyāhataśāsanam nityapramāṇapratiṣedhasiddhau yadapramāṇatvamanityabhāve vibhāvayannāha kṛtī tadaṃśe vimohadaṃśāpaha eṣa mārgaḥ svayaṃ nirasyāpi parasya sādhanānyasaṅgatau vārtikakārakīrtane na nirvṛtiścet punarasya varṇanāda varaṃ hi tadvarṇanayaiva vikramaḥ yad yat kāryaṃ tat tad buddhimatpūrvakam yathā ghaṭaḥ  kāryaṃ ca mahīmahīdharādi yad vā yad yat na buddhimatpūrvakaṃ tat tanna kāryam yathā ākāśam  kāryaṃ catarugirisāgarādītyarthataḥ kāryahetuḥ  evamacetanopādānatvam arthakriyākāritvamsvārambhakāvayavasanniveśa nāviśeṣavattvam sthitvā sthitvā kāryakarmāṇi pravṛttidharmakatvaṃca prayojyamiti kathamucyateJanityepyapramāṇateti etacca nityānityayoḥ sādhāraṇameva b  sādhanam  anityatāprakramaṇe tuparasya pramāṇaparyeṣaṇā pravarteta  tadupanyāsanidānatvamātreṇānityaśabdānuvādaḥ  na punaḥasāvanitya eva bhagavān asmābhiriṣyate  tathā hi eko vibhuḥ sarvavidekabuddhisamāśrayaḥ śāśvata īśvarākhyaḥ pramāṇamiṣṭo jagato vidhātā svargāpavargāthibhirarthanīyaḥ atrocyate  kimebhireva hetubhirupadiṣṭaguṇagaṇāgārapuruṣātiśayasādhanamanorathotha hetvantarabalāt  tatra na tāvadādyaḥ pakṣaḥ  tathā hi yat sādhanaṃ yāvatīmartha gati vyāpnoti tatastāvatyeva sidhyati nārthāntaram  na hi yāvānicchayā vyāptorthaḥtāvati pramāṇasya sāmarthyam  api tu yāvati pramāṇasya sāmarthyam tāvatorthasyatannimittā siddhiḥ  na ca kāryatvādi cetanapūrvakatvena vyāpyamānamapi tadekatvādiniyatāṃ matimutpādayituṃ śaktam tadviśeṣaṇe vyāpterevāpratīte anyathā viparītarūpa jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvaloniścayasyāpi prasaṅgāt  na hi dahanasāmānyena vyāptaṃ dhūmamupalabhya kaścid visphuratpañcavarṇaśikhākalāpakamanīyamanalamanumātumīśaḥ nanu tathāpi deśakālaviśeṣa viśeṣaṇamanumimīta eva pakṣadharmatābalāt evaṃbhūdharādāvapi buddhimadadhiṣṭhānādhīnaṃ kāryatvamupalabdhavatobhimatasiddhiradhikaraṇasiddhāntanyāyena bhaviṣyatīti cetna sāmarthyānupapatteḥ  yathā hyetaddeśakālena vahninājanyamānasya na taddeśakālatvamiti dhūmādyanumāne sāmarthyam na tathā cetayiturekatvasarvajñatvādikamantareṇa tarūṇāṃ vāsaniveśādyanupapattimākalayāmaḥ  tataḥ pakṣadharmaṃtābalāt kulālādī tadutpādanasamarthatvasiddhirapi bhavantī nābhimataṃ viśeṣamavalambitumalam nanu yadi bhūdharādinirmāṇasamartha siddhaḥ kimaparaṃ prārthyate  tat kimidānīmapariniṣṭhitavācyarūpeṇa vācakamātreṇa parituṣṭiḥ  na hyevamabhimataprastutavastusiddhiḥ utpādanavyāpāro hi notpitsukāryaṃ prati niyataprāgbhāvitvamātrādatiriktaḥ  sa cācetanasādhāraṇo buddherapi naikasarvagatvādiviśeṣapratibaddhaḥ siddhaḥ  tato vivakṣitasādhyāpekṣayā vacanamātrasiddhayā na kiñcit kaḥ punarevaṃ pratijānāti sarvajñapūrvakā  parvatādaya iti  api tu buddhimaddhetukāityāśaṅkaya sādhanenāntarupahasannāhasthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthānaviśeṣārthakriyādiṣu iṣṭasiddhiriti sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇakarmanirmito hi samasto vasturāśiriṣyate  karmaṃ cācetanasvabhāvamiti sakalajñānahetavosidhyantaḥ sindhubhūdharādayaḥ kimaniṣṭamasmākamāvahantītibhāvaḥ  tanmātrasādhyābhiprāye ca virodhāsiddheḥ sādhanopanyāsavaiyarthyaprasaṅgaḥ  tasmātupāttaviśeṣa evānena a sādhya  na ca tatra sādhanasāmarthyamityuktam  astutarhi sādhanāntarādeva tathā siddhiriti dvitīyapakṣāpekṣayā niścayābhāvamudbhāvayannāhaasiddhirveti na pramāṇāntaraṃ na vā hetvantaramasti yatoyaṃ niścayaḥ syādityarthaḥ  athavāatīndriyatvenādhyakṣāsaṃbhavādanumānamabhyarthanīyam tadarthaṃ ca sarvaṃ hetumadhikṛtyāhaīśvaravādādhikāre vārtika saptaślokī vyākhyānamasiddhirveti uktānumānato hi prativādisādhāraṇasarvaṃkṛccetanamātre siddhepi viśeṣaśaṃsīna kaściddheturyo na svarūpāsiddhonyatra sattāyāḥ tanmātrasattātirekiṇi dharmenumānasyānavasarāt  sattā tu kṣaṇabhaṅgaśaṃsinīti nityaikatvāpekṣayā āhaasiddhirveti viparītasiddhirityarthaḥ  adharmādivat paryudāsena nityepi hi parasādhanavaddūṣaṇasyābhimatatvāt prastāvamātraphalatvādanityokteḥ  vyāpitvāpekṣayā anekāntamadhyāhaasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānta iti vyāptittrasya paramārthatobhāvādeva dṛṣṭānte darśanābhāvānna tena kasyacid dharmasyavyāpti sidhyatītyuktaṃ bhavati  sarvabodhasya tu bhāvepi na vyāpakatvapratītiḥ kuta ityāhadṛṣṭānte saṃśayothavāiti arvāgdarśanena viśeṣaniṣṭhatayā vastuto niścetumaśakyatvāt  tasmādupagītaguṇasyayathoktasādhanebhyo na sākṣānnādhikaraṇasiddhāntanyāyena nāpi sādhanāntarāt siddhiḥiti siddhaḥ sādhakapramāṇavirahaḥ  tadviśeṣavirahiṇi viṣṭasiddhiriti athavā kāryatvādihetuṣūpanyasteṣu sādhyasāmānya viśeṣabhāvena vikalpa itisiddhirasiddhiyāha  tatra karmavāditāprasiddhayā siddhasādhanaṃ vyaktamitya siddhinibandhanaṃviśeṣenugamābhāvamādarśayannāhaasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayothavāiti sādhyasyeti prakṛtam  tatra vibhutvādipratyanīkadharmaṇa kulālāderavivādena siddheḥasiddhiriṣṭasya dṛṣṭānte  atha dehātiriktabhāgasyānisargaduvibhāvasya vaibhavādikamiṣṭamiti matistathāpi saṃśayostu kimidānīmatra nirbandheneti bhāvaḥ sāmānya siddhasādhyatetijñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalītasmāt sādhyavikalpātsandigdhasādhyadharmatvād vā na dṛṣṭānte sādhyena kāryatvādervyāptiriti viśeṣasyāsiddhereva anekāntastu hetudoṣaḥ nanu dhūmānugamepiviśeṣenugamābhāvaḥ sāmānye siddhasādhyatā iti samāno nyāyaḥ tadanayornaikaniyataṃ prāmāṇyamanyad veti  niyataṃ cet  na samīcīnamālocitam  tathā hi na tāvadviśeṣasiddhimavadhūya prāmāṇyamanumānamanubhavatītisiddham  sa tu viśeṣaḥ pakṣāyogavyavacchedamātralakṣaṇastadatiriktaśca saṃbhavati yathāagniratra dhūmāt evaṃrūpo vā  tatra prathamāpahnave syādanumānasyāpalāpaḥ tanmūlatvādatiriktasiddherapi  na cāsau tathānvayānusaraṇamantareṇāpi nirasituṃ śakyaḥ  pakṣadharmohi yatpratibaddhaḥ siddhaḥ sa tena dharmiṇamaviyuktamanādarśayan svarūpasattayaiva bviyujyeta yadi paraṃ kāryahetvadhikāreṇa kālādyapekṣātiricyate  dvitīya siddhistutanmātrasādhyeti tajjanyaviśeṣagrahaṇanāntarīyakatayānvayānusaraṇamantareṇābhavantyapinānumānāpalāpāya prabhavati tadviśeṣavirahiṇā dharmeṇāyogavyavacchedasiddhathāpitasyāścaritārthatvāt  anumānaviśeṣāpalāpastu syāt yathā kaścit pañcavarṇaśikhaṃśikhinamanumātumabhipretya vahniratra dhūmāditi sādhane pareṇa siddhasādhanānanugamābhyāmabhiyujyamānastarhi dhūmamātrocchedeneha cānumānamapi na syāditi bruvāṇa śobheta na tvanumānoccheda eva syāt tadaiva dahanasāmānyānumānasya tena pramāṇīkriyamāṇatvāt  tasmātpakṣāyogavyavacchedamātrabhedena dūṣaṇam iṣṭasiddhabanvayābhāvāvatirikteṣu dūṣaṇam naito dūṣaṇatvedūṣaṇatve vā niyatau viṣayabhedena tu dvayī sthitiriti matam tadvadihāpi jaladhibhūdharādī buddhimadadhiṣṭhānāyogavyavacchedamaṅgīkṛtya vivakṣitaviśeṣāntarāpekṣayā to dūṣaṇamudbhāvayataścitrakāntiśikhānumānoccheda eva prasañjayitumāñjasaḥnānumānocchedaḥ  tatonumāna viśeṣāpekṣayā naikaniyataṃ prāmāṇyamaprāmāṇyaṃ veti yuktaṃna sāmānyena īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam nanu cādyāpi bhedonvayamanapekṣyaiva siddha iti bhedāntare kaḥ pratirodhaḥ  na vainiranvayā kāpi siddhirasti  sāmānyānvaya eva tu taṃ viśeṣamanākṛṣya nāvasthātuṃśaktaḥ  na caivaṃ viśeṣāntarepi tasyāvaśyaṃ śaktiriti śakyam yathopavarṇitaṃ prākanyathā pañcavarṇaśikhādyanumānasya durnivāratvāt  atrāsaṃbhavādikṣepaṇameka cittatvādimati puruṣepi samānam  tādṛganumānodgārastatrāpi samānaḥ  tasmādatireka viśeṣaśaṃsināvaśyamanenānvayaḥ pradarśanīya iti tadabhāvādanekānta eva  buddhimanmātrasādhaneca siddhasādhanamiti sthitam syādetat  buddhimāniti na caitanyamātravān api tupādānādyabhijñaḥ prayatnavān vābhimataḥ tena cānvayo ghaṭādikārye siddha iti bhūdharādāvapi kāryatvamupalabhyamānaṃ tādṛśameva kartāramupasthāpayatīti noktobhayadoṣaḥ  tathā hi tadupādānādyabhijñaityeva sarvajñaḥ deśakālaniyataśca na tadbheda upādīyamāna kāryagrāmanirvartanasamartha syātiti nityatvavibhutvādayopi taddharmāḥ siddhā iti cet  seyaṃ chinnamūla viṭapasyaphalabhogapratyāśā  ekatve hi siddhe siddhireṣāṃ guṇānām anyathā bhinnadeśakālasyakāryasthānekakṛtau saṃbhāvyamānāyāṃ kasya vaibhavādayaḥ svasvavyāpāraviṣayamātravedanāccakasya sārvajñamiti ekatve siddhe  a  sādhyamaśeṣamākṛṣyeta na ca tanniścaye kiñcinnibandhanamasti  na ca kṣityādinirmāṇasamartha siddha ityekavacanaprayogapatanāt tatsiddhiḥpratibandhābhāvāt  pratibandhe vā siddhaikatvaḥ paraḥ kathamenamupekṣeta  jātyapekṣayā tusyādapīti na nirbandhaḥ aparāparadhūmapramitasyeva vahnaḥ  na ca vicitrepi citrakarmaṇisajātīya rekhādyanugamā dekakartṛsiddhivat kāryabhedeṣu guṇaviśeṣānugamāt tadekatvasiddhiḥtathāvidhasya kasyacidanugatasyaivānupalabdheḥ  upālabhyamānaṃ ca kāryatvavastutvādi naikatvasādhanaṃ citravadeva  guṇāntarasaṃbhavepi hi sadṛśa eko vā karteti sandeha eva kiṃpunastadabhāvepyekaniścayaḥ  niyatamidamabhitticitrakarmaiva yadabhedāniścaye sarvajñatvādivyavasīyata iti itarastvāha eva tvamapi kāryotpattyaivāvagantavyam  katham  bahūnāṃ vyāhatamanasāṃ svātantryeṇa parasparavirodhena mitha svānukūlābhiprāyānavabodhena yugapat kāryānutpattiḥ utpannasya vilopanādiprasaṅgaśca syāditi jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvaloatra cintyate bahubhiḥ karaṇe yugapat kāryānutpattiriti bhinnakālānāṃ bhinnadeśānāṃ kāryānutpattirvivakṣitā ekasyaiva vā mahāvayavinaḥ kṣitidharādirūpasyeti pakṣaḥ tatra naikatrāpyanekena karaṇe utpattivirodhaṃ paśyāmaḥ  yathā hyekasya pravṛttistathānyeṣāmapisyād valmīkavat  kiṃ prayojanamabhisandhāya teṣāṃ pravṛttiriti cet  na vicitravṛtti tvānmanasāṃ pravṛttinibandhasya viśeṣaniścāyanāśakteḥ  anyatheśvarasyaiva kimabhipretyeti cintānirbandho nirvoḍhuṃ na śakyaḥ  śakyo vā anyeṣāmabhipretādibādhyatāvadhāraṇapaṭīyasām na mṛduprakṛterīśvarasya nāpi bahūnāṃ parasparavyātiniyama upapādayituṃ śakyaḥ valmīkaukasāmekārambhadarśanāt  puruṣāṇāmahamahamikayā saṃbhāvyata eva taditi cet  sadvivekino hyekakāryārambhiṇaḥ santyapīti tathāvidhairaparairapyatipracuratarairekasya krameṇa sthavīyasaḥ karaṇesaṃbhavini kosmākaṃ nareṣvanurodha  nāpi yugandharāderyugapanniṣpattiḥ vanacidupalabdhāyata ekasyaiva kasyacicchakti saṃbhāvyate  na cāhamahamikayā puruṣeṣvapi vyāghāta niyamaḥ śakyanirvāhaḥ parasparāvyāghātena puruṣasya virodhadvayasyānupapatteḥ  tasmātsaṃbhāvanāmātrametat na pramāṇavartma ityupanyāsamarhati nānekeneṃka mainākāde karaṇamiti samayamātrānusmṛtirvā nanvanekatrāpi pradhānabhūtenekena bhāvyaṃ balīyasā sūtradhāravat senānīvad vāatastasyaiva kartṛtvamitareṣāṃ tadanuvatitvāditi cet  b na tatrāpi niyamābhāvāt svasvaprayojanānurodhena svatantrāṇāmapi keṣāñcideka se tvādighaṭanādarśanāt tatrāpi kaścideva pradhāna prayojaka ityapi nāsti anekasya tathā hṛdayotkalikāyānivārakābhāvāt apradhānasyāpi vā prayojakatvasaṃbhavāt  na tāvataiva prādhānyaṃlokavirodhāt  kiṃ ca sūtradhārasthānīyāparimitaikaikajanasanāthaiḥ sārthairaparimitairevakhaṇḍaśaḥ sthūlārambhasaṃbhavepi kā nāma kāmasiddhiḥ  etena valmīkajantuṣu mukhyopanyāsaḥ pratyuktaḥ api ca yathekahṛdayānuvartibhiranekairabhinirmīyamānasya prāsādasya sukhopadhānāvayavasanniveśaviśeṣa upalabhyate na tathā visaṃsthūlasthūlaśilājālakaliteṣu kulagiriṣvapi yena tathaivekapradhānabhūtapuruṣapūrvakatvameṣāmapi syāt  tasmādekaikakailāsādisampādane bādhitumaśakyonekavyāpāraḥ kathamaparadūrāntarānekadeśakālakaliteṣu bhāveṣubādhya īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyānamāgamā dekatvasiddhistahi iti cet  soyaṃ sannipātāpannasya sapai rakṣābandhavidhirabādhaka eva bauddhānadhikṛtyāgamavicāraikacaturacetasaḥ  yadi hi parīkṣāgamagrahaḥtadāyameva parīkṣākāla iti kastadanurodhodhunaiva  atha parīkṣānapekṣaḥ tadāpi tataevābhimatasamastavastusiddhirastu kimanumānopanyāsavyasanena prayāsaikasāreṇa  kaṣṭo hihetuśodhanavyavasāya sūkṣmaprativedhavidhurabuddhīnāma sukarastu śāstraikadeśapāṭhenābhimatalābhaḥ yadapya yameva vādī prāmāṇyamāgamānāṃ samarthayan na hyapramāṇatve samastāśramiṇāṃsaṃvādo nāma tasyāpramāṇatve kasyacidaprāmāṇyabodhena visaṃvādasyāpi saṃbhāvyatvātsaṃvādaniyamasya ca pramāṇeṣveva pratyakṣādiṣūpapatteriti nāpramāṇāni ṛgyajusāmānisamastāśramiṇāṃ saṃvādijñānasādhanatvāt pratyakṣādivadityādi pañcālakaṃ paṭhati tadapiśiṣyasamitāvevopayujyate  tathā hi saṃvādo nāma pramāṇāntarasaṅgatirarthakriyā vāsyāt na ca tadubhayamapisahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥṛ ve   sa vetti viśvaṃ na ca tasya vettā tula śvetā upa  dyāvābhūmi janayan deva eka āsīttula saiva   ityādivākyārtheṣu svargasādhanāgniṣṭomādau vā kasyacit saṃbhavati āśramiṇastāvad yathaikasya eko vibhuḥ śāśvataḥ sraṣṭā jagatostīti matiḥtathānyasyāpi  tadanurūpānuṣṭhānaṃ ceti cet  sā punareṣāṃ matistadekāgamaprabhavā tādṛganyaprabhavā vā ākasmika vikalpamātrarūpā vā syāt na tu pratyakṣānumānarūpā anāśramiṇāmadhyavakāśaprasaṅgāt pratyakṣādeḥ puruṣāntarai a anaparādhāt  āgamāśrayaṃtu jñānamatatonādṛtavato na syāt bhavāntarābhyāsavāsanāvaśād vā saṃbhavetnānyasyeti yuktam  tatredaṃ svatantratayā na pramāṇam satyasati vā vastuni saṃbhavinaḥabhyāsāt prasūteḥ  tadāgamaprabhavatvena pramāṇāntarasaṅgatiruktā bhavati tādṛkprabhavatvāt tasyāpyaprāmāṇyāt  tadasiddhaṃ yadasiddhena sādhyata iti nyāyaḥ tasmātajñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalautādṛksamayānusmaraṇamātrametadevambhūtaḥ kaścidastīti  kiṃ ca āśrama ityapi darśanamātraṃvidmaḥ tataśca samastāśramiṇāmiti viśeṣaṇāsiddhiḥ bauddhadigambarāde saṃvādāsiddheḥ katipayasaṃvādaśca viparītamatepyastīti nopanyāsaḥ saphalaḥ  ataeva visaṃvādasyātyanta nivṛttirasiddhā yataḥ prāmāṇyamavatiṣṭheta abhimatamāśramiṇāṃ tvanādikālapravṛttasamānasaṃmohasāmarthyādapi syāditi yatkiñcidetat tasmādekatrāpimandarādābaparimitapuruṣavyāpāraviṣayabhāgopādānādivedināṃprayatnavatāṃ katamaḥ sarvavedī  bhinnadeśakālaiśca tādṛśāṃ karaṇe kuto nityavibhutvādayaḥ na cādṛṣṭabhāgajñānāvakāśaḥ tadantareṇāpi kumbhakāreṇa svavyāpāraviṣayasya niṣpādanopalabdheḥ  na ca bahubhirutpāditasyāvaśyaṃ vilopanādiprasaṅge saṅgatiḥ kāciditi ekatvāpāyenumṛtatvamanivāryaṃ sarvajñatvādonāmanumatamiti  evaṃ ca sati etadapyanibandhanamevayadāha  teṣāṃ bahutve sarvajñatve sati sarvakartṛkatvāt taddeśakālapratiniyateṣu kāryeṣu pravṛttauyogapadyapramāṇābhāvāditi sarvajñānakriyayorekādhārāsiddheḥ  ataevaikanirākaraṇe bahutarādyapagamaprasaṅgopi na bādhakaḥ  yadi hi sarvajñāḥ sarvakartāraśca bahavaḥ siddheyurekanirākaraṇamevānupayogi syāt bahutaraprayāsaścābhyupagato bhavati  yadā punaranekamekaikajanakaṃvalmīkajantuvajjantujātamāsajyate prakṛtaguṇāsaṃsparśi tadā kā nāma hāniḥ  na hitadā ta evasvargāpavargāthiṃbhirarthanīyāḥbhaveyuritietena yopi manyate bhavadīyasarvajñavadīśvaropyaneka eva bhaviṣyatīti tadapianavakāśam sarvakriyādhikaraṇasyaikasyāpyasiddheḥ  asmākaṃ tu na sarvakriyayā sarvabodha siddhiḥ ki tvabhyāsāt  sa ca sakalasākṣātkartavyākāravikalpasaṃbhavāt saṃbhavānumānamanvetīti tādṛksārvajñyasiddhiryathaikasya tathānyasyāpi syādiṣyate vā ityadoṣaḥ abhyāsādeva tarhi sarvanirmāṇamapi bhaviṣyatīti cet na aśakyatvāt  tathāhi sthāvarajīvajananaṃ jaṅgamāpattirvā nābhyāsaphalam  pariśiṣṭapratikṛtinirmāṇakalpanāyāmapi b kaścidevamapi syāditi syāt  na tu idameva paridṛśyamānaṃ bhavatuvanādikaṃ na tatheti niścayaḥ viśeṣoddeśena saṃbhavānumānasyāpravṛtteḥ  tatrāpi durlabhaīśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyānambāhyopakaraṇasaṃbhavātiśayaparādhīno na cittamātraparāvṛttivat sukarastadabhyāsa itiadhyavasāyaḥ prabhāvātiśayasahāyāpekṣāyāṃ ki śilpena  na tadantareṇa tasya śaktiritiapramāṇakam tathaivānyatra darśanāditi cet  na dṛṣṭakrameṇa garbhasthaśarīrādinirmāṇaprāpteḥ  tadavaśyaṃ prabhāvetaraḥ  na ca tādṛkprabhāvādhigataye mārgasya kaścinniścayaḥ  astuvā vyāpiśilpasiddhirādiśabdasaṃgrāhyaścābhyāsa  tathāpyāha sanniveśādiṣu hetuṣuiṣṭasyā kartṛtvasya siddhirasiddhirvā asiddhireva upayogābhāvāt na hi narakādinā tāvat kaścidupayogaḥ saṃvittyānuṣṭhātuḥ sukhopakaraṇamātrasṛṣṭāvapi nārthaḥ śrameṇa svaśreyasaḥ saṃbhave hi tānyanyathā bhavanti bhūtāni vā sukhamādhāsyanti  yadi paraṃ tanmārgamaviduṣāṃ tadupadeśa evānugrahakaraḥ atastadarthaṃ mārgasākṣātkaraṇābhyāsa eva śreyāniti vaiyarthyānadhyavasāyābhyāṃ nābhyāsaḥ  tarhi pratiparamāṇujñānābhyāsepi kathaṃ tadvad vā sarvakaraṇepi na kṣatirityāha sarvasarvavididṛṣṭānte saṃśayothavāiti upayuktasarvajñapakṣasya mukhyatayā vakṣyamāṇatvāt  athavā vaiyarthyānadhyavasāyayostatrasaṃśayo nābhāvaniścaya ityarthaḥ  uddeśaścānyatropadarśanamiti na pareṇa saha sāmyam tataḥ prakṛtahetubhyaḥ prayatnavatāṃ siddhāvapi na kṣatiriti nanu prayatnavatā jantujātena janitā gandhamādanādaya iti bhavatāmaniṣṭameva tataḥprakārāntarābhāvenānekato nivartamānaḥ prayatnavāneka eva sakalakāryakartā sidhyan sarvajñatvādikamapi pratyujjīvayatīti cet  naitadasti vastupratibandhānupapattericchāyāḥ tatkṛtāyā anekato nivṛtterasādhanatvāt  yadi ca kathañcidasau na svīkurute svīkārayituṃtarhi caraṇamadanādinārādhanīya  prativādītināyaṃ nyāya  svatantrasya prasaṅgopi na saṅgataḥ prasaukyamapāyesya na hyanekatvamīhitam viparyaya paryavasāyivyāpāratvāt tasyeti nanūbhayathāpi tāvat parasyāniṣṭameva na hi sattvalokaḥ sakalopi prayatnadvāreṇakāraṇamiṣyate api tu cetanālakṣaṇakarmādhipatyamātreṇa tataḥ prayatnavannāntarīyakaṃjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalokāryatvamekamanekaṃ vā prayatnavantamantike dadhānaṃ sādhanamaniṣṭasyaiveti cet  tat kimi dānīṃ parāniṣṭamātrasiddhaye sādhanamupanyastam kiṃ nu svasādhyasiddhaye  tatra ca pareṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvātmana iti na a  kiñcit sādhanopanyāsaphalamiti vaktumāhasthityā pravṛttyādiṣu iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvāiti  samānamidamubhayasādhanāṅgavacanatvanibandhanamānarthakyāditi bhāvaḥ  na ca paraeva sādhanavādī yatosya dvidhāniṣṭamāpādyamānaṃ śobheta  aniṣṭamadhyasya prakaraṇāpannaṃnityaikasarvajñatve tattvameva viśvasyāpādayitumārabdhaṃ na yatkiñciditi  evaṃ tarhi sādhanopa nyāsepi kimasiddhinibandhana miti vaktavyam yatpunaruktamviśeṣenugamābhāvaiti tatra yadyapi sarvagasarvaṃjñatvādibhiranvayesiddhisaṃśayau yathāyogam tathāpyekatvenamā bhūtām tadekaprayatnavat kartṛsiddhau siddhamaśeṣaṃ sādhyam  dṛṣṭaśca kulāla ekonekaghaṭapiṭharādikāraka ityāśaṅkaya ekatvepyanvayamāpādayannāhadṛṣṭānteiti  asiddhiriti vartate  ayamabhiprāyaḥ  na prakṛtameva ghaṭapiṭharādikāryamekenakṛtamiti sarvasya tathābhāvaḥ  tatrānekakulālādivyāpāra sphuṭamavadhāryate  tat kutaekena yatnavatā dṛṣṭakāryāṇāmanvaya iti  athavā kulālo nāmaikaḥ kaścidasti bhūtabhautikasaṃvittirāśirayaṃ kumbhakārādiprajñaptiviṣayaḥ karacaraṇasamudāyo veti  vastutaḥkenaikena karaṇaṃ kumbhāderupalambhagocara ityarthaḥ atha kimanena nirbandhena  yādṛśa eva kaścidekavyahāragocaro dṛṣṭaḥ tādṛśaḥsaṃhatasvabhāva evaikaḥ kartā sarvasyopādānādyabhijñaḥ sidhyan sarvajña eva sidhyati  tatoguṇāntaratiraskārepi tāvataivopādeyatvamubhayapuruṣārthaśaṃsitirasyopapadyata itikācit kṣatiriti atrāpi pakṣe tenaiva sarvemī kāryatvādihetavo vyabhicāriṇa itivyaktamanaikāntikatvamabhipretyāhanaīśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamsaṃśayothavāiti  sādhyasyeti śeṣaḥ  kulālavat saṃghātamātratayā kāryatvasanniveśādibhāvepi prayatna vatkartṛpūrvaṃkatvasyābhāvāt etadabhāvepi vā tasya bhāvāt  tatrāpyanyatkārakeṣṭīvā anavasthānādapratipattiḥ nanu cācetanasvabhāvaḥ svayamutpattau paraṃ cotpādayituṃ prayatnavantamapekṣate  sa tusvayameva tathāvidhabuddhayādhāra iti kimapareṇa  na hi jaḍā ghaṭādayaḥ prakāśamapekṣantaiti prakāśenāpyaparaḥ prakāśopekṣitavya ityasti niyamaḥ  tataḥ keyamanavastheti evaṃ tahi kulālasaṃjñita eva prayatnavān buddhīndriyādikalāpaḥ kathamaparamapekṣate tasmāccetanocetano vā kalāpaḥ svabhāvenaivāparacetanamapekṣya jāyate janayati vetyupagantavyamityanavasthaiva  atha cetanavargaścetanāntaranirapekṣa eveṣyate tadā ghaṭādivartinaḥkāryatvādayobhimatakārakādhiṣṭhāyaka viparītanāntarīyakāḥ sidhyanto na virodhadūṣaṇaparihāreṇa sthitimanubhaveyuḥ  tathāvidhādhiṣṭhānasvīkāre tu svabhāvaviprakarṣādanupalabdhāvapi tadvyāpāra saṃbhāvanāyāṃ na b tadviparītadṛṣṭaikanāntarīyakatvameṣāmitiviparyayavyāpterabhāvādabhāvo viruddhavyavahārasya syāt  tadāpi yadi kāryakāraṇavyavasthānāya vyatirekacintācaturaḥ kaścinna pratyavasthānamādriyate na cedānīṃ tadā rabdhamityāstāṃ tāvattat kimanena nirbandhena  nirbaṃndhe vā virodhyadhyakṣasthūladoṣāvatāraprasaṅgāttathāpyasiddhirveti viparītasiddhiryojayiṣyata iti sāntargarvo gajanimīlitenaiva vāḍavadhīrya yathaivānena sarvakāryotpattau nimittakāraṇamīśvaro gṛhītaḥ tathainaṃ saṃbhāvya cetanasyāpi cetanāntarāpekṣāyāmanabasthānabhī rostenaivāvyabhicārānāśritya saṃśayamāha  athaprayatnavānapi kulālo na svaśarīre kiṃ tu kumbhādau tataḥ svaśarīrasiddhaye kiṃ naparamapekṣeta  tarhīśvarābhimatopi parakaraṇaprayatnavān na svaśarīra eva svātmanikāritravirodhāditi kiṃ na paramapekṣeta  na cāpekṣate  tato yadarthakāri kāryādi vātatpratiyatnavadadhiṣṭhitamiti tattenaiva vyabhicārīti saṃśayasiddhiḥ nanu tasya śarīrameva nāstīti kutonekānta eṣaḥ  tadetat prakaraṇavismaraṇaphalam  tathā hyanvayopadarśanasamīyā kulāle sāṃvṛtamekatvamaṅgīkṛtya tādṛksāṃvṛtaikapuruṣanirmeyatvaṃ jagato bhavataiva svīkṛtamityayamasmākamavakāśaḥ  yadi tu vāstavamevajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalīekatvaṃ śarīrasahacāraviruddhamanurudhyate na tarhi sāṃvṛtamekatvamupanetavyaṃ dṛṣṭānte vyāpakatvenakāryāde  nāpi nāmamātrapareṇa tena vyāptā tattvatastathāsiddhipratyāśā phalavatī  nakhalu dahanopacaritamāṇavakapratibaddhavacanaviśeṣādikāryamupalabhya pāramārthikaṃ kaściddahanamanumīyate askhalansī ekapratītiḥ puruṣāvayavinīti cet  kaḥ punariha sākṣādupacāratvamāha  atasmiṃstadvyavahārastu dvayoḥ samāna ityucyate  śarīratvevayavabādhakātekādhyavasāyasya bhramatvamavasātavyam sattvepi vāvayatrinaḥ śarīrāvayavī karādyavayavā buddhirityeṣa kalāpa ekaśabdābhidheyaḥ bhūtādikalāpo vetyapāramārthikatvaṃ siddhamadhiṣṭhātuḥ sthādetat  puruṣa eva tatrādhiṣṭhātā kartā vā sa ca śarīrādibhyo labdhavyatireka eka eveti cet saṃdṛṣṭakā raṇakalāpakṛtepi kāryajanmanyadṛṣṭamaparaṃ parikalpyate yat tatrāpi dṛṣṭamavadhūya tadeva taccanānekamityanavardhirvividho vimohaḥ adṛṣṭasya tāvad bhāva eva duravadhāraḥ sahajavaiṣamyādatrānumānasyetyuktam tasyāpi dṛṣṭānupalambhasacivapratyakṣasādhya kāraṇabhāvaḥ  sa ca dṛṣṭavyavacchedena tasyaiva anyathā karacaraṇāderapi vyāpārasaṃbhave tasyāpyanumānaprasaṅge punaḥ sa eva vyabhicāraḥ anyathā puruṣasyāpyanumānamanibandhanaṃ syāt  etena caitanyasantānasyaikapuruṣatva parikalpanaṃ pratyuktam asyāpi karacaraṇādisahakṛtasyaiva a śaktipratīteḥ kāryāttattvatta evānumānaprasaṅgo dhūmādiva sendhanaśikhinaḥ caitanyamātreṇa vyāptirgṛhyate nāpareṇāpīti cet  na samānanyāyatayā vibhāgasya kartumaśakyatvāditi  tadayaṃ buddhiśarīrāvyatirekiṇa kāraṇatāmanyayogavyavacchedenaiva vaktumarhati yatastanmātramanumātumapratibandhena śaknuyāt pāramārthikaikatvenaca vyāpti grahītum  tathā ca sati dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭānvayavyatirekaṃ kārakasamudāyamapahāyānyadevakāraṇaṃ kalpitamityayamaparo dhikkāraḥ  tadapi yadi kathañcidakaṃ syād viphala sakaloīśvaravādādhikāre vārtika saptaślokī vyākhyānamyana ityekameva parikalpanoyamityākāśakamalaparimalākṛṣṭamadhukarakolāhalaprāyamidamakhilamākalayāmaḥ tadalaṃ dehādivyatiriktopakṣepeṇa  tasmāt prayatnavataḥ karturekatvena vyāptirna mukhyākartṛvācyasya kulālādestattvata ekatvānupapatteḥ  sāṃvṛtāśraye ca tādṛśasyaivānumānaprasaṅgenateneva vyabhicāraḥ kāryatvāderiti saṃśayaḥ sādhyasyetyuktam nanu tathāpi tādṛśaḥsādhyasyāsiddhau kena vyabhicāra siddhau ca vyabhicāraḥkiṃ kariṣyati  vyabhicārādasiddhireveti cet  asiddhau tahi vyabhicāropi nāstītikutosiddhiriti siddhiriti vā vyavatiṣṭhate  kāryatvādeśca vastudharmasya vastusanneva dharmībhavitumarhatīti na codyam abhyupagamavirodhasthānena krameṇa pratipādayitumārabdhatvāttattvataḥ  asti cāsau sādhyasya sādhanatrairūpyeṇa trirūpasādhanasya ca yathābhimatasādhyenatatra sādhyasattve vipakṣavyatirekasyāsattvāt svābhyupagamasiddhatayā pramāṇasiddhamitisādhāraṇānaikāntikamucyatetatrābhyupāyaḥ kāryāṅgamiti vacanāt  parābhyupagama khalu na pramāṇamiti yuktam tadbādhanāyaiva pravṛtteḥ ataeva na svatantrahetāvasyāśrayaḥ  prasaṅgasya ca viparyaṃya eva phalam  svopagamasyatvapramāṇatve vacanoccāraṇameva na syāt  svadṛṣṭārthaprakāśanaṃ ca vacanaṃ parārthānumānāt na caivaṃ svadṛṣṭarūpa trayaprakāśanamanena kṛtaṃ bhavatīti tadvādinosādhanāṅgavacanaṃ nigrahasthānamucitam  parasya tu doṣodbhāvanameveti sthitam  athavā anvayaghaṭanārthamevaikenakaraṇamupanītamāśaṅkayāhadṛṣṭānte saṃśayothavāpra vā  iti  dṛṣṭāntesiddhireva tāvadekena karaṇasya  siddhāvapi vā sandeha eva kasya yadarthamupanīyate dṛṣṭāntaḥ  sarvopasaṃhāravatyā vyāpteriti yāvat  tathā hi na dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭamityeva yasya kasyacid vastuno vyāpyavyāpakabhāvapratītiḥ atiprasaṅgāt api tupratibandhasiddheḥ  na ceha kiñcinnibandhanamastīti sādhyadharmaṇi sidhyantopi kartṛtvādayo naikatvaniyatamātmānamātanvantīti viparyaṃye bādhakapramāṇābhāvāt prayatnavatkartṛjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvaloniyatā b api kāryatvādaya ekakartṛṛtve sādhye sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatayāsaṃśaya hetava eveti tathā ca śaṃkara evāha na karturekatvenācetanopādānatvasyāvyabhicāra ityādi yat punarāha na caivamacetanopādānatvasya prayatnavadadhiṣṭhānamātreṇa vyabhicāra iti natanmātreṇa prastute kaścidupayogaḥ  vivādādhāradharmasiddhestatsiddhau pratibaddhatvasya pūrvaṃpratipādanāditi  prathamaḥ khaṇḍaḥ tadevaṃ sādhyaviśeṣāpekṣayā vyāptidūṣaṇamabhidhāya prayatnavanmātrepyabhidhātuṃvitarkayannāhasthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthāna viśeṣārthakriyādiṣu iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayothavā iti  dṛṣṭonto dṛṣṭāntaḥ siddhānta iti yorthaḥ prayatnavanmātreṇa vyāpteḥ siddhatvātekānekarūpānatikramāñca vastunaḥ  sthitvā pravṛttyādiṣūpanyasteṣu vādina iṣṭasiddhiḥ kimastuekatvapakṣe asiddhimātraṃ vānekatve atha vyāptireva nāstīti siddhānte saṃśaya evaubhayatrāpīti praśnārthaḥ atra cānantaramabhedasādhanādhikāreṇa sandigdha vipakṣavyāvṛttikatvodbhāvanenadattamevottaram  atastṛtīya eva pakṣaḥ  na hi prayatnopayogamantareṇāpi kāryajanmanisaṃbhāvyamāne bādhakaṃ kiñcidālocayāmaḥ  tat kutastatra niyamaḥ kāryāde  athakāladeśādyaniyamaprasaṅgo bādhakaḥ  tadayuktam yataḥ pratiniyataśakterasarvakālabhāvinaḥsvakāraṇāyattasannidheḥ kāraṇadaśāviśeṣasya vyatirekepi vyatirekaḥ kāryasya saṃbhavannaprayatnavannāntarīyakatvamupakalpayituṃ kalpate  sarvaṃthā hetvanapekṣāyāṃ tadbādhakamupapadyamānaṃkāryasya hetumātreṇa vyāpti sādhayet  na tu hetuviśeṣeṇa prayatnavatā nanu kāraṇaṃ nāma sarvatra kalāpa eva saca na vyagrāvasthāyām  tatsaṃhatiścaprayatnavantamantareṇa yadi syāt nityameva syāt  evaṃ deśepi vācyam  tataścasa eva deśakālaniyamaprasaṅga iti caitanyanirapekṣatvena kalāpakāryatvasya vyāpakasyābhāvenakāryatvādayosaṃbhavantaḥ prayatnavadapekṣatvena vyāpyanta iti cet  evaṃ tarhi sopi prayatna vān yadi kṣaṇika prādeśikaśca tatkṣaṇaikadeśatvameva sarvakāryagrāmasya syāditi sanātanaevāṅgīkartavyo vyāpī ca  tataśca sa eva deśakālāniyamodyāpi prasakta itikimasyopagamena  atha sodṛṣṭamapekṣya janayanniyataṃ janayet  jaḍānāṃ tu nādṛṣṭaṃlocana miti evaṃ tarhi tadadṛṣṭaparipākasahāyā eva pratyayā niyatamutpādayiṣyanti nirālocāapīti kiṃ caitanyeneti cet  evaṃ bruvataḥ kulālāderapi vaiyarthyaprasaṅgaḥ na hi tatrāpinādṛṣṭamasti sahakāri  na caivam  tasmād viparyayaḥ  yā yā sāmagrī sā nādṛṣṭāpekṣayā puruṣaprayatnaṃ viphalayati   a  yathā sūtrapiṇḍadaṇḍacakrādiḥ  sāmagrī cajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalogirisāgarādijaniketi viruddhavyāptopalabdhi  prayatnaviphalīkaraṇaṃ hi tadanapekṣatvamambarādau siddhaṃ niṣedhyam  tena yad viruddhaṃ prayatnāpekṣatvaṃ tadvayāptaṃ sāmagrītvam tasthāyatnakāryatvāt atrocyate  yadi prayatnakārya sāmagrī sarvopasaṃhāreṇa sidhyed yuktametat  nacaivam na hi tatrāpi viparyaye bādhakaṃ kiñcidasti  yathā hi kārya svakāraṇāyattasannidheḥkāraṇāvasthāviśeṣasyāpekṣayā asarvakālabhāvi saṃbhāvyate tathā sāmagrathapi kiṃ na syātyato nityaṃ bhāvaprasaṅgaścodyeta  tataścānirvātita vipakṣavṛttiśaṅkā sāmagro yadi prayatnāpekṣāṃniyacchet sākṣātkāryatvādibhireva kīdṛśoparādhaḥ kṛtaḥ yena tadupanyāse saṃśayitasyasāmagrī śaraṇamupakṣipyate  mṛdādayaḥ puruṣādeva milanto dṛṣṭā iti cet  kāryamapi prayatnavata eva jāyamānamupalabdhamiti kiṃ nocyate  yathā ca yadyapi kimapi kāryaṃ prayatnavato dṛṣṭam tathāpikāryāntaraṃ tiraskṛtyāpi buddhimantaṃ bhaviṣyatīti śaṅkā tathā sāmagrayapi saṃbhāvyamānākamarthaṃ puṣṇāti  tatonukkasamametat  tasmāt sāmagrīmapi madhye prakṣipya kumbhādiṣusāmagrayāstathā darśanameva pramāṇayitavyam  tathā ca sati kāryameva pratyakṣānupalambhaiḥprayatnavannāntarīyakaṃ siddhamityeva sādhu  kimatra vyāptisiddhaye bādhakapramāṇopanyāsaśauṭīryeṇa  atha vakṣyamāṇakrameṇa pratyakṣānupalambhā jātiviśeṣameva viṣayīkartuṃ śaknuyuritina kāryamātraṃ prayatnavatā vyāptaṃ sidhyet  tadarthaṃ viparyayabādhāśrayaṇam evaṃ tarhi sāmagrayāapi prayatnavatkāryatve ta eva pratyakṣānupalambhāḥ śaraṇamiti evaṃvidhā saṃhatiḥ prayatnavatākriyata iti yuktaḥ sarvopasaṃhāraḥ  tathā cana vyagrādudayaḥ kacinna ca cayaścaitanyaśūnyād bhavedbhāve ki na sadā sadātanatanorapyeṣa doṣaḥ samaḥ tasyādṛṣṭamapekṣya kālaniyame kiṃ cetasā cet tadākumbhādāvapi śilpino viphalatā naitañca tadvyatyayaḥ kumbhādau yadi darśanādabhividhiḥ kiṃ vyatyaye bādhayāpratyakṣānupalambhataḥ kimu matā na vyāptirevaṃ sati teṣāṃ jātiviśeṣa eva viṣayo yadyevamevaṃvidhovyūhaścetanato bhavediti bhavedanyatra ko niścayaḥ iti saṃgrahaślokau īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamna ca sāmagrayantarasyātatpūrvakatve asthā api mā bhūditi yuktam asarvavyāpināmapi dharmāṇāṃ pradeśavṛtterdarśanāt lohalekhanasyeva pārthive asiddhaśarīrapūrvaṃkatvasyeva vā kārye  tatra bādhakānna sarvavyāpitvamiti cet  tadasphuraṇe tarhisaṃśaya kena nivāryate  yathā hi na parasya bādhakaṃ kalāpāntarepi kāryāntarādau vācetanāpekṣāyāḥ tathā bhavatopi sarvajātau tayāvaśyaṃbhāvyamiti na sādhakamasti yathā ca tava kacidbuddhimadapekṣā darśanamasti tathā parasyāpyekatra dṛṣṭasya b dharmasyabhinnajātīyāvyāptidarśanamasti  tato lohalekhanasya śarīravyāpārasya ca kacidbādhakādarśanaṃ sandehasādhanamupayuktameva parasya anyathā saṃśayasyaiva nirbījatāprasakteḥ na ca sādhāraṇānekāntaḥ prārabdhodhunābhidhātum yatastadvadatra bādhakānupadarśanaṃbādhakaṃ syāt prativadituḥ api tu sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvameva  tacca siddhaṃdṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭimātreṇa vyāpterasiddhe nibandhanāntarasyābhāvāt  etena kṣityādihetūnāmacetanatve sati niyatapravṛttitvena prāsādādihetuvat prayatnavadadhiṣṭhānāsiddhirityapipratyuktam  acetasopi kālādiniyatāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ prayatnavannāntarīyakatvasādhakapramāṇasya tadvadevābhāvāditi nāpi kāryāvirāmaprasaṅgaḥ saṅgatimāvahati aparāparapratyayayogajanyasvabhāvabhedasaṃbhavena bhāveṣvekaśakti nirvāhasya dūrīkṛtatvāt  tataśca karturekatve sandehodbhāvanenasamānanyāyatayā āṃgatameva buddhipratibandhaṃ paraparitoṣāya sādhāraṇānai kāntikatvenadūṣayitumāhasthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthāna viśeṣārthakriyādiṣu iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānteiti  vāśabdaḥ samuccaye  eṣu satsu yadiṣṭaṃ caitanyaṃ tasya dṛṣṭānte sādhanavati dharmaṇisiddhirasiddhiśca ghaṭādau viṭapādau ca yathākramam  tato vyaktaṃ vipakṣaikadeśe vṛttireṣāmitibhāvaḥ  etena yadi kṛtakādivad viparyayabādhābhidhānamaśakyam dhūmādivat pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekapratītiḥ prayatnena saha kāryādīnāṃ bhaviṣyatīti gatyantaramapāstam tamantareṇāpi kāryasyodayād vyatirekasyaivābhāvādityuktam nanu buddhimatvaṃ nāma dṛśyādṛśyaśarīretarasādhāraṇo dharmaḥ kṣamāruhādijanmanivyāpriyamāṇaṃ nāstīti kathamavagantavyam anupalabdhimātrādabhāvāsiddheḥ  yuktametatjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauyadi dṛśyaśarīropādhividhureṇa buddhimātreṇa vyāptirabhimatā syāt  vāḍhameveti cet evaṃ tarhi dhūmavadvyatirekamevādhikṛtyāhasaṃśayotha vāiti  yadā kumbhakāravyāpārāt prāk kalasasya vyatireka pratyetavyaḥ tadā na sādhyābhāvakṛto ghaṭa vyatireka pratītaḥ syāt sādhyābhāvasya sandehāt  na hi tathāvidha śarīropādhikena cetasā vyāptirjijñāsitā yatonupalabdhi viśeṣeṇa niṣedhaḥ sidhyetkiṃ tu prayatnavanmātreṇa  tasya ca yathā vṛkṣādijanmasamaye saṃbhāvanā niṣedhasyāśakyakhāt tathādyāpīti tatsaṃbhavepi saṃbhāvyamānaḥ kumbhābhāvastadabhāvaprayuktatvamātmanobodhayituṃ na śaknotīti sandigdhavyatirekaḥ nanu sādhyābhāve sādhanasya bhāvasaṃśaye sandigdho vyatireka iti yuktam na tukulālavyāpārāt prāk kumbhabhāva sandihyata iti cet  tadayuktam sādhyavyatirekaprayukto vyatireka sādhanasya a vyāptivādinā darśayitavyaḥ  saca sādhyābhāvasandehād vā svayamatopi na darśitaḥ  sādhyābhāvepi vā svabhāvasandehāditi nakaścid viśeṣaḥ ubhayathāpi tasya saviśeṣaṇasya sandigdhatvāditi  ataeva sandigdhasādhyasādhanadharmitvaṃ dṛṣṭāntayordoṣa ucyate yadi tu sādhanābhāvamātramabhidhīyeta sādhyābhāvamanapekṣya tadā yuktametat na ca tāvatā vyāptigrahaḥ  anyathā pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ vyāpti pratipadya pavanopaghāta sādhanopanīyamānaḥ kampo yadā mardanādisaṃbhavena kampena sādhāraṇaṃ kriyate tadāstimitamārutamasparśaṃyogyatayā niṣeddhumaśakyaṃ saṃbhāvya pariharannanivārya syāt tatra viśeṣasādhanād vyabhicāra eveti cet  kutaḥ punaretadviśeṣastena sādhyataiti  upahatiśabdastvaśarīravyāpāravat tadanurūpa viṣayo bhaviṣyati pratyakṣānupalambhena vyāptivarṇanāditi cet  tadapi bhavataḥ samānam yathā cāsya tādṛgmarunmātrāpekṣayā adṛśyatvena vyabhicāraparihāre vyāptigrahaṇakāledṛśyatvenaiva vyatirekāsiddhistathā bhavatopi śarīravirahiṇi caitanyamātre  tato yadā tadabhāvasaṃśayepikāryābhāvamātreṇa vyāptigrahaṇābhimānastathā aspṛśyaprabhañjanābhāvasaṃśayepi kampābhāvaḥsiddha iti syād vyāptiḥ īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamatha na kaścit dehavateva dehavirahiṇāpi vyāpti karoti kiṃ tu caitanyamātreṇatutacca kāyavatkālepyasti viśeṣasaṃbhave sāmānyasyāvaśyaṃbhāvāditi tadapekṣayā vyāptigrahaḥsāmānya viṣaya evāvatiṣṭhate vahnāviva vahnayantarasvarūpānupraveśāditi  etadapi samānaṃsamīrānumāne  na ca kaścit cetanāvān vepathumātreṇa mārutamanumimīte sarvagatvā dhyavasāyepi kampamātrasya sādhanasāmarthyāpratīte  na hi rājyamiṣṭamiti tannāmakaraṇānantaramupajāyamānamapi tadupāyavādinaṃ pramāṇīkaroti sādhanamapi vā kṛtakatvaṃ vastutaḥasādhanāṅgo vyāpakatvenopanīyamānamanityatāsiddhau tasmāt na koṣṭhaśuddhayā prameyatathābhāvena paritoṣa pramāṇaguṇastu nirūpyate na ca kampasya marunmātreṇa vyāptisiddhau kiñcid viparyaye bādhakamasti pratyakṣānupalambhāstu svagocarībhāvayogyameva svabhāvadeśakālaviprakṛṣṭamapi tadā tvasannihitentarbhāvayituṃ śaknuvantītyavaśyameṣitavyam nānyam  anyathā vyāptigrahaṇavadvyabhicāropi tanniṣṭha eva prasajyeta  tato yathā viśeṣaviṣayāvanvayavyatireko pratyakṣādyagocaracaitanyamarunmātraviṣayau vyavasthitau tathāpi viśeṣaviṣayo vyabhicāropi tanmātraviṣayaḥ kiṃ na vyavasthāpyate  na hi lābhe praveśaḥ chede niḥsaraṇamiti labhyam vahnistu deśakālaviprakṛṣṭopi tadātmā sannihita iva svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭa bpratyakṣādiyogyatayā tadanupraveśamāsādayatīti yuktam yatastadekādhyavasāyāt sarva evadhūmavyāpakatayāvadhāryamāṇo na duṣyati jāṭharaṃ tadayogyatayā tathā niścāyi  ata evadhūmādabhimate śikhini pravṛttirasaṃśayānasya yujyate  itarathā pratyakṣāyogyenāpi vyāptiḥāśrayabhujā gṛhyamāṇā dhūmasya tadyogyāyogyadahanasāmānyaviṣayaiva vyavatiṣṭhata ititārṇādibheda ivābhimatepi rūpe sandihāno na tatsādhyārthakriyālābhaikāgrabuddhi pravarteta pratibandhavaikalyavad vā asati jāṭharatva ityāmṛṣataḥ pravṛttiḥ syāt  na caivam tasmānnasvarūpaviśeṣaniṣṭhaṃ pramāṇaṃ sāmānyena vyāpti prapadyate anityatvena tu kṛtakatvasya vyāpti viparyayabādhakapramāṇamadhigacchad bhūtvābhavanamātreṇa viśeṣānavacchinnena pravṛttamiti sāmānyenaivādhigacchati  nāpi kṛtakātpravartamānobhimatānityai kāgrabuddhiḥ kaścit pravṛttimarhati  ataśca sāmānyaparyavasitamapipramāṇaṃ na viśeṣeṇa vyāpti gṛhṇātīti siddham  uktaṃ ca nyāyānusāriṇā śaṃkareṇa yatpramāṇaṃ yāvatīmarthaṃgati vyāpnotītyādi  yat pramāṇaṃ yatsvabhāvasāpekṣapravṛttikaṃ tannaivataditarasvabhāvena kasyacid vyāpti pratipadyate yathā viparyayabādhakaṃ bhūtvābhavanamātrājñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalīpekṣamanitya viśeṣeṇa kṛtakatvasya  yathā vābhimatasvarūpaviśeṣāpekṣamadhyakṣānupalambhamagnerjāṭharasādhāraṇena rūpeṇa dhūmasya  svarūpaviśeṣāpekṣapravṛttayaśca pratyakṣānupalambhāḥprabhañjanena kampasya vyāptigrahaṇa iti vyāpaka viruddhopalabdhiḥ mātariśvalaghutvavatpratyakṣapravṛtterabhāvāt nāpyanekāntaḥ  vivakṣitasvabhāvena hi kasyacit vyāptigrahaṇaṃ pramāṇasya tatsva rūpāpekṣapravṛttikatvena vyāptam anyathātiprasaṅgaḥ pravṛttisaṃkaraśca doṣaḥ  tadviruddhā cataditarasvabhāvāpekṣā pravṛttiḥ tasmāt svarūpaviśeṣāpekṣaṃ pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ nānilamātreṇastimitetarasādhāraṇena kampasya vyāpti pratipadyata iti pramāṇārtha  tato na paramārthataḥkampena pavanānumānamasti atha ca na kācid bhavadīyasamayasamādhānakalpanā yā nainamanudhāvati nacaitadīyamaprāmāṇyanibandhanaṃ kimapi yanna bhāvatkamanumānamupanīyate tataśca vahnidhūmavat prayatnavatkāryayoyadi vyāptisiddhayedhyakṣānupalambha śaraṇamāśriyate tadā tatpravṛttiyogyasvarūpāpekṣayā prayatnavato niyato vyabhicāra kāryamātreṇa tṛṇādinā atha vyabhicāracamatkārāgocareṇa cetanāvatā vyāptiriṣyate tadā mahoruhādijanmanīva śilpivyāpārādapi prāk niṣeddhumaśakye prayatnavanmātravyāpāre lavyatiricyamāno ghaṭādiḥ kasyābhāvaprayuktābhāvovadhāryatām yatastena vyāptaḥ sidhyediti sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatayā punaranekāntaḥ pūrvaṃ dṛśyādṛśyaviśeṣamanapekṣyaviparyaye bādhakābhāvaṃ svayamupadayaṃ kṛtaḥ idānīṃ vādina evābhyupagamena tadiṣṭapramāṇāpekṣayā vyatirekāsiddheriti bhedaḥ  vipakṣabādhakaṃ tu hetumātreṇa vyāpti pratīyāt natadviśeṣaṇabuddhimatetyuktam nanu vṛkṣādayaḥ pakṣīkṛtā iti kathaṃ tairvyābhicāra   trividho hi bhāvarāśiḥsandigdhakartṛko buddhimatkartṛkokartṛkaśceti  tatra buddhimatkartṛke ghaṭādau pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ vyāptimādāya sandehapade bhūdharādau kāryatvamupasaṃhṛtya prayatnavān sādhyate na punarasau vyabhicāraviṣayo bhavitumarhati yadāha na ca sādhyenaiva vyabhicāra iti tadayuktam  na hi vyabhicāraviṣayaeva pakṣo bhavitumarhatiīśvaravādādhikāre vātika saptaślokī vyākhyānamsandigdhe hetuvacanād vyasto heturanāśrayaḥ pra vā  iti nyāyāt  tataśca kṣmādharādireva sandigdhakartṛka pakṣīkartumucitaḥ  kṣamāruhādiḥtvacetanakartṛka iti caturtho rāśireṣitavyaḥ  vyāptisamīhayā pratyakṣayogyābhimatasyavṛkṣādijanmanyanupalabdheriti kathaṃ pakṣīkaraṇam  mā bhūdaśeṣasādhāraṇānaikāntikocchedaḥ kāryatvasya vipakṣavṛttihataye saṃbhāvyatetīndriyaḥkartā ced vyatirekasiddhividhurā vyāptiḥ kathaṃ sidhyati bādhā tvāhitahetumātra niyatirbhedena na vyāptayenāpyardho vyabhicāragocaracara pakṣīkriyāyāṃ kṣamaḥ iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ nanu tathāpi kathamavyāptirākāśasya vyatirekagrahaṇādhikaraṇasya saṃbhavāt yadāha buddhimatkāraṇasadbhāve bhāvo ghaṭādāvutpattyādeḥ abhāve cābhāvo gaganādiṣusaca tathā prasiddhīvinābhāvo yatraiva kṣityādāvupalabhyate tatraiva tadvinirmāṇasamarthakartṛbuddhi tadvido janayatīti  utpattyāderiti kāryatvāderityarthaḥ  atrābhidhīyate  nasādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa vā dṛṣṭāntamātramastīti sādhyasiddhiḥ yadṛcchopanatāvapi tathāsaṃbhavāt  tasmānnidarśanaṃ nāma gṛhītavismṛta pratibandhasādhakapramāṇasmaraṇadvāreṇaivahetāvupayogi na svasannidhimātreṇa saca pratibandho dvārāntareṇa vā gṛhīto vihāyasā smaryeta svādhikaraṇapramāṇaprasiddho vā  tatra tāvat prathamakalpanamapāstaṃ prāgeva dṛśyaśarīropādhinā dhīmātreṇavā kāryatvāderghaṭāvapi pratibandhagrahaṇopāyāpāyāt  caramaṃ cāsaṃbhava tathā hiyadi nāma vyogni dvayanivṛttirupalabdhā tathāpyekābhāvaprayuktatvaniścayāyogādanyābhāveviśvarūpasya ca tatrāvṛtteḥ kasya kena saṃbandhabodha syāt  karabhagardabhāderapi bkāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇaprasaṅgācca  anyatrānvayadarśana sahāyasya tathā pratītiriti cet nanu sahadarśana mevānvayārthaḥ tacca kadācit karabhāderapyastīti sādhvī vyavasthā sa ca buddhina sahṛdarśanamanvayasyārtha ki tvekasaṃbhavaprayuktonyabhāvaḥ matkāryatvayorasti nānyatreti cet  na tadbhāvaprayuktatvaṃ nāmāparabhāvasya na tadvyāpārātjñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalīprāgabhāvinaḥ sattālābhādanyaḥ prāgabhāvaśca nānupalabdhivyāpāramantareṇeti pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekayoniścaye saṃśayoṃ nāma kīdṛk hetuphalasthitāviti tatpratītipratibandhasmaraṇameva vihāyasā vidhīyata iti prathamapakṣa evāyam kiṃ ca kimidamīśvarenujo vivṛttāvivṛttāviṣkaraṇamātramatrabhavataḥ uta prati  vandīkṛte  dhūmānumānepi saiva gatiḥ ekatrobhayasaṃbhavamupalakṣyāntarīkṣe ekavyāpāranivṛttauanyanivṛtterupalakṣaṇād vyāptigraha iti  yadyeṣa eva nyāya tadā tadicchatāmanibandhanaḥprakṛtapradveṣaḥ kevalamevaṃ vilayatā dahanānumānamapi hāritaṃ dūratarā tu prakṛtasiddhiḥuktakrameṇa gardabhenāpi tasya prasaṅge vahnāvapi hastakatyāgāt  yadā tu gatyaṃntara mapi tatraprakṛtāsaṃbhavi saṃbhavi tadā kuto vandīkaraṇaṃ śaraṇam evaṃ tarhi pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāraḥ tadatiprasaṅgabhayādevāśrīyate na tu sa evasamaya iti cet  evaṃ sati bhavataiva kimayamatiprasaṅge bharo datto neti kośapānaṃkartavyam yo hi pratyakṣānupalabdhī vihāya vihāyasi vavyāpāranivṛttyā dhūmanivṛttimādāya vyāptimabhidhatte taṃ prati yathā vastumātrasyāpi tatra vyāpāroparamāttenāpivyāptisiddhiḥ syādityatiprasaṅgaḥ tathā yopi pratyakṣānupalabdhīruddhūya tadyogyapuruṣa viśeṣavyāpāraviraheṇa vyomani ghaṭādikāryatvanivṛtti darśayitvā tena vyāptimasyamanyate taṃ prati puruṣamātrasyāpi tatra nivṛttyā tenāpi vyāptiḥ tathā kāryāntaratvasyāpinivṛttyā tasyāpi syāditi vyaktamatiprasaṅgamātrametat na nyāya iti paśyāmaḥ dhūme gardabha divyabhicāradarśanāśa vastumātreṇa vyāptiriti yuktam puruṣamātrasyatu vyabhicārānupalabdherna damatiprasaṅgamātrodbhāvanaṃ bhaviṣyati  naivaṃ samānanyāyānāmekatra bādhakadarśanamanyatrāpi śaṅkāmutpādayati  yadi hi vihāyasi ubhayanivṛttidarśanaṃpratibandhasādhakaṃ bhavet vastudhūmayorapi na bādhyeta tatra tu bādhyamānamanyatrāpi kathamekāntāvasāyasādhanaṃ syāt  na ca pakṣīkṛte neva vyabhicāra ityapi na pakṣīkaraṇaṃmantraprabhāvaḥ kiṃ tu vyāptigrāhakadārḍhyam  tacca yadi nabhasi ubhayābhāvamātram tadātatra bādhakādhigaterastaṃ dāḍhamiti satyapi a  pakṣīkaraṇavyabhicārāśaṅkā nanivartata iti vyomāsti vyatirekabhūmiriti ced dhūmasya dhūmadhvajādutpattāvapi ki sa eva samayo nātiprasaṅgodayāt īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamyadyevaṃ bhavataiva kiṃ vinihito nātiprasaṅgetarastasmin bādhavilokanaṃ punarihāpyārekamākarṣati iti saṃgrahaḥ tasmāt nākāśe dvayanivṛttyā vyāptisiddhiḥ siddhavyāptikayostvabhāvadarśanaṃgṛhītavyāptismaraṇakāraṇaṃ syāt  na ca vyāptigrāhakaṃ kiñcidupapadyata ityuktam  tasmātanvayamātrabhāvepi vyatirekābhāvādanekānta eveti sthitam  vastutastu vyatirekavadanvayopyasya durlabha eva  yasya hi pratyakṣāgocaratayā abhāvaprayuktaḥ kāryābhāva itipratyetumaśakyaṃ tasyānvayo dūrotsārita eva pratyakṣagrāhyatvāt tasya  pratyakṣaṃ hi paridṛśyamānevastuni deśakālaviprakṛṣṭamapi svapravṛttiyogyamevāntarbhāvya vyāptimavakalpayet na svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭamapīti uktaprāyam  tataścānvayamātraṃ gajanimīlitenāvadhīrya vyatirekābhāvenaivaduṣaṇamuktam  vastutastu nānvayo na vyatireka iti prayatnavanmātre sādhye kāryatvamasādhāraṇameveti vā darśayitumāhasaṃśayothavāiti  pratyakṣādiyogyāpekṣayā sādhāraṇānaikāntikam caitanyamātrāpekṣayā asādhāraṇamityartha  nanu śarīropādhibuddhikṛtaṃ kārya sidhyat buddhimātrakṛtaṃ sidhyatyeva śiśapākṛtamivavṛkṣakṛtam viśeṣe sāmānyānapavāditi kathamucyatenvayābhāvaḥ  evaṃ sati vyatirekopitadapekṣayā syāditi cet  kā no hāniḥ buddhimati kāryahetoranvayavyatirekavattvābhyupagamāditi  uktamatra evamanvayavyatirekakalpane jāṭharacitrakā digatenāpi rūpeṇa dhūmādanumitamagni saṃśayāno nābhimataikāgracittaḥ pravarttatetyādi api ca na tatra saṃbhavītyeva pratyakṣeṇa yatkiñcidvastuno rūpaṃ kāryasya vyāpakamavadhāryate api tvadhyavasāyāpekṣayā  adhyavasāyaśca puruṣeṇa kṛta eva iti buddhimatāveti viśiṣṭa viṣaya eva pravartate tādṛśyeva puruṣādiśabdasya rūḍhe  na tu karādivyāpāranirapekṣeṇa caitanyamātreṇeti caitanyamātraṃ sadapyudāsīnamanvayagrahaṇakāledhyavasāyasya viśeṣonmukhenaiva pravṛtteḥ sāmānyaśabdatvepi vā prakṛtaviśeṣamākṣipyaivāgnivyāptivat  sa cādhyavasāya pratyakṣavyāpārānusārī tadyogyameva rūpaṃ bahiḥ kuryātna tu tadayogyamapi jāṭharādivat tārṇādivacca evaṃ puruṣeṇāpi vyāptī kasyacitjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalośarīropādhividhurasya buddhimātrasya tadayogyasya pratikṣepaḥ syādeva  apratikṣepastu kharvādibhedasyaiya  ayameva nyāyaḥ sarvatra pratyakṣeṇānvayagrahaṇe b athāṅgārasaṅgādagurukhaṇḍajanitaṃ dhūmamupalabdhavataḥ pratyakṣayogyatayāindhanādyantareṇāpi tadanvayaprasaṅga iti cet  tatkimidānīṃ pramāṇaviṣayapratiniyamamanādṛtya yatra kacit pravṛttamadhyakṣaṃ yena kenacidanvayaṃ pratyetviti vivakṣitam  evaṃsati hetumadābhāsavyavasthāvilopāt sarvasya sarvasiddhiriti pratiniyatasādhanānveṣoviphalaḥ atha pratyakṣeṇa svayogyamullaṃghyāpi vyāptigṛhītetyucyate  tadasiddham  yadāpipratyakṣaṃ svapravṛttiyogyepi vastunyavāntarabhedāpekṣayā sāmānyamudāsayadanvayaṃ pratipadyatetadā kaiva kathā svapravṛttyayogyasyātyantaṃ vijātīyasya  na cāsmākaṃ pakṣa pratyakṣayogyeṇasarveṇa vyāptiriti kiṃ tu pratyakṣayogyeṇaiva tatkṛtā vyāptiriti  anyathā gardabhādibhirapidhūmakumbhāderevānvayaprasaṅgaḥ  kimataḥ param  kathaṃ punaratrāvāntarabhedāpekṣa eva vyāptigrahona darśanayogyatāmātrāpekṣaḥ  vikalpastu vāsanāprabodhamātrārthamapekṣitapratyakṣādisannidhiraniyatodayākāratayā na pratiniyataṃ viśeṣamāveśayitumarhatīti satyam ataeva vyatirekasādhanyā anupalabdheravatāraḥ  tatra yathā vahni puruṣābhyāṃ dhūmakumbhayoranvayādhyavasāye sahāyatāmanupalabdhi pratipadyate pūrvasthitiranyatautpattiranyata āgamanamiti tridhā bhinnasaṃbhavavyatirekaṃ sādhayantītarathānupayogāttathā yadi gardabhānvaye vedanamātrānvaye vā pratipadyeta syādeva tābhyāmapi vyāptiḥnānyathā yato na pratyakṣamātraṃ vyāpti pratipadyate nāpyanupalambhamātraṃ kiṃ tu pratyakṣānupalambhāvanyonyasahāyāviti nirṇītaṃ śāstre bahuśa  asmābhirapi trika pañcaka cintāyāṃkiñciditi na ca gadaṃbhādyanvaye tasyāḥ sāhāyakamasti  etena dhūmaviśeṣāpekṣayānupalambhavyāpārābhāvo vyākhyāta iti naivavādini kaścit paryanuyogaḥ  yastu pratyakṣa gocarepitatkṛtāṃ vyāptimupavarṇayati tasya tadviṣaya eva vyāptigrahaviraha iti duḥsthā vyavasthā tataśca tasyaivāsau paryaṃnuyogaḥ  tasyāpyanupalabdhivyāpārābhāvānneti cet na yataḥpratyakṣa yogyepi tatkṛtavyāptivādinonupalambhavyāpāravirahepi tatkṛtavyāptimicchataḥīśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamkaḥ pratiroddhā  yadi hyasya vrīḍā syādapratyakṣayogya eva tadvayāpāraṃ kathaṃ varṇayet athopādānādividā prayatnavatā kāraṇadarśanādeva gardabhasya nirāsaḥ kimatrānupalabdhyā evaṃ tarhi dṛśyamānenaiva vyāptimupavarṇayan  na ca darśanapathātikrāntena na caśarīropādhi vyavadhūya caitanyamātramupalabdhaṃ kacit  yadi ca darśanabalādeva vyavasthācaitanyamātrādhiṣṭhitaṃ śarīraṃ kumbhādi janayat dṛṣṭameveti na gardabhenānvayavirodhaḥ tatkathamanupalabdhiapratikṣepa  vyāpakagatā sāmānyadharmā eva vyāptau sādhakāḥitareṣāṃ vyabhicāradarśanenānyatra śaṃkāvakā śā  deva na gardabhenānvaya iti cet  nanuvyabhicāradarśana miti tadabhāvepi bhāvadarśana mityanupalabdhivyāpārābhāvesādhanatvamupanīyamānamanupalabdhereva sādhanāṅga niścaye vyāpāraṃ paridīpayati yadi ca viśeṣe vyāpāraśaṃkākula sāmānyamanusarati bhavān upādānādyabhijñamapi viśeṣamapahāya caitanyamātreṇa gadaṃbhasādhāraṇena siddhasādhanayogyena tatopivā sāmānyena kāraṇamātreṇa vyāptimabhidhattām  evaṃ hi sati sarvathā dūrīkṛtaḥśaṃkāvakāśaḥ syāditi  etāvattu sāmānyamavamanya upādānādyabhijña viśeṣe sthitirnatu tadapyavajñāya yathādṛṣṭa iti kimatra sāmarthyamanyatra jāḍyāt  pratyakṣānupalambhavādiśaṃkāvakāśininastu yāvati yādṛśi sāmānye pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāro na tatra śaṃkācana vyāpāra iti nāsī kacana svayamicchayā vyāptimupanayatyapanayati vā pramāṇenaivasamarpaṇāditi na doṣaḥ nanu sopi hetumātrakṛtaṃ vā kāryagrāmaṃ bruvan pratyakṣayogyepi pratyakṣavyāpāropalambha ki na paśyati  paśyatyeva viparyaṃyabādhakādāgamācca tasya tadābhyupagamāt pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ tu śarīraviśeṣādhika eva cetasi sa pramāṇayati  icchāyāmapikarādivyāpāroparame kāryābhāvāt taddvāreṇaiva kulālādivyapadeśaviṣayasya samudāyasyapratyakṣatvavyavahārāt  na tviyaṃ gatiḥ prayatnasacivacittamātre  tadāpyanumānādanvayaḥpratyeṣyate  na ca pratyakṣasyaiva kaścidanurodhaḥ  upalambhānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekaniścayaḥ kartavyaḥ  sa copalambhaḥ pratyakṣarūponumānarūpo veti nātra nirbandhaḥ atra cintyate  kiṃ tadeva śarīropādhikaṃ cittaṃ prayatnavañcittamātraśabdenābhimatam utānyat  tattve kimanumānena pratyakṣasiddhau vivādābhāvāt  tena cānvayavyatirekau siddhau kāryamātreṇa ca tadvyabhicāro vyaktaḥ  anyatve liṅgābhāvadoṣaḥjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaubhāṣaṇāde kāryastha śarīriṇaiva caritārthatvāt  na ca tenānumitenāpi vyāptiḥ svīkriyate vyatirekāniścayāt pūrvavat  evaṃ tarhi bahiṣāpi dhūmasya vyāptinaṃ deśakālāvasthāniyatena kiṃtu vahnimātreṇa  tacca dṛśyamānādanyenaiveti vikalpe vyabhicārādidoṣa sādhāraṇa iti tādagviśeṣavirahiṇā sāmānyena vyāptirvaktavyā tathehāpīti cet  evamapi jāṭharādigatenāpi rūpeṇa vyāptiprasaṅgo dhūmasya tasmānna sāmānyamityeva vyāptāvadhikriyate nāpi viśeṣa ityeva pratikṣipyate b dhūmānumānasyaivocchedāt abhimate śikhani pravṛttisandehāt  tato yadi na svecchevasaṃgrahaparicchedasādhanī tadā pramāṇavyāpāramanviṣya vyavasthāprakrame kiñcit sāmānyaṃsvīkārapravṛttenāpi pratyakṣeṇa pratikṣiptamarthādeṣitavyam yadviśeṣātikrameṇa nāsyāvatāraḥ yathā jvaladbhāsurākāra pātikrame dhūmavyāptigrāhiṇa  kiñcittu pratyakṣasvīkṛtamapyanupalabdhi pratikṣipati pīṭharādivat sāmarthyāt sā hi dahanābhāve kāryābhimatābhāvaṃ sādhayantī dahanabhāvaprayuktatadbhāvavibhāvanādayogavyavacchedena tatkāryaṃtā sādhanapravṛttāpyanyasya hetutāṃ sādhayatyeva yadabhāvesvayaṃ na vartate  anupalambhapūrvake tu pratyakṣa prāgbhāvādibādhana pravṛttayānupalabdhyānekavasturūpasattvābhāvebhāvasiddhau
