yadekavastusvabhāvasannidhau sannidhiradhyakṣeṇa pratīyate prāgapitadabhāvaprayuktābhāvavibhāvanāt taddhetubhāvasādhane yadapravṛttiyogyatayā pratikṣiptamadhyakṣeṇa tatpratikṣiptameva tato na jāṭharāderanvayaḥ  nāpi kāladeśadaśā bhedabhinna svabhāvapratikṣepaḥsarva pratyakṣa svajanmayogyatayā svīkārāt  nāpyanupalabdhyā sā hyatādṛvasvabhāvābhāvebhavantī tadvijātīyahetutāṃ pratikṣipatīti yuktam na tu tasyaiva anyathā tadāśrayaṇaveyarthyāt  nanu deśādibhinnasvabhāvābhāvevyayaṃ dhūmo dṛṣṭaḥ na deśādibhinnasyāpyekākārapratyavamaśaṃpratyayena paridṛśyamānarūpeṇa sahakīkaraṇāt darśanāyogyasvabhāvādanyatra  ataeva vahnimātraśabdābhidheyaṃ tadeva paridṛśyamānayogyādbhedākṛṣṭāvapyabhedāvabhāsāt nanu deśādiviprakṛṣṭamapyadarśanayogyameva  satyaṃ kevalaṃ kadācit kacit  svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭaṃ tu satyatyanta vijātīyatayā svīkāraparihārayorbhedena vṛttinaṃ virudhyate tato yathānumānavādinā sāmānyamanusaraṇīyamavyāptimasaṃbhavaṃ vā parihartu tathāīśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamdṛśyaviśeṣāpekṣayātiriktasāmānyamapi parihartavyamativyāptiparihārāya evaṃ sati yathādarśanāyogyavahvisāmānyaparihāreṇa tadyogyāvāntarasāmānyena vyāptirekatvavyavasthā cayuktā na prayatnavanmātreṇa pratyakṣa pratikṣiptatvāditi tatra vyāmohāt pramāṇāntareṇānvayamicchan tattvānyatvābhyāṃ paryaṃnuyujyate dahane tu tatpakṣeṇaiva samādhirityuktam  tasmāt pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ vyāptijighṛkṣāyāṃa tadyogyasāmānyāpekṣāyā ghaṭaviṭapādau dṛṣṭānta iṣṭasya siddhirasiddhiśceti sādhāraṇānaikrāntikatvaṃ kāryasya  caitanyamātreṇa tu tadayogyenānvayavyatirekayorekasyāpyaniścayātsandigdhānvayavyatirekatvaṃ vaktuṃ yuktamuktamsaṃśayothaveti siddhaya siddhayoriti prakaraṇāt  tābhyāṃ bhāvābhāvāvuktau  yathāha  upalabdhirevasattā anupalabdhirasatteti  tataḥ kāryatvādisādhanavati dharmiṇi dṛṣṭānte sādhyatveneṣṭasyaprayatnavanmātreṇa sasvāsattvasandehāt tadadhiṣṭhānānadhiṣṭhānābhyāṃ ca sarvasaṃgrahādekatānvayavyatirekānupapatteryuktamasādhāraṇānakāntikatvam nanu tathāpyanekāntopyastu anvayamātraṃ kimiti pratikṣipyate kāryotpattībuddhereva vyāpāradarśanāt  jāṭharasādhāraṇenāpi rūpeṇa tarhi dhūmenvayaprasaṅgaḥ dahanavyāpāradarśanāt  tataśca tadapekṣo vyatirekopi syāditi prācīnadoṣaḥ  pratyakṣapratikṣepastusādhāraṇaḥ nanu jāṭharādyabhāvepi dhūmabhāvānna prācīnadoṣaḥ satyapyanvaya iti cet  kailāsakaraṇakauśala vikalenāpi kalasasya karaṇaṃ kiṃ na kīrtyate  atha karaṇakauśalasāmānye nānvayotra  tatrāpi dāhakamātreṇeti na vyaktayupakṣepeṇa kiñcit  jātyapekṣayā tutadānyadāpīti kathaṃ tadabhāvepi dhūmabhāvaḥ  atha dāhakatvamātraṃ paridṛṣṭaviśeṣād bhinnāṃjātimāsthāya vyabhicāra ucyate tadā tadapekṣayānvayopi kutaḥ pratyakṣeṇa viśiṣṭāyāeva jāte radhigamāt  anvaye vā punavrvyābhicārānupapatteriti yatpunaḥ sajātīyena pratyakṣataḥ pratibandhaniścayamāśaṃkya na hi sarvatra samānajātiranumīyate pratyakṣaśca yasmādasamānajātiḥ apratyakṣadha rūpādivyaktibhiranumīyatecakṣurādigrāmaḥ tathā candramasaḥ pṛthivyāśca parabhāgādhobhāgāvityuktam tadapipāpīyaḥ  tathāhi na tāvad vyāptiśūnyamanumānam vyāptiśca sāmānyena sāmānyasyajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvaloṃbhavantī kathamasamānānumānamanusaheta  tathā ca sā dvidhaiva pratyakṣānupalambhataḥ viparyayabādhakād vā  ubhayathāpi dṛṣṭāntadṛṣṭasajātīyasyaivānumānam  anyathānyajātīyena dharmeṇavyāptimupādāyānyajātīyamanuminotīti mahatī prekṣā sāmānyato dṛṣṭānumānepi hi yadeva gatisāmānyamanyasthāna prāpti nibandhanamupalabdhamtadevādhikaraṇāntare niścīyata iti kathaṃ vijātīyadharmānumānam  athādhārabhedāpekṣayāsāmarthyasādhyamavāntarabhedamabhipretyocyate tadanuktasamam  na hi kaścit anumānavādotanmātreṇa viśeṣamanicchan b phalinamanumānaṃ samarthayitumīśaḥ  yadi ceśvarānumānepitādṛśo vyāptiḥ syāt tanmātra viśeṣa siddhayā ceṣṭasiddhiḥ syāt kastatra matsaramācaret na ca tanmātraviśeṣāpekṣayā na hi sarvatra samānajātiranumīyata iti vaktuṃ yuktamkacidasamānajātyanumānepi tathocyate tanmātraviśeṣaśca sarvatrānumānesti  viśeṣatodṛṣṭasya sāmānyepi tadeva niścīyata iti tadapekṣayā na sarvatra tadevānumīyata iti vaktavyambhedādhiṣṭhānatvāt samānajāticintāyāḥ tat punaraprakṛtameva  sa tu na sarva pratyakṣonumīyata iti  yadi prakṛtamagnivatpratibandhagra he pramāṇamadhikṛtyocyate tadā pratyakṣasyaiva sarvatrānumānam anyatrāpadiṣṭapramāṇapravṛtteḥ  atha viparyayabādhakāpekṣayā tadā na vaktavyaṃ na kaścidviśeṣognisādhanātīśvarānumānasyeti  anityasādhanāditi tu vaktumucitam  atha kāryahetutāmātreṇaivamucyate tadā kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ pratyakṣānupalambhasādhana eveti sa eva doṣaḥ  na caviparyayabādhakaṃ kiñcidastīti carcitameva  deśādyaniyamaprasaṅgaśca hetumātrāpatti sādhayatyapi  tasmāt prakṛtaprameyānavagāhanāt lavata etat na sarvaḥ pratyakṣonumīyata iti anumānakālāpekṣayā tu sarva parokṣa evānumoyate na ca tatra kācid vimatiḥityanuktasamam  indriyaṃ tu na sākṣād buddheranumātuṃ śakyam pratibandhāgrahaṇāt  buddhikāryaṃtu keṣucit satsvabhāvābhāvavattatirikta kāraṇasāpekṣatāmāvahatīti tādṛśīndriyaghoṣaṇā tatrārādiṣu dṛṣṭajātīyameva sāpekṣatvaṃ yathā sādhyate tathā parabhāgādhobhāgāvapighaṭādikāryeṣu  avagaikasāmagrī pratibaddhau sāmānyato dṛṣṭāvevānumoyete iti sādhyaśūnyamudāharaṇamapi ityalaṃ bahunā  athavā kāraṇasāmānyena kāryasāmānyaṃ vyāpyate kāraṇa viśeṣeṇa tu kāryaviśeṣa eveti nyāyaḥ  adhyavasāyamātrato vā kāraṇasāmānyena kāryaviśeṣaiti pravādaḥ  tatrāyaṃ kāraṇaviśeṣeṇa buddhimatā kāryasāmānyaṃ vyāpta mitibruvāṇaḥpramāṇāvaṣṭambhena nāma prasiddhimullaṅghayet īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyānamtacca pramāṇaṃ vyāptisādhakaṃ dvividhameva pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ vā viparyayabādhakaṃ vāanayoḥ pratyakṣānumānasvabhāvatvāt anyato niścayāyogāt  tatra tāvaduktakrameṇakāryasāmānyasyano bhedena vipakṣabādhakavaśād vyāptiḥ samastasya capratyakṣānupalambhato na tadatajjātīyabhedaspṛśaḥ prāgbhāvādiniṣedhapūrvakatayā dhūmādivajjanmadhīranvetīdṛśamīdṛśāditi yataḥ sāmānyabhedadvayam idamupalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptamanupalabdhamasyopalambha upalabhyata ityevaṃ a  hipratyakṣānupalambhayorvyāptigrahaṇakramaḥ  tatredamityekajātīyatayā eka pratyavamarśapratibhāsidhūmādikamanekakāryajātyantaravyudāsenānekakāraṇajātyantaravyudāsena cāsyeti vahnayādeḥityarthaḥ  tataḥ kāryakāraṇayoḥ pratyekaṃ tajjātīyetarayoritaretarato bhede parāmarśapūrvikāpravṛttiḥ anyathā sāmathvaiyarthyābhyāmanupayogāt tathā hyakāryarāśivyavacchedena vā kāryāntaravyavacchedena vā idametad bhāvābhāvānuvidhāyītyavadhāryeta  ādye pakṣe etāni vastuni etanniyatāni ityayamarthonetadvastviti ekākāravirahādekākārapratyavamarśānupapatteḥ  nanu kāryatvādinā sāmānyenaidamiti kāryaṃ sanniveśo vetyādi vaktuṃ śakteḥ asiddhametaditi cet  ucyate ihbhāvābhāvavidhānabuddhidvidhā saṃbhavati dharmiviṣayā dharmaviṣayā ca kāryasya nirvavikāyabhedena dvaividhyāt  tatrādyā sarvātmanotpattiniścayamupādāya dharmiṇameva viśiṣṭākārakroḍīkṛtaṃ kāladeśādibhedabhinnamapi svabhāvamanta rbhāvyai kapratyavamarśād viṣayīkarotīti tadviṣayetyucyate  sa hi saṃbhavinamapyatadākārabhedavirodhinaṃ dharmaṃmudāsayatidhūmādiṣu dhavalatādivat yatra punaravasthitasyaiva dharmiṇo dharmāntaramudayamāsādayati tatra dharmamātrasyaivahetubhiranvayavyatirekāviti dharmaviṣayetyucyate  sā punarākāramevodāsayantī dharmamātramadhiṣṭhānīkaroti rāgādivat  na hyākārakriyādivaijātyamatyantamanubhavantaḥ paṭakūṭādayaḥsādhāraṇa rāgayogino gṛhītasāmarthya rāgadravyāntarayogamanumāpya tṛpyanti prathamā tvākāraśaraṇaiva sarvātmanotpatteḥ  yathaiva hi viśiṣṭākāroparaktaṃ vastu kutaścidupajāyatetathaiva tadvalotpannenendrijñānenānubhūyānantaraṃ vikalpadvāreṇa vyavahāragocarīkriyata itijñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalokathamākāraparihāra  ataeva dhūmakumbhādivyaktirekatrānupalabhyaprabhavā upalabhamānasyaanyatra tadaiva yadyuktibhedena vyāptisiddhistatraiva tatkāraṇāvasāyo jāyate nānyatravyabhicāradarśanādarśanamapekṣyāpi  anantaraṃ tvākāramudāsayet kevalaṃ vyavasthite dharmaṇidharmamātrodayadarśinaḥ na ca vyavasthite kumbhādau kāryatvādidharmamātrotpattirīkṣyate kṣitidharādauvābhyupeyate yenākāramanādṛtya rāgavattanmātrameva hetumanumāpayet  sanniveśastarhi sthitaeva tadātmani kumbhakārāditi cet ta drāgapi saṃsthāna vinākṛtāyā mṛdonupalabdheḥ atha tādṛśasyābhāva eva pūrva yaḥ kumbhaprajñaptigocara iti cet  tadeva saṃsthānaṃ tarhipuruṣāditi na tāvanmātravyāptiḥtathāpi yadi saṃsthānasāmānye puruṣakriyā haridrādravyayogopi b varṇamātra vidhāyakaḥ nanu tathāpi na pūrvasiddhadarśanamityeva vyaktyantare gṛhyamāṇāyā vyāptervyāghātaḥtadvalātvanumānameva tatretyanantarameva samarthitam  na ca tāvatā varṇamātraṃ kusumbhasaṃbhavasādhanasādhu vyabhicārālambanaṃ tu durbalamiti kimatra prāptam guṇepi dravyavat tasmāt sajātīyaparigrahaḥ tatpūrvasiddhepyanumā na varṇāt kuṅkumasya ca tanniyataviśeṣāpari hi rāgādapi kutaḥ kuṅkumānumā  davīyasī tu varṇamātrāt  varṇavacca saṃsthānasyāpi vicitrameva vaijātyamanubhavaviṣayaḥ  tadanayorekatrajātiniyamena vyāptivyavasthānamaniyamena vā vyaktau vyabhicāro naikaniyataḥ  tasmādvarṇavadanekajātini saṃsthānepi tattvaṃ sāmānyamanuvartamānamapi vyāptigrahād bahirbhūtameva  evamarthaṃkriyāpi pūrvamasati vastuni puruṣāditi vaktumaśakyam  sarvasāmarthya virahiṇaḥ prāgabhāvaprasaṅgenāpūrvotpattiprāpteriti viśiṣṭe vārthakriyāpi puruṣānvayavyatirekānuvidhāyinīti siddham tasmādevaṃvidhā dharmaviṣayāpi vyāptibuddhirna sāmānyamanudhāvati  yadā tukārya hetvadhikāreṇa dharmiviṣayeva tadā yathāparidṛṣṭākārārthakriyāsāmānyaṃ samāśrityayathā kāraṇe pratiniyatasvarūpasāmānyena vyāpakatvāvasāyinī tathā kāryepi pratiniyatākā sāmānya puraskāreṇeva vyāpyatvāvasāyinī samakṣabuddhiriti na sandehaḥ īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamanyathā kāryavat kāraṇepi buddhimadādiviśeṣavyudāsena pravṛttimatī matiḥ kimabhimatamupanayet  tasmāt kāraṇavat kāryepi tathābhūtākāraviśeṣamevamayamavasātumarhati tatredānīṃ tadākārabahirbhūteṣu bhūtalādiṣu sadapi kāryatvamabhidhīyamānamanupayuktameva dharmaviṣayahetuphalagrāhipratyakṣavyāpārāpekṣayā dharmamātrasāmyasyākiñcitkaratvāt na hi tadevākārārthakriyādirūpaṃ tatsāmyonmīlanaheturvā  tadanena sāmyaṃ na kiñcidarthaṃpuṣṇāti agauṇakāryaśabdapravṛtteranyatra  sa hi saṅkalpaniveśinyudayārthamapekṣitaparavyāpāramātre artha akārādikamudāsya kṛtasamaya iti na tasya vyāghātaḥ  upapattyantareṇa vyāpakatayā yaḥ pratīto dharmaḥ tatraiva nāśavatpratyakṣavyāpāra eva tu svodayasamayaparisphuradākārādisādṛśyamapekṣate deśādikṛtabhede tu vesadṛśyāvasāya iti navirodhaḥ tasmādekakāra ṇa virahāt pratyekaṃ pratyakṣānupalambhāpekṣāyāmetāni vastūnietatkāraṇānugāmīnītyanenaivākāreṇa vyāptiniścaya  kārya  kevalamadyāpi na vyaktikāryenopayoga iti sarvakāryaprakāre vekaika viṣayovatiṣṭhate  sa a cāśakyaḥkramayaugapadyābhyāmayogāt  tathā hi na tāvat sakṛdeva teṣāmanvayaḥ sarvaprakāropanipātedarśanasya draṣṭurevāntardhānaprāpteḥ  vyatireko vā śakyaniścaya aśakyaparihāratvātkeṣāñcidādhārālokaśarīrādīnām nāpyekena narāyuṣā kṣamamidaṃ sarvaprakārekṣaṇaṃkāryasyāntaviyogataḥ katipayāpekṣāsu kātsnyaṃ kutaḥ na khalu bhūyasopi bhāgasyābhividhibodhe nirvṛttiḥ na hi tadapi yadyat kāryaṃ tattadevamiti śakyamabhidhātum etāvaditi tu syāt yatpunarekatra pravṛtto vicāra sarvabhāvāṃstathābhāve vyavasthāpayatītyucyatetatsādhāraṇākārapravṛttimadhikṛtyākṛtyādivyudāsena pramāṇāntarāvalambanāt  pratyakṣavyāpāra eva hyekajātigrahaniyama uktaḥ  nanu tatrāpyavāntarānekabhedasaṃbhavādayamevamityabhidhātumaśakteranāśvāsaḥ  atra vā bhedatiraskāreṇa dhūmādijātyantaramavalambyasaṃvyavahāre kāryatāmāśritya jātyanta reṣvapi kīdṛśo doṣa iti cet  na vayaṃ svecchayākaścida tiraskurmaḥ puraskurmo vā kāmapi jātim  adhyakṣapūrvakastu saṃkalpo yathāarthānupasthāpayati bhedenābhedena vā tathā hetuphalabhāvavyavahāramavatarāmaḥ  sa tujñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalīprakṛtiviśeṣamāsādya yadi sūkṣmasthūlabhāvena bhedeṣvabhibhūtisāmarthyāsāmarthyābhyāṃ bhinattivṛttim kimatra kaiścitakartavyaṃ tadvivartastu cintyaḥ  tatradhūmovāntara bhedavatyapi yathā jātyantarāpohitaṃsārūpyaṃ viṣayīkaroti hṛdayaṃ ki kāryamātre tathā eka saṃsthānādyanugamānanugamayoḥ pratyātmavedyatvāt nāparamatra prārthyate nirṇayanibandhanam anyathā ca vyapadeśārthakriyāviniyogādisaṃkaraprasaṅgaḥ  tasmānna kacitkāraṇe sarvakāryaprakāraṇāṃ krameṇa yaugapadyena vā adhyakṣānupalambhasaṃbhavā vyāptirupapādayituṃ śakyeti kimābhyām  ata evaṃmukhena sarvakāryavyāptivādinaḥ svābhiprāyanivedanamātrametad vartmani sthāṇūpadeśaghoṣaṇavat  tathā ca sati icchāmātraṃ sādhanamastviti sphuṭamanayorapārthaṃkatvam  tasmādābhyāmata idamiti matiḥ kāryāntaravyavacchedenaiva bhavantīna kārya mātragocarokara gasaṃvādamāsādayati  tato niścayamupādānādividopanudannāha Isaṃśayothaveti pareṣṭasiddhirna parasya bādhane prasādhane vedanayatnamātrayoḥ ananvayobhīṣṭaviśeṣasādhane vipakṣasandehasahaṃ tu sādhanam sādhye ca dṛśye vyabhicāra eva dṛśyaṃ na cenna vyatirekasiddhiḥ na cānvayopi vyatirekavad vā vyāptirviśeṣeṇa na cetarasya  keciditi mātṛkāyām dvitīyaḥ khaṇḍaḥ evaṃ sati satyapi vyāptiraśakyaniścayā saṃbhāvyata iti kimatra sāmpratamitib cet  paśyakāryaṃ tāvadanekajāti janakaścaiko jaḍo vīkṣatenānābhedavato na caikaniyamajñānenyabhedepi tat yadyajjātikame kahetuviditaṃ tattattadaṅgaṃ tatonaivaṃ cedatisañjanaṃ na ca mataḥ sādhyopameyannayaḥ na hi nānāprakārakāryaṃjananaṃ nāma prayatnavatyeva niyatam vahnayāderapi vividhasāmagrīmadhyamadhyāsīnasya dhūmabhasmāṅgārāṅgatāpapākapāradotsāraṇavīkṣaṇakṣatiprabhṛtivicitrakāryakriyādarśanāt  yadi paraṃ prayatnavatodhiṣṭhānenetyatra vivādaḥ na caikasya tatraniyame jñāte kāryāntarepi niyamajñānamupapadyate yathoktaṃ prāk  tato yāvantaḥ prakārāekahetavo niścitāḥ tāvantastasya hetoścetanasyetarasya vā sādhanaṃ yujyante  anyathāstimitendhanasakhena śikhinā gṛhītadhūmavyāptiraparicitatatkāryaṃbhāvairbhasmādibhirapidahanamanuminuyāt  na caivaṃ tasmāttajjātibhedo vyakto vyāptigrahaśca pṛthak pṛthagapekṣyamāṇo yatra kacittadgrahaṇena yena kenacidanumānamunmūlayati kaḥ punarevamāha yatra kacidgṛhītavyāptiryena kenacidanumimītāmiti ekadharmānuvṛttivirahe hetorevābhāvāt  na hi tadā bhasmasādhanamavyāpteḥ  nāpi dhūmosiddheḥ kuṭakūṭādau kāryatvamevānyadharmānanuvṛttāvapyanumāne vartamānaṃ hetu syāditi cet  nakāryatvasyāpi prāgavyāptevistareṇa sādhanāt  tatra yathā kulagiriḥ kulālavyāpārakālesvabhāvavaikalyādikalitaniyamaḥ tathā sadapi kāryatvaṃ prāmāṇyapravṛttyā dhūmajanmanīvarāsabha iti pramāṇena vyāptigrahavirahe na kaścidviśeṣaḥ  tadayaṃ ghaṭādau kāryaviśeṣegṛhītavyāptiḥ sarvato na kāryatāmātreṇa vā vyāpakamanumātu  na tu vyāptigrahaṇasādhanavyavasthayobhinnādhikaraṇatāmatikrāmatīti kathamatiprasaṅgopālambhaparihāra tasmānnaikadharmānuvṛttimātreṇopayogaḥ  kena vā dhūmasaṃbhavinaḥ kāryatvavastutvādayobhasmani bhasmasādeva kṛtā  santopi vyabhicāriṇa iti cet  nanu savyabhicārovyāptiviyogādeva vyāptau tadgandhasyābhāvāt  sa ca vyāptyabhāvaḥ kāryatvenāpiavajita iti tatrāpi vyabhicāro dunivāraḥ  āhtyādarśanaṃ tu viprakarṣādapi syāt jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalona tāvatā tadabhāva eva tanmūlabhūtāyā avyāptestādavasthyāt  yadi tu vyāptāvevasavyabhicāraḥ tadā nitarāmavyāptāvityalaṃ mithyābhiniveśena  tad yadyapi sādhāraṇadharmā tanmātraṃ vyāptimanādṛtya sādhanamiṣyate kiṃ na bhinna evaṃ bhūdharādisādhāraṇaṃ dharmamanādṛtyetyatiprasaṅgastadavasthaḥnāpyayaṃ nayaḥ sādhyasamānīkṛte kalasādāvapyasti tatrāpi yathāyathā pratisaraśarābodañcanādiṣu kumbhakārakṛtimupalabhāmahe a tathātathaivamapīdamapyanena sṛjyataiti pratiyantaḥ paricitakriyebhya eva prakārebhyastadvayāpāramavadhārayāmaḥ anyathātaddoṣānativṛttiḥ  tasmād yadi paramārthataḥ prayatnavannāntarīyaka evāyaṃ sakalaprakārakāryagrāmaḥ tathāpi svayamakiñcitakara iti pramāṇavṛttyapekṣayāsiddhaṃ yādṛgadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvābhāvānuvṛttimat sanniveśādi tadyuktaṃ tasmād yadanumīyate iti  yadṛṣṭerakriyādarśinopi kṛtabuddhirbhavati śūnyanagaraparidṛṣṭadevakulādivat sanniveśādipra vā  taccāsiddhamityākṛtam tādgeva yadīkṣyeta tannagādiṣu dharmiṣu yuktaṃ tatsādhanādasmādyathābhīṣṭasya sādhanam nanu bhavatyevāsmākaṃ sarvatra pauruṣeyabuddhiḥ kṛtabuddhiḥ sā sādhyabuddhirevānumānamiti niyamaḥ kathañcit kasyacittatrāpyabhāvāt  kiṃ ca kṛtabuddhiriti kāryamātrabuddhirvā puruṣamātrabuddhirvā  yadi kṛtamātrabuddhiḥ sā bauddhasthāpi siddhā sindhubhūdharādiṣu  sāvayavatvācca tadārambhasaṃbha vitvameva kṛtatvam  atha pauruṣeyabuddhiḥ kṛtabuddhi sā sādhyabuddhirevānumānamiti cocyate tatastadabhāvānnānumānamiti kathamucyamānaṃnopaplavate yadāha naca vyāmohāt kasyacit sādhyabuddhayabhāve hetorasiddhatādoṣaḥ sarvānumāneṣu tadbhāvaprasaṅgāditi  yadapīdamucyate tādṛkkāryatvādi niṣiddhamacalādiṣvitiīśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamtatrāpi na kāryatvādinā kailāsakalasādeḥ kiñcidviśeṣamupalabhāmahe  āha ca nāpikaścidviśeṣaḥ kṣityādihetūnāṃ prāsādādihetubhyo yenāmī nirabhiprāyāḥ santaḥ prayatnanirapekṣā  pratiniyamavatā ca vyāpāreṇa tadvantaḥ syuḥ na hyanadhiṣṭhitānāṃ prayatnavatākaraṇadharmāṇāṃ kriyāsu svātantryamupalabdhipūrvam sarvatra buddhimadadhiṣṭhiteṣveva prāsādādiprasavopalabdheriti atrocyate neyaṃ kṛtabuddhiḥ siddhāntābhiniveśavāsitabuddhīnadhikṛtya kīrtitākiṃ tu saṃvyavahārapragalbhapuruṣamātrāpekṣayā  tasya ca pūrvapratītapratibandhasmaraṇavataḥkāraṇaparāmarśave mukhyābhāve bhavatyeva devakulādau tādṛśī buddhinaṃ tu malayamakarālayādī tadanayorasyā dhiyo bhāvābhāvau na jātibhedamavyavasthāpya sthātuṃ prabhavataḥ dhūmadvaya darśanepi tathābhāvaprasaṅgāt  iyaṃ ca kāmaṃ sādhyabuddhireva kaḥ punarenāmetadvatonumānanibandhanamāha tadabhāvād vā bhūdharādau tadabhāvam  kiṃ tu jātibhedamātropalakṣaṇārthamasyābhāvābhāvopanyāsaḥ samānajanāpekṣayā kasyacid durvidagdhabuddheḥ pratibodhasādhanāya jātibhede hi tāvati siddhe naikatra pravṛttamadhyakṣānupalambhamanyatra pratibandhasādhanasamarthamitivaktuṃ samarthaḥ syāt tato nāpratibaddhāt santri  b veśāde sādhyasiddhiḥ pratibaddhaścāsiddha itikathamanumānamityantatonumānaniṣedhāyopanyāsepi naikasyaiva tadabhāvāttadabhāva ityuktaṃbhavati  nanu tathāpyanyasyānumānodayābhāvādanyasyāpi na bhavitavyamityuktaṃ bhavati tacca kathaṃ saṅgatimālambeta  uktaṃ hi na ca vyāmohādityādi  tadayuktam  samānasādhanasāmagrīsaṃbhave sādhyasyaikapratiniyamānupapatteḥ  yad yena viśiṣṭasāmagrīkaṃ tattenāviśiṣṭaphalameva yathā sādhāraṇadhūmasādhanendhanadahanā disamudāyaṃ pradeśadvayamanyonyam aviśiṣṭānumānasādhanapratibandhagrahaṇādisāmagrīkaśca bhavatā saha sāṃvyavahārika puruṣa iti svabhāvahetuḥ prasaṅgaḥ  bhavatopi hi pratyakṣānupalambhameva pramāṇaṃpratibandhasādhanaṃ devakulasūtradhārādyadhikāreṇa pravṛttam  etacca parasyāpi sādhāraṇam asādhāraṇaṃ tu viparyaṃyabādhakapramāṇameva durabhyūhatayā bhavet  tacca bhavatopi nāstītiprāk prakāśitam tad yadi svamatābhiniveśamātramanubhavato nāvṛṇoti cetaḥ kiṃ tu tadeva sādhanamitarasādhāraṇam tadā tasyāpi paṣṭadevakulavinmerumandarādāvapipauruṣeyānumānamanivāryam  na caivam  tato yasya yatpratibandhagrāhakapramāṇavyāpārejñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalauyathāvatsmaraṇavato yaddarśanānna tadanumānaṃ na tasya tatra pratibandhaḥ siddho yathāgnau dhūmapratibandhasyānusmarato gardabhadarśanādagnimananuminvataḥ  na bhavati ca cetanena devakulādipratibandhasmṛtimato malayahimālayādī puruṣānumānamiti kāryānupalabdhi smaraṇakāraṇānusaraṇave mukhyādipratyayāntarasaṃbhave prācīnapratibandhasādhaka pramāṇena viṣayīkaraṇavaikalyaṃ sādhayati  tacca na jātibhedātiśayamantareṇāvāntarabhedavatopigardabhavat dhūmādvyāptigrahaṇasmaraṇayoraparādhe tu neyamiṣṭasiddhiḥ  tadarthaṃ yathāvadgrahaṇam  tatrasmaraṇāparādhe devakulāntarādapi nānumimīta grahaṇāparādhopi pratyakṣāpekṣayāsaṃbhavīekapratyavamarśayogyatāyā evābhāvādityukteḥ  anyathā jaladharādyathinopi kumbhakārasūtradhārādīnapekṣeran  apekṣata eva tatrāpi sūtradhārasthānīyonyo yathā kumbhakārasthānīyaḥ kacit sūtradhāra iti cet na kārya jātivaisadṛśyābhāve kāraṇa sāmarthya vaisadṛśyāpekṣānupapatteḥ  anyathā kumbhāntarepi na kulālamātreṇa toṣamaśnuvota  tadvad vā kṛṣīvalakulālapauruṣāpaneyānāvṛṣṭikaṣṭaḥ sthāditi siddha eva tādṛśo jātibhedaḥ tasmādekākārapratyavamarśānupapatteradhyakṣa sādhyā vyāptirviśiṣṭaviṣayatayā na durgrahadoṣamāvati yatonumānābhāvepi jātibhedātiśayasyāsiddheḥ siddhasādhanadoṣa syāt a tataśca yathāvad grahaṇasiddheryatra nānumānaṃ tatra vyāpterevāgrahāditi nānekāntaḥ  kathaṃ punaranumānahānameva tādṛśi lokasyāva gantavyamiti cet  uktādevajaladharāthinopi kulālajaṅghāmardanaprasaṅgāt paracakrākrāntikātarasya vā kulagirijaladhivyavadhimabhilaṣataḥ cetanamātreṇa vyāpti pratīmo na kumbhakārādyavasthāniyatenatena nāyaṃ prasaṅga iti cet  tadavasthāniyatenaiva vyāptigrahe kīdṛśo doṣa iti kimatravaktavyam  na ca samayāpakṣālakalāṅkitadhiyaṃ bhavantaṃ prati kāciñcintā api tu lokaṃprati  sopi vyabhicārānna tena pratipadyate iti cet  evaṃ tarhi kalasāntarādapinānumānamayaṃ kuryāt anyatraiva vyabhicāradarśanādatra ko doṣa iti cet  tadetajjātivaisadaśyesatina labhyate  tataśca viśiṣṭāyāmeva jātau vyāptigrāhi pratyakṣaṃ pravṛttamato nānyatra tadvayāpārānumānamityevaṃ kiṃ nocyate kimatra vyabhicāropakṣepeṇa  avaśyaṃ ca pratyakṣasyapratiniyatajātivyavasāya eṣitavyonyathā vyabhicārāgocaramapi pratyakṣaṃ na niyatajātikamiti kalasāntaramapyāskandet  tathā ca sati sa eva doṣaḥ  vyāptigrāhiṇaivaīśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamkalasāntarasyādhiṣṭhitatvāditi cet  nanu tadadhiṣṭhita eva viṣaye vyabhicāracāri cetaḥpracarat kathaṃ tameva pariharet ubhayoniyataviṣayatve tu nāyaṃ doṣaḥ  kevalamidānīmadhyakṣeṇa viśiṣṭaviṣayasvīkārānna vyabhicāropanyāsaḥ saphalaḥ  vyāptigrāhiṇastu pramāṇasya viśiṣṭaviṣayapravṛttismaraṇādhānārthamupayujyate mūḍhaṃ prati  na tu parito visāriṇī vyāptigṛhītirasyaniyataviṣayā kriyate vyabhicāreṇa  nāpyanumānakhaṇḍanamātramuktanyāyādeva  tasmādviśiṣṭaviṣayaiva vyāptiḥ kumbhakārādinā gṛhyate sidhyatītyapi siddham  tat kathaṃ sāmānyenavyāptimabhidadhānaḥ samayānuvādamātreṇa nopālambhamarhati  yadi tu puruṣamātreṇavyāpti jighṛkṣoradhyakṣapratikṣepeṇa pramāṇāntaraṃ śaraṇam tadā naiṣa doṣaḥ  tattu vicāritam  yadi veśvaraprasādādasya vādino jagataścitrākāraparihāreṇa sarvatrekākāraṃpratyakṣamudayamāsādayati taccāsādhāraṇamiti na vyavahārāṅgam  saśarīrāśarīrayoḥprayatnavatorna kaścidviśeṣa dṛṣṭastāvaddharmibhedena dharmabheda iti cet  yadrūpapuraskāreṇa pratibandhasādhaka pramāṇavṛttistasyābhede bhidyamānāpi dharmijātirabhinnavadābhāsamānā na bādhikā tadbhede tu tadgataṃ dharmāntaramabhidyamāanamapi bhinnavadābhāsamānaṃ na sādhaka mitinyāyaḥ  anyathā jaladharāthināpi kumbhakārasya paryeṣaṇāprasaṅgaḥ  tadapāyespi vihāyasibalāhakodayadarśanānneti cet  na tatprabhavasyaiva ghaṭasyeva tasya maruto kṣepaḥ kiṃ nasaṃbhāvyate  atha ca vāridhāritvamātramubhayatra dṛṣṭamiti yathā tatra saṃjñābhedamātrabhedovyavasthāpyate tathātrāpīti yuktam  pratibandhaniścayo hi pramāṇaviṣayasvabhāvaniyame satibhavati tadviruddhāniyamarūpaṃ ca sādhāraṇatvam pramāṇapratibaddho hi niścayastadviṣayasvarūpollaṅghepi bhavan pramāṇāpramāṇasādhyaḥsyāt  na caivam tasmānnānekāntaḥ  nāpyasiddhiradhyakṣavyāpārānusārāt  tadihapāṇḍutvasyāgnivyabhicāro dṛṣṭa iti dṛṣṭāntasya sādhyaśūnyatāniṣedha eṣaḥ  ata evanānumāna miti pratibandhābhāvādaniścayaphalamidamubhayatra  na tu siddhavyāptikayordahanapāṇḍutayorvyābhicāreṇa sādhanavaidhuryam vyāptisiddhāvanumānāpavādasyāśakyasādhanatvāt vyabhicārasyaivāyogāt pratyāsattibheda iti saṃjñāmātraṃ śaraṇamāpatitam tena dharmijātibhedasya dharmabhedakatvaṃ siddhamapīti kathaṃ sarvatra tanniṣedha  athasarvatraiva yadbhedakatvaṃ tanniṣidhyate kacidabhedakatvamapītyartha tadā siddhasādhanam  uktaṃhi pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpāpekṣayā tadubhayavyavasthānamiti  tathā ca sati bhedasthitirevajñānaśrī tatobhūtvābhavanābhidhānadharmamātrasya bhūtvābhavanena dharmeṇa vyāptisādhakaṃ dharmiṇoyadi jātibhedamudāsayati dhūmasyāgninā vyāptisābdhakameva mahānasādi tadā prastutekimāyātam yatra pratyakṣavyāpārāpekṣayā jātibhedaniṣṭheva vyāptigṛhītirītiriti  yadi tuprakṛtepi kāryavastustomagatāḥ kāryatvādaya eva dharmāḥ pratītavyāptayaḥ syuḥ tadāyaṃ nadoṣaḥ abhede tu tadapinirāspadam  na hi sajātīyakumbhāntare tadvijātīyasya nirmātuḥ siddhirityanubhavātabhyupagamād vā bhinnaiva jātiranayorna samānaṃ hetumāvahati saṃjñāmātrasāmyepīti kaḥ punarayaṃ niyamo kaścitpratibandhasādhana vidhilaṃbdhavyo yaḥ kumbhakāreṇamṛnmayamātravyāptiprasaṅgaparihārakārī prayatnavatā kāryamātravyāpti sādhayiṣyatīti bhāvaḥ kumbhakāreṇa hi kāryamātra vyāptisādhanāya prabhavatastadviśeṣa mṛnmayasya sāṃdhane kaḥ śaktivyāghātaḥ  astu vā prakāradvayenaiva vyāptigrahaḥ  yattūktamno bhedena vipakṣabādhakavaśādityāditatonyathā bhaviṣyatīti āśaṅkaya jaladharārthinā kāraṇamātrasya siddhe  yadāpi pratyakṣāpekṣayāhetuviśeṣeṇa kulālena karaṇavyāpāropadheyaviśeṣasya kumbhādikāryaviśeṣasya vyāptistadāpikutastatprasaṅgaḥ  yadāpyadhyavasāyamātrāpekṣayā sāmānyena viśeṣasya tadāpyayaṃ dūrataraḥ evaṃ tu vyavasthātonyathāvyāptigrahaṇe viśeṣeṇa sāmānyasya bhavatīti kathaṃ mṛnmayātkulālānumānamaprasaṅga  tatkāryakumbhādyapekṣayā atyantavisadṛśādapi prasaṅge dṛṣṭavyāptikasyeti daṇḍāpūpanyāya eṣa iti darśayituṃ mṛnmayagrahaṇam ZA PRVNAREA POjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalonanūbhayathā vyākhyānepi vyabhicārādeva nānumānaṃ tatkathamatiprasaṅga iticet  uktakrameṇopakāraka eva vyabhicārosmākaṃ na bādhakaḥ  tathāhi pramādvayavyāpārātikramenantaraprakārabahirbhāva vā pratijñāta pratibandhaniścayābhāvasādhaka evavyabhicāra iti  api ca vyabhicāro nāma sāmānyena gṛhītāyā vyāpteniyataviṣayāpekṣayā vighātamātanoti atha vyāptigrahaṇameva tanna bhavatīti vibhāvayati athasatyapi vyāptiprasa renumānamātraṃ khaṇḍayati ataevābādhita viṣayatvamapi liṅgalakṣaṇamākhyātamiti pakṣāḥ tatra prathamapakṣe sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ anyatrāpi tadvalādeva sādhyapratyāśā sā caniścitāpi khaṇḍitā kaciditi anyatrāpi śaṅkānivṛtteḥ tata eva tadgrahaṇavaiyarthyāt dvitoye tu na viśeṣaścetane  yathā hi kumbhakāreṇa kāryasāmānyasya pratyakṣeṇavyāptirgṛhītā vyabhicāreṇa durgṛhītā vyavasthāpyate tathā cetanyamātreṇāpi tatrāpipratyakṣavyāpāre viśeṣābhāvāt tṛtīye tu vyāptau satyāmeva vyabhicāreṇānumānamapāsyata iti mahīyasīyam ayogaparamparā  kevalamatra pakṣe etadāpatitaṃ yadīdamatra sādhanaṃ sādhyaṃ vyabhicarya na sthitaṃ tadāsādhyaṃ sādhayatīti  etacca sādhyavidhuraṃ sarvārthasākṣātkāriṇo nānyaḥ kartuṃ śaktaḥ  sa hiya eva dharmī tathāvidhamadhyamadhiśayito na bhavati tameva vā vyabhicāragocaratayā anumānabhājanīkaroti sarvavipakṣānīkṣaṇe tu tanmadhya eva kadācideṣopi sthāditi śaṅkānivṛtteḥ tasmādukta eva nyāya āśrayaṇayogyo vyabhicāraśca vyāptidurgrahaṇameva sādhayatīti kāryamātravyāptiḥ prakṛtakā raga viśeṣeṇāsaṃbhavinyeva sādhuriti gṛhītāyāṃ vyāptau yadi vihatirāśvāsavirahograho nāsau vyāpteb yadi ca na viśeṣo matimati abādhāpekṣāyāṃ na sakalavipakṣekṣaṇamṛtenirātaṅkastasmāna khalu phalamātre grahavidhiḥ iti saṃgrahaḥ ki cādāya samastavastuviṣayāṃ vyāpti punaścenmatātattajjātiṣu bādhakakramavaśātsvavyāpyatattat sthitiḥ īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānamtattajjātiṣu sādhakakramavaśādunnīyate kiṃ na sāyenāyāsakaśaktisaṃśayapadaṃ santo viśantīdṛśam ityantaraślokaḥ aparigaṇito nāma vastuvyāpāraviṣayoparigaṇitatamastvaviṣayaḥ  tatra kaevamanātmīyakāryajātinikarasya pratyekaṃ vyabhicārān dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā svakāryaṃjātiṣvevaniyantuṃ hetumapāravyāpāra pārayate  tathā ca sati yasyaiva sākṣādanīkṣito vyabhicāraḥtadeva tasya gamakamāśaktam  tadā śaṅkāsaṃbhavānneti cet  na kacidatīndriye tarhiniścayamayaṃ kuryāt  yajjātīyoddeśena pravṛttamadhyakṣaṃ sāmānya viṣayamavasthāpitaṃ tatrakaḥ sandeha iti cet  evaṃ tarhi parāparatadīyavyāpyajātiṣu tathaiva saṃśayapravṛttipratyanīkapramāṇavṛttyanusaraṇe āyātastṛtīyapādāpatitorthaḥ  tasmānna kāraṇaviśeṣeṇa buddhimatākāryamātrasya vyāptiḥ pratyetuṃ śakyetisiddha yādṛgityādisiddhāntaḥ athavā yaduktaṃ na śarīranirapekṣaprayatnavanmātreṇa kāryasya vyāptiḥ pratipattuṃ pāryatepratyakṣeṇa pratikṣepāt tādṛśasyetyādi tadevopasaṃharati siddhamitiyāvṛkṣosau śarīrādiyogī adhiṣṭhātā ceti  śeṣaṃ subodham  tādṛśaśca pratyakṣabādhādidoṣaviṣaya ityākūtam  nanu śarīravatyapi cetanatvaṃ dṛṣṭamitaratrāpi saṃbhavati iti yathāśarīriṇā vyāptaṃ kāryādi sidhyati tathābhimatenāpi ityatrāpi prāguktanyāyāt saṃjñāmātrādavaśiṣyamānāt sādhanamanorathamunmathnannāha vastubhede kumbhādau prasiddhasyakulālāderyo vācakaḥ śabdaśca tana iti tanmātrādabhidyamānasyābhimatasya pramāṇavyāpārāpekṣayā dūrīkṛtasya na yuktānumitiriti vyāptābhimatād vastuna iti prakṛtamarthāpanaṃ vākathamivetyāhapāṇḍudravyādivaddhutāśana iti ayamabhiprāyaḥ yadi śabdamātrasāmyenābhidyamānasyānumānaṃ śabdasāmyenābhidyamānādapi pāṇḍumna kiṃ na dhūmadhvajasyānumānam  atha tatra viśiṣṭa kāryasvabhāvāpekṣamjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvaloadhyakṣamanyavyāpti pratikṣipatīti nānumānamucyate tathā cetanamātrapratikṣepeṇāpipratyakṣaṃ ki na tadanumānaṃ nirasyati  etena yadā daśyamapi kāryāntaraṃ tiraskarotipratyakṣaṃ tadā keva kathā dṛkpathātiriktasya cetanamātrasyeti  astu tāvad vyāpyāpekṣayā vibhāga eva loke tathaiva pratīteḥ anyathātiprasaṅgācca vyāpakāpekṣayā tu yadyeṣa niyamo na syāt ko doṣa ityāśaṅkhyā pūrvoktamevetiprasaṅgaṃ bhaṅgayantareṇa taruṇayati anyathetyādi  valmīkasyeti valmīkajantorityarthaḥ tatkṛtiriti ghaṭādikṛtiḥ  a ayamarthaḥ yadi viśeṣeṇāpi vyāptimavasāya cetanamātraṃ sāmānyamanumātavyam tadā kumbhādikaraṇasya kulāle niyatasya cetanamātra paryaṃvasitatvāt ghaṭāderapi valmīkajantuḥ kartānumeya syāt yathāhi kumbhādeḥ kumbhakāreṇavyāptigrahaṇe caitanyamātreṇāviśeṣāt tasyāpyanumānamevaṃ valmīkaukasopi caitanyenānyāviśeṣāt kiṃ nānumānam  yadā ca śarīriṇā vyāptigrahe śarīriṇopyanyasya pratikṣepaḥtadā kā vārtātyanta visadṛśasyeti  na cātra bahutvenopayogaḥ ekātmanopi cetanyāditi valmīkasyeti nirdeśaḥ  etena dhūmāderapi jāṭharāderanumānākṣepo vyaktaḥ  vyabhicāracarcāyāṃ ca pūrvavat sarvamāvartanīyamiti yaduktaṃ prayatnavatā yadvaghāptaṃ sanniveśādi tanna siddhaṃ sindhubhūdharādau yacca siddhaṃtantra vyāpta miti tatrai tatsyāt nanu jātyuttaramidaṃ dharmabhedavikalpanāt tato yathāyatkṛtakaṃ tadanityaṃ ghaṭavaditi kṛte kaścidāha yadi ghaṭagataṃ kṛtakatvaṃ hetustadasiddha śabdeśabdagataṃ tvanitya saṃghāte ghaṭapaṭādāvabhāvādviruddham  atha sapakṣavad vipakṣetrapi nāstītimatiḥ tadā asādhāraṇamanaikāntikamiti  na ca tāvatā kṛtakatvaṃ tattvatośaktamevaanityatvasādhane tathedamapi  tathāhi yacca siddhaṃ tanna vyāptamityanena sapakṣāvṛttevirodhaḥvipakṣādapi nivṛttipakṣe vā asādhāraṇatvamākṛṣṭamiti  atha prakṛtakāryānurodhādadūṣaṇamevedamudghoṣyate  tathā sati kṛtakatvāderapi asādhanatvaprasaṅgaḥ sūtrakāravirodhaśca kāryasamasaṃjñayā asya dūṣaṇasya tena pratijñānāt  yadāhakāryatvānyatvaleśena yatsādhyāsiddhicodanam tatkāryasamametattu tridhā vaktrabhisandhitaḥ katiratyanteti mātṛkāsthaḥ pāṭhaḥ īśvaravādādhikāre vārtika saptaślokī vyākhyānamiti upacāramātrakṛttvenānyatvasya leśa uktaḥ vaktrabhiprāyeṇa traividhyaṃ ca darśita miti tadetadubhayamapyasāram prathamapakṣasya tāvat pūrvameva pratikṣepāt  uktaṃ hivyāptisādhakapramāṇapuraskṛtasvarūpasyābhede bhidyamānā api saṃbandhino vidhūtabhedāiva bhāsamānā na bādhakāḥ  tasya tu bhede abhedinopi bhinnavadābhāsamānāḥ kāryatvādayo dharmā na tadvayāpakasya sādhakā iti  vyāptigrahaṇaprakramaśca dvividho darśitaḥ tatra yadi nāśena kṛtakatvasyeva viparyabādhakabalād buddhimatāpi kāryatvāderavinābhāvagraha syāt tadā abhūtvā bhavanamātramiva kāraṇatvācca  na cakāraṇameva anārabdhadhūmasyāpi saṃbhavāditi na codyam trividhasyāpi vyavacchedasyasiddheḥ tathā hisāmagrayapekṣayānyasya cchede dravyavyapekṣayā yogyatāyāmayogasya siddhotyantaṃ ca miṣṭaṃ śeṣā upaplavāḥ pra vā yat punarastaṃ gatepi vastunyākārāntarabhāji vā sthirākāratayā bhāvanāyasya nirālambanatvamāpāditaṃ sarvasya tadapi vastubhāvanāpakṣe śobhate na vastudharmaṃbhāvanāpakṣe  vastudharmāṃśca kṣaṇikatvādayaḥ saṃsāraverāgyāt sphuṭībhāvabhājo bhāvayitumupakrāntāḥ  athaikatra pramāṇapariśuddhepi bhāvanājanitaveśadyasya vastuni visaṃvādasaṃdarśanādanyatrāpi ka āśvāsaḥ pramāṇapariśuddhimantareṇāśvāsa he torapyasyābhāvāttasyāśca saṃvādaniyatāvasāmarthyāt  tanna sthirāsthiraviṣayatvena viśeṣāt  asthiraṃhi vastu pradhvaṃsavikārābhyāṃ grasthata iti na saṃvādaḥ a vastudharmāstukṣaṇikatvādayo na kadācidvicchidyanta iti tadviṣaya sphuṭībhāvaḥ sarvadā sālambanaeva nanvetadapi na yuktam  na hi kṣaṇikatvādikaṃ nāma kiñcidasti vastu satve vātadeva nityamāsaktamiti sarvamayatnaśīrṇam  avastutve ca tadeva nirālambanatvam  tasmādbhavanmatepi kṣaṇikatvaṃ nāma kṣaṇikā eva bhāvarāśayoparāmṛṣṭabhedāḥ bhedāntaratiraskāreṇocyante  tathā ca sati kṣaṇikatvabhāvanetyapi kṣaṇikapadārthasārthabhāvanetyevārthaḥ  tāvatātānyeva vastūni bhāvyamānāni sphuṭībhavantīti sa eva doṣaḥ  athābhinnānyapi kṣaṇikatvādoni bhinnānīva tāvatpratibhānti  tathāpyadhyavasāyād vastugatānyeva bhāvyanta iti nataddoṣānmuktiḥ taṭasthatayā bhāvayitumaśakyatvāt  tathā ca truṭyadrūpametad vastujātamityayamevākāro bhāvanāyāḥ tatkathaṃ vastutattvabhāvanāpakṣepi vastusaṃsparśaparihāra  parihāre cāvastvantarabhāvanaiva syānna dharmabhāvanā  satyam  yadyapi vastutattvabhāvanathāpi sāmānyenākṣiptaṃ vastutathāpi na tasya sphuṭībhāvaḥ tattvamātratātparya paryavasānāt  tattvabhāvanaiva hi sphuṭībhavantīsaṃsārāpasāraṇasaraṇiḥ  na hi kāminīkalevaraṃ sākṣātkṛtaṃ rāgasaṃkocamācarati kiṃtvanityaduḥkhāditvameva  atastatraiva tātparyāt tadeva vaiśadyamāpadyate bhāvanayā na vastu nanu tatra tātparyepi vastudharma sphuṭībhavati na vastviti kā saṅgatiḥ bhāvanayā dvayorapikroḍīkaraṇāt  kīdṛśo vā dharmiṇamaspṛśato dharmamātrasya sphuṭībhāvaḥ  tadetadākāśacitraṇam na khalu hālikasyāpi pratyayamātanoti yoginirṇayaprakaraṇamnaiṣa doṣaḥ dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭībhāvamaspṛśatopi dharmamātrasya sphuṭībhāvadarśanāt kevalaṃ vastupratyāsatyanapekṣya na sphuṭasphuraṇamiti syāt  sphuṭībhāvopi tasya tadviṣayasannidhau yatnamanapekṣya jhagiti tajjñāne tattadākārasphuraṇaṃ nāma vastuprattyāsatyapekṣā tuna kṣīyate dharmatvādeva priyatvādivat  tathā hi nimbarasādau tāvat priyatvamabhyasyamānaṃsphuṭībhavadṛṣṭam  naca nimbādeḥ sa dharma iti tadbhāvanayā nimbādyapi svajanmadeśasthaṃrasanāprasaṅgi vā sphuṭaṃ sphuradasti yāvanna viparyayabhāvanābhiyogaprakarṣaḥ  na ca sphuṭībhūtaṃpriyatvamapi taṭasthamupalabhyate nimbādyanubhavamanapekṣya kiṃ tu yadā yadā nimbādyanubhavatadā tadā jhagiti priyatvamanubhavaviṣayaḥ na prāgivodvejakamanubhayaṃ vetyeṣa eva dharmasphuṭībhāvārthaḥ yathā hi kāminyādivastuni sphuṭobhūtepi na yathā samayasiddhastattvasphuṭībhāvaḥtathā tattvabhāvanayāpi na vastusphuṭībhāva ubhayo parasparāvyabhicārepīti kīdṛśodoṣa  atha na karmākṣepānmātrayā tathopalabdheḥ  vidyamānānāṃca kṣaṇānāmavaśyaṃ vaisadṛśyamaṇīyopi saṃbhavi anyathā sarvātmanā sādṛśye tattvaprasaṅgāt  tat tathāvidhasūkṣmabhedāvadhāraṇadhūryeṇākṣavijñānenaiva sādhyasiddheranarthakaṃyogijñānam etena duḥkhānātmādisākṣātkāro vyākhyātaḥ  puruṣavapuṣā cendriyamantareṇabhavitumaśakyamiti yogijñānamanutpādanīyamastu  tadapyayuktam  na hi saṃbhāvanāmātropanītaṃ netrabalamavalambya saṃvyavahāriṇā prekṣeṇa pramāṇaparāyaṇo mārga parihatuśakyaḥ  tadabhyāsasahakārikameva vā tathāvidhendriyaśaktisādhanamityaparihāryeṇa yogijñānenasamānakakṣatāyāmapi indriyajñānasya na kaścid doṣaḥ  vaiyarthyaa mekasyeti cet katareṇa punaḥ svakāraṇopanidhānadharmaṇoranayoḥ svavyāpāravaiyarthyabhayānnivartitavyambojādiṣvivāntyakṣaṇaprāpteṣu aprāmāṇyamekasyāstviti cet  bījādiṣvapyekasyākāraṇatvamastu  sarveṣāṃsamānasāmarthyānāṃ katamadekamakāraṇamavasthāpayituṃ śakyamiti cet  paricchedabalavatojñānayorapi kimekamapramāṇīkriyatām  parasparāpekṣayā mā bhūdubhayamapi pramāṇamiti cet bījādiṣvapi naikamapi kāraṇatvamastviti samānam  gṛhītagrāhitvaṃ nāma nāstyeva  tarhidoṣa iti cet na kālabhedena tasya svīkārāt  gṛhītagrahaṇaṃ hi taducyate na gṛhyamāṇasthayathā kṛtasya karaṇasvīkārekārakatvam na tu kriyamāṇakaraṇe bījādivadeva  tasmādabhinnakālapakṣe naiṣa doṣaḥ OVERyoginirṇayaprakaraṇamnanu tathāpyā kāradvayasphuraṇaprasaṅga iti cet  satyam satyajñānākārastāvaddhantasamānadeśaḥ anyathā bhramatvaprasaṅgāt  atastāvākārāvapratighau kayā rītyā sphurata itiko nirṇetuṃ kṣamaḥ dāhaacintyā yogināṃ gatiḥpra vā  iti  tasmād dṛṣṭāntābhāvāt kimivāniṣṭaṃ kimiva vā na doṣa ityubhayorapi nāvasaraḥ samasamayatayā tarhīndriyajñānānapekṣāyāṃ svātantryadoṣa uktaḥ kathaṃ parihartavyaḥ  indriyāpekṣayaivaparihariṣyata iti nottaram  tadā hi tadapīndriyajñānameva syāt tadvyāpārānuvidhānāt na yogijñānaṃ nāma kiñcit tadvaramekameva svīkṛtamiti na bhedapakṣaḥ kṣamaḥ  naivam tathā hi mā bhūdindriyāpekṣā  vīkṣaṇaṃ tu yathā svasāmarthyānurūpāṃ yogyadeśāvasthitimapekṣya svavijñānajananepravartate tathā manaindriyamapi pravartiṣyate aprāpyakāritāyā ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇatvātarthavattāyāśca manasopi tadānīmiṣṭatvāt  pṛthagjanasantānasya tu na tādṛśī śaktiḥyato netraśrotravanmanopi tādṛṅmaryādayā yogyadeśasthamarthasahakāriṇamāsādya vedanamutpādayediti nātiprasaṅgaḥ  taddaśāyāṃ tu śrutinayanayoriva manasopi kiyavareṇaviṣayasannidhivyavastheti ka evaṃ pramātuṃ kṣama  kevalametāvaducyate yāvattena śakyamadhigantuṃ svākārārpaṇasahaṃ sahakāri vastu tāvaditarajanāsādhāraṇatruṭyadrūpatayā tasyagocarībhavati  tathā ca sati vastvākāro vastukṛta eva na bhāvanājanita iti navisaṃvādaśaṅkā nanu cakṣurādestāvadvarataragocarīkaraṇe dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ manasastu nendriyātikrameṇasarvaviṣayasyeti cet na paracittajñānādīnāṃ saṃbhavāt  tadapi neṣṭamekeṣāmiticet  adṛṣṭamātreṇa pratikṣepāyogāt  upāyābhāvāditi cet  upāyābhāvepinānupalambhamātrādanya upāya  tasmād yadyevaṃ syāt tadā yogi bnāmindriyamanojñānayorbhedapakṣepi na nirvāha ityupakṣepārthaḥ  nirvāhastvanyathāpi darśita eva evaṃca sati kālabhedapakṣepi na doṣaḥ yadi sā prathamaṃ manojñānavṛttiḥ yadicendriyapathātikrameṇa vṛttiḥ  indriyajñānaṃ tu tasya tadapekṣayā prāmāṇyavirahepi navyathayatītyalaṃ vistareṇa jñānaśrīmitra nibandhāvalotadevaṃ yogijñāne tattvabhāvanādhikārādarthākārorthakṛta eva  bhāvanayā punastadīyasantāne netra ivāñjanaviśeṣeṇa śaktiratiśayavatī kācidarpitā yayetarajanāsādhāraṇaṃdarśanamasya  yathoktaṃ prāk  yadi tarhi viṣayajanyameva yogijñānamatītānāgataparijñānasyakā vārtā  tadetatprastāvānavagāhanasya phalam  upayuktasarvajñādhikāreṇa hi vastudharmabhāvanopakṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ  na sarvasarvajñapakṣāpekṣayā tatotītānāgatamapratīyamānamapi na bādhakam tāvataiva duḥkhanirodhasiddheḥ parasmai ca niṣkampadeśanāvatārāt yat punaḥ kaṇikāyāṃ kṣaṇikāditattvabhāvanādvāreṇa taddharmiṇāṃ samastavastūnāmevabhāvanayā tadākārajñānotpādanātsākṣātkaraṇamutthāpya dūṣaṇamabhidhīyate yogijñānasyatadavadhoraṇīyameva vārtikabhāṣyādivādabahirbhāvāt  anyathārabdheva nityaduḥkhādibhāvanāsā ca sarvasarvajñatvamevārpayatoti yadyabhipretaṃ syāt kathaṃ yatnenotthāpya tatparihārovārtikenāsmābhiḥ śakyate jñātumiti santoṣa iṣyateityādinā bhāṣye ca  yadi punastadavasthāprāptau nirāvaraṇāntaḥkaraṇasya kāruṇyātiśayātsarvākāraparārtha prārthanaparatayā sakalagocaracāriṇi cetasi ciravirūḍhotsāhasya tādṛgupāyaviśeṣādhigamo bhaviṣyati yamanutiṣṭhataḥ pratiparamāṇu sarvavastuviṣayaṃ yathādeśakālaṃ pratyavasthānukāri sphuṭataraṃ jñānamudīyāt  tadā na tāvadvastuvyabhicārakṛtaṃ visaṃvāditvam nāpinirālambanatvam vastūnāmeva pratibhāsanāt athotpattisārūpyābhyāmālambanavyavasthābhinnakālaṃ kathaṃ grāhyamiti ced grāhyatāṃ viduḥ hetutvameva yuktijñā jñānākārāpaṃṇakṣamam pra vā iti vacanāt tataḥ sārūpyamekama kiñcitkaramiti kathamanālambanatvaparihāra tadayuktam tat khalu lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthagjanāpekṣayā bahirathaṃ prati samasamayabhāvinānupakāryeṇa jñānena grahaṇaniṣedhaparam tathā prastāvāt  tattvatastu yadeva yatra pratibhāsatetadeva tasyālambanamucyate  yathendriyapratyakṣe bāhyamanyatra svākāraḥ pratibhāsavaśātyoginirṇayaprakaraṇampratyakṣasya grahaṇāṃgrahaṇe iti hi prathamaparicchedavṛttiḥ  tatra bāhyasya pratibhāso nāmatadākārotpattimātram  tathā hi bahivicchinnākārodayasaṃvedanamātrādidaṃ dṛṣṭamitibhavati  na khalu tatsaṃkalpakāle utpattiraparāpekṣyate a tasyāḥ paścānniśceyatvātphalaprāptayā vā abhyāsena vā  sa ca tadākārodaya indriyapratyakṣerthād bhrame viplavāt vikalpe vāsanātaḥ  tatrārthajanye saṃvādonyatra viparyayo bahirapekṣayā svarūpe sarvatrasaṃvādaniyamāt  tatobhipretasaṃvāde vedane tadutpattimantareṇa na saṃvādo nāpi tādrdhyamititatra tadutpattiprārthanā  ataeva tadākārataiva prāmāṇyam sārūpyatadutpattī ca saṃvedyalakṣaṇamityubhayamavirodhi yatra tu bhāvanāviśeṣabalādeva devatādhipatyāt satyasvapnavadarthākāramarthayāthātmyanāntaroyakaṃ jñānam tatra na kiñcit tadutpattyā  yad vārtikam  rūpādeścetasaścaivam aviśuddhadhiyaṃ prati grāhya grāhaka cinteyamacintyā yogināṃ gatiḥ iti  tasmād bāhye pṛthagjanasya sārūpyotpattibhyāṃ vedyasthitiḥ yoginaḥ sārūpyamātreṇāpi  svarūpe yogyatāmātreṇaiveti nyāyaḥ  bhāvibhūtayostahi yadi svarūpasphuraṇaṃvartamānataiva syāt pra vā  atha svarūpamasannihitaṃ jñānameva tadākāramiti nirālambanaṃ niyamena tadapināsti  yasmādasannihitepyarthe bhāvanābalāñcet taddeśakālānukāri vijñānaṃ kathamanālambanam  sphuraṇarītiviśeṣeṇa tu kālabhedavikalpodayāt tadanurūpānuṣṭhāne niyatatvāttatprāpteḥ  yadbhāṣyamyathā sa dṛṣṭaḥ śaradādikālayuktastathā tasya na bādhitatvam iti  yadvā saṃcityeva kālabhedabhāgivasturūpapratītayebhedādhyavasāyaḥ  yathoktamyad yadicchati vai boddhumpra vā bhā  samādhisamāpattervyutthāne kālaityādi  krameṇa tvanābhogamapi jñānamavirodhi  jñānamātrasya tattvataḥ sphuraṇācca na tula ratna niba pṛ   ta sa  jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalauṃvartamānatāprasaṅgaḥ yathā nirākāravāde vastusvarūpasyaiva sphuraṇāditi  yadyapi cavartamānepi jñānākārasyaiva sphuraṇaṃ tathāpi vartamānatayaivādhyavasāyastatra  evaṃdūrāsannādibhedepi veditavyam  tatra yathādhyavasāyaprāptau niyamena saṃvādāt prāmāṇyamanyadā viparyayaḥ yathā svapnakāminyādau  pratibhāsvargasādhanāgniṣṭomādivikalpe cabhāvinaḥ spaṣṭarūpasya pratibhāsābhāvādeva na cintā  na ca tatra prekṣavyāvahārikasyaprāptiniyamaniścayosti prastutepi ko niścaya iti cet  kasya punaratra niścayaścintyate tasya tadanyasyavā  yadi tasya tadā yathābhyāsāt parito nirastavibhramāśaṅka sādhanajñāne pṛthagjanasyatathā yoginopyatyantābhyāsād bhāvibhūtādipratibhāsa kena vāryate  athānyasyatadedamāyātam  yāvadanyasya na prāmāṇyabodhastāvanna pramāṇam  yāvacca na pramāṇaṃtāvannānyasya prāmāṇyabodhobhrānta iti na kiñcitpramāṇaṃ syāt  tannābhiveśapāravaśyenakiñcit  tasmādupāyaviśeṣab sacivabhāvanābhedasyāhatyāsphuraṇāt tādṛsiddhāvevasaṃśayo na tu siddhepi nirālambanatvādidoṣairupadravaḥ śakyaḥ yacca vikalpena bāhyasyāgrahaṇepyadhyavaseyatayā sphuṭībhāvamāśaṃkya yadanumānenagṛhyate yaccādhyavasoyate te dvenyanivṛttī na vastunī svalakṣaṇāvagāhitvebhilāpasaṃsagaṃyogyapratibhāsānupapatterityāha tadapyasaṃbaddham  tathā hi yathā tathā vā bauddhasiddhāntagandhenavyavahāraḥ kāminyākāravikalpabhāvanavat kṣaṇikākārasyāpi paryante viśadopādeyakṣaṇaprasavastu dunivāraḥ  yadi punarīdṛgapohasthitiḥ kṣaṇika vikalpaikatalpaśāyinī na kāminyādivikalpamanvetītyupapādayiṣyasi tathaiva grahīṣyāmaḥ  na cādhyavaseyamavastunivṛttimātraṃ vā dharmottarepi hi mate svalakṣaṇamadhyavaseyamiti sthitiḥ nanu vahniḥ pratoto mayetyadhyavasāyākāraḥ  tatra ca svalakṣaṇasphuraṇamitisāhasam vikalpādhyavasāyayorekārthatvāt  satyam na tu tatra sphuratīti tāvatāsvalakṣaṇamadhyavasitamucyate  asphuraṇe tarhyabodhāt kathamavasāya  sphuraṇepi pratibhāsa evāsau kathamadhyavasāyaḥ  na ca pratibhāsādhyavasāyāvadhyekārthau  pratibhāsohi sākṣāt sphuraṇamasphuraṇepi pravṛttiviṣayīkaraṇamekavyāvṛtyullekhasāmarthyādadhyavasāyobhāṣyamataḥ  ato yadanurūpamanuṣṭhānaṃ tadadhyavaseyam pratibhāsamānarūpānanupraviṣṭameva tacca kacidāropitamātram  kacivasturūpam  prakṛtaṃ tu pramāṇavyāpārasvīkārād vasturūpameveti kathamucyate nivṛttimātramavastu vādhyavaseyamityāstāṃ tāvadanārabdhanirbaṃndhaḥ yoginirṇayaprakaraṇampratibhāsopi vikalpe vyāvṛttākārasya na vyāvṛttimātrasya yadyanubhavānusāraḥ  sarvadāyad vā tad vā rākṣasādi pratibhāseta  bhāvanayā punaradhyavasitākāreṇa pariṇatiabādhyā tatrāropitamātredhyavaseye nirālambanatvam  sati tu tadevālambanaṃ yathānantaramuktam yattvāha arthaṃsyālambanapratyayatvaṃ vijñānaṃ pratīndriyāpekṣatvena vyāptam  taccāsmāt svaviruddhopalabdhyā nivartamānamālambanapratyayatvamapyarthasya nivartayatīti tatrāvyāpaka viruddhopalambanapratyayatvendriyāpekṣatvayorvyāpyakabhāvamaprasādhyapramāṇenalabdhi sphuṭayatīti mahadvaidagdhyam  tathā darśanāditi cet  darśanā darśanameva hipramāṇīkṛtya sthīyatām kimevaṃvidhapramāṇopanyāsavyasanena  tasmādindriyamanapekṣyāpi yadyālambanabhāvaṃ bhāvaḥ svīkuryāt na bādhakamutpaśyāmaḥ  athātroktameva nakhalvindhanaviśeṣo dhūmaheturiti vināpi dahanaṃ sahasreṇāpi saṃskārairdhūmamādhatte  tadādhāne vā samastakārya hetvanumānocchedaprasaṅgaḥ  tasmāt jñānamapīndriyasāpekṣādarthādutpattidharmakam pratyālambanabhāvaindriyavyāpāravirahe ca samastā la parakāraṇasannidhāvasannidhīyamānasattākaṃtatpratibaddhaṃ siddhamiti kathamindriyānapekṣyasyārthasya svavijñānaṃiti cet  etadapi paracittajñānasaṃbhavena prativyūḍham  iṣṭāśca paracittavedinaścārvāka mīmāṃsakavyatiriktaiḥ  cārvākāderapi sandehānnāparā gatiḥ  sandehe ca vipakṣādekāntavyāvṛtterayogaḥ  nanu jñāna kāryasyendriyāpekṣā niyamādeva nānyatra sandeho dahanāpekṣadhūmavat  yadyevaṃ rūpajñānasya vīkṣaṇāpekṣaṇe yādṛśī sāmagrī sā na saṃcaraṇaviśeṣasyacaraṇāpekṣaṇe kalayāpi hīyate tat kathaṃ na dhūmadṛṣṭāntaścaraṇavirahiṇāmuragādīnāṃgamananiṣedhāya prabhurabhūt  kathaṃ vā karādivyāpārasaṅga sāvegamantrodgāraparamparāsādhyamekeṣāṃ viṣaśamanādikāryaṃ samādhimātrādanyasya  na caivaṃ dhūmopi kacidindhanedahanānapekṣodayo dṛṣṭo yatotrāpi tathā śaṅkayeta tasmād bahirbhuvo bhāvā yathā hetuphalabhāvenopalambhabhāja te tathaiva niyatavṛttayaḥ  cittasantānasya tu vicitrakarmābhisaṃskārasāmarthyād vicitra eva vivartaḥ atastadāśrayakāryamekatra yāvadapekṣaṃ tāvadapekṣamanyatrāpīti na niyantuṃ śakyam  tatkathaṃ paracittavedanāderabhāva eva  yadi ca dhūmavadanalamanapekṣya nendriyaṃ buddhiḥ tadāsvaviṣayepyutkarṣaghoṣaṇāvīkṣaṇādīnāṃ dīnaiva syāt  tathā hi yāvaddeśaṃ dahanendhanādijñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalaudhūmādisādhanamupalabdhaṃ na tāvaddeśātikrame samartham  evaṃ yāvaddeśesmākaṃ viṣayendriyādivedanamutpāditavat kathaṃ tadatikrame gṛdhrādīnāmutpādayet  utpādane vā nendhanadahanādikakṣāṃ kṣamate cittasantānāśrayā sāmagrī  nāpi dhūmakakṣāṃ buddhiḥ ataḥ sahakāriṇotivyavadhānavaduvaikalyepi ki na kutaścit viśeṣātsaṃbhāvyate  jātikṛtosau vibhāgaḥ na cittasantānāśrayāditi cet na jātirapihi vicitrakarmādhipatyādeva vicitrasvarūpopasaṃhārasvabhāvā karma ca na cittādanyaditina cittāśrayatvaparihāraḥ  athendriyasya prādhyakāritayā sarvaiva vijñānajananasāmagrīsādhāraṇadeśetyucyate  tathāpi kasmāt punastāvad dūradeśasthitimati kacillocanaruḍhāṃśaśleṣa kacidavagiva viśrāma iti kimatra vaktavyaṃ karmādhipatyādanyatra  tasmāttadāśrayasya cittasantānasya citraiva śaktiḥ nahi bahirapi śakyamevam  anyathā sadṛśapradeśasthāyinoḥ pradīpayoralpakasyakasyacid dūrasāriṇī kiraṇasaṃhatiritarasya punarkhācīnacāriṇī syāt  atha mantraprabhāvādevamapi syāt sarīsṛpadṛśā ca māndyamādadhātīti cet  sa tarhi cittasantatereva prabhāvaḥ  mantrepi puruṣamāhātmyakṛta eva  yathā vārtike nirṇītamapauruṣeyatvepi mantrāṇāṃ na puruṣanirapekṣāṇāṃ b śakti  tataśca puruṣa evamantrādyupāyena bāhyavastuśaktivyavasthāṃ dusthayatīti āyātamiti prastute kimasaṃbhāvanam yathā ca locanāpekṣaḥ padārthasyālambanabhāvo dṛṣṭa iti tanniyata iṣṭaḥ tathālokāpekṣopidṛṣṭa iti na saṃtamase paśyeyurulūkādayaḥ  tathā dṛṣṭatvānna doṣa iti cet  tathādṛṣṭatvādeva hatosi  tathā hi netrālokayo samānepyapekṣāsādhananyāye cittasyācintyaśaktitayā anyatarollaṅghanadarśanamanyadapi śaṅkayā kalaṅkayati  na tvadarśane śakyamevam  atha tādṛśi jñānatvasāmānyavantyapi kāryāṇītarajātibhedabhāñjīti nānapekṣyasādhanasāmagrībhedamudiyurityucyate kena punaḥ prakṛtajñānasyāpyalaukikasya pṛthagjaajñānena sahraikajātitāyāṃ pratāritosi  asattvādeva tarhi tasya na jātibheda iti cet  asattvamiti jātibhedābhāvādevendriyāpekṣayā niyamasaṃbhavāditītaretarāśrayaḥ  tasmāt sādhāraṇakarmanirjātānāmasmadādīnāmanubhavabhedaṃ pratīndriyāpekṣatvamālambanatvasya vyāpakamapi na svanivṛttyā anubhavamātraṃ prati nivartaka bhavitumarhati viśeṣoddeśenaiva vyāptisiddheḥ athānubhavamātramekīkṛtya vyāptiriṣyate  tadā viparyayādhakābhāvāt vyāptireva nayoginirṇayaprakaraṇamsidhyati hetuphalaniyamāśrayastu dhvasto dhūmādisādhāraṇyānupapatte vicitrakarmābhisaṃskārādacintyaśaktisvāntasantānasaṃbhāvinonubhavamātrasya  viśeṣāśraye ca na sarvopasaṃhāravatī vyāptiriti sa eva doṣo viśeṣavatvaṃ nāma yadapyayamāha bhāvanāyāścābhūtārthāyā arthānapekṣāyā eva viśadajñānajananasāmathyamupalabdhaṃ kāmāturādivartanyā iti bhūtārthāpi tannirapekṣaiva samartheti nārthasyaālambanapratyayatvaṃ doṣakṣayo bhāvīti mārgābhyāsapravṛtti ravyāhṛtā bhavati  prāpyasaṃkalpo hi sarvatrapravartakaḥ  sa cedasti vastutathābhāvavyatirekepi kaḥ pravṛtti nivartayati  yena hitahi tathānumānena niścitaṃ kṣaṇikatādi tasya pravṛttiriti cet  niścayasya sātmībhāvābhāvādanādyavidyāvāsanāvaśīkṛtena cetasā niścayānucitasyaiva vyavahārasya pravartanāt ataeva darśanamārgepi labdhe bhāvanāmārgāpekṣaṇamuktaṃ vārtikenveṣaṇīyam  tasmāttatphalalābhādarvāgabhyāsovidyayeva saṃpādyate  abhyāsācca siddhaḥ sarvajña iti nyāyabhūṣaṇasya ca yogācārapakṣāpekṣayā dūṣaṇamaprastutam bahirarthamabhyupagamyaivasādhanaprakramāt  tatrāpi sarvasarvajñapakṣopakṣipto bādhastadanabhyupagamādeva nirastaḥ na cāsau bādha eva saṃśayamātrasādhanatvāt  tathā hi yattāvadatītānāgataviṣayatvaniṣedhārthamuktam na hyasataḥ kaścidākārostīti satyamidānīmevametat  tatastajanyajñānenāgrahaṇamapi satyam  satyasvapnādivadanyathāpi tu saṃbhāvanā na śakyaniṣedhetidarśitam  na ca yathedānīṃ na kaścidākārastathā kālāntarepi bhūtabhāvinoḥ  tathāsati bhūtabhāvitvamapi na syāt karikesaravat  abhramāvisaṃvādauca prāgevacintitau yatpunarāha na cāvisaṃvāditvamapi tvanmate yuktam yataḥ prāpyārthadarśakatvaṃ vāpravṛttiviṣayopadarśakatvaṃ vāvabhātārthakriyāniṣpattirvā bhavatāmavisaṃvāditvamabhipretam na caitadatītādyarthajñānasya saṃbhavati vartamānārthajñānasyāpi kṣaṇikatvapakṣe nopapadyata tula ratna niba pṛ   tula saiva pṛ   tula saiva pṛ   tulasaiva pṛ jñānaśrīmitra nibandhāvaloṃeveti  tadapīrṣyāpāravaśyamātram upapattividhuratvād  yadi tāvad bhāvibhūtayoḥkālavyavadhānena tathocyate tadā deśavyavadhānepi eṣa prasaṅga iti pravṛttiyogyadeśepipradarśakamapramāṇaṃ syāt  tadasti tāvaditi cet  anyadapi bhāvi bhūtaṃ vā tatkālenāstīti cet  taddeśe vartamānamapi nāstīti samānam  arthakriyāpi yathā taddeśasannidhau tathā tatkālasannidhāviti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ  vartamānasya kṣaṇikatvepiekatvāropasāmarthyānna vyāvahārikaṃ prati pramāṇatāyāḥ kṣatiḥ tadabhiprāyāt saṃvādasyavyavasthitatvāditi yañca kaumārilaiḥ a sarvasarvavidi kāraṇānupalabdhimupakramya tasya kāraṇamindriyajñānaṃ vā mānasaṃ vā bhāvanābalajaṃ vā bhāvanābalajamapi cākṣuṣaṃ mānasaṃ vetivikalpya dūṣaṇamārabdham tat saṃbhāvanādaurbalyāviṣkaraṇamātraṃ nābhāvaniścayaphalamyathendriyāpekṣālambanatvacintāyāṃ carcitam  na ca kāraṇānupalabdheraniścayaḥ phalamtata eva dharmādharmaviṣayepi bhāvanābalajasya balamapalapitumaśakyam  tataḥ kāśikākārasthāpi yogināṃ dharmādharmayoraparokṣapratibhāsaṃ jñānaṃ nāsti indriya sannikarṣābhāvādasmadādivadityanumānamanaikāntikam vipakṣavyāvṛttarekāntena pratipattumaśakyatvāt  kiṃ ca dharmādharmajñānamiti karmaphalasaṃbandha mātraparijñānametat  tacca jātismaratvasaṃbhave durnivāram  tataḥ parijñānasaṃbhavāt bhāvanāpariniṣpattau idaṃ suvarṇādyevaṃprayujyamānametatsādhanamiti jhagiti vikalpotpādanapaṭīyaḥ pratyakṣamudayamāsādayeditikisanupapannam  kevalaṃ jātismṛtau pratipattavyam  tatra cādarśanamātramapramāṇamiti nasarvathā niṣedhābhidhānaṃ sādhu  yathā hi sannipātādibhirabhyastavismaraṇasaṃbhavepismaraṇamapi keṣāñcid dṛṣṭam tathā garbhāvāsapīḍayāpi kasyacit prajñātaikṣṇyātpuṇyodayāt pīḍāmāndyācca samanantarajātismaraṇamapi bhavat sarvathā niṣeddhumaśakyamacārvākaṇa saṃbhave cāsyānekajanmāntaragocarīkaraṇasyāpi saṃbhavāt krameṇa sarvaviṣayasaṃkalpasaṃbhavāvirodhād viṣayānavagamakṛto bhāvanānudayadoṣaḥ parihṛtaḥ āgamāccalokasanniveśaṃ yathāvat parigṛhya bhāvanāsaṃbhavāt  yadyapi nāgamaḥ pramāṇam tathāpigambhīra pramāṇāntarasaṃvādasaṃdarśinaḥ śraddhāvataḥ kiṃ na saṃbhavet  tatprameyasyāvaitathye casiddhaṃ sādhyam  samudāyavikalpābhyāmevāvayavasyāpi sphuṭībhāvo dṛṣṭa eva  krameṇasūkṣmādyabhivyaktiśceti  ślo vā kāśikā prathamasaṃpuḍhe pū yoginirṇayaprakaraṇametena tadapi nirastaṃ yadabhyastaikaśāstrasyānyatrāśaktirubhayā vā bahu bahudhāpratirūpate paramapuruṣārthā padādibhiḥ  na hyatra vimatiḥ  idaṃ punarasti prathamaśāstrābhyāseprayāso yāvān na tāvān vijātīyābhidheyepyanyatra  evaṃ pāṭavaprakarṣaparamparāyāmaśrutepi kasyacit tathā prakarṣo yathā nānyasya śrutepi  tato janmāntarasmṛtisaṃbhavebhūyobhyāsādanabhyasteṣvapi vasturūpeṣūhāpohasaṃbhavānna niḥkleśāvasthaḥ parārthasamarthatayātāvataiva sthāsyati  yad vā sarvasaṃkalpasaṃbhavād bhāvanābhiyuktā vyaktīkariṣyantisarva svecchāto yoginaḥ  ata eva sarvāvagatipakṣe bhāvanānarthakyodbhāvanamapyanarthakamniṣpannāvaśya kārya b caturāyaṃsatyabhāvanasya sarvaviṣayānumānasaṃbhave svecchāyāḥpratipādanāt atha sarvavastusākṣātkārenyadeva sukhaṃ parārthasādhanaṃ veti paśyenna bhāvanayāparikheda kaścittadavasthasya sukaraśca sarvasphuṭībhāva saṃbhavatīti mahodadhināpi nādhikaṃkiñciduktam  uktaṃ ca tāvataiva pratyuktam  tasmād yathā yathā cintyate saṃśayamātraphala sarvavidi dūṣaṇopanyāso naikāntena bāṃdhe vikalpa  prakṛtasarvajñasya tu sādhanamekāntenaiva  tatrāpi na deśakālapuruṣaniyama iti cet  na tadapekṣāyāṃ sādhanasyaaprayuktatvāt  sarvathāpavādinaṃ prati hi sādhanametat  tacca deśādyaniyamepi kṛtārtham tathā caivaṃvidhamudbheditamasmābhiḥ sarvajñasiddhāviti  vākyetra pāṭhāśuddhiḥ  yoginirṇayo nāma prakaraṇaṃ samāptam  advaitabinduprakaraṇam iha bahirarthābhiniveśino manoratho yad yathā pratīyate tat tathā saditivyavasthāpyate yathā kuvalayaṃ nīlarūpatayā  vijñānād vyatiriktarūpatayā ca pratīyanteghaṭādaya iti svabhāvahetuḥ  nātrāsiddhiḥ grāhakāṅgād vicchinnena tarjanīnirdeśayogyenapurovasthāyinā rūpeṇa ghaṭādyākārasya pratibhāsādhyavasāyābhyāṃ kroḍīkaraṇāt  tathāhyayaṃ ghaṭo nāyaṃ ghaṭa iti pratītiḥ pratyātmavedyā sarvapuruṣāṇāmavyutpanna saṃketānāmapisaṃjñāviśeṣollekha vimukhastadanurūpa evāntarjanya  bālopi sukhasādhanaṃ stanamavalokyatadabhimukhe karamukhe prahiṇvan bahiravasāyasacivamātmānamātanoti  tataśca vyatiriktenarūpeṇa ghaṭādyākārasya pratītirnāsiddhipathaprasthāyinī  nāpi virodhinī sādhyena sapakṣesaṃbhavasya darśitatvāt  viparyayavyāptasya ca viruddhasya tadasaṃbhavāt ataeva ca nāsādhāraṇatvam nāpi sandigdhānvayatvam vipakṣedarśanācca nasādhāraṇānekāntaḥ  na ca vaktavyaṃ kāmalinaḥ pītaśaṅkhapratītāvapi na tathaiva vyavasthākeśoṇḍūkapratītau vā taimirikasya ataḥ sādhāraṇatvameveti bādhakagrastatvena tatpratīteḥbhrāntatvena pratyakṣavyāpāravirahāt  prastutastu bādhakābhāvādbhrāntyasiddheradhyakṣavyāpāraeva  na ca kadācidatrāpi syād bādhakamityanāśvāsaḥ sarvatra pratyakṣavyāpārocchedaprasaṅgāt  tasmātdeśakālanarānyatve bādhake sati nākṣajam ghaṭādibhedabodhastu pratyakṣastadabhāvataḥ evaṃ tarhi pratyakṣavyāpāre kimanumānenetyapi na codyam vyavahārasādhanasyavivakṣitatvāt  pratyakṣagocare hi vivādasaṃbhavo nānumānaprayojye viśrāmyati  tatrayathā pratyakṣepi gavi kutaścidāropāt mūḍhastadvayavahāramapravartayan sāsnādisamudāyātmakatvena pravattyaṃte abhāvavyavahāraṃ vānupalabdhyā tathā pratyakṣepi grāhyagrāhakayorbhedaāgamāntarānusārī tathāpratītyā vyavahāryaṃta iti na doṣaḥ  sa cāyaṃ vyavahāraḥtanmātranibandhanaḥ a  sakṛtpravartanādeva siddhaḥ  na hi kuvalayādāvapi nīlādijñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauvyavahāre tathā pratibhāsādhyavasāyābhyāmanyadadhikaṃ vā kiñcit nimittamasti tanmātratopravṛttiprasaṅgāt arthakriyāsaṃvādopi hi prathamāyāṃ pravṛttau gaveṣyate  abhyāsavastutanmātranibandhana evāsau vyavahāraḥ  prastute tu bhedavyavahāre sarvatra evānādikālikābhyāsapāṭavabhṛto lakṣyante  uktaṃ hibālospi hiityādi tasmād vyavahārapragalbhasya tathā pratītimātrapratibaddhastathāvyavahāraḥ  tasminsādhye tathā pratīyamānatvaṃ tadanyānapekṣatvena vyāpyate  yadi ca kacit tathā pratītāvapitathā vyavahāravirahaḥ syāt tadā tadanyāpekṣaṃ syāditi sādhyasya tadvayavahārayogyatvasyaabhāve vyāpakaviruddhopalabdhyā avadhūyamānaṃ tathā pratīyamānatvamapetabādhake viṣayetathā vyavasthāyogyatayaiva vyāpyata iti vyāptisiddheḥ sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvamapinopanyastasya hetorantikamupasapaṃtīti siddhamadhyakṣa viṣayasyāpi jñānajñeyabhedasyoktānumānavyavahāryatvamahāryamiti atrocyate  kimidaṃ vijñānaṃ nāma yato bhedena pratītiḥ tathā vyavahāraṃ sādhayet yadi hi jñāyateneneti jñānaṃ jānātīti vā ubhayathāpi jñeyāpekṣaṃ lakṣaṇametat  na cabāhyāpalāpino jñeyaṃ nāma kiñcidasti siddham yatastadadhigatisādhanaṃ jñānaṃ syāt  tathāhi idaṃ jñānamidaṃ jñeyamiti vyavahāro vyāpāraviśeṣakṛto vā syāt dvaitavādinojātiniyato vā  prathamapakṣe jñānasya vā jñeye jñeyasya vā jñāne vyāpāra  parasparaṃ vobhayoḥ atrāpi prathamapakṣe nirvartako vikārako veti vikalpāḥ tatra na tāvat jñeye jñānavyāpāro nirvartakaḥ śakyobhidhātum adṛśyaviṣayavyālopaprasaṅgāt  na ca tathaivābhyupagamo yuktaḥ tadaiva kenacit dṛṣṭeḥ  tajjñānenanivartanābhyupagame ca parokṣasyāpi sthiteranapahnavaḥ  sa ca tena paścād dṛśyamānaḥtajjñānasyaiva nirvartako jāta iti na viṣaya syāt  sa na tasya dṛśya tajjñānajanyastvanyaeveti cet  ekasthānānupapatti  apratighatve prakāśarūpasya pratyātmavedyasya parāgocarasya vijñānarūpataiva mukhāntareṇa samarthitā syāt  nīlarūpatvānnaivamiti cet advaitabinduprakaraṇamkena punavijñānasya nīlākārotpattiniṣedhaḥ siddhaḥ tatsādhanāya sādhanānavadhānaprasaṅgāt tasmānna parokṣamasadeveti dvayavādino yuktam na cāyamabhyupagamopyasyeti nātra nirbaṃndhaḥ  pramāṇābhāve prameyābhāvamicchatopihi na parokṣasya sarvathābhāva evābhimataḥ api tu sannavaśyaṃ kasyacitpramāṇasya viṣaya syātstokāntareṇeti b anyathā satsaṃprayoge satīndriyāṇāṃ puruṣasya buddhijanmetyavācyaṃsyāt jñānāt prāk sato virahāt  sa punarabhyupagamo na nyāyya iti kimanena tanmātrasyavivakṣitatvādityalaṃ vistareṇa vikāryapakṣe tu yasya jñānasya yo vikāryorthaḥ sa grāhya iti vyavasthāyāṃ śokādinopahatāyā buddhevikāryamindriyamapi grāhyaṃ syāt malina mukhacchāyādayo vā  duḥkhajanitosauvikāra iti cet na upahatākārasaṃvedanādanyasya tasyānupalabdheḥ  nirloṭhitaṃ caitacchāstraityalaṃ prayāsena  atha naitādṛśotiśayaḥ prameyasya jñānāt kiṃ tarhi prakāśarūpasyotpattiriticet  atrāpi pakṣe ekagocaraḥ sarvagocaraḥ syāt  tadīyajñānanivṛttau tadrūpanivṛtteranyasthāpyadarśanaprasaṅgaḥ anyasthāpi tadupāyayogānnevamiti cet  tasyāpi nivṛttajñānasya tatprakāśaprasaṅgaḥ  tajjñānanivṛttau tadrūpānivṛttāvapyeṣa eva doṣaḥ  na hi kulālaprayatnaparihṛtāyāmṛdastameva prati ghaṭībhāvaḥ  dahanādvā dahanopadhāyakameva prati ghaṭasya gaurabhāvaḥ  evaṃtarhi upakāritvamapi svarūpamasya sarvasādhāraṇaṃ syāt na caivam  tato yathā ghaṭatvenasādhāraṇopyeṣa nārthaṃkāriṇā rūpeṇa tathā prakāśarūpeṇāpi na sthāditi koyaṃ prasaṅgaḥ athopakāryaviśeṣopakāritāsya sādhāraṇī  puruṣaviśeṣāpekṣaprakāśatāpyasya sarvasādhāraṇītisamānam na samānam  upakāritvaṃ hi nāma sākṣādupakāraḥ pravṛttiyogyatāmātraṃ vāabhimataṃ syāt  tatra yogyatāmātraṃ sarvasādhāraṇamiti na tatra vivādaḥ  prathamapakṣetu upakāralakṣaṇa kāryakarmaṇi sahakāribhāvosya yathaikatra tathānyatrāpi ki na syāditicodyārthaḥ  na cāyaṃ nyāya avyavadhānādyapekṣatvāt  tato yatsantānavartinaḥ upādāna syopanidhiḥ tatraiva sāhāyakamasyeti kathaṃ vyavahitādau puṣṭiḥ  tathā yadi prakāśaityapi kāryāntarajananadvāreṇa vyavahāra iṣṭaḥ syāt tadā syādapyevam  yathāhureke tula jaiminisū   jñānaśromitranibandhāvalobuddhilakṣaṇavyaktijanakatvameva tasya vyaktatvamiti  tadā hi yasyaiva buddherupādānaṃ samanantarasaṃkhyātaṃ nopanipātabhāgi sādhanāntaraṃ vā tasyaiva nāsau sahakāradānavirahād vyakto yuktaḥ dūṣaṇāntaraṃ ca tatrāpi vakṣyāmaḥ na caivaṃ yujyate jñānāt prakāśarūpasyaiva viṣayasyotpattirityetasya pakṣasyavicintyamānatvāt  kāryāntaradvāreṇa tu vyaktavyavahāre na tatastathotpanna iti prakṛtakṣatiḥ  tathotpattau durvāra sādhāraṇatva prasaṅgaḥ  upakārakatvamapi hi yāvadeva bhinnasantānavati sukhādijanakatvaṃ tāvadeva tadapekṣayā a sādhāraṇam  yadā tu sukhādirūpatvamevābhyupagamyeta tadā ka sādhāraṇatvaniṣedhāya prabhuḥ  nanu tathāpi yadekasyasukhaṃ na tadanyasyeti cet  arthasya dharma sādhāraṇatvamasādhāraṇatvaṃ jñānasya tataḥtadātmaniyataṃ sukhādi na parasādhāraṇamanugrahādirūpatveneti yuktam  bāhyarūpaṃ tu svīkriyamāṇaṃ sādhāraṇameva tatkāryatvepi hyanugrahasya sukhasaṃvidupādeyakṣaṇāntararūpatvāt  tadvadevasādhāraṇatvamasādhāraṇatvaṃ ceti evaṃ na caitrajanitaṃ maitrasya tatputratvaṃ nāma kiñcid gauratvamiva yat sādhāraṇaṃsyāt api tu tajjanitatvamevāsya tatputratvaṃ vyavahrayate  sa ca jananavyāpāraścaitrasyanānyasādhāraṇaḥ  tathā tannimittopi vyapadeśaḥ tajjanitavyapadeśavat  gauratvaṃ tu tatkṛtamapina tatkṛtameva guṇāntaratvāditi sādhāraṇaṃ yuktam  na hyasau pitureva gauraḥ kiṃ tu parasyāpi evaṃ na jñānakṛtatvamevārthasya vyaktatvaṃ vyavahitādya viśiṣṭarūpasya kiṃ tu tadatiśāyinaḥprakāśarūpasyotpattirityabhyupagama  anyathā na vyakta ukto viṣayaḥ syāt  tathā vyavahāra mātraṃ tu tannimittaṃ syāt yathā gauratvameva tajjanyatāmātreṇa vyavaharataḥ sautrāntikasya vātajjanakatvena  yathā ca tasya janakajñānāntarasya viṣayatāprasaṅgaḥ tathāsyāpi janyajñānasyetijñānārthayorhetuphalabhāvasamayātikramamātramatiricyate  sādhāraṇatvaparihārastūbhayorapi  natu vyaktirūpārthotpattinirvāha itosya siddhaḥ prakāśotpādane sarva prati prākāśyasaṃbhavaḥ  utpādanāprakāśatvasthitau naikamapi prati iti saṃgrahaḥ yathāhi niviḍāndhakārapihitayorāmapakaghaṭayorekatra vahnijanitatvamevavyaktatvamabhidadhāno nākṣayogyatāṃ tattvataḥ samādhātumīśaḥ tathāyamapi jñānajanitatvaadvaitabinduprakaraṇammeva dṛśyatāmiti  yadi tu pradopādiva prakāśarūpasyotpatti vijñānādapi svīkriyatetadā parokṣaghaṭādasya viparyayaḥ paryavasyati  sādhāraṇadoṣastu dustyajaḥ pradīpavyaktopi tarhi ghaṭa sarvasya prakāśa syāditi cet  yādṛśī pradīpakṛtāprakāśatā anandhakārāvasthā yogyadeśasthatvādyapekṣajñānajananayogyatārūpā sā sādhāraṇīeva  jñānakṛtaiva tu vikalpasmṛtyabhilāṣādinā pravṛttyādisādhanī niyatā  sāpiyadi bhāsurateva tasya niṣpannā khyāyate hanta sādhāraṇī pravṛttyādestatkālasātādināvā sādhanī sarvasya syādityuktaprāyam  tasmātutpādamātretiśayāntare vājñānātprakāśo na hi bāhyarāśeḥ prakāśarūpasya samudbhave tuprasahya sādhāraṇatāprasaṅgaḥ b tasmāt jñānavyāpāro na grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇavyavasthānibandhanamiti astu tarhi jñeyasya jñāne vyāpārād grāhyatvamiti cet na indriyasyāpiprasaṅgāt  sarūpajanakasya vā tattve samanantarapratyayaviśeṣeṇa vyabhicārāt  bāhyatvesatīti viśeṣaṇasya ca tadvādinyeva śobhāsaṃbhavāditi nāyamapi pakṣaḥ kṣamaḥ  mā bhūtsārūpyamarthādutpadyamānaṃ jñānaṃ tadadhigativyāpāreṇa grāhakamityubhayavyāpārapakṣostu tatrārthavyāpārānnāvyāpṛtānāṃ grahaṇaṃ jñānavyāpārāśrayānnendriyasyāpi na hi jñānasya tatrādhigativyāpāra iti cet  nāyamapi nyāyaḥ  sāhiadhigativiṣayasvarūpā jñānarūpārthāntaraṃ jñānāntaraṃ vā syāt  prathame pakṣe viṣayātmavattasya api siddherjñānavyāpāravirahaḥ  tadvad vā viṣayasyāpi jñānavyāpārāpekṣaṇeprācīno doṣaḥ  dvitīye tu jñānasyātmanyeva vyāpāra iti vyāhatam vyāpāra evādhigatirityatrāpyetadeva dūṣaṇam vyāpāratadvatorabhedasiddheḥ  evameva jñānajñeyadharmatvaparikalpanamapāstaṃ draṣṭavyam arthāntaratve ca viṣayasya kimāyātam yathendriyasya  yato nīlaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nendriyamiti syāt tasya sādhigatiriti cet  jñānajanyāyā kiṃkṛtastatsaṃbandha  tasyāpivyāpārāditi cet  evaṃ tarhi ubhayorubhayavyāpārasiddhā sādhigatiriti parasparaṃgrāhyatvaṃ grāhakatvaṃ vā syāt  na caivamindriyagrahaṇaprasaṅga parihāraḥ  na hi cākṣurvyāpāramantareṇa rūpedhigatiḥ jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalauathendriyasya jñāna eva vyāpāro nādhigatau rūpasya tu tatrāpīti cet  konāma vibhāgamīdṛśaṃ katu samarthonyatra jāḍyāt  na hi jñānajñeyābhyāṃ bhinnamarthāntaramadhigamarūpameva kiñcidupalabhyate yatra yāvat jñānasyaiva vyāpāraḥ parikalpyeta tatra caviṣayasyāpyasti nendriyasya kalyāṇakāmatāmātrametat  adhigaterarthasya ca viṣayaviṣayībhāvalakṣaṇa eva saṃbandha iti cet  nanu sa evāyaṃ viṣayaviṣayībhāvo vyāpāravikalpena parīkṣyate  sa ca yasya na jñānajñeyayoḥ siddhaḥ tasyādhigamaviṣayayorapi kathaṃsidhyet  adhigatervā viṣayatvamakasmādicchan jñānasya kathaṃ pratikṣipet  astitāvadayaṃ vyavahāra iti cet  asti kevalaṃ kimasya mūlamiti cintyate  asaṃkīrṇalakṣaṇasvarūpavyavasthā vā anādivitathavikalpābhyāsavāsanā veti stamkimasyā bījamiti cet  kimanena  na hi pareṇa tadaparijñāne asmābhirabhimatāsaṃkīrṇamanayorlakṣaṇamupadarśitaṃ bhavati  etena jñānāntaratvaparikalpanamadhigaterapātasyāpi tadvadeva tadviṣaa  yatvasyāsiddheḥ  atadviṣayayā cādhigatyāsortho jñāta iti mahatī prekṣā  etena jñānavyāpāraṃ vādakāle nārthaṃ kurvatī vikurvatīvā buddhistadviṣayocyate kiṃ tu tadadhigatimātramātanvatīti kalpanamapāstam  tasmānnavyāpāradvāreṇāyaṃ jñānajñeyavyavahāra iti sthitam nāpi jātiniyataḥ kacit kadācit kasyacit kenacit jñeyatayā vyavasthāpanāt  na hi nisarganiyatānāṃ gotvādīnāmīdṛśī vyavasthā  adyāpi vāvaśyavācyolakṣaṇabhedo na ca śakya iti tadabhāve tu sattāmātraṃ jñānasya jñeyasya vā tattvanimittamiti sarvaḥ sarvārthabodha sidhyet  na vā kaścidapi viprakarṣābhāvāt  nanu cāstipratyāsattirindriyāṇāmarthaiḥ saṃyogasamavāyādilakṣaṇā tadbalādupajāyamānaṃ jñānaṃ tattadarthaniyataṃ ṣoḍhāsannikarṣavirahaviprakṛṣṭārthavyāvṛttaṃ ca sidhyatīti kathamatiprasaṅgaḥ  etadapiyatkiñcat  utpattiniyamo hyanena sidhyet na tu kañcit prati grāhakatvaniyamovijñānasya  tathā hi saṃyogādisannikarṣabalādarthena jñānaṃ janyate na tadvirahiṇāvyavahitādineti bhavatu kasya punastadgrāhakamiti na niścayaḥ  yenaiva tajjanitamiticet  ātmamanokṣasaṃyogādayopi grāhyā iti nātiprasaṅganivṛttiḥ  na hi viṣayābhimatepyasya kaścidupayoga indriyādiṣu saṃbhavī yena grahaṇavibhāga syāt paricchittijananaṃ vyāpārāntaraṃ vā anantarameva cintitam advaitabinduprakaraṇamtatra tasyaiva prakāśanaṃ tena nātiprasaṅga iti cet  grāhyagrāhakābhimatabhāgayoḥaśakyāpahnavaḥ prakāśosti karaṇādhikaraṇaśaktinibandhanaṃ tu yadi kiñcidasti taducyatām  na ca sahaprakāśanamātrameva nibandhanaṃ candradvayasya tayoreva vā parasparagrahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ  nīlapītayorvā  ekaścandro mṛṣā dvitīyabhāgo jaḍaḥ  manasaśca dvayorekadāvṛttyabhāvādityādi tu bāhyārthavādasthitī yuktam  tadarthaṃcāyaṃ vicāra iti  yadā tubhāgayorapi na sahaprakāśanaṃ jñānasya jñānāntareṇa sahabhuvānanubhaveṣṭeḥ tadeyamapigatirnāsti  yadi tu durnītasamayānurodho na bādhakastadāntaḥ parisphuratprītiparitāpādyākārastuṣārakarādyākāraśca samasamayameva vedyata iti tadapi nibandhanamanucintyate na cakṣamata iti sthitam iti  tasyāpikiṃ ca ghaṭenendriyasannikarṣo noṣṭreṇeti tadanubhavādeva niśceyam  tadanubhavatvaṃ cāsyatatsannikarṣeṇotpatteritītaretarāśrayadoṣaḥ prakārāntareṇa tadanubhavasiddhau vā sannikarṣottarasyavaiyarthyāt  api ca tatsannikarṣeṇotpattestadanubhavatve vikalpamātravyavasthāpitospaṣṭapratibhāsorthasyānubhava syāt na spaṣṭaḥ maitrasya caitraputratvatadgauratvavacceti dṛṣṭakṣatiḥ  tadayaṃspaṣṭatayā pratibhāsa b mānorthābhimato bhāga kārakānta vyāpāracintāvaidhuryātprītiparitāpādivat svayaṃ viditamevātmānamākalayati yospi manyatepūrvikaiva tu sāmagrī sajñānaṃ viṣayakṣaṇam sālokarūpavat kuryād yena syāt sahavedanam sāmagrathā yadi niṣpanno vyaktortho vedanena kim sādhāraṇatvadoṣaśca nāvyaktau ca sphuṭābhatā ekasāmagrathadhīnatvamātreṇaivaṃvyavasthiteḥ kiṃ caivamindriyasyāpi prakāśatvaṃ prasajyate sthairye tu viṣayopyekasāmagrījanitaḥ katham viṣayeṇa ca vijñānaṃ saṃvedyata sahasphurat atha vittirasaṃvittiḥ sarvameva subhāṣitam svasaṃvedyatvapakṣedya duḥsaṃvedyamidaṃ bahiḥ jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalausāmagrayā eva śakteścedvibhakto vedyavedako rasarūpavadutpanna svabhāve konuyujyatām vedyavedakayo rūpaṃ niyataṃ yadi lakṣitam tadutpādanaparyeṣṭeḥ sāmagrī śaktirucyatām nairogye tu svarūpeṇa siddhe vācyaṃ bhiṣagbalam vedyavedakayo rūpaṃ na cādyāpi nirūpyate tataḥ svarūpe vaktavye sāmagrī parivartanam aprastutābhidhānaṃ vā ḍiṇḍikācāra eva vā tasmānna vedakaṃ kiñcinna vedyaṃ na ca vedanam yadapekṣya tadā stheyaṃ svaprakāśamidaṃ jagat prakāśate hi nīlādinaṃ cānyat tatprakāśakam tatsvaprakāśatā siddhā vijñānatvaṃ tadeva naḥ ityantaraślokāḥ evaṃ sati na vijñānaṃ nāma kiñcit niyatamasti yato bhedena pratīyamānatvaṃghaṭādyākārasya tadbhedaṃ sādhayedityaprasiddha viśeṣaṇo heturasiddhidoṣagrastaḥ  sādhyaśca tatobhedavyavahāro viśeṣaṇāsiddhereva na prakṛtopayogaṃ puṣṇāti  vijñānarūpatvepi hi ghaṭasya yataḥkutaścidvijñānāntarādapi bhedasiddherna bhedamātrasiddhayopayogaḥ  tasmād viśiṣṭāvadhitvenasādhyo bhedo na ca tamavadhi sphuṭayituṃ śakta iti vyartha upanyāsaḥ nanu vijñānavādinopi vijñānavyavahārosti  sa yathā tathā vā bhavannasmākamapitadupādhisādhane śaraṇībhaviṣyati  loke ca kiñcid vijñānamiti pratītamasti  tata evabhedaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ  nātrāsmallakṣaṇena kiñcit na ca vastubalapravṛttānumāne samayānurodha iti cet vijñānavādinastāvad vijñānatvaṃ prakāśatā grāhya grāhakasaṃkhyātabhāgayoḥ sadṛśī ca sā advaitabinduprakaraṇamjñānānnāma tato bhedaḥ prakāśatvādvibhinnatā sā pratijñāyamānaiva vyastāmīṣu ghaṭādiṣu hetvasiddhiśca na hi na prakāśante ghaṭādayaḥ ebhyastvanyo yadā dharmī dharmāsiddhistadā sphuṭā bhedena jñāyamānatvasvarūpāsiddhireva capuna prakāśamāsthāturhetvasiddhayādayaḥ punaḥ tanna prativādimatāpekṣayā kṣamaḥ loke cāntaḥsphuradidaṃ vijñānamiti gīyate tadajñeyātmanastasmādbhedasi addhayāpi ki phalam vedyavedakarūpeṇa siddhayodi sādhyate bhedavyavahṛtirnīlajñānayoḥ pauruṣaṃ bhavet avedyavedakākārasvaprakāśasvabhāvayoḥasādhāraṇayorantarbahirvyavasitispṛśoḥ ahaṅkārāṅgaghaṭayorbhedena yadi tuṣyasi bhinnasantānayoḥ kiṃ na bhedasiddhirmude tava atha na sphuraṇaṃ bhinnasantānapathavartinaḥ vedyavedakatāhānirbhānepi na kimīkṣyate bhinnasantānayoraikyaṃ na kaścinmanyate yadi yadi manyeta tatrāpi bhedasādhanasādhunā aho mahatparākāntaṃ sthāne bāhyāpavādinā santāna bhedepi yadā tu buddhayorvedāntikādiḥ pravadatyabhedam na nīlabuddhayorapi caikyamanyastadā ka eṣa vyasanābhiyogaḥ santi hi vijñānavādinopi svayaṃ nātaḥ pareṇeti na kiṃ matiḥ dṛṣṭopi bhedavyāpāraḥ prastute yadi nocitaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ sthāpyabhede tu bhavadbhiḥ kalpyate katham tunanu prakāśabhedī yaḥ svayamityādi dṛśyate tatrāpi nātmani vyāptasvabhāvastu tathocyate evaṃ prakāśate buddhiḥ svayamityapi gamyatām khe svayaṃ śūnyatā yadvat paravyāpāravāraṇāt advaitabinduprakaraṇamtathātmavyāpṛtibhrāntibhraṃśanāya paraśrutiḥ na vyāpāravaśā vṛttistadrūpaṃ tu tathā tadā yathā nirlepamākāśaṃ prakāśaṃ ca svayaṃ tathā asādhāraṇametañca pūrvameva samarthitam tataḥ prakāśatā nāma sādhāraṇyaparakriye sarvatra tulyadoṣatvānnirākṛtya vyavasthitā tābhyāṃ virodho yuktyāto labdhastādrūpyanirṇayaḥ tasmādviparyaṃye hetorvirodhādeva na sthitiḥ prakāśatā ca siddheti jñānarūpāḥ śitādayaḥ taddbāhyarūpapratyāśā pratyāśaiva hi kevalā yadi svarūpamākārāścitra taika dhiyaḥ katham bhedaḥ pratyaṇu vā buddheḥ tathā nānyonyavedanam mithastathāpi vā vittī bāhyavallakṣaṇakṣatiḥ bhedepyevaṃ dhiyasteṣāṃ prakāśaghaṭanā katham athaivameva nirbhāsaḥ svasantānadhiyo dhiyā alīkākārarāśervā koparādhī bahilarbhuvaḥ alīkavedane kiṃ ca prakāśaṃ ca na cāparam ato vipakṣasāmānyo hetuḥ saṃśayasādhanaḥ alīkamanyatvetīdaṃ  vyāvṛttyantaramīritam prakāśasyāstu bodhatā SETTIERTjñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalaubhedābhedavikalpopi na prakāśasya bādhakaḥ na vā yathoktasādhyena vyāpteriti kimarthaṃkaḥ pareṇa parasaṃvitti yobhimanyeta taṃ prati śeṣaṃ syādapi doṣāya brūmaḥ svapnepi na tvidam ekānekatvavirahāt niḥsvabhāvamidaṃ jaḍam yathā tathā na kiñcittaṃ sattaikasya kathaṃ tataḥ prakāśamānaṃ nīlādi jaḍaṃ vājaḍameva vā iti prakaraṇesmābhirbuddhive heturucyate tatraikānekaviraho yadi dharmāntarārpakaḥ kiṃ naśchinnaṃ tāvatāpi nīlāderjaḍatā na hi sattāyāṃ nanu siddhāyāṃ jaḍaṃ vājaḍameva vā asatturaṅgaśṛṅgādi na hi tattvenumīyate tathāpya prastutamidaṃ sattācintāviyogataḥ siddhāyāmeva sattāyāṃ viśeṣaścintyate yataḥ sattāyāṃ saṃśayepyasmāt sacced vijñānameva tat tataścādūṣaṇākhyātirasattāsiddhibādhayoḥ prasiddhimātrarūpeṇa dharmitvānnāpyanāśrayaḥ anyathā niḥsvabhāvatvahetorapyāśrayaḥ katham tasminna bhāvamātraṃ cet jñānatāmātramatra ca bāhyavastutvasiddhistu dvayorapi virodhinī vastutopādhibodhatvaṃ sādhyamatra tvayeti cet bodhatvamātra prastāve viśeṣa kuta īdṛśaḥ jñānatvaṃ vastutāvyāptaṃ tadabhāve bhavenna cet viruddhāvyabhicāraḥ ka doṣo yadvāstu vastutā advaitabinduprakaraṇamkiṃ ca prakāśamātrātmavyatiriktānyathāthavā sattā niṣeddhayābhimatā niḥsvabhāvatvahetunā niṣedhe vyatiriktāyā na prakāśātmavāraṇam asyaiva vāraṇe kena vāraṇādhyakṣabhāsinaḥ anumānaṃ pramāṇatvād bādhakaṃ yadi kasyacit pratyakṣamapi tadbhāvāt sādhakaṃ kiṃ na kasyacit avaśyamantedhyakṣasya prāmāṇyamanumāśrayet prakāśamātrarūpe ca nānumāpekṣamakṣajam athāyamanumānasya viṣayokṣadhiyoparaḥ prakāśarūpedhyakṣatvādanumāvasaraḥ kutaḥ atha pratyakṣasiddhaṃ yanna tasyeva nirākriyā vyāvṛttibhedaḥ kaścātra vicārāsahatā yadi vijñānasyaiva dharmostu śaśaśṛṅgasamaṃ bahiḥ arthaśaktiviyoge vā dharmostu dhiya eva saḥ arthaśaktiviyogaśca vicārāsahtā ca sā jñānasyaiva na bāhyasyetyayate kimataḥ param prakāśasyaiva cinteyaṃ tadgandhopi bahinaṃ hi tannāgaśṛṅgasāmyesya siddhe ki na kṛtārthatā bahivaṃdavabhāseṣu prajñaptā rūparāśitā saṃskārādvedanāsaṃjñe b abhinne kiṃ na bhedi te mūlamevāprakāśasya duḥsthaṃ sattāvyavasthiteḥ prakāśarūpasya sato dharmāntaramabādhakam prakāśasyāpi taddoṣād yadi sattā davīyasī aprakāśopyasattāyāḥ kimanyat sādhayiṣyati jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalauasattaivāprakāśasya prakāśasya tu nātmanā tenaivāsattvamityuktaṃ kalpite na tu yujyate prakāśamānasya punaḥ prakāśādeva satyatā abhāvovasitenaiva keśasyāpi jaḍātmanā prakāśasaṃmatasyāpi nīlāderata eva hi satyamarthakriyaivoktā tāṃ vinā na bhidā dvayoḥ kriyāmātrānubandhācca vijñānasyāpyanityatā kriyābhāvo yadā tvasmin sattā mukhyaiva bhāsanāt na kṣaṇitvaṃ tadā tasya sattvaṃ ca vyabhicāyaṃtaḥ sattvamarthakriyārūpaṃ sādhanaṃ tanna duṣyati na vā tasyāpyanityatvaṃ parihṛtya daśāntaram tatkṣaṇasyaiva saṃvitteranyathā na bhidā kacit kāryakāraṇabhāvoyamāyātastahiṃ cennanu sāṃvṛtasyāniṣedhotra kṣaṇitāpyasya sāṃvṛtī tattvato nityarūpaṃ cet saṃvṛtāvapi yanna sat anityapratiṣedhācet tathāpyasthāgatiḥ kutaḥ bhāvaṃ kañcit puraskṛtya bhedābhedāvudīrayet deśakālādibhedena svavinmātre tu kaḥ kramaḥ svarūpaṃ buddhiraparairna yauti na bhinatti ca svaparapravibhāgo hi dhiyo yācitamaṇḍanam anyasyāvācyatā
